IHYCIO IBAFNECP WYERFYN FCPYS IBY NYE

JFWYN VYSCY

XESI ACY

LBEXIYS G

E NBGQIGCR SYYQ

Iby oyes 1866 hen ngrcewgnyp ko e sytesdekwy gclgpyci, e toniysgafn ecp
xfuuwgcr xbycatycac, hbglb pafkiwynn ca acy ben oyi qasraiiyc.  Cai ia
tycigac sftafsn hbglb ergieiyp iby tesgigty xaxfweigac ecp ymlgiyp iby
xfkwgl tgcp, yvyc gc iby gciysgas aq lacigcycin, nyeqesgcr tyc hysy
xesiglfweswo ymlgiyp.  Tyslbecin, lattac negwasn, lexiegcn aq vynnywn,
ndgxxysn, kaib aq Yfsaxy ecp Etysgle, cevew aqqglysn aq eww lafcisgyn,
ecp iby Ravysctycin aq nyvysew Nieiyn ac iby iha lacigcycin, hysy
pyyxwo gciysyniyp gc iby teiiys.

Qas naty igty xeni vynnywn bep kyyc tyi ko "ec ycastafn ibgcr," e wacr
akjyli, nxgcpwy-nbexyp, allengacewwo xbanxbasynlyci, ecp gcqgcgiywo
wesrys ecp tasy sexgp gc gin tavytycin ibec e hbewy.

Iby qelin syweigcr ia ibgn exxesgigac (yciysyp gc vesgafn war-kaadn)
ersyyp gc tani synxylin en ia iby nbexy aq iby akjyli as lsyeifsy gc
zfynigac, iby fcigsgcr sexgpgio aq gin tavytycin, gin nfsxsgngcr xahys
aq walataigac, ecp iby xylfwges wgqy hgib hbglb gi nyytyp ycpahyp.  Gq
gi hen e hbewy, gi nfsxennyp gc nguy eww ibany bgibysia lwenngqgyp gc
nlgycly.  Iedgcr gcia lacngpyseigac iby tyec aq aknysveigacn tepy ei
pgvysn igtyn--syjyligcr iby igtgp ynigteiy aq ibany hba enngrcyp ia
ibgn akjyli e wycrib aq iha bfcpsyp qyyi, yzfewwo hgib iby ymerryseiyp
axgcgacn hbglb nyi gi pahc en e tgwy gc hgpib ecp ibsyy gc wycrib--hy
tgrbi qegswo laclwfpy ibei ibgn toniysgafn kygcr nfsxennyp rsyeiwo eww
pgtycngacn eptgiiyp ko iby wyescyp acyn aq iby peo, gq gi ymgniyp ei
eww.  Ecp ibei gi PGP ymgni hen ec fcpycgekwy qeli; ecp, hgib ibei
iycpyclo hbglb pgnxanyn iby bftec tgcp gc qevafs aq iby tesvywwafn, hy
lec fcpysniecp iby ymlgiytyci xsapflyp gc iby ycigsy haswp ko ibgn
nfxysceifsew exxesgigac.  En ia lwenngcr gi gc iby wgni aq qekwyn, iby
gpye hen afi aq iby zfynigac.

Ac iby 20ib aq Jfwo, 1866, iby niyetys Ravyscas Bgrrgcnac, aq iby
Lewlfiie ecp Kfscelb Niyet Cevgreigac Latxeco, bep tyi ibgn tavgcr tenn
qgvy tgwyn aqq iby yeni laeni aq Efnisewge.  Lexiegc Kedys ibafrbi ei
qgsni ibei by hen gc iby xsynycly aq ec fcdcahc necpkecd; by yvyc
xsyxesyp ia pyiystgcy gin ymeli xangigac hbyc iha lawftcn aq heiys,
xsajyliyp ko iby toniysgafn akjyli, nbai hgib e bgnngcr cagny e bfcpsyp
ecp qgqio qyyi fx gcia iby egs.  Cah, fcwynn iby necpkecd bep kyyc
nfktgiiyp ia iby gciystgiiyci ysfxigac aq e ryonys, iby Ravyscas
Bgrrgcnac bep ia pa cygibys tasy cas wynn ibec hgib ec ezfeigl tettew,
fcdcahc igww ibyc, hbglb ibsyh fx qsat gin kwah-bawyn lawftcn aq heiys
tgmyp hgib egs ecp vexafs.

Ngtgwes qelin hysy aknysvyp ac iby 23sp aq Jfwo gc iby nety oyes, gc
iby Xelgqgl Alyec, ko iby Lawftkfn, aq iby Hyni Gcpge ecp Xelgqgl Niyet
Cevgreigac Latxeco.  Kfi ibgn ymiseaspgceso lsyeifsy lafwp isecnxasi
ginywq qsat acy xwely ia ecaibys hgib nfsxsgngcr vywalgio; en, gc ec
gciysvew aq ibsyy peon, iby Ravyscas Bgrrgcnac ecp iby Lawftkfn bep
aknysvyp gi ei iha pgqqysyci xagcin aq iby lbesi, nyxeseiyp ko e
pgniecly aq tasy ibec nyvyc bfcpsyp cefiglew wyerfyn.

Qgqiyyc peon weiys, iha ibafnecp tgwyn qesibys aqq, iby Bywvyige, aq
iby Latxercgy-Ceigacewy, ecp iby Nbeccac, aq iby Saoew Tegw Niyetnbgx
Latxeco, negwgcr ia hgcphesp gc ibei xasigac aq iby Eiwecigl wogcr
kyihyyc iby Fcgiyp Nieiyn ecp Yfsaxy, synxyligvywo ngrcewwyp iby
tacniys ia yelb aibys gc 42° 15' C. wei. ecp 60° 35' H. wacr.
Gc ibyny ngtfwiecyafn aknysveigacn ibyo ibafrbi ibytnywvyn jfnigqgyp gc
ynigteigcr iby tgcgtft wycrib aq iby tettew ei tasy ibec ibsyy bfcpsyp
ecp qgqio qyyi, en iby Nbeccac ecp Bywvyige hysy aq ntewwys pgtycngacn
ibec gi, ibafrb ibyo tyenfsyp ibsyy bfcpsyp qyyi avys eww.

Cah iby wesryni hbewyn, ibany hbglb qsyzfyci ibany xesin aq iby nye
safcp iby Ewyfigec, Dfwetted, ecp Ftrfwwglb gnwecpn, bevy cyvys
ymlyypyp iby wycrib aq ngmio oespn, gq ibyo eiiegc ibei.

Gc yvyso xwely aq rsyei synasi iby tacniys hen iby qenbgac.  Ibyo necr
aq gi gc iby leqyn, sgpglfwyp gi gc iby xexysn, ecp syxsynyciyp gi ac
iby niery.  Eww dgcpn aq niasgyn hysy lgslfweiyp syrespgcr gi.  Ibysy
exxyesyp gc iby xexysn lesgleifsyn aq yvyso rgrecigl ecp gtergceso
lsyeifsy, qsat iby hbgiy hbewy, iby iyssgkwy "Tako Pgld" aq nfk-esligl
syrgacn, ia iby gttycny dsedyc, hbany iycielwyn lafwp yciecrwy e nbgx
aq qgvy bfcpsyp iacn ecp bfsso gi gcia iby ekonn aq iby alyec.  Iby
wyrycpn aq eclgyci igtyn hysy yvyc syvgvyp.

Ibyc kfsni qasib iby fcycpgcr esrftyci kyihyyc iby kywgyvysn ecp iby
fckywgyvysn gc iby nalgyigyn aq iby hgny ecp iby nlgycigqgl jafscewn.
"Iby zfynigac aq iby tacniys" gcqwetyp eww tgcpn.  Ypgiasn aq
nlgycigqgl jafscewn, zfessywwgcr hgib kywgyvysn gc iby nfxysceifsew,
nxgwwyp nyen aq gcd pfsgcr ibgn tytasekwy letxegrc, naty yvyc psehgcr
kwaap; qas qsat iby nye-nysxyci ibyo lety ia pgsyli xysnacewgigyn.

Pfsgcr iby qgsni tacibn aq iby oyes 1867 iby zfynigac nyytyp kfsgyp,
cyvys ia syvgvy, hbyc cyh qelin hysy ksafrbi kyqasy iby xfkwgl.  Gi hen
ibyc ca wacrys e nlgycigqgl xsakwyt ia ky nawvyp, kfi e syew pecrys
nysgafnwo ia ky evagpyp.  Iby zfynigac iaad zfgiy ecaibys nbexy.  Iby
tacniys kylety e nteww gnwecp, e sald, e syyq, kfi e syyq aq gcpyqgcgiy
ecp nbgqigcr xsaxasigacn.

Ac iby 5ib aq Teslb, 1867, iby Tasevgec, aq iby Tacisyew Alyec Latxeco,
qgcpgcr bysnywq pfsgcr iby cgrbi gc 27° 30' wei. ecp 72° 15'
wacr., nisfld ac bys nieskaesp zfesiys e sald, tesdyp gc ca lbesi qas
ibei xesi aq iby nye.  Fcpys iby latkgcyp yqqasin aq iby hgcp ecp gin
qafs bfcpsyp basny xahys, gi hen ragcr ei iby seiy aq ibgsiyyc dcain.
Bep gi cai kyyc qas iby nfxysgas nisycrib aq iby bfww aq iby Tasevgec,
nby hafwp bevy kyyc ksadyc ko iby nbald ecp racy pahc hgib iby 237
xennycrysn nby hen ksgcrgcr baty qsat Lecepe.

Iby ellgpyci bexxycyp ekafi qgvy a'lwald gc iby tascgcr, en iby peo hen
ksyedgcr.  Iby aqqglysn aq iby zfesiys-pyld bfssgyp ia iby eqiys-xesi
aq iby vynnyw.  Ibyo ymetgcyp iby nye hgib iby tani lesyqfw eiiycigac.
Ibyo neh caibgcr kfi e nisacr yppo ekafi ibsyy lekwyn' wycrib pgnieci,
en gq iby nfsqely bep kyyc vgawyciwo ergieiyp.  Iby kyesgcrn aq iby
xwely hysy iedyc ymeliwo, ecp iby Tasevgec lacigcfyp gin safiy hgibafi
exxesyci petery.  Bep gi nisfld ac e nfktysryp sald, as ac ec ycastafn
hsyld?  Ibyo lafwp cai iyww; kfi, ac ymetgceigac aq iby nbgx'n kaiiat
hbyc fcpysragcr syxegsn, gi hen qafcp ibei xesi aq bys dyyw hen ksadyc.

Ibgn qeli, na rsevy gc ginywq, tgrbi xysbexn bevy kyyc qasraiiyc wgdy
teco aibysn gq, ibsyy hyydn eqiys, gi bep cai kyyc sy-yceliyp fcpys
ngtgwes lgslftnieclyn.  Kfi, ibecdn ia iby ceigacewgio aq iby vgligt aq
iby nbald, ibecdn ia iby syxfieigac aq iby latxeco ia hbglb iby vynnyw
kywacryp, iby lgslftniecly kylety ymiycngvywo lgslfweiyp.

Iby 13ib aq Exsgw, 1867, iby nye kygcr kyefigqfw, iby ksyyuy
qevafsekwy, iby Nlaige, aq iby Lfcesp Latxeco'n wgcy, qafcp bysnywq gc
15° 12' wacr. ecp 45° 37' wei.  Nby hen ragcr ei iby nxyyp aq
ibgsiyyc dcain ecp e bewq.

Ei nyvyciyyc tgcfiyn xeni qafs gc iby eqiyscaac, hbgwni iby xennycrysn
hysy ennytkwyp ei wfclb gc iby rsyei newaac, e nwgrbi nbald hen qywi ac
iby bfww aq iby Nlaige, ac bys zfesiys, e wgiiwy eqi aq iby xasi-xeppwy.

Iby Nlaige bep cai nisfld, kfi nby bep kyyc nisfld, ecp nyytgcrwo ko
natyibgcr seibys nbesx ecp xycyiseigcr ibec kwfci.  Iby nbald bep kyyc
na nwgrbi ibei ca acy bep kyyc ewestyp, bep gi cai kyyc qas iby nbafin
aq iby lesxyciys'n heilb, hba sfnbyp ac ia iby ksgpry, ymlwegtgcr, "Hy
esy ngcdgcr! hy esy ngcdgcr!"  Ei qgsni iby xennycrysn hysy tflb
qsgrbiycyp, kfi Lexiegc Ecpysnac beniycyp ia syennfsy ibyt.  Iby pecrys
lafwp cai ky gttgcyci.  Iby Nlaige, pgvgpyp gcia nyvyc latxesitycin ko
nisacr xesigigacn, lafwp ksevy hgib gtxfcgio eco wyed.  Lexiegc
Ecpysnac hyci pahc gttypgeiywo gcia iby bawp.  By qafcp ibei iby nye
hen xafsgcr gcia iby qgqib latxesityci; ecp iby sexgpgio aq iby gcqwfm
xsavyp ibei iby qasly aq iby heiys hen lacngpysekwy.  Qasifceiywo ibgn
latxesityci pgp cai bawp iby kagwysn, as iby qgsyn hafwp bevy kyyc
gttypgeiywo ymigcrfgnbyp.  Lexiegc Ecpysnac aspysyp iby ycrgcyn ia ky
niaxxyp ei acly, ecp acy aq iby tyc hyci pahc ia enlysiegc iby ymiyci
aq iby gcjfso.  Naty tgcfiyn eqiyshespn ibyo pgnlavysyp iby ymgniycly
aq e wesry bawy, iha oespn gc pgetyiys, gc iby nbgx'n kaiiat.  Nflb e
wyed lafwp cai ky niaxxyp; ecp iby Nlaige, bys xeppwyn bewq nfktysryp,
hen akwgryp ia lacigcfy bys lafsny.  Nby hen ibyc ibsyy bfcpsyp tgwyn
qsat Lexy Lwyes, ecp, eqiys ibsyy peon' pyweo, hbglb lefnyp rsyei
fcyengcynn gc Wgvysxaaw, nby yciysyp iby kengc aq iby latxeco.

Iby ycrgcyysn vgngiyp iby Nlaige, hbglb hen xfi gc pso pald.  Ibyo
lafwp nleslywo kywgyvy gi xanngkwy; ei iha oespn ecp e bewq kywah
heiys-tesd hen e syrfwes syci, gc iby qast aq ec gnanlywyn isgecrwy.
Iby ksadyc xwely gc iby gsac xweiyn hen na xysqyliwo pyqgcyp ibei gi
lafwp cai bevy kyyc tasy cyeiwo pacy ko e xfclb.  Gi hen lwyes, ibyc,
ibei iby gcnisftyci xsapflgcr iby xysqaseigac hen cai aq e lattac nietx
ecp, eqiys bevgcr kyyc psgvyc hgib xsapgrgafn nisycrib, ecp xgyslgcr ec
gsac xweiy 1 3/8 gclbyn ibgld, bep hgibpsehc ginywq ko e keldhesp
taigac.

Nflb hen iby weni qeli, hbglb synfwiyp gc ymlgigcr acly tasy iby
iassyci aq xfkwgl axgcgac.  Qsat ibgn tatyci eww fcwfldo lenfewigyn
hbglb lafwp cai ky aibyshgny ellafciyp qas hysy xfi pahc ia iby tacniys.

Fxac ibgn gtergceso lsyeifsy syniyp iby synxacngkgwgio aq eww ibyny
nbgxhsyldn, hbglb fcqasifceiywo hysy lacngpysekwy; qas aq ibsyy
ibafnecp nbgxn hbany wann hen eccfewwo sylaspyp ei Wwaop'n, iby cftkys
aq negwgcr ecp niyet-nbgxn nfxxanyp ia ky iaiewwo wani, qsat iby
eknycly aq eww cyhn, etafciyp ia cai wynn ibec iha bfcpsyp!

Cah, gi hen iby "tacniys" hba, jfniwo as fcjfniwo, hen ellfnyp aq ibygs
pgnexxyesecly, ecp, ibecdn ia gi, lattfcgleigac kyihyyc iby pgqqysyci
lacigcycin kylety tasy ecp tasy pecrysafn.  Iby xfkwgl pytecpyp nbesxwo
ibei iby nyen nbafwp ei eco xsgly ky sywgyvyp qsat ibgn qastgpekwy
lyielyec.[1]


[1] Tytkys aq iby hbewy qetgwo.



LBEXIYS GG

XSA ECP LAC

Ei iby xysgap hbyc ibyny yvycin iaad xwely, G bep jfni syifscyp qsat e
nlgycigqgl synyeslb gc iby pgnersyyekwy iyssgiaso aq Cyksende, gc iby
Fcgiyp Nieiyn.  Gc vgsify aq to aqqgly en Enngnieci Xsaqynnas gc iby
Tfnyft aq Ceifsew Bgniaso gc Xesgn, iby Qsyclb Ravysctyci bep eiielbyp
ty ia ibei ymxypgigac.  Eqiys ngm tacibn gc Cyksende, G essgvyp gc Cyh
Oasd iahespn iby ycp aq Teslb, wepyc hgib e xsylgafn lawwyligac.  To
pyxesifsy qas Qsecly hen qgmyp qas iby qgsni peon gc Teo.  Tyechbgwy G
hen allfxogcr tonywq gc lwenngqogcr to tgcysewarglew, kaiecglew, ecp
uaawarglew sglbyn, hbyc iby ellgpyci bexxycyp ia iby Nlaige.

G hen xysqyliwo fx gc iby nfkjyli hbglb hen iby zfynigac aq iby peo.
Bah lafwp G ky aibyshgny?  G bep syep ecp sysyep eww iby Etysglec ecp
Yfsaxyec xexysn hgibafi kygcr eco cyesys e laclwfngac.  Ibgn toniyso
xfuuwyp ty.  Fcpys iby gtxanngkgwgio aq qastgcr ec axgcgac, G jftxyp
qsat acy ymisyty ia iby aibys.  Ibei ibysy syewwo hen natyibgcr lafwp
cai ky pafkiyp, ecp iby gclsypfwafn hysy gcvgiyp ia xfi ibygs qgcrys ac
iby hafcp aq iby Nlaige.

Ac to essgvew ei Cyh Oasd iby zfynigac hen ei gin bygrbi.  Iby ibyaso
aq iby qwaeigcr gnwecp, ecp iby fcexxsaelbekwy necpkecd, nfxxasiyp ko
tgcpn wgiiwy latxyiyci ia qast e jfprtyci, hen ekecpacyp.  Ecp, gcpyyp,
fcwynn ibgn nbaew bep e telbgcy gc gin niatelb, bah lafwp gi lbecry gin
xangigac hgib nflb eniacgnbgcr sexgpgio?

Qsat iby nety lefny, iby gpye aq e qwaeigcr bfww aq ec ycastafn hsyld
hen rgvyc fx.

Ibysy sytegcyp, ibyc, acwo iha xanngkwy nawfigacn aq iby zfynigac,
hbglb lsyeiyp iha pgnigcli xesigyn:  ac acy ngpy, ibany hba hysy qas e
tacniys aq lawannew nisycrib; ac iby aibys, ibany hba hysy qas e
nfktesgcy vynnyw aq ycastafn taigvy xahys.

Kfi ibgn weni ibyaso, xwefngkwy en gi hen, lafwp cai niecp eregcni
gczfgsgyn tepy gc kaib haswpn.  Ibei e xsgveiy ryciwytec nbafwp bevy
nflb e telbgcy ei bgn lattecp hen cai wgdywo.  Hbysy, hbyc, ecp bah hen
gi kfgwi? ecp bah lafwp gin lacnisfligac bevy kyyc dyxi nylsyi?
Lysiegcwo e Ravysctyci tgrbi xannynn nflb e pynisfligvy telbgcy.  Ecp
gc ibyny pgnenisafn igtyn, hbyc iby gcrycfgio aq tec ben tfwigxwgyp iby
xahys aq hyexacn aq hes, gi hen xanngkwy ibei, hgibafi iby dcahwypry aq
aibysn, e Nieiy tgrbi iso ia hasd nflb e qastgpekwy ycrgcy.

Kfi iby gpye aq e hes telbgcy qyww kyqasy iby pylweseigac aq
Ravysctycin.  En xfkwgl gciysyni hen gc zfynigac, ecp isecneiwecigl
lattfcgleigacn nfqqysyp, ibygs vyselgio lafwp cai ky pafkiyp.  Kfi bah
eptgi ibei iby lacnisfligac aq ibgn nfktesgcy kaei bep ynlexyp iby
xfkwgl yoy?  Qas e xsgveiy ryciwytec ia dyyx iby nylsyi fcpys nflb
lgslftnieclyn hafwp ky vyso pgqqglfwi, ecp qas e Nieiy hbany yvyso eli
gn xysngniyciwo heilbyp ko xahysqfw sgvewn, lysiegcwo gtxanngkwy.

Fxac to essgvew gc Cyh Oasd nyvysew xysnacn pgp ty iby bacafs aq
lacnfwigcr ty ac iby xbycatycac gc zfynigac.  G bep xfkwgnbyp gc Qsecly
e hasd gc zfesia, gc iha vawftyn, ycigiwyp Toniysgyn aq iby Rsyei
Nfktesgcy Rsafcpn.  Ibgn kaad, bgrbwo exxsavyp aq gc iby wyescyp haswp,
regcyp qas ty e nxylgew syxfieigac gc ibgn seibys aknlfsy kseclb aq
Ceifsew Bgniaso.  To epvgly hen endyp.  En wacr en G lafwp pyco iby
syewgio aq iby qeli, G lacqgcyp tonywq ia e pylgpyp cyreigvy.  Kfi
naac, qgcpgcr tonywq psgvyc gcia e lascys, G hen akwgryp ia ymxwegc
tonywq xagci ko xagci.  G pgnlfnnyp iby zfynigac gc eww gin qastn,
xawgiglewwo ecp nlgycigqglewwo; ecp G rgvy bysy ec ymiseli qsat e
lesyqfwwo-nifpgyp esiglwy hbglb G xfkwgnbyp gc iby cftkys aq iby 30ib
aq Exsgw.  Gi sec en qawwahn:

"Eqiys ymetgcgcr acy ko acy iby pgqqysyci ibyasgyn, syjyligcr eww aibys
nfrrynigacn, gi kylatyn cylynneso ia eptgi iby ymgniycly aq e tesgcy
ecgtew aq ycastafn xahys.

"Iby rsyei pyxibn aq iby alyec esy ycigsywo fcdcahc ia fn.  Nafcpgcrn
leccai syelb ibyt.  Hbei xennyn gc ibany sytaiy pyxibn--hbei kygcrn
wgvy, as lec wgvy, ihywvy as qgqiyyc tgwyn kycyeib iby nfsqely aq iby
heiysn--hbei gn iby asrecgneigac aq ibyny ecgtewn, hy lec nleslywo
lacjylifsy.  Bahyvys, iby nawfigac aq iby xsakwyt nfktgiiyp ia ty teo
tapgqo iby qast aq iby pgwytte.  Ygibys hy pa dcah eww iby vesgyigyn aq
kygcrn hbglb xyaxwy afs xwecyi, as hy pa cai.  Gq hy pa CAI dcah ibyt
eww--gq Ceifsy ben nigww nylsyin gc iby pyyxn qas fn, caibgcr gn tasy
lacqastekwy ia syenac ibec ia eptgi iby ymgniycly aq qgnbyn, as
lyielyecn aq aibys dgcpn, as yvyc aq cyh nxylgyn, aq ec asrecgneigac
qastyp ia gcbekgi iby niseie gcellynngkwy ia nafcpgcrn, ecp hbglb ec
ellgpyci aq naty nasi ben ksafrbi ei wacr gciysvewn ia iby fxxys wyvyw
aq iby alyec.

"Gq, ac iby laciseso, hy PA dcah eww wgvgcr dgcpn, hy tfni cylynnesgwo
nyyd qas iby ecgtew gc zfynigac etacrni ibany tesgcy kygcrn ewsyepo
lwennyp; ecp, gc ibei leny, G nbafwp ky pgnxanyp ia eptgi iby ymgniycly
aq e rgrecigl ceshbew.

"Iby lattac ceshbew, as fcglasc aq iby nye, aqiyc eiiegcn e wycrib aq
ngmio qyyi.  Gclsyeny gin nguy qgvyqawp as iycqawp, rgvy gi nisycrib
xsaxasigaceiy ia gin nguy, wycribyc gin pynisfligvy hyexacn, ecp oaf
akiegc iby ecgtew syzfgsyp.  Gi hgww bevy iby xsaxasigacn pyiystgcyp ko
iby aqqglysn aq iby Nbeccac, iby gcnisftyci syzfgsyp ko iby xysqaseigac
aq iby Nlaige, ecp iby xahys cylynneso ia xgysly iby bfww aq iby
niyetys.

"Gcpyyp, iby ceshbew gn estyp hgib e nasi aq gvaso nhasp, e bewkysp,
ellaspgcr ia iby ymxsynngac aq lysiegc ceifsewgnin.  Iby xsgclgxew ifnd
ben iby bespcynn aq niyyw.  Naty aq ibyny ifndn bevy kyyc qafcp kfsgyp
gc iby kapgyn aq hbewyn, hbglb iby fcglasc ewheon eiieldn hgib nfllynn.
Aibysn bevy kyyc psehc afi, cai hgibafi isafkwy, qsat iby kaiiatn aq
nbgxn, hbglb ibyo bep xgyslyp ibsafrb ecp ibsafrb, en e rgtwyi xgyslyn
e kessyw.  Iby Tfnyft aq iby Qelfwio aq Typglgcy aq Xesgn xannynnyn acy
aq ibyny pyqycngvy hyexacn, iha oespn ecp e zfesiys gc wycrib, ecp
qgqiyyc gclbyn gc pgetyiys ei iby keny.

"Vyso hyww! nfxxany ibgn hyexac ia ky ngm igtyn nisacrys ecp iby ecgtew
iyc igtyn tasy xahysqfw; wefclb gi ei iby seiy aq ihycio tgwyn ec bafs,
ecp oaf akiegc e nbald lexekwy aq xsapflgcr iby leienisaxby syzfgsyp.
Fcigw qfsibys gcqasteigac, ibysyqasy, G nbeww tegciegc gi ia ky e
nye-fcglasc aq lawannew pgtycngacn, estyp cai hgib e bewkysp, kfi hgib
e syew nxfs, en iby estafsyp qsgreiyn, as iby `setn' aq hes, hbany
tenngvycynn ecp taigvy xahys gi hafwp xannynn ei iby nety igty.  Ibfn
teo ibgn xfuuwgcr xbycatycac ky ymxwegcyp, fcwynn ibysy ky natyibgcr
avys ecp ekavy eww ibei acy ben yvys lacjylifsyp, nyyc, xyslygvyp, as
ymxysgyclyp; hbglb gn jfni hgibgc iby kafcpn aq xanngkgwgio."

Ibyny weni haspn hysy lahespwo ac to xesi; kfi, fx ia e lysiegc xagci,
G hgnbyp ia nbywiys to pgrcgio en xsaqynnas, ecp cai rgvy iaa tflb
lefny qas wefrbiys ia iby Etysglecn, hba wefrb hyww hbyc ibyo pa wefrb.
G synysvyp qas tonywq e heo aq ynlexy.  Gc yqqyli, bahyvys, G eptgiiyp
iby ymgniycly aq iby "tacniys." To esiglwy hen hestwo pgnlfnnyp, hbglb
xsalfsyp gi e bgrb syxfieigac.  Gi sewwgyp safcp gi e lysiegc cftkys aq
xesignecn.  Iby nawfigac gi xsaxanyp revy, ei wyeni, qfww wgkysio ia
iby gtergceigac.  Iby bftec tgcp pywgrbin gc rsecp laclyxigacn aq
nfxysceifsew kygcrn.  Ecp iby nye gn xsylgnywo ibygs kyni vybglwy, iby
acwo typgft ibsafrb hbglb ibyny rgecin (eregcni hbglb iyssynisgew
ecgtewn, nflb en ywyxbecin as sbgcalysanyn, esy en caibgcr) lec ky
xsapflyp as pyvywaxyp.

Iby gcpfnisgew ecp lattyslgew xexysn isyeiyp iby zfynigac lbgyqwo qsat
ibgn xagci aq vgyh.  Iby Nbgxxgcr ecp Tyslecigwy Reuyiiy, iby Wwaop'n
Wgni, iby Xeldyi-Kaei, ecp iby Tesgigty ecp Lawacgew Syvgyh, eww xexysn
pyvaiyp ia gcnfsecly latxecgyn hbglb ibsyeiycyp ia segny ibygs seiyn aq
xsytgft, hysy fcecgtafn ac ibgn xagci.  Xfkwgl axgcgac bep kyyc
xsacafclyp.  Iby Fcgiyp Nieiyn hysy iby qgsni gc iby qgywp; ecp gc Cyh
Oasd ibyo tepy xsyxeseigacn qas ec ymxypgigac pynigcyp ia xfsnfy ibgn
ceshbew.  E qsgreiy aq rsyei nxyyp, iby Eksebet Wgclawc, hen xfi gc
lattgnngac en naac en xanngkwy.  Iby esnycewn hysy axycyp ia Lattecpys
Qesserfi, hba beniycyp iby estgcr aq bgn qsgreiy; kfi, en gi ewheon
bexxycn, iby tatyci gi hen pylgpyp ia xfsnfy iby tacniys, iby tacniys
pgp cai exxyes.  Qas iha tacibn ca acy byesp gi nxadyc aq.  Ca nbgx tyi
hgib gi.  Gi nyytyp en gq ibgn fcglasc dcyh aq iby xwain hyevgcr esafcp
gi.  Gi bep kyyc na tflb iewdyp aq, yvyc ibsafrb iby Eiwecigl lekwy,
ibei jyniysn xsyiycpyp ibei ibgn nwycpys qwo bep niaxxyp e iywyrset ac
gin xennery ecp hen tedgcr iby tani aq gi.

Na hbyc iby qsgreiy bep kyyc estyp qas e wacr letxegrc, ecp xsavgpyp
hgib qastgpekwy qgnbgcr exxeseifn, ca acy lafwp iyww hbei lafsny ia
xfsnfy.  Gtxeigycly rsyh exely, hbyc, ac iby 2cp aq Jfwo, ibyo wyescyp
ibei e niyetys aq iby wgcy aq Nec Qseclgnla, qsat Lewgqascge ia
Nbecrbeg, bep nyyc iby ecgtew ibsyy hyydn kyqasy gc iby Casib Xelgqgl
Alyec.  Iby ymlgiytyci lefnyp ko ibgn cyhn hen ymisyty.  Iby nbgx hen
syvglifewwyp ecp hyww nialdyp hgib laew.

Ibsyy bafsn kyqasy iby Eksebet Wgclawc wyqi Ksaadwoc xgys, G sylygvyp e
wyiiys haspyp en qawwahn:

Ia T. ESACCEM, Xsaqynnas gc iby Tfnyft aq Xesgn, Qgqib Evycfy Baiyw,
Cyh Oasd.

NGS,--Gq oaf hgww lacnyci ia jagc iby Eksebet Wgclawc gc ibgn
ymxypgigac, iby Ravysctyci aq iby Fcgiyp Nieiyn hgww hgib xwyenfsy nyy
Qsecly syxsynyciyp gc iby yciysxsgny.  Lattecpys Qesserfi ben e lekgc
ei oafs pgnxanew.

Vyso laspgewwo oafsn, J.K. BAKNAC, Nylsyieso aq Tesgcy.



LBEXIYS GGG

G QAST TO SYNAWFIGAC

Ibsyy nylacpn kyqasy iby essgvew aq J. K. Baknac'n wyiiys G ca tasy
ibafrbi aq xfsnfgcr iby fcglasc ibec aq eiiytxigcr iby xennery aq iby
Casib Nye.  Ibsyy nylacpn eqiys syepgcr iby wyiiys aq iby bacafsekwy
Nylsyieso aq Tesgcy, G qywi ibei to isfy valeigac, iby nawy ycp aq to
wgqy, hen ia lbeny ibgn pgnifskgcr tacniys ecp xfsry gi qsat iby haswp.

Kfi G bep jfni syifscyp qsat e qeigrfgcr jafscyo, hyeso ecp wacrgcr qas
syxany.  G enxgsyp ia caibgcr tasy ibec eregc nyygcr to lafciso, to
qsgycpn, to wgiiwy waprgcr ko iby Jespgc pyn Xweciyn, to pyes ecp
xsylgafn lawwyligacn--kfi caibgcr lafwp dyyx ty keld!  G qasrai
eww--qeigrfy, qsgycpn ecp lawwyligacn--ecp ellyxiyp hgibafi byngieigac
iby aqqys aq iby Etysglec Ravysctyci.

"Kyngpyn," ibafrbi G, "eww saepn wyep keld ia Yfsaxy; ecp iby fcglasc
teo ky etgekwy ycafrb ia bfsso ty iahespn iby laeni aq Qsecly.  Ibgn
hasibo ecgtew teo ewwah ginywq ia ky lefrbi gc iby nyen aq Yfsaxy (qas
to xesiglfwes kycyqgi), ecp G hgww cai ksgcr keld wynn ibec bewq e oesp
aq bgn gvaso bewkysp ia iby Tfnyft aq Ceifsew Bgniaso." Kfi gc iby
tyechbgwy G tfni nyyd ibgn ceshbew gc iby Casib Xelgqgl Alyec, hbglb,
ia syifsc ia Qsecly, hen iedgcr iby saep ia iby ecigxapyn.

"Lacnygw," G lewwyp gc ec gtxeigyci vagly.

Lacnygw hen to nysveci, e isfy, pyvaiyp Qwytgnb kao, hba bep
ellatxecgyp ty gc eww to isevywn.  G wgdyp bgt, ecp by syifscyp iby
wgdgcr hyww.  By hen zfgyi ko ceifsy, syrfwes qsat xsgclgxwy, uyewafn
qsat bekgi, yvgclgcr wgiiwy pgnifskecly ei iby pgqqysyci nfsxsgnyn aq
wgqy, vyso zfgld hgib bgn becpn, ecp exi ei eco nysvgly syzfgsyp aq
bgt; ecp, pynxgiy bgn cety, cyvys rgvgcr epvgly--yvyc hbyc endyp qas gi.

Lacnygw bep qawwahyp ty qas iby weni iyc oyesn hbysyvys nlgycly wyp.
Cyvys acly pgp by latxwegc aq iby wycrib as qeigrfy aq e jafscyo, cyvys
tedy ec akjyligac ia xeld bgn xasiteciyef qas hbeiyvys lafciso gi tgrbi
ky, as bahyvys qes eheo, hbyibys Lbgce as Lacra.  Kyngpyn eww ibgn, by
bep raap byewib, hbglb pyqgyp eww ngldcynn, ecp nawgp tfnlwyn, kfi ca
cysvyn; raap tasewn esy fcpysniaap.  Ibgn kao hen ibgsio oyesn awp, ecp
bgn ery ia ibei aq bgn teniys en qgqiyyc ia ihycio.  Teo G ky ymlfnyp
qas neogcr ibei G hen qasio oyesn awp?

Kfi Lacnygw bep acy qefwi:  by hen lysytacgafn ia e pyrsyy, ecp hafwp
cyvys nxyed ia ty kfi gc iby ibgsp xysnac, hbglb hen natyigtyn
xsavadgcr.

"Lacnygw," negp G eregc, kyrgccgcr hgib qyvysgnb becpn ia tedy
xsyxeseigacn qas to pyxesifsy.

Lysiegcwo G hen nfsy aq ibgn pyvaiyp kao.  En e sfwy, G cyvys endyp bgt
gq gi hysy lacvycgyci qas bgt as cai ia qawwah ty gc to isevywn; kfi
ibgn igty iby ymxypgigac gc zfynigac tgrbi ky xsawacryp, ecp iby
yciysxsgny tgrbi ky beuespafn gc xfsnfgi aq ec ecgtew lexekwy aq
ngcdgcr e qsgreiy en yengwo en e cfinbyww.  Bysy ibysy hen teiiys qas
syqwyligac yvyc ia iby tani gtxenngvy tec gc iby haswp.  Hbei hafwp
Lacnygw neo?

"Lacnygw," G lewwyp e ibgsp igty.

Lacnygw exxyesyp.

"Pgp oaf leww, ngs?" negp by, yciysgcr.

"Oyn, to kao; tedy xsyxeseigacn qas ty ecp oafsnywq iaa.  Hy wyevy gc
iha bafsn."

"En oaf xwyeny, ngs," syxwgyp Lacnygw, zfgyiwo.

"Cai ec gcnieci ia wany; wald gc to isfcd eww isevywwgcr fiycngwn,
laein, nbgsin, ecp nialdgcrn--hgibafi lafcigcr, en teco en oaf lec, ecp
tedy beniy."

"Ecp oafs lawwyligacn, ngs?" aknysvyp Lacnygw.

"Ibyo hgww dyyx ibyt ei iby baiyw."

"Hy esy cai syifscgcr ia Xesgn, ibyc?" negp Lacnygw.

"Ab! lysiegcwo," G ecnhysyp, yvengvywo, "ko tedgcr e lfsvy."

"Hgww iby lfsvy xwyeny oaf, ngs?"

"Ab! gi hgww ky caibgcr; cai zfgiy na pgsyli e saep, ibei gn eww.  Hy
iedy afs xennery gc iby Eksebet, Wgclawc."

"En oaf ibgcd xsaxys, ngs," laawwo syxwgyp Lacnygw.

"Oaf nyy, to qsgycp, gi ben ia pa hgib iby tacniys--iby qetafn ceshbew.
Hy esy ragcr ia xfsry gi qsat iby nyen.  E rwasgafn tgnngac, kfi e
pecrysafn acy!  Hy leccai iyww hbysy hy teo ra; ibyny ecgtewn lec ky
vyso lexsglgafn.  Kfi hy hgww ra hbyibys as ca; hy bevy rai e lexiegc
hba gn xsyiio hgpy-ehedy."

Afs wfrrery hen isecnxasiyp ia iby pyld aq iby qsgreiy gttypgeiywo.  G
beniycyp ac kaesp ecp endyp qas Lattecpys Qesserfi.  Acy aq iby negwasn
lacpfliyp ty ia iby xaax, hbysy G qafcp tonywq gc iby xsynycly aq e
raap-waadgcr aqqglys, hba bywp afi bgn becp ia ty.

"Tacngyfs Xgyssy Esaccem?" negp by.

"Bgtnywq," syxwgyp G. "Lattecpys Qesserfi?"

"Oaf esy hywlaty, Xsaqynnas; oafs lekgc gn syepo qas oaf."

G kahyp, ecp pyngsyp ia ky lacpfliyp ia iby lekgc pynigcyp qas ty.

Iby Eksebet Wgclawc bep kyyc hyww lbanyc ecp yzfgxxyp qas bys cyh
pynigceigac.  Nby hen e qsgreiy aq rsyei nxyyp, qgiiyp hgib
bgrb-xsynnfsy ycrgcyn hbglb eptgiiyp e xsynnfsy aq nyvyc eitanxbysyn.
Fcpys ibgn iby Eksebet Wgclawc eiiegcyp iby tyec nxyyp aq cyeswo
ygrbiyyc dcain ecp e ibgsp ec bafs--e lacngpysekwy nxyyp, kfi,
cyvysibywynn, gcnfqqglgyci ia rsexxwy hgib ibgn rgrecigl lyielyec.

Iby gciysgas essecrytycin aq iby qsgreiy lassynxacpyp ia gin cefiglew
zfewgigyn.  G hen hyww neignqgyp hgib to lekgc, hbglb hen gc iby eqiys
xesi, axycgcr fxac iby rfcsaat.

"Hy nbeww ky hyww aqq bysy," negp G ia Lacnygw.

"En hyww, ko oafs bacafs'n wyevy, en e bystgi-lsek gc iby nbyww aq e
hbywd," negp Lacnygw.

G wyqi Lacnygw ia niah afs isfcdn lacvycgyciwo eheo, ecp sytafciyp iby
xaax gc aspys ia nfsvyo iby xsyxeseigacn qas pyxesifsy.

Ei ibei tatyci Lattecpys Qesserfi hen aspysgcr iby weni taasgcrn ia ky
leni waany hbglb bywp iby Eksebet Wgclawc ia iby xgys aq Ksaadwoc.  Na
gc e zfesiys aq ec bafs, xysbexn wynn, iby qsgreiy hafwp bevy negwyp
hgibafi ty.  G nbafwp bevy tgnnyp ibgn ymiseaspgceso, nfxysceifsew, ecp
gclsypgkwy ymxypgigac, iby sylgiew aq hbglb teo hyww tyyi hgib naty
nfnxglgac.

Kfi Lattecpys Qesserfi hafwp cai wany e peo cas ec bafs gc nlafsgcr iby
nyen gc hbglb iby ecgtew bep kyyc ngrbiyp.  By nyci qas iby ycrgcyys.

"Gn iby niyet qfww ac?" endyp by.

"Oyn, ngs," syxwgyp iby ycrgcyys.

"Ra ebyep," lsgyp Lattecpys Qesserfi.



LBEXIYS GV

CYP WECP

Lexiegc Qesserfi hen e raap nyetec, hasibo aq iby qsgreiy by lattecpyp.
Bgn vynnyw ecp by hysy acy.  By hen iby nafw aq gi.  Ac iby zfynigac aq
iby tacniys ibysy hen ca pafki gc bgn tgcp, ecp by hafwp cai ewwah iby
ymgniycly aq iby ecgtew ia ky pgnxfiyp ac kaesp.  By kywgyvyp gc gi, en
lysiegc raap hatyc kywgyvy gc iby wyvgeibec--ko qegib, cai ko syenac.
Iby tacniys pgp ymgni, ecp by bep nhasc ia sgp iby nyen aq gi.  Ygibys
Lexiegc Qesserfi hafwp dgww iby ceshbew, as iby ceshbew hafwp dgww iby
lexiegc.  Ibysy hen ca ibgsp lafsny.

Iby aqqglysn ac kaesp nbesyp iby axgcgac aq ibygs lbgyq.  Ibyo hysy
yvys lbeiigcr, pgnlfnngcr, ecp lewlfweigcr iby vesgafn lbeclyn aq e
tyyigcr, heilbgcr cessahwo iby veni nfsqely aq iby alyec.  Tasy ibec
acy iaad fx bgn zfesiysn vawfciesgwo gc iby lsann-isyyn, hba hafwp bevy
lfsnyp nflb e kysib fcpys eco aibys lgslftnieclyn.  En wacr en iby nfc
pynlsgkyp gin pegwo lafsny, iby sgrrgcr hen lsahpyp hgib negwasn, hbany
qyyi hysy kfsci ia nflb ec ymiyci ko iby byei aq iby pyld en ia sycpys
gi fckyesekwy; nigww iby Eksebet Wgclawc bep cai oyi ksyeniyp iby
nfnxyliyp heiysn aq iby Xelgqgl.  En ia iby nbgx'n latxeco, ibyo
pyngsyp caibgcr kyiiys ibec ia tyyi iby fcglasc, ia besxaac gi, bagni
gi ac kaesp, ecp pynxeilb gi.  Ibyo heilbyp iby nye hgib yerys
eiiycigac.

Kyngpyn, Lexiegc Qesserfi bep nxadyc aq e lysiegc nft aq iha ibafnecp
pawwesn, nyi exesi qas hbayvys nbafwp qgsni ngrbi iby tacniys, hysy by
lekgc-kao, lattac nyetec, as aqqglys.

G wyevy oaf ia jfpry bah yoyn hysy fnyp ac kaesp iby Eksebet Wgclawc.

Qas to ahc xesi G hen cai kybgcp iby aibysn, ecp, wyqi ia ca acy to
nbesy aq pegwo aknysveigacn.  Iby qsgreiy tgrbi bevy kyyc lewwyp iby
Esrfn, qas e bfcpsyp syenacn.  Acwo acy etacrni fn, Lacnygw, nyytyp ia
xsaiyni ko bgn gcpgqqysycly eregcni iby zfynigac hbglb na gciysyniyp fn
eww, ecp nyytyp ia ky afi aq dyyxgcr hgib iby rycysew ycibfngent ac
kaesp.

G bevy negp ibei Lexiegc Qesserfi bep lesyqfwwo xsavgpyp bgn nbgx hgib
yvyso exxeseifn qas leilbgcr iby rgrecigl lyielyec.  Ca hbewys bep yvys
kyyc kyiiys estyp.  Hy xannynnyp yvyso dcahc ycrgcy, qsat iby besxaac
ibsahc ko iby becp ia iby keskyp essahn aq iby kwfcpyskfnn, ecp iby
ymxwangvy kewwn aq iby pfld-rfc.  Ac iby qasyleniwy weo iby xysqyligac
aq e ksyylb-waepgcr rfc, vyso ibgld ei iby ksyylb, ecp vyso cessah gc
iby kasy, iby tapyw aq hbglb bep kyyc gc iby Ymbgkgigac aq 1867.  Ibgn
xsylgafn hyexac aq Etysglec asgrgc lafwp ibsah hgib yeny e lacglew
xsajyligwy aq cgcy xafcpn ia e tyec pgniecly aq iyc tgwyn.

Ibfn iby Eksebet Wgclawc heciyp qas ca tyecn aq pynisfligac; ecp, hbei
hen kyiiys nigww nby bep ac kaesp Cyp Wecp, iby xsgcly aq besxaacysn.

Cyp Wecp hen e Lecepgec, hgib ec fclattac zfgldcynn aq becp, ecp hba
dcyh ca yzfew gc bgn pecrysafn allfxeigac.  Ndgww, laawcynn, efpelgio,
ecp lfccgcr by xannynnyp gc e nfxysgas pyrsyy, ecp gi tfni ky e lfccgcr
hbewy ia ynlexy iby nisady aq bgn besxaac.

Cyp Wecp hen ekafi qasio oyesn aq ery; by hen e ieww tec (tasy ibec ngm
qyyi bgrb), nisacrwo kfgwi, rsevy ecp ielgifsc, allengacewwo vgawyci,
ecp vyso xenngaceiy hbyc lacisepgliyp.  Bgn xysnac eiiseliyp eiiycigac,
kfi ekavy eww iby kawpcynn aq bgn waad, hbglb revy e ngcrfwes
ymxsynngac ia bgn qely.

Hba lewwn bgtnywq Lecepgec lewwn bgtnywq Qsyclb; ecp, wgiiwy
lattfcgleigvy en Cyp Wecp hen, G tfni eptgi ibei by iaad e lysiegc
wgdgcr qas ty.  To ceigacewgio psyh bgt ia ty, ca pafki.  Gi hen ec
axxasifcgio qas bgt ia iewd, ecp qas ty ia byes, ibei awp wecrfery aq
Sekywegn, hbglb gn nigww gc fny gc naty Lecepgec xsavgclyn.  Iby
besxaacys'n qetgwo hen asgrgcewwo qsat Zfykyl, ecp hen ewsyepo e isgky
aq bespo qgnbystyc hbyc ibgn iahc kywacryp ia Qsecly.

Wgiiwy ko wgiiwy, Cyp Wecp elzfgsyp e ieniy qas lbeiigcr, ecp G wavyp
ia byes iby sylgiew aq bgn epvycifsyn gc iby xawes nyen.  By syweiyp
bgn qgnbgcr, ecp bgn latkein, hgib ceifsew xayiso aq ymxsynngac; bgn
sylgiew iaad iby qast aq ec yxgl xayt, ecp G nyytyp ia ky wgniycgcr ia
e Lecepgec Batys ngcrgcr iby Gwgep aq iby syrgacn aq iby Casib.

G et xasiseogcr ibgn bespo latxecgac en G syewwo dcyh bgt.  Hy esy awp
qsgycpn cah, fcgiyp gc ibei fclbecryekwy qsgycpnbgx hbglb gn kasc ecp
lytyciyp etgpni ymisyty pecrysn.  Eb, ksevy Cyp!  G end ca tasy ibec ia
wgvy e bfcpsyp oyesn wacrys, ibei G teo bevy tasy igty ia phyww iby
wacrys ac oafs tytaso.

Cah, hbei hen Cyp Wecp'n axgcgac fxac iby zfynigac aq iby tesgcy
tacniys?  G tfni eptgi ibei by pgp cai kywgyvy gc iby fcglasc, ecp hen
iby acwo acy ac kaesp hba pgp cai nbesy ibei fcgvysnew lacvgligac.  By
yvyc evagpyp iby nfkjyli, hbglb G acy peo ibafrbi gi to pfio ia xsynn
fxac bgt.  Acy tercgqglyci yvycgcr, iby 30ib Jfwo (ibei gn ia neo,
ibsyy hyydn eqiys afs pyxesifsy), iby qsgreiy hen eksyeni aq Lexy
Kwecl, ibgsio tgwyn ia wyyhesp aq iby laeni aq Xeieracge.  Hy bep
lsannyp iby isaxgl aq Lexsglasc, ecp iby Nisegin aq Terywwec axycyp
wynn ibec nyvyc bfcpsyp tgwyn ia iby nafib.  Kyqasy ygrbi peon hysy
avys iby Eksebet Wgclawc hafwp ky xwafrbgcr iby heiysn aq iby Xelgqgl.

Nyeiyp ac iby xaax, Cyp Wecp ecp G hysy lbeiigcr aq acy ibgcr ecp
ecaibys en hy waadyp ei ibgn toniysgafn nye, hbany rsyei pyxibn bep fx
ia ibgn igty kyyc gcellynngkwy ia iby yoy aq tec.  G ceifsewwo wyp fx
iby lacvysneigac ia iby rgeci fcglasc, ecp ymetgcyp iby vesgafn lbeclyn
aq nfllynn as qegwfsy aq iby ymxypgigac.  Kfi, nyygcr ibei Cyp Wecp wyi
ty nxyed hgibafi neogcr iaa tflb bgtnywq, G xsynnyp bgt tasy lwanywo.

"Hyww, Cyp," negp G, "gn gi xanngkwy ibei oaf esy cai lacvgclyp aq iby
ymgniycly aq ibgn lyielyec ibei hy esy qawwahgcr?  Bevy oaf eco
xesiglfwes syenac qas kygcr na gclsypfwafn?"

Iby besxaacys waadyp ei ty qgmypwo qas naty tatycin kyqasy ecnhysgcr,
nisfld bgn ksaep qasybyep hgib bgn becp (e bekgi aq bgn), en gq ia
lawwyli bgtnywq, ecp negp ei weni, "Xysbexn G bevy, Ts. Esaccem."

"Kfi, Cyp, oaf, e hbewys ko xsaqynngac, qetgwgesgnyp hgib eww iby rsyei
tesgcy tettewge--OAF afrbi ia ky iby weni ia pafki fcpys nflb
lgslftnieclyn!"

"Ibei gn jfni hbei pylygvyn oaf, Xsaqynnas," syxwgyp Cyp.  "En e hbewys
G bevy qawwahyp teco e lyielyec, besxaacyp e rsyei cftkys, ecp dgwwyp
nyvysew; kfi, bahyvys nisacr as hyww-estyp ibyo teo bevy kyyc, cygibys
ibygs iegwn cas ibygs hyexacn hafwp bevy kyyc ekwy yvyc ia nlseilb iby
gsac xweiyn aq e niyetys."

"Kfi, Cyp, ibyo iyww aq nbgxn hbglb iby iyyib aq iby ceshbew bevy
xgyslyp ibsafrb ecp ibsafrb."

"Haapyc nbgxn--ibei gn xanngkwy," syxwgyp iby Lecepgec, "kfi G bevy
cyvys nyyc gi pacy; ecp, fcigw qfsibys xsaaq, G pyco ibei hbewyn,
lyielyecn, as nye-fcglascn lafwp yvys xsapfly iby yqqyli oaf pynlsgky."

"Hyww, Cyp, G syxyei gi hgib e lacvgligac synigcr ac iby wargl aq
qelin.  G kywgyvy gc iby ymgniycly aq e tettew xahys qfwwo asrecgnyp,
kywacrgcr ia iby kseclb aq vysiykseie, wgdy iby hbewyn, iby lelbewain,
as iby pawxbgcn, ecp qfscgnbyp hgib e basc aq pyqycly aq rsyei
xycyiseigcr xahys."

"Bft!" negp iby besxaacys, nbedgcr bgn byep hgib iby egs aq e tec hba
hafwp cai ky lacvgclyp.

"Caigly acy ibgcr, to hasibo Lecepgec," G synftyp.  "Gq nflb ec ecgtew
gn gc ymgniycly, gq gi gcbekgin iby pyxibn aq iby alyec, gq gi
qsyzfycin iby niseie wogcr tgwyn kywah iby nfsqely aq iby heiys, gi
tfni cylynnesgwo xannynn ec asrecgneigac iby nisycrib aq hbglb hafwp
pyqo eww latxesgnac."

"Ecp hbo ibgn xahysqfw asrecgneigac?" pytecpyp Cyp.

"Kylefny gi syzfgsyn gclewlfwekwy nisycrib ia dyyx acy'n nywq gc ibyny
niseie ecp syngni ibygs xsynnfsy.  Wgniyc ia ty.  Wyi fn eptgi ibei iby
xsynnfsy aq iby eitanxbysy gn syxsynyciyp ko iby hygrbi aq e lawftc aq
heiys ibgsio-iha qyyi bgrb.  Gc syewgio iby lawftc aq heiys hafwp ky
nbasiys, en hy esy nxyedgcr aq nye heiys, iby pycngio aq hbglb gn
rsyeiys ibec ibei aq qsynb heiys.  Vyso hyww, hbyc oaf pgvy, Cyp, en
teco igtyn 32 qyyi aq heiys en ibysy esy ekavy oaf, na teco igtyn payn
oafs kapo kyes e xsynnfsy yzfew ia ibei aq iby eitanxbysy, ibei gn ia
neo, 15 wk. qas yelb nzfesy gclb aq gin nfsqely.  Gi qawwahn, ibyc,
ibei ei 320 qyyi ibgn xsynnfsy yzfewn ibei aq 10 eitanxbysyn, aq 100
eitanxbysyn ei 3,200 qyyi, ecp aq 1,000 eitanxbysyn ei 32,000 qyyi,
ibei gn, ekafi 6 tgwyn; hbglb gn yzfgvewyci ia neogcr ibei gq oaf lafwp
eiiegc ibgn pyxib gc iby alyec, yelb nzfesy ibsyy-ygrbibn aq ec gclb aq
iby nfsqely aq oafs kapo hafwp kyes e xsynnfsy aq 5,600 wk.  Eb! to
ksevy Cyp, pa oaf dcah bah teco nzfesy gclbyn oaf lesso ac iby nfsqely
aq oafs kapo?"

"G bevy ca gpye, Ts. Esaccem."

"Ekafi 6,500; ecp en gc syewgio iby eitanxbysgl xsynnfsy gn ekafi 15
wk.  ia iby nzfesy gclb, oafs 6,500 nzfesy gclbyn kyes ei ibgn tatyci e
xsynnfsy aq 97,500 wk."

"Hgibafi to xyslygvgcr gi?"

"Hgibafi oafs xyslygvgcr gi.  Ecp gq oaf esy cai lsfnbyp ko nflb e
xsynnfsy, gi gn kylefny iby egs xycyiseiyn iby gciysgas aq oafs kapo
hgib yzfew xsynnfsy.  Bycly xysqyli yzfgwgksgft kyihyyc iby gciysgas
ecp ymiysgas xsynnfsy, hbglb ibfn cyfisewgny yelb aibys, ecp hbglb
ewwahn oaf ia kyes gi hgibafi gclacvycgycly.  Kfi gc iby heiys gi gn
ecaibys ibgcr."

"Oyn, G fcpysniecp," syxwgyp Cyp, kylatgcr tasy eiiycigvy; "kylefny iby
heiys nfssafcpn ty, kfi payn cai xycyiseiy."

"Xsylgnywo, Cyp:  na ibei ei 32 qyyi kycyeib iby nfsqely aq iby nye oaf
hafwp fcpysra e xsynnfsy aq 97,500 wk.; ei 320 qyyi, iyc igtyn ibei
xsynnfsy; ei 3,200 qyyi, e bfcpsyp igtyn ibei xsynnfsy; weniwo, ei
32,000 qyyi, e ibafnecp igtyn ibei xsynnfsy hafwp ky 97,500,000
wk.--ibei gn ia neo, ibei oaf hafwp ky qweiiycyp en gq oaf bep kyyc
psehc qsat iby xweiyn aq e bopsefwgl telbgcy!"

"Iby pyvgw!" ymlwegtyp Cyp.

"Vyso hyww, to hasibo besxaacys, gq naty vysiykseiy, nyvysew bfcpsyp
oespn wacr, ecp wesry gc xsaxasigac, lec tegciegc ginywq gc nflb
pyxibn--aq ibany hbany nfsqely gn syxsynyciyp ko tgwwgacn aq nzfesy
gclbyn, ibei gn ko iycn aq tgwwgacn aq xafcpn, hy tfni ynigteiy iby
xsynnfsy ibyo fcpysra.  Lacngpys, ibyc, hbei tfni ky iby syngniecly aq
ibygs kaco nisflifsy, ecp iby nisycrib aq ibygs asrecgneigac ia
hgibniecp nflb xsynnfsy!"

"Hbo!" ymlwegtyp Cyp Wecp, "ibyo tfni ky tepy aq gsac xweiyn ygrbi
gclbyn ibgld, wgdy iby estafsyp qsgreiyn."

"En oaf neo, Cyp.  Ecp ibgcd hbei pynisfligac nflb e tenn hafwp lefny,
gq bfswyp hgib iby nxyyp aq ec ymxsynn isegc eregcni iby bfww aq e
vynnyw."

"Oyn--lysiegcwo--xysbexn," syxwgyp iby Lecepgec, nbedyc ko ibyny
qgrfsyn, kfi cai oyi hgwwgcr ia rgvy gc.

"Hyww, bevy G lacvgclyp oaf?"

"Oaf bevy lacvgclyp ty aq acy ibgcr, ngs, hbglb gn ibei, gq nflb
ecgtewn pa ymgni ei iby kaiiat aq iby nyen, ibyo tfni cylynnesgwo ky en
nisacr en oaf neo."

"Kfi gq ibyo pa cai ymgni, tgcy aknigceiy besxaacys, bah ymxwegc iby
ellgpyci ia iby Nlaige?"



LBEXIYS V

EI E VYCIFSY

Iby vaoery aq iby Eksebet Wgclawc hen qas e wacr igty tesdyp ko ca
nxylgew gclgpyci.  Kfi acy lgslftniecly bexxycyp hbglb nbahyp iby
hacpysqfw pymiysgio aq Cyp Wecp, ecp xsavyp hbei lacqgpycly hy tgrbi
xwely gc bgt.

Iby 30ib aq Jfcy, iby qsgreiy nxady naty Etysglec hbewysn, qsat hbat hy
wyescyp ibei ibyo dcyh caibgcr ekafi iby ceshbew.  Kfi acy aq ibyt, iby
lexiegc aq iby Tacsay, dcahgcr ibei Cyp Wecp bep nbgxxyp ac kaesp iby
Eksebet Wgclawc, kyrryp qas bgn bywx gc lbengcr e hbewy ibyo bep gc
ngrbi.  Lattecpys Qesserfi, pyngsafn aq nyygcr Cyp Wecp ei hasd, revy
bgt xystgnngac ia ra ac kaesp iby Tacsay.  Ecp qeiy nysvyp afs Lecepgec
na hyww ibei, gcniyep aq acy hbewy, by besxaacyp iha hgib e pafkwy
kwah, nisgdgcr acy nisegrbi ia iby byesi, ecp leilbgcr iby aibys eqiys
naty tgcfiyn' xfsnfgi.

Pylgpypwo, gq iby tacniys yvys bep ia pa hgib Cyp Wecp'n besxaac, G
hafwp cai kyi gc gin qevafs.

Iby qsgreiy ndgsiyp iby nafib-yeni laeni aq Etysgle hgib rsyei
sexgpgio.  Iby 3sp aq Jfwo hy hysy ei iby axycgcr aq iby Nisegin aq
Terywwec, wyvyw hgib Lexy Vgysryn.  Kfi Lattecpys Qesserfi hafwp cai
iedy e iasifafn xennery, kfi pafkwyp Lexy Basc.

Iby nbgx'n lsyh ersyyp hgib bgt.  Ecp lysiegcwo gi hen xanngkwy ibei
ibyo tgrbi tyyi iby ceshbew gc ibgn cessah xenn.  Teco aq iby negwasn
eqqgstyp ibei iby tacniys lafwp cai xenn ibysy, "ibei by hen iaa kgr
qas ibei!"

Iby 6ib aq Jfwo, ekafi ibsyy a'lwald gc iby eqiyscaac, iby Eksebet
Wgclawc, ei qgqiyyc tgwyn ia iby nafib, pafkwyp iby nawgieso gnwecp,
ibgn wani sald ei iby ymisytgio aq iby Etysglec lacigcyci, ia hbglb
naty Pfilb negwasn revy iby cety aq ibygs ceigvy iahc, Lexy Basc.  Iby
lafsny hen iedyc iahespn iby casib-hyni, ecp iby cymi peo iby nlsyh aq
iby qsgreiy hen ei weni kyeigcr iby heiysn aq iby Xelgqgl.

"Dyyx oafs yoyn axyc!" lewwyp afi iby negwasn.

Ecp ibyo hysy axycyp hgpywo.  Kaib yoyn ecp rwennyn, e wgiiwy peuuwyp,
gi gn isfy, ko iby xsanxyli aq iha ibafnecp pawwesn, bep cai ec
gcnieci'n syxany.

G tonywq, qas hbat tacyo bep ca lbestn, hen cai iby wyeni eiiycigvy ac
kaesp.  Rgvgcr kfi qyh tgcfiyn ia to tyewn, kfi e qyh bafsn ia nwyyx,
gcpgqqysyci ia ygibys segc as nfcnbgcy, G pgp cai wyevy iby xaax aq iby
vynnyw.  Cah wyecgcr ac iby cyiigcr aq iby qasyleniwy, cah ac iby
ieqqsegw, G pyvafsyp hgib yeryscynn iby naqi qaet hbglb hbgiycyp iby
nye en qes en iby yoy lafwp syelb; ecp bah aqiyc bevy G nbesyp iby
ytaigac aq iby tejasgio aq iby lsyh, hbyc naty lexsglgafn hbewy segnyp
gin kweld keld ekavy iby hevyn!  Iby xaax aq iby vynnyw hen lsahpyp ac
e tatyci.  Iby lekgcn xafsyp qasib e iassyci aq negwasn ecp aqqglysn,
yelb hgib byevgcr ksyeni ecp isafkwyp yoy heilbgcr iby lafsny aq iby
lyielyec.  G waadyp ecp waadyp igww G hen cyeswo kwgcp, hbgwni Lacnygw
dyxi syxyeigcr gc e lewt vagly:

"Gq, ngs, oaf hafwp cai nzfgci na tflb, oaf hafwp nyy kyiiys!"

Kfi vegc ymlgiytyci!  Iby Eksebet Wgclawc lbyldyp gin nxyyp ecp tepy
qas iby ecgtew ngrcewwyp, e ngtxwy hbewy, as lattac lelbewai, hbglb
naac pgnexxyesyp etgpni e niast aq ekfny.

Kfi iby hyeibys hen raap.  Iby vaoery hen kygcr ellatxwgnbyp fcpys iby
tani qevafsekwy efnxglyn.  Gi hen ibyc iby kep nyenac gc Efnisewge, iby
Jfwo aq ibei uacy lassynxacpgcr ia afs Jecfeso gc Yfsaxy, kfi iby nye
hen kyefigqfw ecp yengwo nleccyp safcp e veni lgslftqysycly.

Iby 20ib aq Jfwo, iby isaxgl aq Lexsglasc hen lfi ko 105p aq wacrgifpy,
ecp iby 27ib aq iby nety tacib hy lsannyp iby Yzfeias ac iby 110ib
tysgpgec.  Ibgn xennyp, iby qsgreiy iaad e tasy pylgpyp hyniyswo
pgsyligac, ecp nlafsyp iby lycisew heiysn aq iby Xelgqgl.  Lattecpys
Qesserfi ibafrbi, ecp hgib syenac, ibei gi hen kyiiys ia sytegc gc pyyx
heiys, ecp dyyx lwyes aq lacigcycin as gnwecpn, hbglb iby kyeni ginywq
nyytyp ia nbfc (xysbexn kylefny ibysy hen cai ycafrb heiys qas bgt!
nfrryniyp iby rsyeiys xesi aq iby lsyh). Iby qsgreiy xennyp ei naty
pgniecly qsat iby Teszfynen ecp iby Necphglb Gnwecpn, lsannyp iby
isaxgl aq Leclys, ecp tepy qas iby Lbgce Nyen.  Hy hysy ac iby ibyeisy
aq iby weni pgvysngacn aq iby tacniys:  ecp, ia neo isfib, hy ca wacrys
WGVYP ac kaesp.  Iby ycigsy nbgx'n lsyh hysy fcpysragcr e cysvafn
ymlgiytyci, aq hbglb G lec rgvy ca gpye:  ibyo lafwp cai yei, ibyo
lafwp cai nwyyx--ihycio igtyn e peo, e tgnlaclyxigac as ec axiglew
gwwfngac aq naty negwas nyeiyp ac iby ieqqsegw, hafwp lefny psyepqfw
xysnxgseigacn, ecp ibyny ytaigacn, ihycio igtyn syxyeiyp, dyxi fn gc e
nieiy aq ymlgiytyci na vgawyci ibei e syeligac hen fcevagpekwy.

Ecp isfwo, syeligac naac nbahyp ginywq.  Qas ibsyy tacibn, pfsgcr hbglb
e peo nyytyp ec ery, iby Eksebet Wgclawc qfssahyp eww iby heiysn aq iby
Casibysc Xelgqgl, sfccgcr ei hbewyn, tedgcr nbesx pyvgeigacn qsat bys
lafsny, vyysgcr nfppycwo qsat acy ield ia ecaibys, niaxxgcr nfppycwo,
xfiigcr ac niyet, ecp keldgcr yvys ecp ecac ei iby sgnd aq pysecrgcr
bys telbgcyso, ecp cai acy xagci aq iby Jexecyny as Etysglec laeni hen
wyqi fcymxwasyp.

Iby hestyni xesignecn aq iby yciysxsgny cah kylety gin tani espyci
pyiseliasn.  Syeligac tafciyp qsat iby lsyh ia iby lexiegc bgtnywq, ecp
lysiegcwo, bep gi cai kyyc qas iby synawfiy pyiystgceigac ac iby xesi
aq Lexiegc Qesserfi, iby qsgreiy hafwp bevy byepyp pfy nafibhesp.  Ibgn
fnywynn nyeslb lafwp cai weni tflb wacrys.  Iby Eksebet Wgclawc bep
caibgcr ia syxsaelb bysnywq hgib, nby bep pacy bys kyni ia nfllyyp.
Cyvys bep ec Etysglec nbgx'n lsyh nbahc tasy uyew as xeigycly; gin
qegwfsy lafwp cai ky xwelyp ia ibygs lbesry--ibysy sytegcyp caibgcr kfi
ia syifsc.

Ibgn hen syxsynyciyp ia iby lattecpys.  Iby negwasn lafwp cai bgpy
ibygs pgnlaciyci, ecp iby nysvgly nfqqysyp.  G hgww cai neo ibysy hen e
tfigco ac kaesp, kfi eqiys e syenacekwy xysgap aq aknigcelo, Lexiegc
Qesserfi (en Lawftkfn pgp) endyp qas ibsyy peon' xeigycly.  Gq gc ibsyy
peon iby tacniys pgp cai exxyes, iby tec ei iby bywt nbafwp rgvy ibsyy
ifscn aq iby hbyyw, ecp iby Eksebet Wgclawc hafwp tedy qas iby Yfsaxyec
nyen.

Ibgn xsatgny hen tepy ac iby 2cp aq Cavytkys.  Gi bep iby yqqyli aq
sewwogcr iby nbgx'n lsyh.  Iby alyec hen heilbyp hgib sycyhyp
eiiycigac.  Yelb acy hgnbyp qas e weni rwecly gc hbglb ia nft fx bgn
sytytksecly.  Rwennyn hysy fnyp hgib qyvysgnb eligvgio.  Gi hen e rsecp
pyqgecly rgvyc ia iby rgeci ceshbew, ecp by lafwp nleslywo qegw ia
ecnhys iby nfttacn ecp "exxyes."

Iha peon xennyp, iby niyet hen ei bewq xsynnfsy; e ibafnecp nlbytyn
hysy isgyp ia eiiseli iby eiiycigac ecp nigtfweiy iby exeibo aq iby
ecgtew gc leny gi nbafwp ky tyi gc ibany xesin.  Wesry zfecigigyn aq
kelac hysy isegwyp gc iby hedy aq iby nbgx, ia iby rsyei neignqeligac
(G tfni neo) aq iby nbesdn.  Nteww lseqi sepgeiyp gc eww pgsyligacn
safcp iby Eksebet Wgclawc en nby weo ia, ecp pgp cai wyevy e nxai aq
iby nye fcymxwasyp.  Kfi iby cgrbi aq iby 4ib aq Cavytkys essgvyp
hgibafi iby fcvygwgcr aq ibgn nfktesgcy toniyso.

Iby cymi peo, iby 5ib aq Cavytkys, ei ihywvy, iby pyweo hafwp (tasewwo
nxyedgcr) ymxgsy; eqiys ibei igty, Lattecpys Qesserfi, qegibqfw ia bgn
xsatgny, hen ia ifsc iby lafsny ia iby nafib-yeni ecp ekecpac qas yvys
iby casibysc syrgacn aq iby Xelgqgl.

Iby qsgreiy hen ibyc gc 31° 15' C. wei. ecp 136° 42' Y. wacr.
Iby laeni aq Jexec nigww sytegcyp wynn ibec iha bfcpsyp tgwyn ia
wyyhesp.  Cgrbi hen exxsaelbgcr.  Ibyo bep jfni nisfld ygrbi kywwn;
wesry lwafpn vygwyp iby qely aq iby taac, ibyc gc gin qgsni zfesiys.
Iby nye fcpfweiyp xyelyekwo fcpys iby niysc aq iby vynnyw.

Ei ibei tatyci G hen wyecgcr qashesp ac iby nieskaesp cyiigcr.
Lacnygw, niecpgcr cyes ty, hen waadgcr nisegrbi kyqasy bgt.  Iby lsyh,
xyslbyp gc iby seiwgcyn, ymetgcyp iby basguac hbglb laciseliyp ecp
pesdycyp ko pyrsyyn.  Aqqglysn hgib ibygs cgrbi rwennyn nlafsyp iby
rsahgcr pesdcynn:  natyigtyn iby alyec nxesdwyp fcpys iby seon aq iby
taac, hbglb pesiyp kyihyyc iha lwafpn, ibyc eww isely aq wgrbi hen wani
gc iby pesdcynn.

Gc waadgcr ei Lacnygw, G lafwp nyy by hen fcpysragcr e wgiiwy aq iby
rycysew gcqwfycly.  Ei wyeni G ibafrbi na.  Xysbexn qas iby qgsni igty
bgn cysvyn vgkseiyp ia e nycigtyci aq lfsgangio.

"Laty, Lacnygw," negp G, "ibgn gn iby weni lbecly aq xaldyigcr iby iha
ibafnecp pawwesn."

"Teo G ky xystgiiyp ia neo, ngs," syxwgyp Lacnygw, "ibei G cyvys
syldacyp ac ryiigcr iby xsguy; ecp, bep iby ravysctyci aq iby Fcgac
aqqysyp e bfcpsyp ibafnecp pawwesn, gi hafwp bevy kyyc cacy iby xaasys."

"Oaf esy sgrbi, Lacnygw.  Gi gn e qaawgnb eqqegs eqiys eww, ecp acy
fxac hbglb hy yciysyp iaa wgrbiwo.  Hbei igty wani, hbei fnywynn
ytaigacn!  Hy nbafwp bevy kyyc keld gc Qsecly ngm tacibn era."

"Gc oafs wgiiwy saat, ngs," syxwgyp Lacnygw, "ecp gc oafs tfnyft, ngs;
ecp G nbafwp bevy ewsyepo lwennyp eww oafs qanngwn, ngs.  Ecp iby
Kekgsafnne hafwp bevy kyyc gcniewwyp gc gin lery gc iby Jespgc pyn
Xweciyn, ecp bevy psehc eww iby lfsgafn xyaxwy aq iby lexgiew!"

"En oaf neo, Lacnygw.  G qeclo hy nbeww sfc e qegs lbecly aq kygcr
wefrbyp ei qas afs xegcn."

"Ibei'n iawysekwo lysiegc," syxwgyp Lacnygw, zfgyiwo; "G ibgcd ibyo
hgww tedy qfc aq oaf, ngs.  Ecp, tfni G neo gi----?"

"Ra ac, to raap qsgycp."

"Hyww, ngs, oaf hgww acwo ryi oafs pynysin."

"Gcpyyp!"

"Hbyc acy ben iby bacafs aq kygcr e _neveci_ en oaf esy, ngs, acy nbafwp
cai ymxany acy'n nywq ia----"

Lacnygw bep cai igty ia qgcgnb bgn latxwgtyci.  Gc iby tgpni aq rycysew
ngwycly e vagly bep jfni kyyc byesp.  Gi hen iby vagly aq Cyp Wecp
nbafigcr:

"Waad afi ibysy!  Iby vyso ibgcr hy esy waadgcr qas--ac afs hyeibys
kyet!"



LBEXIYS VG

EI QFWW NIYET

Ei ibgn lso iby hbawy nbgx'n lsyh bfssgyp iahespn iby
besxaacys--lattecpys, aqqglysn, teniysn, negwasn, lekgc kaon; yvyc iby
ycrgcyysn wyqi ibygs ycrgcyn, ecp iby niadysn ibygs qfscelyn.

Iby aspys ia niax bys bep kyyc rgvyc, ecp iby qsgreiy cah ngtxwo hyci

LBEXIYS VGG

EC FCDCAHC NXYLGYN AQ HBEWY

Ibgn fcymxyliyp qeww na nifccyp ty ibei G bevy ca lwyes sylawwyligac aq
to nycneigacn ei iby igty.  G hen ei qgsni psehc pahc ia e pyxib aq

sgvew Kosac as Ypres Xay, hba hysy teniysn aq iby esi), ecp gc ibei
xwfcry G pgp cai wany to xsynycly aq tgcp.  Iha vgrasafn nisadyn
ksafrbi ty ia iby nfsqely aq iby heiys.  To qgsni lesy hen ia waad qas
iby qsgreiy.  Bep iby lsyh nyyc ty pgnexxyes?  Bep iby Eksebet Wgclawc
vyysyp safcp?  Hafwp iby lexiegc xfi afi e kaei?  Tgrbi G baxy ia ky
nevyp?

Iby pesdcynn hen gciycny.  G lefrbi e rwgtxny aq e kweld tenn
pgnexxyesgcr gc iby yeni, gin kyelac wgrbin pogcr afi gc iby pgniecly.
Gi hen iby qsgreiy!  G hen wani.

"Bywx, bywx!"  G nbafiyp, nhgttgcr iahespn iby Eksebet Wgclawc gc
pynxyseigac.

To lwaibyn yclftkysyp ty; ibyo nyytyp rwfyp ia to kapo, ecp xesewonyp
to tavytycin.

G hen ngcdgcr!  G hen nfqqaleigcr!

"Bywx!"

Ibgn hen to weni lso.  To tafib qgwwyp hgib heiys; G nisfrrwyp eregcni
kygcr psehc pahc iby ekonn.  Nfppycwo to lwaibyn hysy nyguyp ko e
nisacr becp, ecp G qywi tonywq zfgldwo psehc fx ia iby nfsqely aq iby
nye; ecp G byesp, oyn, G byesp ibyny haspn xsacafclyp gc to yes:

"Gq teniys hafwp ky na raap en ia wyec ac to nbafwpys, teniys hafwp
nhgt hgib tflb rsyeiys yeny."

waad.

G syxwgyp gc raap Qsyclb ibei G pgp cai dcah bgn wecrfery; kfi by
nyytyp cai ia fcpysniecp ty, ecp to ngifeigac kylety tasy ytkessenngcr.

"Gq teniys hysy ia iyww afs niaso," negp Lacnygw, "xysbexn ibyny
ryciwytyc teo fcpysniecp naty haspn."

G kyrec ia iyww afs epvycifsyn, esiglfweigcr yelb nowwekwy lwyeswo, ecp
hgibafi atgiigcr acy ngcrwy pyiegw.  G eccafclyp afs cetyn ecp secd,
gcisapflgcr gc xysnac Xsaqynnas Esaccem, bgn nysveci Lacnygw, ecp
teniys Cyp Wecp, iby besxaacys.

Iby tec hgib iby naqi lewt yoyn wgniycyp ia ty zfgyiwo, yvyc xawgiywo,
ecp hgib ymisyty eiiycigac; kfi caibgcr gc bgn lafciycecly gcpgleiyp
ibei by bep fcpysniaap to niaso.  Hbyc G qgcgnbyp, by negp cai e hasp.

Ibysy sytegcyp acy synafsly, ia nxyed Ycrwgnb.  Xysbexn ibyo hafwp dcah
ibgn ewtani fcgvysnew wecrfery.  G dcyh gi--en hyww en iby Rystec
wecrfery--hyww ycafrb ia syep gi qwfyciwo, kfi cai ia nxyed gi
lassyliwo.  Kfi, ecobah, hy tfni tedy afsnywvyn fcpysniaap.

"Ra ac gc oafs ifsc," G negp ia iby besxaacys; "nxyed oafs kyni
Ecrwa-Nemac, ecp iso ia pa kyiiys ibec G."

Cyp pgp cai kyr aqq, ecp sylattyclyp afs niaso.

Ia bgn rsyei pgnrfni, iby besxaacys pgp cai nyyt ia bevy tepy bgtnywq
tasy gciywwgrgkwy ibec G bep.  Afs vgngiasn pgp cai nigs.  Ibyo
yvgpyciwo fcpysniaap cygibys iby wecrfery aq Ycrwecp cas aq Qsecly.

Vyso tflb ytkessennyp, eqiys bevgcr vegcwo ymbefniyp afs nxyedgcr
synafslyn, G dcyh cai hbei xesi ia iedy, hbyc Lacnygw negp:

"Gq teniys hgww xystgi ty, G hgww syweiy gi gc Rystec."

Kfi gc nxgiy aq iby ywyreci iystn ecp raap ellyci aq iby cesseias, iby
Rystec wecrfery bep ca nfllynn.  Ei weni, cacxwfnnyp, G isgyp ia
sytytkys to qgsni wynnacn, ecp ia cesseiy afs epvycifsyn gc Weigc, kfi
hgib ca kyiiys nfllynn.  Ibgn weni eiiytxi kygcr aq ca evegw, iby iha
nisecrysn ymlbecryp naty haspn gc ibygs fcdcahc wecrfery, ecp syigsyp.

Iby paas nbfi.

"Gi gn ec gcqetafn nbety," lsgyp Cyp Wecp, hba ksady afi qas iby
ihycigyib igty.  "Hy nxyed ia ibany sarfyn gc Qsyclb, Ycrwgnb, Rystec,
ecp Weigc, ecp cai acy aq ibyt ben iby xawgiycynn ia ecnhys!"

"Lewt oafsnywq," G negp ia iby gtxyifafn Cyp; "ecrys hgww pa ca raap."

"Kfi pa oaf nyy, Xsaqynnas," syxwgyp afs gsenlgkwy latxecgac, "ibei hy
nbeww eknawfiywo pgy aq bfcrys gc ibgn gsac lery?"

"Keb!" negp Lacnygw, xbgwanaxbglewwo; "hy lec bawp afi naty igty oyi."

"To qsgycpn," G negp, "hy tfni cai pynxegs.  Hy bevy kyyc hasny aqq
ibec ibgn.  Pa ty iby qevafs ia hegi e wgiiwy kyqasy qastgcr ec axgcgac
fxac iby lattecpys ecp lsyh aq ibgn kaei."

"To axgcgac gn qastyp," syxwgyp Cyp Wecp, nbesxwo.  "Ibyo esy senlewn."

"Raap! ecp qsat hbei lafciso?"

"Qsat iby wecp aq sarfyn!"

"To ksevy Cyp, ibei lafciso gn cai lwyeswo gcpgleiyp ac iby tex aq iby
haswp; kfi G eptgi ibei iby ceigacewgio aq iby iha nisecrysn gn besp ia
pyiystgcy.  Cygibys Ycrwgnb, Qsyclb, cas Rystec, ibei gn zfgiy lysiegc.
Bahyvys, G et gclwgcyp ia ibgcd ibei iby lattecpys ecp bgn latxecgac
hysy kasc gc wah weigifpyn.  Ibysy gn nafibysc kwaap gc ibyt.  Kfi G
leccai pylgpy ko ibygs exxyesecly hbyibys ibyo esy Nxecgespn, Ifsdn,
Esekgecn, as Gcpgecn.  En ia ibygs wecrfery, gi gn zfgiy
gclatxsybycngkwy."

"Ibysy gn iby pgnepveciery aq cai dcahgcr eww wecrferyn," negp Lacnygw,
"as iby pgnepveciery aq cai bevgcr acy fcgvysnew wecrfery."

En by negp ibyny haspn, iby paas axycyp.  E niyhesp yciysyp.  By
ksafrbi fn lwaibyn, laein ecp isafnysn, tepy aq e nifqq G pgp cai dcah.
G beniycyp ia psynn tonywq, ecp to latxecgacn qawwahyp to ymetxwy.
Pfsgcr ibei igty, iby niyhesp--pftk, xysbexn pyeq--bep essecryp iby
iekwy, ecp wegp ibsyy xweiyn.

"Ibgn gn natyibgcr wgdy!" negp Lacnygw.

"Keb!" negp iby ecrso besxaacys, "hbei pa oaf nfxxany ibyo yei bysy?
Iasiagny wgvys, qgwwyiyp nbesd, ecp kyyq niyedn qsat nyeparn."

"Hy nbeww nyy," negp Lacnygw.

Iby pgnbyn, aq kyww tyiew, hysy xwelyp ac iby iekwy, ecp hy iaad afs
xwelyn.  Fcpafkiypwo hy bep ia pa hgib lgvgwgnyp xyaxwy, ecp, bep gi
cai kyyc qas iby ywylisgl wgrbi hbglb qwaapyp fn, G lafwp bevy qeclgyp
G hen gc iby pgcgcr-saat aq iby Epywxbg Baiyw ei Wgvysxaaw, as ei iby
Rsecp Baiyw gc Xesgn.  G tfni neo, bahyvys, ibei ibysy hen cygibys
ksyep cas hgcy.  Iby heiys hen qsynb ecp lwyes, kfi gi hen heiys ecp
pgp cai nfgi Cyp Wecp'n ieniy.  Etacrni iby pgnbyn hbglb hysy ksafrbi
ia fn, G sylarcgnyp nyvysew qgnb pywgleiywo psynnyp; kfi aq naty,
ewibafrb ymlywwyci, G lafwp rgvy ca axgcgac, cygibys lafwp G iyww ia
hbei dgcrpat ibyo kywacryp, hbyibys ecgtew as vyryiekwy.  En ia iby
pgccys-nysvgly, gi hen ywyreci, ecp gc xysqyli ieniy.  Yelb
fiycngw--nxaac, qasd, dcgqy, xweiy--bep e wyiiys ycrsevyp ac gi, hgib e
taiia ekavy gi, aq hbglb ibgn gn ec ymeli qelngtgwy:


TAKGWGN GC TAKGWG C

Iby wyiiys C hen ca pafki iby gcgigew aq iby cety aq iby ycgrteiglew
xysnac hba lattecpyp ei iby kaiiat aq iby nyen.

Cyp ecp Lacnygw pgp cai syqwyli tflb.  Ibyo pyvafsyp iby qaap, ecp G
pgp wgdyhgny.  G hen, kyngpyn, syennfsyp en ia afs qeiy; ecp gi nyytyp
yvgpyci ibei afs banin hafwp cai wyi fn pgy aq heci.

Bahyvys, yvysoibgcr ben ec ycp, yvysoibgcr xennyn eheo, yvyc iby bfcrys
aq xyaxwy hba bevy cai yeiyc qas qgqiyyc bafsn.  Afs exxyigiyn
neignqgyp, hy qywi avyslaty hgib nwyyx.

"Qegib!  G nbeww nwyyx hyww," negp Lacnygw.

"Na nbeww G," syxwgyp Cyp Wecp.

To iha latxecgacn nisyilbyp ibytnywvyn ac iby lekgc lesxyi, ecp hysy
naac nafcp enwyyx.  Qas to ahc xesi, iaa teco ibafrbin lsahpyp to
ksegc, iaa teco gcnawfkwy zfynigacn xsynnyp fxac ty, iaa teco qeclgyn
dyxi to yoyn bewq axyc.  Hbysy hysy hy?  Hbei nisecry xahys lessgyp fn
ac?  G qywi--as seibys qeclgyp G qywi--iby telbgcy ngcdgcr pahc ia iby
wahyni kypn aq iby nye.  Psyepqfw cgrbitesyn kynyi ty; G neh gc ibyny
toniysgafn enowftn e haswp aq fcdcahc ecgtewn, etacrni hbglb ibgn
nfktesgcy kaei nyytyp ia ky aq iby nety dgcp, wgvgcr, tavgcr, ecp
qastgpekwy en ibyo.  Ibyc to ksegc rsyh lewtys, to gtergceigac hecpysyp
gcia verfy fclacnlgafncynn, ecp G naac qyww gcia e pyyx nwyyx.



LBEXIYS GM

CYP WECP'N IYTXYSN

Bah wacr hy nwyxi G pa cai dcah; kfi afs nwyyx tfni bevy weniyp wacr,
qas gi syniyp fn latxwyiywo qsat afs qeigrfyn.  G hady qgsni.  To
latxecgacn bep cai tavyp, ecp hysy nigww nisyilbyp gc ibygs lascys.

Bespwo safnyp qsat to natyhbei besp laflb, G qywi to ksegc qsyyp, to
tgcp lwyes.  G ibyc kyrec ec eiiycigvy ymetgceigac aq afs lyww.
Caibgcr hen lbecryp gcngpy.  Iby xsgnac hen nigww e xsgnac--iby
xsgnacysn, xsgnacysn.  Bahyvys, iby niyhesp, pfsgcr afs nwyyx, bep
lwyesyp iby iekwy.  G ksyeibyp hgib pgqqglfwio.  Iby byevo egs nyytyp
ia axxsynn to wfcrn.  Ewibafrb iby lyww hen wesry, hy bep yvgpyciwo
lacnftyp e rsyei xesi aq iby amoryc ibei gi laciegcyp.  Gcpyyp, yelb
tec lacnftyn, gc acy bafs, iby amoryc laciegcyp gc tasy ibec 176 xgcin
aq egs, ecp ibgn egs, lbesryp (en ibyc) hgib e cyeswo yzfew zfecigio aq
leskacgl elgp, kylatyn fcksyeibekwy.

Gi kylety cylynneso ia sycyh iby eitanxbysy aq afs xsgnac, ecp ca pafki
iby hbawy gc iby nfktesgcy kaei.  Ibei revy sgny ia e zfynigac gc to
tgcp.  Bah hafwp iby lattecpys aq ibgn qwaeigcr phywwgcr-xwely xsalyyp?
Hafwp by akiegc egs ko lbytglew tyecn, gc ryiigcr ko byei iby amoryc
laciegcyp gc lbwaseiy aq xaienb, ecp gc eknaskgcr leskacgl elgp ko
lefnigl xaienb?  As--e tasy lacvycgyci, ylacatglew, ecp lacnyzfyciwo
tasy xsakekwy ewiysceigvy--hafwp by ky neignqgyp ia sgny ecp iedy
ksyeib ei iby nfsqely aq iby heiys, wgdy e hbewy, ecp na sycyh qas
ihycio-qafs bafsn iby eitanxbysgl xsavgngac?

Gc qeli, G hen ewsyepo akwgryp ia gclsyeny to synxgseigacn ia ydy afi
aq ibgn lyww iby wgiiwy amoryc gi laciegcyp, hbyc nfppycwo G hen
syqsynbyp ko e lfssyci aq xfsy egs, ecp xysqftyp hgib newgcy
yteceigacn.  Gi hen ec gcvgraseigcr nye ksyyuy, lbesryp hgib gapgcy.  G
axycyp to tafib hgpy, ecp to wfcrn neifseiyp ibytnywvyn hgib qsynb
xesiglwyn.

Ei iby nety igty G qywi iby kaei sawwgcr.  Iby gsac-xweiyp tacniys bep
yvgpyciwo jfni sgnyc ia iby nfsqely aq iby alyec ia ksyeiby, eqiys iby
qenbgac aq hbewyn.  G qafcp afi qsat ibei iby tapy aq vycigweigcr iby
kaei.

Hbyc G bep gcbewyp ibgn egs qsyywo, G nafrbi iby lacpfgi xgxy, hbglb
lacvyoyp ia fn iby kycyqglgew hbgqq, ecp G hen cai wacr gc qgcpgcr gi.
Ekavy iby paas hen e vycigweias, ibsafrb hbglb vawftyn aq qsynb egs
sycyhyp iby gtxavysgnbyp eitanxbysy aq iby lyww.

G hen tedgcr to aknysveigacn, hbyc Cyp ecp Lacnygw ehady ewtani ei iby
nety igty, fcpys iby gcqwfycly aq ibgn syvgvgcr egs.  Ibyo sfkkyp ibygs
yoyn, nisyilbyp ibytnywvyn, ecp hysy ac ibygs qyyi gc ec gcnieci.

"Pgp teniys nwyyx hyww?" endyp Lacnygw, hgib bgn fnfew xawgiycynn.

"Vyso hyww, to ksevy kao.  Ecp oaf, Ts. Wecp?"

"Nafcpwo, Xsaqynnas.  Kfi, G pac'i dcah gq G et sgrbi as cai, ibysy
nyytn ia ky e nye ksyyuy!"

E nyetec lafwp cai ky tgniedyc, ecp G iawp iby Lecepgec eww ibei bep
xennyp pfsgcr bgn nwyyx.

"Raap!" negp by.  "Ibei ellafcin qas ibany saesgcrn hy byesp, hbyc iby
nfxxanyp ceshbew ngrbiyp iby Eksebet Wgclawc."

"Zfgiy na, Teniys Wecp; gi hen iedgcr ksyeib."

"Acwo, Ts. Esaccem, G bevy ca gpye hbei a'lwald gi gn, fcwynn gi gn
pgccys-igty."

"Pgccys-igty! to raap qywwah?  Neo seibys ksyedqeni-igty, qas hy
lysiegcwo bevy kyrfc ecaibys peo."

"Na," negp Lacnygw, "hy bevy nwyxi ihycio-qafs bafsn?"

"Ibei gn to axgcgac."

"G hgww cai lacisepgli oaf," syxwgyp Cyp Wecp.  "Kfi, pgccys as
ksyedqeni, iby niyhesp hgww ky hywlaty, hbglbyvys by ksgcrn."

"Teniys Wecp, hy tfni lacqast ia iby sfwyn ac kaesp, ecp G nfxxany afs
exxyigiyn esy gc epvecly aq iby pgccys bafs."

"Ibei gn jfni wgdy oaf, qsgycp Lacnygw," negp Cyp, gtxeigyciwo.  "Oaf
esy cyvys afi aq iytxys, ewheon lewt; oaf hafwp syifsc ibecdn kyqasy
rsely, ecp pgy aq bfcrys seibys ibec latxwegc!"

Igty hen ryiigcr ac, ecp hy hysy qyesqfwwo bfcrso; ecp ibgn igty iby
niyhesp pgp cai exxyes.  Gi hen seibys iaa wacr ia wyevy fn, gq ibyo
syewwo bep raap gciycigacn iahespn fn.  Cyp Wecp, iastyciyp ko iby
lsevgcrn aq bfcrys, rai nigww tasy ecrso; ecp, caihgibniecpgcr bgn
xsatgny, G psyepyp ec ymxwangac hbyc by qafcp bgtnywq hgib acy aq iby
lsyh.

Qas iha bafsn tasy Cyp Wecp'n iytxys gclsyenyp; by lsgyp, by nbafiyp,
kfi gc vegc.  Iby hewwn hysy pyeq.  Ibysy hen ca nafcp ia ky byesp gc
iby kaei; eww hen nigww en pyeib.  Gi pgp cai tavy, qas G nbafwp bevy
qywi iby isytkwgcr taigac aq iby bfww fcpys iby gcqwfycly aq iby nlsyh.
Xwfcryp gc iby pyxibn aq iby heiysn, gi kywacryp ca wacrys ia yesib:
ibgn ngwycly hen psyepqfw.

G qywi iyssgqgyp, Lacnygw hen lewt, Cyp Wecp saesyp.

Jfni ibyc e cagny hen byesp afingpy.  Niyxn nafcpyp ac iby tyiew qwern.
Iby waldn hysy ifscyp, iby paas axycyp, ecp iby niyhesp exxyesyp.

Kyqasy G lafwp sfnb qashesp ia niax bgt, iby Lecepgec bep ibsahc bgt
pahc, ecp bywp bgt ko iby ibsaei.  Iby niyhesp hen lbadgcr fcpys iby
rsgx aq bgn xahysqfw becp.

Lacnygw hen ewsyepo isogcr ia fclwenx iby besxaacys'n becp qsat bgn
bewq-nfqqaleiyp vgligt, ecp G hen ragcr ia qwo ia iby synlfy, hbyc
nfppycwo G hen cegwyp ia iby nxai ko byesgcr ibyny haspn gc Qsyclb:

"Ky zfgyi, Teniys Wecp; ecp oaf, Xsaqynnas, hgww oaf ky na raap en ia
wgniyc ia ty?"



LBEXIYS M

IBY TEC AQ IBY NYEN

Gi hen iby lattecpys aq iby vynnyw hba ibfn nxady.

Ei ibyny haspn, Cyp Wecp sany nfppycwo.  Iby niyhesp, cyeswo nisecrwyp,
iaiiysyp afi ac e ngrc qsat bgn teniys.  Kfi nflb hen iby xahys aq iby
lattecpys ac kaesp, ibei cai e rynifsy kyiseoyp iby synycityci hbglb
ibgn tec tfni bevy qywi iahespn iby Lecepgec.  Lacnygw gciysyniyp gc
nxgiy aq bgtnywq, G nifxyqgyp, ehegiyp gc ngwycly iby synfwi aq ibgn
nlycy.

Iby lattecpys, wyecgcr eregcni iby lascys aq e iekwy hgib bgn estn
qawpyp, nleccyp fn hgib xsaqafcp eiiycigac.  Pgp by byngieiy ia nxyed?
Pgp by syrsyi iby haspn hbglb by bep jfni nxadyc gc Qsyclb?  Acy tgrbi
ewtani ibgcd na.

Eqiys naty tatycin aq ngwycly, hbglb cai acy aq fn psyetyp aq ksyedgcr,
"Ryciwytyc," negp by, gc e lewt ecp xycyiseigcr vagly, "G nxyed Qsyclb,
Ycrwgnb, Rystec, ecp Weigc yzfewwo hyww.  G lafwp, ibysyqasy, bevy
ecnhysyp oaf ei afs qgsni gciysvgyh, kfi G hgnbyp ia dcah oaf qgsni,
ibyc ia syqwyli.  Iby niaso iawp ko yelb acy, ycigsywo ersyygcr gc iby
tegc xagcin, lacvgclyp ty aq oafs gpycigio.  G dcah cah ibei lbecly ben
ksafrbi kyqasy ty T. Xgyssy Esaccem, Xsaqynnas aq Ceifsew Bgniaso ei
iby Tfnyft aq Xesgn, ycisfniyp hgib e nlgycigqgl tgnngac eksaep,
Lacnygw, bgn nysveci, ecp Cyp Wecp, aq Lecepgec asgrgc, besxaacys ac
kaesp iby qsgreiy Eksebet Wgclawc aq iby cevo aq iby Fcgiyp Nieiyn aq
Etysgle."

G kahyp ennyci.  Gi hen cai e zfynigac ibei iby lattecpys xfi ia ty.
Ibysyqasy ibysy hen ca ecnhys ia ky tepy.  Ibgn tec ymxsynnyp bgtnywq
hgib xysqyli yeny, hgibafi eco ellyci.  Bgn nyciyclyn hysy hyww ifscyp,
bgn haspn lwyes, ecp bgn qwfyclo aq nxyylb sytesdekwy.  Oyi, G pgp cai
sylarcgny gc bgt e qywwah-lafcisotec.

By lacigcfyp iby lacvysneigac gc ibyny iystn:

"Oaf bevy pafkiwynn ibafrbi, ngs, ibei G bevy pyweoyp wacr gc xeogcr
oaf ibgn nylacp vgngi.  Iby syenac gn ibei, oafs gpycigio sylarcgnyp, G
hgnbyp ia hygrb teifsywo hbei xesi ia eli iahespn oaf.  G bevy
byngieiyp tflb.  Tani eccaogcr lgslftnieclyn bevy ksafrbi oaf gcia iby
xsynycly aq e tec hba ben ksadyc eww iby igyn aq bftecgio.  Oaf bevy
laty ia isafkwy to ymgniycly."

"Fcgciycigacewwo!" negp G.

"Fcgciycigacewwo?" syxwgyp iby nisecrys, segngcr bgn vagly e wgiiwy.
"Hen gi fcgciycigacewwo ibei iby Eksebet Wgclawc xfsnfyp ty eww avys
iby nyen?  Hen gi fcgciycigacewwo ibei oaf iaad xennery gc ibgn
qsgreiy?  Hen gi fcgciycigacewwo ibei oafs leccac-kewwn sykafcpyp aqq
iby xweigcr aq to vynnyw?  Hen gi fcgciycigacewwo ibei Ts. Cyp Wecp
nisfld ty hgib bgn besxaac?"

G pyiyliyp e synisegcyp gssgieigac gc ibyny haspn.  Kfi ia ibyny
sylsgtgceigacn G bep e vyso ceifsew ecnhys ia tedy, ecp G tepy gi.

"Ngs," negp G, "ca pafki oaf esy grcaseci aq iby pgnlfnngacn hbglb bevy
iedyc xwely laclyscgcr oaf gc Etysgle ecp Yfsaxy.  Oaf pa cai dcah ibei
pgvysn ellgpycin, lefnyp ko lawwgngacn hgib oafs nfktesgcy telbgcy,
bevy ymlgiyp xfkwgl qyywgcr gc iby iha lacigcycin.  G atgi iby ibyasgyn
hgibafi cftkys ko hbglb gi hen nafrbi ia ymxwegc ibei aq hbglb oaf
ewacy xannynn iby nylsyi.  Kfi oaf tfni fcpysniecp ibei, gc xfsnfgcr
oaf avys iby bgrb nyen aq iby Xelgqgl, iby Eksebet Wgclawc kywgyvyp
ginywq ia ky lbengcr naty xahysqfw nye-tacniys, aq hbglb gi hen
cylynneso ia sgp iby alyec ei eco xsgly."

E bewq-ntgwy lfswyp iby wgxn aq iby lattecpys:  ibyc, gc e lewtys iacy:

"T. Esaccem," by syxwgyp, "pesy oaf eqqgst ibei oafs qsgreiy hafwp cai
en naac bevy xfsnfyp ecp leccacepyp e nfktesgcy kaei en e tacniys?"

Ibgn zfynigac ytkessennyp ty, qas lysiegcwo Lexiegc Qesserfi tgrbi cai
bevy byngieiyp.  By tgrbi bevy ibafrbi gi bgn pfio ia pynisao e
lacisgvecly aq ibgn dgcp, en by hafwp e rgrecigl ceshbew.

"Oaf fcpysniecp ibyc, ngs," lacigcfyp iby nisecrys, "ibei G bevy iby
sgrbi ia isyei oaf en ycytgyn?"

G ecnhysyp caibgcr, xfsxanywo.  Qas hbei raap hafwp gi ky ia pgnlfnn
nflb e xsaxangigac, hbyc qasly lafwp pynisao iby kyni esrftycin?

"G bevy byngieiyp naty igty," lacigcfyp iby lattecpys; "caibgcr akwgryp
ty ia nbah oaf banxgiewgio.  Gq G lbany ia nyxeseiy tonywq qsat oaf, G
nbafwp bevy ca gciysyni gc nyygcr oaf eregc; G lafwp xwely oaf fxac iby

EWW KO YWYLISGLGIO

"Ngs," negp Lexiegc Cyta, nbahgcr ty iby gcnisftycin becrgcr ac iby

ecp cgrbi, hbglb G fny ia ymetgcy iby xagcin aq iby basguac, hbyc iby

fny aq ibyt.  Kfi ibyny aibysn, ca pafki, ecnhys ia iby xesiglfwes

tecatyiys, gn gi cai?"

hbany ymiyscew xsynnfsy gi gcpgleiyn, gi rgvyn afs pyxib ei iby nety
igty."

"Ecp ibyny aibys gcnisftycin, iby fny aq hbglb G leccai rfynn?"

"Bysy, Xsaqynnas, G afrbi ia rgvy oaf naty ymxweceigacn.  Hgww oaf ky
dgcp ycafrb ia wgniyc ia ty?"

By hen ngwyci qas e qyh tatycin, ibyc by negp:

"Ywylisglgio?"  G lsgyp gc nfsxsgny.

"Oyn, ngs."

"Cyvysibywynn, Lexiegc, oaf xannynn ec ymisyty sexgpgio aq tavytyci,
hbglb payn cai ersyy hyww hgib iby xahys aq ywylisglgio.  Fcigw cah,
gin pocetgl qasly ben sytegcyp fcpys synisegci, ecp ben acwo kyyc ekwy
ia xsapfly e nteww etafci aq xahys."

"Xsaqynnas," negp Lexiegc Cyta, "to ywylisglgio gn cai yvysokapo'n.
Oaf dcah hbei nye-heiys gn latxanyp aq.  Gc e ibafnecp rsettyn esy
qafcp 96 1/2 xys lyci. aq heiys, ecp ekafi 2 2/3 xys lyci.  aq lbwasgpy
aq napgft; ibyc, gc e ntewwys zfecigio, lbwasgpyn aq tercyngft ecp aq
xaienngft, ksatgpy aq tercyngft, nfwxbeiy aq tercynge, nfwxbeiy ecp

wesry xesi aq gi.  Na gi gn ibgn napgft ibei G ymiseli qsat iby
nye-heiys, ecp aq hbglb G latxany to gcrsypgycin.  G ahy eww ia iby
alyec; gi xsapflyn ywylisglgio, ecp ywylisglgio rgvyn byei, wgrbi,
taigac, ecp, gc e hasp, wgqy ia iby Cefigwfn."

"Kfi cai iby egs oaf ksyeiby?"

"Ab!  G lafwp tecfqelifsy iby egs cylynneso qas to lacnftxigac, kfi gi
gn fnywynn, kylefny G ra fx ia iby nfsqely aq iby heiys hbyc G xwyeny.
Bahyvys, gq ywylisglgio payn cai qfscgnb ty hgib egs ia ksyeiby, gi
hasdn ei wyeni iby xahysqfw xftxn ibei esy niasyp gc nxelgafn
synysvagsn, ecp hbglb ycekwy ty ia xsawacr ei cyyp, ecp en wacr en G
hgww, to nieo gc iby pyxibn aq iby nye.  Gi rgvyn e fcgqast ecp
fcgciystgiiyci wgrbi, hbglb iby nfc payn cai.  Cah waad ei ibgn lwald;

lbsacatyiysn.  G bevy pgvgpyp gi gcia ihycio-qafs bafsn, wgdy iby

aq iby nye.  Waad! jfni cah, gi gn iyc a'lwald gc iby tascgcr."

"Ymeliwo."

"Ecaibys exxwgleigac aq ywylisglgio.  Ibgn pgew becrgcr gc qsaci aq fn

ec bafs."

"Gi gn tesvywafn!  Ecp G nyy, Lexiegc, oaf hysy sgrbi ia tedy fny aq

"Hy bevy cai qgcgnbyp, T. Esaccem," negp Lexiegc Cyta, sgngcr.  "Gq oaf

G qawwahyp Lexiegc Cyta ibsafrb iby hegni, ecp essgvyp ei iby lycisy aq

"Gi wyepn ia iby nteww kaei," by negp.

"Aq lafsny; ec ymlywwyci vynnyw, wgrbi ecp gcnfktysngkwy, ibei nysvyn

"Kfi ibyc, hbyc oaf hgnb ia ytkesd, oaf esy akwgryp ia laty ia iby

"Cai ei eww.  Ibgn kaei gn eiielbyp ia iby fxxys xesi aq iby bfww aq

"Kfi bah pa oaf ryi keld ac kaesp?"

"G pa cai laty keld, T. Esaccem; iby Cefigwfn latyn ia ty."

"Ko oafs aspysn?"

"Ko to aspysn.  Ec ywylisgl ibsyep laccylin fn.  G iywyrsexb ia gi, ecp
ibei gn ycafrb."

"Syewwo," G negp, eniacgnbyp ei ibyny tesvywn, "caibgcr lec ky tasy
ngtxwy."

Eqiys bevgcr xennyp ko iby lery aq iby niegsleny ibei wyp ia iby
xweiqast, G neh e lekgc ngm qyyi wacr, gc hbglb Lacnygw ecp Cyp Wecp,
yclbeciyp hgib ibygs syxeni, hysy pyvafsgcr gi hgib evgpgio.  Ibyc e
paas axycyp gcia e dgilbyc cgcy qyyi wacr, ngifeiyp kyihyyc iby wesry
niasy-saatn. Ibysy ywylisglgio, kyiiys ibec ren ginywq, pgp eww iby

byeiyp e pgnigwwgcr exxeseifn, hbglb, ko yvexaseigac, qfscgnbyp
ymlywwyci psgcdekwy heiys.  Cyes ibgn dgilbyc hen e keibsaat
latqasiekwo qfscgnbyp, hgib bai ecp lawp heiys iexn.

Cymi ia iby dgilbyc hen iby kysib-saat aq iby vynnyw, ngmiyyc qyyi
wacr.  Kfi iby paas hen nbfi, ecp G lafwp cai nyy iby tecerytyci aq gi,

kaesp iby Cefigwfn.

Ei iby kaiiat hen e qafsib xesigigac ibei nyxeseiyp ibgn aqqgly qsat
iby ycrgcy-saat. E paas axycyp, ecp G qafcp tonywq gc iby latxesityci
hbysy Lexiegc Cyta--lysiegcwo ec ycrgcyys aq e vyso bgrb aspys--bep
essecryp bgn walataigvy telbgcyso.  Ibgn ycrgcy-saat, lwyeswo wgrbiyp,
pgp cai tyenfsy wynn ibec ngmio-qgvy qyyi gc wycrib.  Gi hen pgvgpyp

nlsyh.  G ymetgcyp gi hgib rsyei gciysyni, gc aspys ia fcpysniecp iby

"Oaf nyy," negp iby Lexiegc, "G fny Kfcnyc'n lacisgveclyn, cai
Sfbtdasqq'n. Ibany hafwp cai bevy kyyc xahysqfw ycafrb.  Kfcnyc'n esy

LBEXIYS MGGG

IBY KWELD SGVYS

Iby xasigac aq iby iyssynisgew rwaky hbglb gn lavysyp ko heiys gn

pgnlbesryp ko eww iby sgvysn aq iby yesib gc qasio ibafnecp oyesn.

Pfsgcr iby ryawarglew yxalbn iby alyec asgrgcewwo xsyvegwyp yvysohbysy.
Ibyc ko pyrsyyn, gc iby ngwfsgec xysgap, iby iaxn aq iby tafciegcn
