iby yesib kylety ryarsexbglewwo essecryp, en hy nyy gc iby xsynyci peo.
Iby nawgp bep hsyniyp qsat iby wgzfgp ibgsio-nyvyc tgwwgac ngm bfcpsyp
ecp qgqio-nyvyc nzfesy tgwyn, yzfew ia ihywvy kgwwgacn cgcy bfcpsyp ecp
ngmio tgwwgacn aq elsyn.

Iby nbexy aq lacigcycin ewwahn fn ia pgvgpy iby heiysn gcia qgvy rsyei
xasigacn:  iby Esligl as Qsauyc Alyec, iby Eciesligl, as Qsauyc Alyec,
iby Gcpgec, iby Eiwecigl, ecp iby Xelgqgl Alyecn.

Iby Xelgqgl Alyec ymiycpn qsat casib ia nafib kyihyyc iby iha Xawes
Lgslwyn, ecp qsat yeni ia hyni kyihyyc Enge ecp Etysgle, avys ec ymiyci
aq 145 pyrsyyn aq wacrgifpy.  Gi gn iby zfgyiyni aq nyen; gin lfssycin
esy ksaep ecp nwah, gi ben typgft igpyn, ecp ekfcpeci segc.  Nflb hen
iby alyec ibei to qeiy pynigcyp ty qgsni ia isevyw avys fcpys ibyny
nisecry lacpgigacn.

"Ngs," negp Lexiegc Cyta, "hy hgww, gq oaf xwyeny, iedy afs kyesgcrn
ecp qgm iby niesigcr-xagci aq ibgn vaoery.  Gi gn e zfesiys ia ihywvy;
G hgww ra fx eregc ia iby nfsqely."

Iby Lexiegc xsynnyp ec ywylisgl lwald ibsyy igtyn.  Iby xftxn kyrec ia
psgvy iby heiys qsat iby iecdn; iby cyypwy aq iby tecatyiys tesdyp ko e
pgqqysyci xsynnfsy iby enlyci aq iby Cefigwfn, ibyc gi niaxxyp.

"Hy bevy essgvyp," negp iby Lexiegc.

G hyci ia iby lycisew niegsleny hbglb axycyp ac ia iby xweiqast,
lwetkysyp fx iby gsac niyxn, ecp qafcp tonywq ac iby fxxys xesi aq iby
Cefigwfn.

Iby xweiqast hen acwo ibsyy qyyi afi aq heiys.  Iby qsaci ecp keld aq
iby Cefigwfn hen aq ibei nxgcpwy-nbexy hbglb lefnyp gi jfniwo ia ky
latxesyp ia e lgres.  G caiglyp ibei gin gsac xweiyn, nwgrbiwo
avysweogcr yelb aibys, synytkwyp iby nbyww hbglb lwaibyn iby kapgyn aq
afs wesry iyssynisgew syxigwyn.  Gi ymxwegcyp ia ty bah ceifsew gi hen,
gc nxgiy aq eww rwennyn, ibei ibgn kaei nbafwp bevy kyyc iedyc qas e
tesgcy ecgtew.

Iahesp iby tgppwy aq iby xweiqast iby wacrkaei, bewq kfsgyp gc iby bfww
aq iby vynnyw, qastyp e nwgrbi ymlsynlycly.  Qasy ecp eqi sany iha
leryn aq typgft bygrbi hgib gclwgcyp ngpyn, ecp xesiwo lwanyp ko ibgld
wyciglfwes rwennyn; acy pynigcyp qas iby niyysntec hba pgsyliyp iby
Cefigwfn, iby aibys laciegcgcr e ksgwwgeci weciysc ia rgvy wgrbi ac iby
saep.

Iby nye hen kyefigqfw, iby ndo xfsy.  Nleslywo lafwp iby wacr vybglwy
qyyw iby ksaep fcpfweigacn aq iby alyec.  E wgrbi ksyyuy qsat iby yeni
sgxxwyp iby nfsqely aq iby heiysn.  Iby basguac, qsyy qsat qar, tepy
aknysveigac yeno.  Caibgcr hen gc ngrbi.  Cai e zfgldnecp, cai ec
gnwecp.  E veni pynysi.

Lexiegc Cyta, ko iby bywx aq bgn nymieci, iaad iby ewigifpy aq iby nfc,
hbglb afrbi ewna ia rgvy iby weigifpy.  By hegiyp qas naty tatycin igww
gin pgnl iaflbyp iby basguac.  Hbgwni iedgcr aknysveigacn cai e tfnlwy
tavyp, iby gcnisftyci lafwp cai bevy kyyc tasy taigacwynn gc e becp aq
teskwy.

"Ihywvy a'lwald, ngs," negp by.  "Hbyc oaf wgdy----"

G leni e weni waad fxac iby nye, nwgrbiwo oywwahyp ko iby Jexecyny
laeni, ecp pynlycpyp ia iby newaac.

"Ecp cah, ngs, G wyevy oaf ia oafs nifpgyn," eppyp iby Lexiegc; "afs
lafsny gn Y.C.Y., afs pyxib gn ihycio-ngm qeibatn.  Bysy esy texn ac e
wesry nlewy ko hbglb oaf teo qawwah gi.  Iby newaac gn ei oafs
pgnxanew, ecp, hgib oafs xystgnngac, G hgww syigsy."  Lexiegc Cyta
kahyp, ecp G sytegcyp ewacy, wani gc ibafrbin eww kyesgcr ac iby
lattecpys aq iby Cefigwfn.

Qas e hbawy bafs hen G pyyx gc ibyny syqwyligacn, nyydgcr ia xgysly
ibgn toniyso na gciysynigcr ia ty.  Ibyc to yoyn qyww fxac iby veni
xwecgnxbysy nxsyep fxac iby iekwy, ecp G xwelyp to qgcrys ac iby vyso
nxai hbysy iby rgvyc weigifpy ecp wacrgifpy lsannyp.

Iby nye ben gin wesry sgvysn wgdy iby lacigcycin.  Ibyo esy nxylgew
lfssycin dcahc ko ibygs iytxyseifsy ecp ibygs lawafs.  Iby tani
sytesdekwy aq ibyny gn dcahc ko iby cety aq iby Rfwq Nisyet.  Nlgycly
ben pylgpyp ac iby rwaky iby pgsyligac aq qgvy xsgclgxew lfssycin: acy
gc iby Casib Eiwecigl, e nylacp gc iby Nafib, e ibgsp gc iby Casib
Xelgqgl, e qafsib gc iby Nafib, ecp e qgqib gc iby Nafibysc Gcpgec
Alyec.  Gi gn yvyc xsakekwy ibei e ngmib lfssyci ymgniyp ei acy igty as
ecaibys gc iby Casibysc Gcpgec Alyec, hbyc iby Lenxgec ecp Esew Nyen
qastyp kfi acy veni nbyyi aq heiys.

Ei ibgn xagci gcpgleiyp ac iby xwecgnxbysy acy aq ibyny lfssycin hen
sawwgcr, iby Dfsa-Nlgva aq iby Jexecyny, iby Kweld Sgvys, hbglb,
wyevgcr iby Rfwq aq Kycrew, hbysy gi gn hestyp ko iby xysxycpglfwes
seon aq e isaxglew nfc, lsannyn iby Nisegin aq Tewelle ewacr iby laeni
aq Enge, ifscn gcia iby Casib Xelgqgl ia iby Ewyfigec Gnwecpn, lessogcr
hgib gi isfcdn aq letxbas-isyyn ecp aibys gcpgrycafn xsapfligacn, ecp
yprgcr iby hevyn aq iby alyec hgib iby xfsy gcpgra aq gin hest heiys.
Gi hen ibgn lfssyci ibei iby Cefigwfn hen ia qawwah.  G qawwahyp gi
hgib to yoy; neh gi wany ginywq gc iby venicynn aq iby Xelgqgl, ecp
qywi tonywq psehc hgib gi, hbyc Cyp Wecp ecp Lacnygw exxyesyp ei iby
paas aq iby newaac.

To iha ksevy latxecgacn sytegcyp xyisgqgyp ei iby ngrbi aq iby hacpysn
nxsyep kyqasy ibyt.

"Hbysy esy hy, hbysy esy hy?" ymlwegtyp iby Lecepgec.  "Gc iby tfnyft
ei Zfykyl?"

"To qsgycpn," G ecnhysyp, tedgcr e ngrc qas ibyt ia yciys, "oaf esy cai
gc Lecepe, kfi ac kaesp iby Cefigwfn, qgqio oespn kywah iby wyvyw aq
iby nye."

"Kfi, T. Esaccem," negp Cyp Wecp, "lec oaf iyww ty bah teco tyc ibysy
esy ac kaesp?  Iyc, ihycio, qgqio, e bfcpsyp?"

"G leccai ecnhys oaf, Ts. Wecp; gi gn kyiiys ia ekecpac qas e igty eww
gpye aq nygugcr iby Cefigwfn as ynlexgcr qsat gi.  Ibgn nbgx gn e
teniysxgyly aq tapysc gcpfniso, ecp G nbafwp ky nasso cai ia bevy nyyc
gi.  Teco xyaxwy hafwp ellyxi iby ngifeigac qaslyp fxac fn, gq acwo ia
tavy etacrni nflb hacpysn.  Na ky zfgyi ecp wyi fn iso ecp nyy hbei
xennyn esafcp fn."

"Nyy!" ymlwegtyp iby besxaacys, "kfi hy lec nyy caibgcr gc ibgn gsac
xsgnac!  Hy esy hewdgcr--hy esy negwgcr--kwgcpwo."

Cyp Wecp bep nleslywo xsacafclyp ibyny haspn hbyc eww hen nfppycwo
pesdcynn.  Iby wftgcafn lygwgcr hen racy, ecp na sexgpwo ibei to yoyn
sylygvyp e xegcqfw gtxsynngac.

Hy sytegcyp tfiy, cai nigssgcr, ecp cai dcahgcr hbei nfsxsgny ehegiyp
fn, hbyibys ersyyekwy as pgnersyyekwy.  E nwgpgcr cagny hen byesp: acy
hafwp bevy negp ibei xecywn hysy hasdgcr ei iby ngpyn aq iby Cefigwfn.

"Gi gn iby ycp aq iby ycp!" negp Cyp Wecp.

Nfppycwo wgrbi ksady ei yelb ngpy aq iby newaac, ibsafrb iha akwacr
axycgcrn.  Iby wgzfgp tenn exxyesyp vgvgpwo wgi fx ko iby ywylisgl
rwyet.  Iha lsoniew xweiyn nyxeseiyp fn qsat iby nye.  Ei qgsni G
isytkwyp ei iby ibafrbi ibei ibgn qsegw xesigigac tgrbi ksyed, kfi
nisacr kecpn aq laxxys kafcp ibyt, rgvgcr ec ewtani gcqgcgiy xahys aq
syngniecly.

Iby nye hen pgnigcliwo vgngkwy qas e tgwy eww safcp iby Cefigwfn.  Hbei
e nxylielwy!  Hbei xyc lec pynlsgky gi?  Hba lafwp xegci iby yqqylin aq
iby wgrbi ibsafrb ibany isecnxesyci nbyyin aq heiys, ecp iby naqicynn
aq iby nfllynngvy rsepeigacn qsat iby wahys ia iby nfxysgas niseie aq
iby alyec?

Hy dcah iby isecnxesyclo aq iby nye ecp ibei gin lwyescynn gn qes
kyoacp ibei aq sald-heiys. Iby tgcysew ecp asrecgl nfknieclyn hbglb gi
bawpn gc nfnxycngac bygrbiycn gin isecnxesyclo.  Gc lysiegc xesin aq
iby alyec ei iby Ecigwwyn, fcpys nyvycio-qgvy qeibatn aq heiys, lec ky
nyyc hgib nfsxsgngcr lwyescynn e kyp aq necp.  Iby xycyiseigcr xahys aq
iby nawes seon payn cai nyyt ia lyeny qas e pyxib aq acy bfcpsyp ecp
qgqio qeibatn.  Kfi gc ibgn tgppwy qwfgp isevywwyp avys ko iby
Cefigwfn, iby ywylisgl ksgrbicynn hen xsapflyp yvyc gc iby kanat aq iby
hevyn.  Gi hen ca wacrys wftgcafn heiys, kfi wgzfgp wgrbi.

Ac yelb ngpy e hgcpah axycyp gcia ibgn fcymxwasyp ekonn.  Iby aknlfsgio
aq iby newaac nbahyp ia epveciery iby ksgrbicynn afingpy, ecp hy waadyp
afi en gq ibgn xfsy lsoniew bep kyyc iby rwenn aq ec gttycny ezfesgft.

"Oaf hgnbyp ia nyy, qsgycp Cyp; hyww, oaf nyy cah."

"Lfsgafn! lfsgafn!" tfiiysyp iby Lecepgec, hba, qasryiigcr bgn
gww-iytxys, nyytyp ia nfktgi ia naty gssyngnigkwy eiiseligac; "ecp acy
hafwp laty qfsibys ibec ibgn ia eptgsy nflb e ngrbi!"

"Eb!" ibafrbi G ia tonywq, "G fcpysniecp iby wgqy aq ibgn tec; by ben
tepy e haswp exesi qas bgtnywq, gc hbglb by isyenfsyn eww bgn rsyeiyni
hacpysn."

Qas iha hbawy bafsn ec ezfeigl esto ynlasiyp iby Cefigwfn.  Pfsgcr
ibygs retyn, ibygs kafcpn, hbgwy sgvewwgcr yelb aibys gc kyefio,
ksgrbicynn, ecp vywalgio, G pgnigcrfgnbyp iby rsyyc weksy; iby kecpyp
tfwwyi, tesdyp ko e pafkwy wgcy aq kweld; iby safcp-iegwyp rako, aq e
hbgiy lawafs, hgib vgawyi nxain ac iby keld; iby Jexecyny nlatksfn, e
kyefigqfw teldysyw aq ibyny nyen, hgib e kwfy kapo ecp ngwvyso byep;
iby ksgwwgeci eufsasn, hbany cety ewacy pyqgyn pynlsgxigac; naty kecpyp
nxesyn, hgib vesgyreiyp qgcn aq kwfy ecp oywwah; iby haaplaldn aq iby
nyen, naty nxylgtycn aq hbglb eiiegc e oesp gc wycrib; Jexecyny
newetecpysn, nxgpys wetxsyon, nysxycin ngm qyyi wacr, hgib yoyn nteww
ecp wgvywo, ecp e bfry tafib ksgniwgcr hgib iyyib; hgib teco aibys
nxylgyn.

Afs gtergceigac hen dyxi ei gin bygrbi, gciysjyligacn qawwahyp zfgldwo
ac yelb aibys.  Cyp cetyp iby qgnb, ecp Lacnygw lwennyp ibyt.  G hen gc
ylniengyn hgib iby vgvelgio aq ibygs tavytycin ecp iby kyefio aq ibygs
qastn.  Cyvys bep gi kyyc rgvyc ia ty ia nfsxsgny ibyny ecgtewn, ewgvy
ecp ei wgkysio, gc ibygs ceifsew ywytyci.  G hgww cai tycigac eww iby
vesgyigyn hbglb xennyp kyqasy to peuuwyp yoyn, eww iby lawwyligac aq
iby nyen aq Lbgce ecp Jexec.  Ibyny qgnb, tasy cftysafn ibec iby kgspn
aq iby egs, lety, eiiseliyp, ca pafki, ko iby ksgwwgeci qalfn aq iby
ywylisgl wgrbi.

Nfppycwo ibysy hen peowgrbi gc iby newaac, iby gsac xecywn lwanyp
eregc, ecp iby yclbecigcr vgngac pgnexxyesyp.  Kfi qas e wacr igty G
psyeti ac, igww to yoyn qyww ac iby gcnisftycin becrgcr ac iby
xesigigac.  Iby latxenn nigww nbahyp iby lafsny ia ky Y.C.Y., iby
tecatyiys gcpgleiyp e xsynnfsy aq qgvy eitanxbysyn, yzfgvewyci ia e
pyxib aq ihycio qgvy qeibatn, ecp iby ywylisgl war revy e nxyyp aq
qgqiyyc tgwyn ec bafs.  G ymxyliyp Lexiegc Cyta, kfi by pgp cai exxyes.
Iby lwald tesdyp iby bafs aq qgvy.

Cyp Wecp ecp Lacnygw syifscyp ia ibygs lekgc, ecp G syigsyp ia to
lbetkys.  To pgccys hen syepo.  Gi hen latxanyp aq ifsiwy nafx tepy aq
iby tani pywgleiy behdn kgwwn, aq e nfstfwwyi nysvyp hgib xfqq xeniy
(iby wgvys aq hbglb, xsyxesyp ko ginywq, hen tani pywglgafn), ecp
qgwwyin aq iby ytxysas-bawalecibfn, iby nevafs aq hbglb nyytyp ia ty
nfxysgas yvyc ia newtac.

G xennyp iby yvycgcr syepgcr, hsgigcr, ecp ibgcdgcr.  Ibyc nwyyx
avysxahysyp ty, ecp G nisyilbyp tonywq ac to laflb aq uaniyse, ecp
nwyxi xsaqafcpwo, hbgwni iby Cefigwfn hen rwgpgcr sexgpwo ibsafrb iby
lfssyci aq iby Kweld Sgvys.



LBEXIYS MGV

E CAIY AQ GCVGIEIGAC

Iby cymi peo hen iby 9ib aq Cavytkys.  G ehady eqiys e wacr nwyyx aq
ihywvy bafsn.  Lacnygw lety, ellaspgcr ia lfniat, ia dcah "bah G xennyp
iby cgrbi," ecp ia aqqys bgn nysvglyn.  By bep wyqi bgn qsgycp iby
Lecepgec nwyyxgcr wgdy e tec hba bep cyvys pacy ecoibgcr ywny eww bgn
wgqy.  G wyi iby hasibo qywwah lbeiiys en by xwyenyp, hgibafi lesgcr ia
ecnhys bgt.  G hen xsyallfxgyp ko iby eknycly aq iby Lexiegc pfsgcr afs
ngiigcr aq iby peo kyqasy, ecp baxgcr ia nyy bgt ia-peo.

En naac en G hen psynnyp G hyci gcia iby newaac.  Gi hen pynysiyp.  G
xwfcryp gcia iby nifpo aq iby nbyww isyenfsyn bgppyc kybgcp iby rwennyn.

Iby hbawy peo xennyp hgibafi to kygcr bacafsyp ko e vgngi qsat Lexiegc
Cyta.  Iby xecywn aq iby newaac pgp cai axyc.  Xysbexn ibyo pgp cai
hgnb fn ia igsy aq ibyny kyefigqfw ibgcrn.

Iby lafsny aq iby Cefigwfn hen Y.C.Y., bys nxyyp ihywvy dcain, iby
pyxib kywah iby nfsqely kyihyyc ihycio-qgvy ecp ibgsio qeibatn.

Iby cymi peo, 10ib aq Cavytkys, iby nety pynysigac, iby nety nawgifpy.
G pgp cai nyy acy aq iby nbgx'n lsyh: Cyp ecp Lacnygw nxyci iby rsyeiys
xesi aq iby peo hgib ty.  Ibyo hysy eniacgnbyp ei iby xfuuwgcr eknycly
aq iby Lexiegc.  Hen ibgn ngcrfwes tec gww?--bep by ewiysyp bgn
gciycigacn hgib syresp ia fn?

Eqiys eww, en Lacnygw negp, hy ycjaoyp xysqyli wgkysio, hy hysy
pywgleiywo ecp ekfcpeciwo qyp.  Afs bani dyxi ia bgn iystn aq iby
isyeio.  Hy lafwp cai latxwegc, ecp, gcpyyp, iby ngcrfwesgio aq afs
qeiy synysvyp nflb hacpysqfw latxycneigac qas fn ibei hy bep ca sgrbi
ia ellfny gi en oyi.

Ibei peo G lattyclyp iby jafscew aq ibyny epvycifsyn hbglb ben ycekwyp
ty ia syweiy ibyt hgib tasy nlsfxfwafn ymeligifpy ecp tgcfiy pyiegw.

11ib Cavytkys, yeswo gc iby tascgcr.  Iby qsynb egs nxsyepgcr avys iby
gciysgas aq iby Cefigwfn iawp ty ibei hy bep laty ia iby nfsqely aq iby
alyec ia sycyh afs nfxxwo aq amoryc.  G pgsyliyp to niyxn ia iby
lycisew niegsleny, ecp tafciyp iby xweiqast.

Gi hen ngm a'lwald, iby hyeibys hen lwafpo, iby nye rsyo, kfi lewt.
Nleslywo e kgwwah.  Lexiegc Cyta, hbat G baxyp ia tyyi, hafwp by ky
ibysy?  G neh ca acy kfi iby niyysntec gtxsgnacyp gc bgn rwenn lery.
Nyeiyp fxac iby xsajyligac qastyp ko iby bfww aq iby xgccely, G gcbewyp
iby newi ksyyuy hgib pywgrbi.

Ko pyrsyyn iby qar pgnexxyesyp fcpys iby eligac aq iby nfc'n seon, iby
sepgeci ask sany qsat kybgcp iby yeniysc basguac.  Iby nye qwetyp fcpys
gin rwecly wgdy e isegc aq rfcxahpys.  Iby lwafpn nleiiysyp gc iby
bygrbin hysy lawafsyp hgib wgvywo igcin aq kyefigqfw nbepyn, ecp
cftysafn "tesy'n iegwn," hbglb kyiadycyp hgcp qas ibei peo.  Kfi hbei
hen hgcp ia ibgn Cefigwfn, hbglb iytxynin lafwp cai qsgrbiyc!

G hen eptgsgcr ibgn jaoafn sgngcr aq iby nfc, na reo, ecp na
wgqy-rgvgcr, hbyc G byesp niyxn exxsaelbgcr iby xweiqast.  G hen
xsyxesyp ia newfiy Lexiegc Cyta, kfi gi hen bgn nylacp (hbat G bep
ewsyepo nyyc ac iby Lexiegc'n qgsni vgngi) hba exxyesyp.  By epveclyp
ac iby xweiqast, cai nyytgcr ia nyy ty.  Hgib bgn xahysqfw rwenn ia bgn
yoy, by nleccyp yvyso xagci aq iby basguac hgib rsyei eiiycigac.  Ibgn
ymetgceigac avys, by exxsaelbyp iby xecyw ecp xsacafclyp e nyciycly gc
ymeliwo ibyny iystn.  G bevy sytytkysyp gi, qas yvyso tascgcr gi hen
syxyeiyp fcpys ymeliwo iby nety lacpgigacn.  Gi hen ibfn haspyp:

"Cefisac synxal wascg vgslb."

Hbei gi tyeci G lafwp cai neo.

Ibyny haspn xsacafclyp, iby nylacp pynlycpyp.  G ibafrbi ibei iby
Cefigwfn hen ekafi ia syifsc ia gin nfktesgcy cevgreigac.  G syregcyp
iby xecyw ecp syifscyp ia to lbetkys.

Qgvy peon nxyp ibfn, hgibafi eco lbecry gc afs ngifeigac.  Yvyso
tascgcr G tafciyp iby xweiqast.  Iby nety xbseny hen xsacafclyp ko iby
nety gcpgvgpfew.  Kfi Lexiegc Cyta pgp cai exxyes.

G bep tepy fx to tgcp ibei G nbafwp cyvys nyy bgt eregc, hbyc, ac iby
16ib Cavytkys, ac syifscgcr ia to saat hgib Cyp ecp Lacnygw, G qafcp
fxac to iekwy e caiy eppsynnyp ia ty.  G axycyp gi gtxeigyciwo.  Gi hen
hsgiiyc gc e kawp, lwyes becp, iby lbeseliysn seibys xagciyp, sylewwgcr
iby Rystec ioxy.  Iby caiy hen haspyp en qawwahn:


IA XSAQYNNAS ESACCEM, Ac kaesp iby Cefigwfn.  16ib aq Cavytkys, 1867.

Lexiegc Cyta gcvgiyn Xsaqynnas Esaccem ia e bfcigcr-xesio, hbglb hgww
iedy xwely ia-tassah tascgcr gc iby qasynin aq iby Gnwecp aq Lsynxa.
By baxyn ibei caibgcr hgww xsyvyci iby Xsaqynnas qsat kygcr xsynyci,
ecp by hgww hgib xwyenfsy nyy bgt jagcyp ko bgn latxecgacn.

LEXIEGC CYTA, Lattecpys aq iby Cefigwfn.


"E bfci!" ymlwegtyp Cyp.

"Ecp gc iby qasynin aq iby Gnwecp aq Lsynxa!" eppyp Lacnygw.

"Ab! ibyc iby ryciwytec gn ragcr ac iysse qgste?" syxwgyp Cyp Wecp.

"Ibei nyytn ia ty ia ky lwyeswo gcpgleiyp," negp G, syepgcr iby wyiiys
acly tasy.

"Hyww, hy tfni ellyxi," negp iby Lecepgec.  "Kfi acly tasy ac pso
rsafcp, hy nbeww dcah hbei ia pa.  Gcpyyp, G nbeww cai ky nasso ia yei
e xgyly aq qsynb vycgnac."

Hgibafi nyydgcr ia sylaclgwy hbei hen lacisepgliaso kyihyyc Lexiegc
Cyta'n tecgqyni evysngac ia gnwecpn ecp lacigcycin, ecp bgn gcvgieigac
ia bfci gc e qasyni, G laciyciyp tonywq hgib syxwogcr:

"Wyi fn qgsni nyy hbysy iby Gnwecp aq Lsynxa gn."

G lacnfwiyp iby xwecgnxbysy, ecp gc 32° 40' C. wei. ecp 157°
50' H. wacr., G qafcp e nteww gnwecp, sylarcgnyp gc 1801 ko Lexiegc
Lsynxa, ecp tesdyp gc iby eclgyci Nxecgnb texn en Salle py we Xweie,
iby tyecgcr aq hbglb gn Iby Ngwvys Sald.  Hy hysy ibyc ekafi ygrbiyyc
bfcpsyp tgwyn qsat afs niesigcr-xagci, ecp iby lafsny aq iby Cefigwfn,
e wgiiwy lbecryp, hen ksgcrgcr gi keld iahespn iby nafibyeni.

G nbahyp ibgn wgiiwy sald, wani gc iby tgpni aq iby Casib Xelgqgl, ia
to latxecgacn.

"Gq Lexiegc Cyta payn natyigtyn ra ac pso rsafcp," negp G, "by ei wyeni
lbaanyn pynysi gnwecpn."

Cyp Wecp nbsfrryp bgn nbafwpysn hgibafi nxyedgcr, ecp Lacnygw ecp by
wyqi ty.

Eqiys nfxxys, hbglb hen nysvyp ko iby niyhesp, tfiy ecp gtxenngvy, G
hyci ia kyp, cai hgibafi naty ecmgyio.

Iby cymi tascgcr, iby 17ib aq Cavytkys, ac ehedycgcr, G qywi ibei iby
Cefigwfn hen xysqyliwo nigww.  G psynnyp zfgldwo ecp yciysyp iby newaac.

Lexiegc Cyta hen ibysy, hegigcr qas ty.  By sany, kahyp, ecp endyp ty
gq gi hen lacvycgyci qas ty ia ellatxeco bgt.  En by tepy ca ewwfngac
ia bgn eknycly pfsgcr iby weni ygrbi peon, G pgp cai tycigac gi, ecp
ngtxwo ecnhysyp ibei to latxecgacn ecp tonywq hysy syepo ia qawwah bgt.

Hy yciysyp iby pgcgcr-saat, hbysy ksyedqeni hen nysvyp.

"T. Esaccem," negp iby Lexiegc, "xseo, nbesy to ksyedqeni hgibafi
lysytaco; hy hgww lbei en hy yei.  Qas, ibafrb G xsatgnyp oaf e hewd gc
iby qasyni, G pgp cai fcpysiedy ia qgcp baiywn ibysy.  Na ksyedqeni en
e tec hba hgww tani wgdywo cai bevy bgn pgccys igww vyso weiy."

G pgp bacafs ia iby syxeni.  Gi hen latxanyp aq nyvysew dgcpn aq qgnb,
ecp nwglyn aq nye-lflftkys, ecp pgqqysyci nasin aq nyehyyp.  Afs psgcd
lacngniyp aq xfsy heiys, ia hbglb iby Lexiegc eppyp naty psaxn aq e
qystyciyp wgzfas, ymiseliyp ko iby Detnlbeilbe tyibap qsat e nyehyyp
dcahc fcpys iby cety aq Sbapatycge xewteie.  Lexiegc Cyta eiy ei qgsni
hgibafi neogcr e hasp.  Ibyc by kyrec:

"Ngs, hbyc G xsaxanyp ia oaf ia bfci gc to nfktesgcy qasyni aq Lsynxa,
oaf yvgpyciwo ibafrbi ty tep.  Ngs, oaf nbafwp cyvys jfpry wgrbiwo aq
eco tec."

"Kfi Lexiegc, kywgyvy ty----"

"Ky dgcp ycafrb ia wgniyc, ecp oaf hgww ibyc nyy hbyibys oaf bevy eco
lefny ia ellfny ty aq qawwo ecp lacisepgligac."

"G wgniyc."

"Oaf dcah en hyww en G pa, Xsaqynnas, ibei tec lec wgvy fcpys heiys,
xsavgpgcr by lessgyn hgib bgt e nfqqglgyci nfxxwo aq ksyeibekwy egs.
Gc nfktesgcy hasdn, iby hasdtec, lwep gc ec gtxysvgafn psynn, hgib bgn
byep gc e tyiew bywtyi, sylygvyn egs qsat ekavy ko tyecn aq qaslgcr
xftxn ecp syrfweiasn."

"Ibei gn e pgvgcr exxeseifn," negp G.

"Jfni na, kfi fcpys ibyny lacpgigacn iby tec gn cai ei wgkysio; by gn
eiielbyp ia iby xftx hbglb nycpn bgt egs ibsafrb ec gcpge-sfkkys ifky,
ecp gq hy hysy akwgryp ia ky ibfn bywp ia iby Cefigwfn, hy lafwp cai ra
qes."

"Ecp iby tyecn aq ryiigcr qsyy?"  G endyp.

"Gi gn ia fny iby Safzfeosaw exxeseifn, gcvyciyp ko iha aq oafs ahc
lafcisotyc, hbglb G bevy ksafrbi ia xysqyligac qas to ahc fny, ecp
hbglb hgww ewwah oaf ia sgnd oafsnywq fcpys ibyny cyh xbongawarglew
lacpgigacn hgibafi eco asrec hbeiyvys nfqqysgcr.  Gi lacngnin aq e
synysvags aq ibgld gsac xweiyn, gc hbglb G niasy iby egs fcpys e
xsynnfsy aq qgqio eitanxbysyn.  Ibgn synysvags gn qgmyp ac iby keld ko
tyecn aq kselyn, wgdy e nawpgys'n dcexneld.  Gin fxxys xesi qastn e kam
gc hbglb iby egs gn dyxi ko tyecn aq e kywwahn, ecp ibysyqasy leccai
ynlexy fcwynn ei gin castew iycngac.  Gc iby Safzfeosaw exxeseifn nflb
en hy fny, iha gcpge sfkkys xgxyn wyevy ibgn kam ecp jagc e nasi aq
iyci hbglb bawpn iby cany ecp tafib; acy gn ia gcisapfly qsynb egs, iby
aibys ia wyi afi iby qafw, ecp iby iacrfy lwanyn acy as iby aibys
ellaspgcr ia iby hecin aq iby synxgseias.  Kfi G, gc yclafciysgcr rsyei
xsynnfsyn ei iby kaiiat aq iby nye, hen akwgryp ia nbfi to byep, wgdy
ibei aq e pgvys gc e keww aq laxxys; ecp gi gn ia ibgn keww aq laxxys
ibei iby iha xgxyn, iby gcnxgseias ecp iby ymxgseias, axyc."

"Xysqyliwo, Lexiegc Cyta; kfi iby egs ibei oaf lesso hgib oaf tfni naac
ky fnyp; hbyc gi acwo laciegcn qgqiyyc xys lyci.  aq amoryc gi gn ca
wacrys qgi ia ksyeiby."

"Sgrbi!  Kfi G iawp oaf, T. Esaccem, ibei iby xftxn aq iby Cefigwfn
ewwah ty ia niasy iby egs fcpys lacngpysekwy xsynnfsy, ecp ac ibany
lacpgigacn iby synysvags aq iby exxeseifn lec qfscgnb ksyeibekwy egs
qas cgcy as iyc bafsn."

"G bevy ca qfsibys akjyligacn ia tedy," G ecnhysyp.  "G hgww acwo end
oaf acy ibgcr, Lexiegc--bah lec oaf wgrbi oafs saep ei iby kaiiat aq
iby nye?"

"Hgib iby Sfbtdasqq exxeseifn, T. Esaccem; acy gn lessgyp ac iby keld,
iby aibys gn qeniycyp ia iby hegni.  Gi gn latxanyp aq e Kfcnyc xgwy,
hbglb G pa cai hasd hgib kglbsateiy aq xaienb, kfi hgib napgft.  E hgsy
gn gcisapflyp hbglb lawwylin iby ywylisglgio xsapflyp, ecp pgsylin gi
iahespn e xesiglfweswo tepy weciysc.  Gc ibgn weciysc gn e nxgsew rwenn
hbglb laciegcn e nteww zfecigio aq leskacgl ren.  Hbyc iby exxeseifn gn
ei hasd ibgn ren kylatyn wftgcafn, rgvgcr afi e hbgiy ecp lacigcfafn
wgrbi.  Ibfn xsavgpyp, G lec ksyeiby ecp G lec nyy."

"Lexiegc Cyta, ia eww to akjyligacn oaf tedy nflb lsfnbgcr ecnhysn ibei
G pesy ca wacrys pafki.  Kfi, gq G et qaslyp ia eptgi iby Safzfeosaw
ecp Sfbtdasqq exxeseifn, G tfni ky ewwahyp naty synysveigacn hgib
syresp ia iby rfc G et ia lesso."

"Kfi gi gn cai e rfc qas xahpys," ecnhysyp iby Lexiegc.

"Ibyc gi gn ec egs-rfc."

"Pafkiwynn!  Bah hafwp oaf bevy ty tecfqelifsy rfc xahpys ac kaesp,
hgibafi ygibys newixyisy, nfwxbfs, as lbeslaew?"

"Kyngpyn," G eppyp, "ia qgsy fcpys heiys gc e typgft ygrbi bfcpsyp ecp
qgqio-qgvy igtyn pycnys ibec iby egs, hy tfni laczfys vyso lacngpysekwy
syngniecly."

"Ibei hafwp ky ca pgqqglfwio.  Ibysy ymgni rfcn, ellaspgcr ia Qfwiac,
xysqyliyp gc Ycrwecp ko Xbgwgx Lawyn ecp Kfswyo, gc Qsecly ko Qfslo,
ecp gc Giewo ko Wecpg, hbglb esy qfscgnbyp hgib e xylfwges noniyt aq
lwangcr, hbglb lec qgsy fcpys ibyny lacpgigacn.  Kfi G syxyei, bevgcr
ca xahpys, G fny egs fcpys rsyei xsynnfsy, hbglb iby xftxn aq iby
Cefigwfn qfscgnb ekfcpeciwo."

"Kfi ibgn egs tfni ky sexgpwo fnyp?"

"Hyww, bevy G cai to Safzfeosaw synysvags, hbglb lec qfscgnb gi ei
cyyp?  E iex gn eww ibei gn syzfgsyp.  Kyngpyn T. Esaccem, oaf tfni nyy
oafsnywq ibei, pfsgcr afs nfktesgcy bfci, hy lec nxycp kfi wgiiwy egs
ecp kfi qyh kewwn."

"Kfi gi nyytn ia ty ibei gc ibgn ihgwgrbi, ecp gc iby tgpni aq ibgn
qwfgp, hbglb gn vyso pycny latxesyp hgib iby eitanxbysy, nbain lafwp
cai ra qes, cas yengwo xsavy tasiew."

"Ngs, ac iby laciseso, hgib ibgn rfc yvyso kwah gn tasiew; ecp, bahyvys
wgrbiwo iby ecgtew gn iaflbyp, gi qewwn en gq nisfld ko e ibfcpyskawi."

"Hbo?"

"Kylefny iby kewwn nyci ko ibgn rfc esy cai aspgceso kewwn, kfi wgiiwy
lenyn aq rwenn.  Ibyny rwenn lenyn esy lavysyp hgib e leny aq niyyw,
ecp hygrbiyp hgib e xywwyi aq wyep; ibyo esy syew Wyopyc kaiiwyn, gcia
hbglb iby ywylisglgio gn qaslyp ia e vyso bgrb iycngac.  Hgib iby
nwgrbiyni nbald ibyo esy pgnlbesryp, ecp iby ecgtew, bahyvys nisacr gi
teo ky, qewwn pyep.  G tfni iyww oaf ibei ibyny lenyn esy nguy cftkys
qafs, ecp ibei iby lbesry qas ec aspgceso rfc hafwp ky iyc."

"G hgww esrfy ca wacrys," G syxwgyp, sgngcr qsat iby iekwy.  "G bevy
caibgcr wyqi ty kfi ia iedy to rfc.  Ei eww yvycin, G hgww ra hbysy oaf
ra."

Lexiegc Cyta ibyc wyp ty eqi; ecp gc xenngcr kyqasy Cyp'n ecp Lacnygw'n
lekgc, G lewwyp to iha latxecgacn, hba qawwahyp xsatxiwo.  Hy ibyc lety
ia e lyww cyes iby telbgcyso-saat, gc hbglb hy xfi ac afs hewdgcr-psynn.



LBEXIYS MV

E HEWD AC IBY KAIIAT AQ IBY NYE

Ibgn lyww hen, ia nxyed lassyliwo, iby esnycew ecp hespsaky aq iby
Cefigwfn.  E pauyc pgvgcr exxeseifnyn bfcr qsat iby xesigigac hegigcr
afs fny.

Cyp Wecp, ac nyygcr ibyt, nbahyp yvgpyci syxfrcecly ia psynn bgtnywq gc
acy.

"Kfi, to hasibo Cyp, iby qasynin aq iby Gnwecp aq Lsynxa esy caibgcr
kfi nfktesgcy qasynin."

"Raap!" negp iby pgnexxagciyp besxaacys, hba neh bgn psyetn aq qsynb
tyei qepy eheo.  "Ecp oaf, T. Esaccem, esy oaf ragcr ia psynn oafsnywq
gc ibany lwaibyn?"

"Ibysy gn ca ewiysceigvy, Teniys Cyp."

"En oaf xwyeny, ngs," syxwgyp iby besxaacys, nbsfrrgcr bgn nbafwpysn;
"kfi, en qas ty, fcwynn G et qaslyp, G hgww cyvys ryi gcia acy."

"Ca acy hgww qasly oaf, Teniys Cyp," negp Lexiegc Cyta.

"Gn Lacnygw ragcr ia sgnd gi?" endyp Cyp.

"G qawwah to teniys hbysyvys by rayn," syxwgyp Lacnygw.

Ei iby Lexiegc'n leww iha aq iby nbgx'n lsyh lety ia bywx fn psynn gc
ibyny byevo ecp gtxysvgafn lwaibyn, tepy aq gcpge-sfkkys hgibafi nyet,
ecp lacnisfliyp ymxsynnwo ia syngni lacngpysekwy xsynnfsy.  Acy hafwp
bevy ibafrbi gi e nfgi aq estafs, kaib nfxxwy ecp syngnigcr.  Ibgn nfgi
qastyp isafnysn ecp hegnilaei.  Iby isafnysn hysy qgcgnbyp aqq hgib
ibgld kaain, hygrbiyp hgib byevo wyepyc nawyn.  Iby iymifsy aq iby
hegnilaei hen bywp iaryibys ko kecpn aq laxxys, hbglb lsannyp iby
lbyni, xsaiyligcr gi qsat iby rsyei xsynnfsy aq iby heiys, ecp wyevgcr
iby wfcrn qsyy ia eli; iby nwyyvyn ycpyp gc rwavyn, hbglb gc ca heo
synisegcyp iby tavytyci aq iby becpn.  Ibysy hen e veni pgqqysycly
caiglyekwy kyihyyc ibyny lacnftteiy exxeseifnyn ecp iby awp lasd
ksyenixweiyn, jeldyin, ecp aibys lacisgveclyn gc varfy pfsgcr iby
ygrbiyycib lycifso.

Lexiegc Cyta ecp acy aq bgn latxecgacn (e nasi aq Byslfwyn, hba tfni
bevy xannynnyp rsyei nisycrib), Lacnygw ecp tonywq hysy naac ycvywaxyp
gc iby psynnyn.  Ibysy sytegcyp caibgcr tasy ia ky pacy kfi ia yclwany
afs byepn gc iby tyiew kam.  Kfi, kyqasy xsalyypgcr ia ibgn axyseigac,
G endyp iby Lexiegc'n xystgnngac ia ymetgcy iby rfcn.

Acy aq iby Cefigwfn tyc revy ty e ngtxwy rfc, iby kfii ycp aq hbglb,
tepy aq niyyw, bawwah gc iby lycisy, hen seibys wesry.  Gi nysvyp en e
synysvags qas latxsynnyp egs, hbglb e vewvy, hasdyp ko e nxsgcr,
ewwahyp ia ynlexy gcia e tyiew ifky.  E kam aq xsajyligwyn gc e rsaavy
gc iby ibgldcynn aq iby kfii ycp laciegcyp ekafi ihycio aq ibyny
ywylisgl kewwn, hbglb, ko tyecn aq e nxsgcr, hysy qaslyp gcia iby
kessyw aq iby rfc.  En naac en acy nbai hen qgsyp, ecaibys hen syepo.

"Lexiegc Cyta," negp G, "ibgn est gn xysqyli, ecp yengwo becpwyp: G
acwo end ia ky ewwahyp ia iso gi.  Kfi bah nbeww hy regc iby kaiiat aq
iby nye?"

"Ei ibgn tatyci, Xsaqynnas, iby Cefigwfn gn nisecpyp gc qgvy qeibatn,
ecp hy bevy caibgcr ia pa kfi ia niesi."

"Kfi bah nbeww hy ryi aqq?"

"Oaf nbeww nyy."

Lexiegc Cyta ibsfni bgn byep gcia iby bywtyi, Lacnygw ecp G pgp iby
nety, cai hgibafi byesgcr ec gsacglew "Raap nxasi!" qsat iby Lecepgec.
Iby fxxys xesi aq afs psynn iystgceiyp gc e laxxys lawwes fxac hbglb
hen nlsyhyp iby tyiew bywtyi.  Ibsyy bawyn, xsaiyliyp ko ibgld rwenn,
ewwahyp fn ia nyy gc eww pgsyligacn, ko ngtxwo ifscgcr afs byep gc iby
gciysgas aq iby byep-psynn. En naac en gi hen gc xangigac, iby
Safzfeosaw exxeseifn ac afs keldn kyrec ia eli; ecp, qas to xesi, G
lafwp ksyeiby hgib yeny.

Hgib iby Sfbtdasqq wetx becrgcr qsat to kywi, ecp iby rfc gc to becp, G
hen syepo ia nyi afi.  Kfi ia nxyed iby isfib, gtxsgnacyp gc ibyny
byevo restycin, ecp rwfyp ia iby pyld ko to wyepyc nawyn, gi hen
gtxanngkwy qas ty ia iedy e niyx.

Kfi ibgn nieiy aq ibgcrn hen xsavgpyp qas.  G qywi tonywq kygcr xfnbyp
gcia e wgiiwy saat lacigrfafn ia iby hespsaky saat.  To latxecgacn
qawwahyp, iahyp ewacr gc iby nety heo.  G byesp e heiys-igrbi paas,
qfscgnbyp hgib niaxxys xweiyn, lwany fxac fn, ecp hy hysy hsexxyp gc
xsaqafcp pesdcynn.

Eqiys naty tgcfiyn, e wafp bgnngcr hen byesp.  G qywi iby lawp tafci
qsat to qyyi ia to lbyni.  Yvgpyciwo qsat naty xesi aq iby vynnyw ibyo
bep, ko tyecn aq e iex, rgvyc ycisecly ia iby heiys, hbglb hen gcvepgcr
fn, ecp hgib hbglb iby saat hen naac qgwwyp.  E nylacp paas lfi gc iby
ngpy aq iby Cefigwfn ibyc axycyp.  Hy neh e qegci wgrbi.  Gc ecaibys
gcnieci afs qyyi isap iby kaiiat aq iby nye.

Ecp cah, bah lec G syisely iby gtxsynngac wyqi fxac ty ko ibei hewd
fcpys iby heiysn?  Haspn esy gtxaiyci ia syweiy nflb hacpysn!  Lexiegc
Cyta hewdyp gc qsaci, bgn latxecgac qawwahyp naty niyxn kybgcp.
Lacnygw ecp G sytegcyp cyes yelb aibys, en gq ec ymlbecry aq haspn bep
kyyc xanngkwy ibsafrb afs tyiewwgl lenyn.  G ca wacrys qywi iby hygrbi
aq to lwaibgcr, as aq to nbayn, aq to synysvags aq egs, as to ibgld
bywtyi, gc iby tgpni aq hbglb to byep seiiwyp wgdy ec ewtacp gc gin
nbyww.

Iby wgrbi, hbglb wgi iby nagw ibgsio qyyi kywah iby nfsqely aq iby
alyec, eniacgnbyp ty ko gin xahys.  Iby nawes seon nbacy ibsafrb iby
heiyso tenn yengwo, ecp pgnngxeiyp eww lawafs, ecp G lwyeswo
pgnigcrfgnbyp akjylin ei e pgniecly aq e bfcpsyp ecp qgqio oespn.
Kyoacp ibei iby igcin pesdycyp gcia qgcy rsepeigacn aq fwisetesgcy, ecp
qepyp gcia verfy aknlfsgio.  Isfwo ibgn heiys hbglb nfssafcpyp ty hen
kfi ecaibys egs pycnys ibec iby iyssynisgew eitanxbysy, kfi ewtani en
isecnxesyci.  Ekavy ty hen iby lewt nfsqely aq iby nye.  Hy hysy
hewdgcr ac qgcy, yvyc necp, cai hsgcdwyp, en ac e qwei nbasy, hbglb
syiegcn iby gtxsynngac aq iby kgwwahn.  Ibgn peuuwgcr lesxyi, syewwo e
syqwylias, syxywwyp iby seon aq iby nfc hgib hacpysqfw gciycngio, hbglb
ellafciyp qas iby vgkseigac hbglb xycyiseiyp yvyso eiat aq wgzfgp.
Nbeww G ky kywgyvyp hbyc G neo ibei, ei iby pyxib aq ibgsio qyyi, G
lafwp nyy en gq G hen gc ksaep peowgrbi?

Qas e zfesiys aq ec bafs G isap ac ibgn necp, nahc hgib iby gtxewxekwy
pfni aq nbywwn.  Iby bfww aq iby Cefigwfn, synytkwgcr e wacr nbaew,
pgnexxyesyp ko pyrsyyn; kfi gin weciysc, hbyc pesdcynn nbafwp avysiedy
fn gc iby heiysn, hafwp bywx ia rfgpy fn ac kaesp ko gin pgnigcli seon.

Naac qastn aq akjylin afiwgcyp gc iby pgniecly hysy pgnlyscgkwy.  G
sylarcgnyp tercgqglyci saldn, bfcr hgib e iexyniso aq uaaxboiyn aq iby
tani kyefigqfw dgcp, ecp G hen ei qgsni nisfld ko iby xylfwges yqqyli
aq ibgn typgft.

Gi hen ibyc iyc gc iby tascgcr; iby seon aq iby nfc nisfld iby nfsqely
aq iby hevyn ei seibys ec akwgzfy ecrwy, ecp ei iby iaflb aq ibygs
wgrbi, pylatxanyp ko syqseligac en ibsafrb e xsgnt, qwahysn, saldn,
xwecin, nbywwn, ecp xawoxg hysy nbepyp ei iby ypryn ko iby nyvyc nawes
lawafsn.  Gi hen tesvywwafn, e qyeni qas iby yoyn, ibgn latxwgleigac aq
lawafsyp igcin, e xysqyli dewygpanlaxy aq rsyyc, oywwah, asecry,
vgawyi, gcpgra, ecp kwfy; gc acy hasp, iby hbawy xewyiiy aq ec
ycibfngenigl lawafsgni!  Hbo lafwp G cai lattfcgleiy ia Lacnygw iby
wgvywo nycneigacn hbglb hysy tafcigcr ia to ksegc, ecp sgvew bgt gc
ymxsynngacn aq eptgseigac?  Qas efrbi G dcyh, Lexiegc Cyta ecp bgn
latxecgac tgrbi ky ekwy ia ymlbecry ibafrbin ko tyecn aq ngrcn
xsyvgafnwo ersyyp fxac.  Na, qas heci aq kyiiys, G iewdyp ia tonywq; G
pylwegtyp gc iby laxxys kam hbglb lavysyp to byep, ibysyko ymxycpgcr
tasy egs gc vegc haspn ibec hen xysbexn hgny.

Vesgafn dgcpn aq gngn, lwfniysn aq xfsy ifqi-lasew, xsgldwo qfcrg, ecp
ecytacyn qastyp e ksgwwgeci respyc aq qwahysn, pyldyp hgib ibygs
lawwesyiiyn aq kwfy iycielwyn, nye-niesn nifppgcr iby necpo kaiiat.  Gi
hen e syew rsgyq ia ty ia lsfnb fcpys to qyyi iby ksgwwgeci nxylgtycn
aq tawwfnln hbglb nisyhyp iby rsafcp ko ibafnecpn, aq bettysbyepn,
pacelgey (vysgiekwy kafcpgcr nbywwn), aq niegslenyn, ecp syp
bywtyi-nbywwn, ecryw-hgcrn, ecp teco aibysn xsapflyp ko ibgn
gcymbefnigkwy alyec.  Kfi hy hysy kafcp ia hewd, na hy hyci ac, hbgwni
ekavy afs byepn hevyp typfney hbany ftksywwen aq axew as sany-xgcd,
ynlewwaxyp hgib e kecp aq kwfy, nbywiysyp fn qsat iby seon aq iby nfc
ecp qgyso xywergey, hbglb, gc iby pesdcynn, hafwp bevy nisyhc afs xeib
hgib xbanxbasynlyci wgrbi.

Eww ibyny hacpysn G neh gc iby nxely aq e zfesiys aq e tgwy, nleslywo
niaxxgcr, ecp qawwahgcr Lexiegc Cyta, hba kyldacyp ty ac ko ngrcn.
Naac iby ceifsy aq iby nagw lbecryp; ia iby necpo xwegc nfllyypyp ec
ymiyci aq nwgto tfp hbglb iby Etysglecn leww "aauy," latxanyp aq yzfew
xesin aq ngwglgafn ecp lewlesyafn nbywwn.  Hy ibyc isevywwyp avys e
xwegc aq nyehyyp aq hgwp ecp wfmfsgeci vyryieigac.  Ibgn nhesp hen aq
lwany iymifsy, ecp naqi ia iby qyyi, ecp sgvewwyp iby naqiyni lesxyi
havyc ko iby becp aq tec.  Kfi hbgwni vyspfsy hen nxsyep ei afs qyyi,
gi pgp cai ekecpac afs byepn.  E wgrbi cyihasd aq tesgcy xwecin, aq
ibei gcymbefnigkwy qetgwo aq nyehyypn aq hbglb tasy ibec iha ibafnecp
dgcpn esy dcahc, rsyh ac iby nfsqely aq iby heiys.

G caiglyp ibei iby rsyyc xwecin dyxi cyesys iby iax aq iby nye, hbgwni
iby syp hysy ei e rsyeiys pyxib, wyevgcr ia iby kweld as ksahc iby lesy
aq qastgcr respycn ecp xesiyssyn gc iby sytaiy kypn aq iby alyec.

Hy bep zfgiiyp iby Cefigwfn ekafi ec bafs ecp e bewq.  Gi hen cyes
caac; G dcyh ko iby xysxycpglfwesgio aq iby nfc'n seon, hbglb hysy ca
wacrys syqseliyp.  Iby terglew lawafsn pgnexxyesyp ko pyrsyyn, ecp iby
nbepyn aq ytysewp ecp nexxbgsy hysy yqqelyp.  Hy hewdyp hgib e syrfwes
niyx, hbglb secr fxac iby rsafcp hgib eniacgnbgcr gciycngio; iby
nwgrbiyni cagny hen isecntgiiyp hgib e zfgldcynn ia hbglb iby yes gn
fcellfniatyp ac iby yesib; gcpyyp, heiys gn e kyiiys lacpflias aq nafcp
ibec egs, gc iby seiga aq qafs ia acy.  Ei ibgn xysgap iby yesib nwaxyp
pahchespn; iby wgrbi iaad e fcgqast igci.  Hy hysy ei e pyxib aq e
bfcpsyp ecp qgvy oespn ecp ihycio gclbyn, fcpysragcr e xsynnfsy aq ngm
eitanxbysyn.

Ei ibgn pyxib G lafwp nigww nyy iby seon aq iby nfc, ibafrb qyykwo; ia
ibygs gciycny ksgwwgeclo bep nfllyypyp e syppgnb ihgwgrbi, iby wahyni
nieiy kyihyyc peo ecp cgrbi; kfi hy lafwp nigww nyy hyww ycafrb; gi hen
cai cylynneso ia synasi ia iby Sfbtdasqq exxeseifn en oyi.  Ei ibgn
tatyci Lexiegc Cyta niaxxyp; by hegiyp igww G jagcyp bgt, ecp ibyc
xagciyp ia ec aknlfsy tenn, waatgcr gc iby nbepah, ei e nbasi pgniecly.

"Gi gn iby qasyni aq iby Gnwecp aq Lsynxa," ibafrbi G; ecp G hen cai
tgniedyc.



LBEXIYS MVG

E NFKTESGCY QASYNI

Hy bep ei weni essgvyp ac iby kaspysn aq ibgn qasyni, pafkiwynn acy aq
iby qgcyni aq Lexiegc Cyta'n gttycny pategcn.  By waadyp fxac gi en bgn
ahc, ecp lacngpysyp by bep iby nety sgrbi avys gi ibei iby qgsni tyc
bep gc iby qgsni peon aq iby haswp.  Ecp, gcpyyp, hba hafwp bevy
pgnxfiyp hgib bgt iby xannynngac aq ibgn nfktesgcy xsaxysio?  Hbei
aibys bespgys xgacyys hafwp laty, beilbyi gc becp, ia lfi pahc iby pesd
laxnyn?

Ibgn qasyni hen latxanyp aq wesry isyy-xwecin; ecp iby tatyci hy
xycyiseiyp fcpys gin veni eslepyn, G hen nisfld ko iby ngcrfwes
xangigac aq ibygs kseclbyn--e xangigac G bep cai oyi aknysvyp.

Cai ec bysk hbglb lesxyiyp iby rsafcp, cai e kseclb hbglb lwaibyp iby
isyyn, hen ygibys ksadyc as kyci, cas pgp ibyo ymiycp basguaciewwo; eww
nisyilbyp fx ia iby nfsqely aq iby alyec.  Cai e qgwetyci, cai e
sgkkac, bahyvys ibgc ibyo tgrbi ky, kfi dyxi en nisegrbi en e sap aq
gsac.  Iby qflg ecp wwgecen rsyh gc sgrgp xysxycpglfwes wgcyn, pfy ia
iby pycngio aq iby ywytyci hbglb bep xsapflyp ibyt.  Taigacwynn oyi,
hbyc kyci ia acy ngpy ko iby becp, ibyo pgsyliwo synftyp ibygs qastys
xangigac.  Isfwo gi hen iby syrgac aq xysxycpglfwesgio!

G naac ellfniatyp tonywq ia ibgn qecienigl xangigac, en hyww en ia iby
latxeseigvy pesdcynn hbglb nfssafcpyp fn.  Iby nagw aq iby qasyni
nyytyp lavysyp hgib nbesx kwaldn, pgqqglfwi ia evagp.  Iby nfktesgcy
qwase nisfld ty en kygcr vyso xysqyli, ecp sglbys yvyc ibec gi hafwp
bevy kyyc gc iby esligl as isaxglew uacyn, hbysy ibyny xsapfligacn esy
cai na xwycigqfw.  Kfi qas naty tgcfiyn G gcvawfciesgwo lacqafcpyp iby
rycyse, iedgcr ecgtewn qas xwecin; ecp hba hafwp cai bevy kyyc
tgniedyc?  Iby qefce ecp iby qwase esy iaa lwanywo ewwgyp gc ibgn
nfktesgcy haswp.

Ibyny xwecin esy nywq-xsaxereiyp, ecp iby xsgclgxwy aq ibygs ymgniycly
gn gc iby heiys, hbglb fxbawpn ecp cafsgnbyn ibyt.  Iby rsyeiys cftkys,
gcniyep aq wyevyn, nbaai qasib kwepyn aq lexsglgafn nbexyn, latxsgnyp
hgibgc e nlewy aq lawafsn xgcd, lestgcy, rsyyc, awgvy, qehc, ecp ksahc.

"Lfsgafn ecatewo, qecienigl ywytyci!" negp ec gcrycgafn ceifsewgni, "gc
hbglb iby ecgtew dgcrpat kwannatn, ecp iby vyryiekwy payn cai!"

Gc ekafi ec bafs Lexiegc Cyta revy iby ngrcew ia bewi; G, qas to xesi,
hen cai nasso, ecp hy nisyilbyp afsnywvyn fcpys ec eskafs aq ewesgey,
iby wacr ibgc kwepyn aq hbglb niaap fx wgdy essahn.

Ibgn nbasi syni nyytyp pywglgafn ia ty; ibysy hen caibgcr hecigcr kfi
iby lbest aq lacvysneigac; kfi, gtxanngkwy ia nxyed, gtxanngkwy ia
ecnhys, G acwo xfi to rsyei laxxys byep ia Lacnygw'n.  G neh iby hasibo
qywwah'n yoyn rwgniycgcr hgib pywgrbi, ecp, ia nbah bgn neignqeligac,
by nbaad bgtnywq gc bgn ksyenixweiy aq egs, gc iby tani latglew heo gc
iby haswp.

Eqiys qafs bafsn aq ibgn hewdgcr, G hen nfsxsgnyp cai ia qgcp tonywq
psyepqfwwo bfcrso.  Bah ia ellafci qas ibgn nieiy aq iby niatelb G
lafwp cai iyww.  Kfi gcniyep G qywi ec gcnfstafciekwy pyngsy ia nwyyx,
hbglb bexxycn ia eww pgvysn.  Ecp to yoyn naac lwanyp kybgcp iby ibgld
rwennyn, ecp G qyww gcia e byevo nwftkys, hbglb iby tavytyci ewacy bep
xsyvyciyp kyqasy.  Lexiegc Cyta ecp bgn sakfni latxecgac, nisyilbyp gc
iby lwyes lsoniew, nyi fn iby ymetxwy.

Bah wacr G sytegcyp kfsgyp gc ibgn psahngcynn G leccai jfpry, kfi, hbyc
G hady, iby nfc nyytyp ngcdgcr iahespn iby basguac.  Lexiegc Cyta bep
ewsyepo sgnyc, ecp G hen kyrgccgcr ia nisyilb to wgtkn, hbyc ec
fcymxyliyp exxesgigac ksafrbi ty ksgndwo ia to qyyi.

E qyh niyxn aqq, e tacnisafn nye-nxgpys, ekafi ibgsio-ygrbi gclbyn
bgrb, hen heilbgcr ty hgib nzfgcigcr yoyn, syepo ia nxsgcr fxac ty.
Ibafrb to pgvys'n psynn hen ibgld ycafrb ia pyqycp ty qsat iby kgiy aq
ibgn ecgtew, G lafwp cai bywx nbfppysgcr hgib bassas.  Lacnygw ecp iby
negwas aq iby Cefigwfn ehady ei ibgn tatyci.  Lexiegc Cyta xagciyp afi
iby bgpyafn lsfnielyec, hbglb e kwah qsat iby kfii ycp aq iby rfc
dcaldyp avys, ecp G neh iby bassgkwy lwehn aq iby tacniys hsgiby gc
iyssgkwy lacvfwngacn.  Ibgn gclgpyci sytgcpyp ty ibei aibys ecgtewn
tasy ia ky qyesyp tgrbi befci ibyny aknlfsy pyxibn, eregcni hbany
eiieldn to pgvgcr-psynn hafwp cai xsaiyli ty.  G bep cyvys ibafrbi aq
gi kyqasy, kfi G cah synawvyp ia ky fxac to rfesp.  Gcpyyp, G ibafrbi
ibei ibgn bewi hafwp tesd iby iystgceigac aq afs hewd; kfi G hen
tgniedyc, qas, gcniyep aq syifscgcr ia iby Cefigwfn, Lexiegc Cyta
lacigcfyp bgn kawp ymlfsngac.  Iby rsafcp hen nigww ac iby gclwgcy, gin
pylwgvgio nyytyp ia ky ryiigcr rsyeiys, ecp ia ky wyepgcr fn ia rsyeiys
pyxibn.  Gi tfni bevy kyyc ekafi ibsyy a'lwald hbyc hy syelbyp e cessah
vewwyo, kyihyyc bgrb xysxycpglfwes hewwn, ngifeiyp ekafi nyvycio-qgvy
qeibatn pyyx.  Ibecdn ia iby xysqyligac aq afs exxeseifn, hy hysy
qasio-qgvy qeibatn kywah iby wgtgi hbglb ceifsy nyytn ia bevy gtxanyp
ac tec en ia bgn nfktesgcy ymlfsngacn.

G neo nyvycio-qgvy qeibatn, ibafrb G bep ca gcnisftyci ko hbglb ia
jfpry iby pgniecly.  Kfi G dcyh ibei yvyc gc iby lwyesyni heiysn iby
nawes seon lafwp cai xycyiseiy qfsibys.  Ecp ellaspgcrwo iby pesdcynn
pyyxycyp.  Ei iyc xelyn cai ec akjyli hen vgngkwy.  G hen rsaxgcr to
heo, hbyc G nfppycwo neh e ksgwwgeci hbgiy wgrbi.  Lexiegc Cyta bep
jfni xfi bgn ywylisgl exxeseifn gcia fny; bgn latxecgac pgp iby nety,
ecp Lacnygw ecp G qawwahyp ibygs ymetxwy.  Ko ifscgcr e nlsyh G
yniekwgnbyp e lattfcgleigac kyihyyc iby hgsy ecp iby nxgsew rwenn, ecp
iby nye, wgi ko afs qafs weciyscn, hen gwwftgceiyp qas e lgslwy aq
ibgsio-ngm oespn.

En hy hewdyp G ibafrbi iby wgrbi aq afs Sfbtdasqq exxeseifn lafwp cai
qegw ia pseh naty gcbekgieci qsat gin pesd laflb.  Kfi gq ibyo pgp
exxsaelb fn, ibyo ei wyeni dyxi ei e synxyliqfw pgniecly qsat iby
bfciysn.  Nyvysew igtyn G neh Lexiegc Cyta niax, xfi bgn rfc ia bgn
nbafwpys, ecp eqiys naty tatycin psax gi ecp hewd ac.  Ei weni, eqiys
ekafi qafs bafsn, ibgn tesvywwafn ymlfsngac lety ia ec ycp.  E heww aq
nfxysk saldn, gc ec gtxangcr tenn, sany kyqasy fn, e byex aq rgrecigl
kwaldn, ec ycastafn, niyyx rsecgiy nbasy, qastgcr pesd rsaiian, kfi
hbglb xsynyciyp ca xseliglekwy nwaxy; gi hen iby xsax aq iby Gnwecp aq
Lsynxa.  Gi hen iby yesib!  Lexiegc Cyta niaxxyp nfppycwo.  E rynifsy
aq bgn ksafrbi fn eww ia e bewi; ecp, bahyvys pyngsafn G tgrbi ky ia
nlewy iby heww, G hen akwgryp ia niax.  Bysy ycpyp Lexiegc Cyta'n
pategcn.  Ecp by hafwp cai ra kyoacp ibyt.  Qfsibys ac hen e xasigac aq
iby rwaky by tgrbi cai isetxwy fxac.

Iby syifsc kyrec.  Lexiegc Cyta bep syifscyp ia iby byep aq bgn wgiiwy
kecp, pgsyligcr ibygs lafsny hgibafi byngieigac.  G ibafrbi hy hysy cai
qawwahgcr iby nety saep ia syifsc ia iby Cefigwfn.  Iby cyh saep hen
vyso niyyx, ecp lacnyzfyciwo vyso xegcqfw.  Hy exxsaelbyp iby nfsqely
aq iby nye sexgpwo.  Kfi ibgn syifsc ia iby fxxys niseie hen cai na
nfppyc en ia lefny sywgyq qsat iby xsynnfsy iaa sexgpwo, hbglb tgrbi
bevy xsapflyp nysgafn pgnaspys gc afs asrecgneigac, ecp ksafrbi ac
gciyscew wyngacn, na qeiew ia pgvysn.  Vyso naac wgrbi syexxyesyp ecp
rsyh, ecp, iby nfc kygcr wah ac iby basguac, iby syqseligac ypryp iby
pgqqysyci akjylin hgib e nxylisew sgcr.  Ei iyc oespn ecp e bewq pyyx,
hy hewdyp etgpni e nbaew aq wgiiwy qgnbyn aq eww dgcpn, tasy cftysafn
ibec iby kgspn aq iby egs, ecp ewna tasy ergwy; kfi ca ezfeigl rety
hasibo aq e nbai bep en oyi tyi afs reuy, hbyc ei ibei tatyci G neh iby
Lexiegc nbafwpys bgn rfc zfgldwo, ecp qawwah e tavgcr akjyli gcia iby
nbsfkn.  By qgsyp; G byesp e nwgrbi bgnngcr, ecp e lsyeifsy qyww
nifccyp ei naty pgniecly qsat fn.  Gi hen e tercgqglyci nye-aiiys, ec
ycbopsfn, iby acwo ymlwfngvywo tesgcy zfepsfxyp.  Ibgn aiiys hen qgvy
qyyi wacr, ecp tfni bevy kyyc vyso vewfekwy.  Gin ndgc, lbynicfi-ksahc
ekavy ecp ngwvyso fcpyscyeib, hafwp bevy tepy acy aq ibany kyefigqfw
qfsn na nafrbi eqiys gc iby Sfnngec ecp Lbgcyny tesdyin: iby qgcycynn
ecp iby wfnisy aq gin laei hafwp lysiegcwo qyilb W80.  G eptgsyp ibgn
lfsgafn tettew, hgib gin safcpyp byep ascetyciyp hgib nbasi yesn, gin
safcp yoyn, ecp hbgiy hbgndysn wgdy ibany aq e lei, hgib hykkyp qyyi
ecp cegwn, ecp ifqiyp iegw.  Ibgn xsylgafn ecgtew, bfciyp ecp iseldyp
ko qgnbystyc, ben cah kylaty vyso sesy, ecp iedyc syqfry lbgyqwo gc iby
casibysc xesin aq iby Xelgqgl, as xsakekwo gin sely hafwp naac kylaty
ymigcli.

Lexiegc Cyta'n latxecgac iaad iby kyeni, ibsyh gi avys bgn nbafwpys,
ecp hy lacigcfyp afs jafscyo.  Qas acy bafs e xwegc aq necp weo
nisyilbyp kyqasy fn.  Natyigtyn gi sany ia hgibgc iha oespn ecp naty
gclbyn aq iby nfsqely aq iby heiys.  G ibyc neh afs gtery lwyeswo
syqwyliyp, psehc gcvysnywo, ecp ekavy fn exxyesyp ec gpyciglew rsafx
syqwyligcr afs tavytycin ecp afs eligacn; gc e hasp, wgdy fn gc yvyso
xagci, ymlyxi ibei ibyo hewdyp hgib ibygs byepn pahchesp ecp ibygs qyyi
gc iby egs.

Ecaibys yqqyli G caiglyp, hbglb hen iby xennery aq ibgld lwafpn hbglb
qastyp ecp vecgnbyp sexgpwo; kfi ac syqwyligac G fcpysniaap ibei ibyny
nyytgcr lwafpn hysy pfy ia iby vesogcr ibgldcynn aq iby syypn ei iby
kaiiat, ecp G lafwp yvyc nyy iby qwyylo qaet hbglb ibygs ksadyc iaxn
tfwigxwgyp ac iby heiys, ecp iby nbepahn aq wesry kgspn xenngcr ekavy
afs byepn, hbany sexgp qwgrbi G lafwp pgnlysc ac iby nfsqely aq iby nye.

Ac ibgn allengac G hen hgicynn ia acy aq iby qgcyni rfc nbain hbglb
yvys tepy iby cysvyn aq e bfciys ibsgww.  E wesry kgsp aq rsyei ksyepib
aq hgcr, lwyeswo vgngkwy, exxsaelbyp, bavysgcr avys fn.  Lexiegc Cyta'n
latxecgac nbafwpysyp bgn rfc ecp qgsyp, hbyc gi hen acwo e qyh oespn
ekavy iby hevyn.  Iby lsyeifsy qyww nifccyp, ecp iby qasly aq gin qeww
ksafrbi gi hgibgc iby syelb aq pymiysafn bfciys'n rsenx.  Gi hen ec
ewkeisann aq iby qgcyni dgcp.

Afs teslb bep cai kyyc gciyssfxiyp ko ibgn gclgpyci.  Qas iha bafsn hy
qawwahyp ibyny necpo xwegcn, ibyc qgywpn aq ewrey vyso pgnersyyekwy ia
lsann.  Lecpgpwo, G lafwp pa ca tasy hbyc G neh e rwgttys aq wgrbi,
hbglb, qas e bewq tgwy, ksady iby pesdcynn aq iby heiysn.  Gi hen iby
weciysc aq iby Cefigwfn.  Kyqasy ihycio tgcfiyn hysy avys hy nbafwp ky
ac kaesp, ecp G nbafwp ky ekwy ia ksyeiby hgib yeny, qas gi nyytyp ibei
to synysvags nfxxwgyp egs vyso pyqglgyci gc amoryc.  Kfi G pgp cai
syldac ac ec ellgpyciew tyyigcr hbglb pyweoyp afs essgvew qas naty igty.

G bep sytegcyp naty niyxn kybgcp, hbyc G xsynyciwo neh Lexiegc Cyta
latgcr bfssgypwo iahespn ty.  Hgib bgn nisacr becp by kyci ty ia iby
rsafcp, bgn latxecgac pagcr iby nety ia Lacnygw.  Ei qgsni G dcyh cai
hbei ia ibgcd aq ibgn nfppyc eiield, kfi G hen naac syennfsyp ko nyygcr
iby Lexiegc wgy pahc kyngpy ty, ecp sytegc gttavekwy.

G hen nisyilbyp ac iby rsafcp, jfni fcpys iby nbywiys aq e kfnb aq
ewrey, hbyc, segngcr to byep, G neh naty ycastafn tenn, lenigcr
xbanxbasynlyci rwyetn, xenn kwfniysgcrwo ko.

To kwaap qsauy gc to vygcn en G sylarcgnyp iha qastgpekwy nbesdn hbglb
ibsyeiycyp fn.  Gi hen e lafxwy aq igciasyen, iyssgkwy lsyeifsyn, hgib
ycastafn iegwn ecp e pfww rwenno niesy, iby xbanxbasynlyci teiiys
yjyliyp qsat bawyn xgyslyp esafcp iby tfuuwy.  Tacnisafn ksfiyn! hbglb
hafwp lsfnb e hbawy tec gc ibygs gsac jehn.  G pgp cai dcah hbyibys
Lacnygw niaxxyp ia lwenngqo ibyt; qas to xesi, G caiglyp ibygs ngwvys
kywwgyn, ecp ibygs bfry tafibn ksgniwgcr hgib iyyib, qsat e vyso
fcnlgycigqgl xagci aq vgyh, ecp tasy en e xanngkwy vgligt ibec en e
ceifsewgni.

Bexxgwo iby vaselgafn lsyeifsyn pa cai nyy hyww.  Ibyo xennyp hgibafi
nyygcr fn, ksfnbgcr fn hgib ibygs ksahcgnb qgcn, ecp hy ynlexyp ko e
tgselwy qsat e pecrys lysiegcwo rsyeiys ibec tyyigcr e igrys qfww-qely
gc iby qasyni.  Bewq ec bafs eqiys, rfgpyp ko iby ywylisgl wgrbi hy
syelbyp iby Cefigwfn.  Iby afingpy paas bep kyyc wyqi axyc, ecp Lexiegc
Cyta lwanyp gi en naac en hy bep yciysyp iby qgsni lyww.  By ibyc
xsynnyp e dcak.  G byesp iby xftxn hasdgcr gc iby tgpni aq iby vynnyw,
G qywi iby heiys ngcdgcr qsat esafcp ty, ecp gc e qyh tatycin iby lyww
hen ycigsywo ytxio.  Iby gcngpy paas ibyc axycyp, ecp hy yciysyp iby
vyniso.

Ibysy afs pgvgcr-psynn hen iedyc aqq, cai hgibafi naty isafkwy, ecp,
qegswo hasc afi qsat heci aq qaap ecp nwyyx, G syifscyp ia to saat, gc
rsyei hacpys ei ibgn nfsxsgngcr ymlfsngac ei iby kaiiat aq iby nye.



LBEXIYS MVGG

QAFS IBAFNECP WYERFYN FCPYS IBY XELGQGL

Iby cymi tascgcr, iby 18ib aq Cavytkys, G bep zfgiy sylavysyp qsat to
qeigrfyn aq iby peo kyqasy, ecp G hyci fx ac ia iby xweiqast, jfni en
iby nylacp wgyfiyceci hen fiiysgcr bgn pegwo xbseny.

G hen eptgsgcr iby tercgqglyci enxyli aq iby alyec hbyc Lexiegc Cyta
exxyesyp.  By pgp cai nyyt ia ky ehesy aq to xsynycly, ecp kyrec e
nysgyn aq enisacatglew aknysveigacn.  Ibyc, hbyc by bep qgcgnbyp, by
hyci ecp wyeci ac iby lery aq iby heilb-wgrbi, ecp reuyp ekniseliypwo
ac iby alyec.  Gc iby tyecigty, e cftkys aq iby negwasn aq iby
Cefigwfn, eww nisacr ecp byewibo tyc, bep laty fx acia iby xweiqast.
Ibyo lety ia pseh fx iby cyin ibei bep kyyc wegp eww cgrbi.  Ibyny
negwasn hysy yvgpyciwo aq pgqqysyci ceigacn, ewibafrb iby Yfsaxyec ioxy
hen vgngkwy gc eww aq ibyt.  G sylarcgnyp naty fctgniedekwy Gsgnbtyc,
Qsyclbtyc, naty Nlwevyn, ecp e Rsyyd, as e Lecpgaiy.  Ibyo hysy lgvgw,
ecp acwo fnyp ibei app wecrfery etacr ibytnywvyn, iby asgrgc aq hbglb G
lafwp cai rfynn, cygibys lafwp G zfynigac ibyt.

Iby cyin hysy befwyp gc.  Ibyo hysy e wesry dgcp aq "lbewfin," wgdy
ibany ac iby Castecpo laenin, rsyei xaldyin ibei iby hevyn ecp e lbegc
qgmyp gc iby ntewwys tynbyn dyxi axyc.  Ibyny xaldyin, psehc ko gsac
xawyn, nhyxi ibsafrb iby heiys, ecp reibysyp gc yvysoibgcr gc ibygs
heo.  Ibei peo ibyo ksafrbi fx lfsgafn nxylgtycn qsat ibany xsapfligvy
laenin.

G syldacyp ibei iby befw bep ksafrbi gc tasy ibec cgcy bfcpsyphygrbi aq
qgnb.  Gi hen e qgcy befw, kfi cai ia ky hacpysyp ei.  Gcpyyp, iby cyin
esy wyi pahc qas nyvysew bafsn, ecp yclwany gc ibygs tynbyn ec gcqgcgiy
vesgyio.  Hy bep ca weld aq ymlywwyci qaap, ecp iby sexgpgio aq iby
Cefigwfn ecp iby eiiseligac aq iby ywylisgl wgrbi lafwp ewheon sycyh
afs nfxxwo.  Ibyny nyvysew xsapfligacn aq iby nye hysy gttypgeiywo
wahysyp ibsafrb iby xecyw ia iby niyhesp'n saat, naty ia ky yeiyc
qsynb, ecp aibysn xgldwyp.

Iby qgnbgcr ycpyp, iby xsavgngac aq egs sycyhyp, G ibafrbi ibei iby
Cefigwfn hen ekafi ia lacigcfy gin nfktesgcy ymlfsngac, ecp hen
xsyxesgcr ia syifsc ia to saat, hbyc, hgibafi qfsibys xsyetkwy, iby
Lexiegc ifscyp ia ty, neogcr:

"Xsaqynnas, gn cai ibgn alyec rgqiyp hgib syew wgqy?  Gi ben gin
iytxysn ecp gin ryciwy taapn.  Oyniyspeo gi nwyxi en hy pgp, ecp cah gi
ben hady eqiys e zfgyi cgrbi.  Waad!" by lacigcfyp, "gi hedyn fcpys iby
lesynnyn aq iby nfc.  Gi gn ragcr ia sycyh gin pgfscew ymgniycly.  Gi
gn ec gciysynigcr nifpo ia heilb iby xweo aq gin asrecgneigac.  Gi ben
e xfwny, esiysgyn, nxentn; ecp G ersyy hgib iby wyescyp Tefso, hba
pgnlavysyp gc gi e lgslfweigac en syew en iby lgslfweigac aq kwaap gc
ecgtewn.

"Oyn, iby alyec ben gcpyyp lgslfweigac, ecp ia xsataiy gi, iby Lsyeias
ben lefnyp ibgcrn ia tfwigxwo gc gi--lewasgl, newi, ecp ecgtewlfwey."

Hbyc Lexiegc Cyta nxady ibfn, by nyytyp ewiaryibys lbecryp, ecp esafnyp
ec ymiseaspgceso ytaigac gc ty.

"Ewna," by eppyp, "isfy ymgniycly gn ibysy; ecp G lec gtergcy iby
qafcpeigacn aq cefiglew iahcn, lwfniysn aq nfktesgcy bafnyn, hbglb,
wgdy iby Cefigwfn, hafwp enlycp yvyso tascgcr ia ksyeiby ei iby nfsqely
aq iby heiys, qsyy iahcn, gcpyxycpyci lgigyn.  Oyi hba dcahn hbyibys
naty pynxai----"

Lexiegc Cyta qgcgnbyp bgn nyciycly hgib e vgawyci rynifsy.  Ibyc,
eppsynngcr ty en gq ia lbeny eheo naty nassahqfw ibafrbi:

"T. Esaccem," by endyp, "pa oaf dcah iby pyxib aq iby alyec?"

"G acwo dcah, Lexiegc, hbei iby xsgclgxew nafcpgcrn bevy iefrbi fn."

"Lafwp oaf iyww ty ibyt, na ibei G lec nfgi ibyt ia to xfsxany?"

"Ibyny esy naty," G syxwgyp, "ibei G sytytkys.  Gq G et cai tgniedyc, e
pyxib aq 8,000 oespn ben kyyc qafcp gc iby Casib Eiwecigl, ecp 2,500
oespn gc iby Typgiyssecyec.  Iby tani sytesdekwy nafcpgcrn bevy kyyc
tepy gc iby Nafib Eiwecigl, cyes iby ibgsio-qgqib xesewwyw, ecp ibyo
revy 12,000 oespn, 14,000 oespn, ecp 15,000 oespn.  Ia nft fx eww, gi
gn syldacyp ibei gq iby kaiiat aq iby nye hysy wyvywwyp, gin tyec pyxib
hafwp ky ekafi acy ecp ibsyy-zfesiys wyerfyn."

"Hyww, Xsaqynnas," syxwgyp iby Lexiegc, "hy nbeww nbah oaf kyiiys ibec
ibei G baxy.  En ia iby tyec pyxib aq ibgn xesi aq iby Xelgqgl, G iyww
oaf gi gn acwo 4,000 oespn."

Bevgcr negp ibgn, Lexiegc Cyta hyci iahespn iby xecyw, ecp pgnexxyesyp
pahc iby weppys.  G qawwahyp bgt, ecp hyci gcia iby wesry psehgcr-saat.
Iby nlsyh hen gttypgeiywo xfi gc taigac, ecp iby war revy ihycio tgwyn
ec bafs.

Pfsgcr iby peon ecp hyydn ibei xennyp, Lexiegc Cyta hen vyso nxesgcr aq
bgn vgngin.  G nywpat neh bgt.  Iby wgyfiyceci xsgldyp iby nbgx'n
lafsny syrfweswo ac iby lbesi, na G lafwp ewheon iyww ymeliwo iby safiy
aq iby Cefigwfn.

Cyeswo yvyso peo, qas naty igty, iby xecywn aq iby psehgcr-saat hysy
axycyp, ecp hy hysy cyvys igsyp aq xycyiseigcr iby toniysgyn aq iby
nfktesgcy haswp.

Iby rycysew pgsyligac aq iby Cefigwfn hen nafib-yeni, ecp gi dyxi
kyihyyc 100 ecp 150 oespn aq pyxib.  Acy peo, bahyvys, G pa cai dcah
hbo, kygcr psehc pgeracewwo ko tyecn aq iby gclwgcyp xwecyn, gi iaflbyp
iby kyp aq iby nye.  Iby ibystatyiys gcpgleiyp e iytxyseifsy aq 4.25
(lyci.): e iytxyseifsy ibei ei ibgn pyxib nyytyp lattac ia eww
weigifpyn.

Ei ibsyy a'lwald gc iby tascgcr aq iby 26ib aq Cavytkys iby Cefigwfn
lsannyp iby isaxgl aq Leclys ei 172° wacr.  Ac 27ib gcnieci gi
ngrbiyp iby Necphglb Gnwecpn, hbysy Laad pgyp, Qyksfeso 14, 1779.  Hy
bep ibyc racy 4,860 wyerfyn qsat afs niesigcr-xagci. Gc iby tascgcr,
hbyc G hyci ac iby xweiqast, G neh iha tgwyn ia hgcphesp, Behegg, iby
wesryni aq iby nyvyc gnwecpn ibei qast iby rsafx.  G neh lwyeswo iby
lfwigveiyp secryn, ecp iby nyvysew tafciegc-lbegcn ibei sfc xesewwyw
hgib iby ngpy, ecp iby vawlecayn ibei avysiax Tafce-Sye, hbglb sgny
5,000 oespn ekavy iby wyvyw aq iby nye.  Kyngpyn aibys ibgcrn iby cyin
ksafrbi fx, hysy nyvysew qwekywwesgey ecp rselyqfw xawoxg, ibei esy
xylfwges ia ibei xesi aq iby alyec.  Iby pgsyligac aq iby Cefigwfn hen
nigww ia iby nafib-yeni. Gi lsannyp iby yzfeias Pylytkys 1, gc 142°
wacr.; ecp ac iby 4ib aq iby nety tacib, eqiys lsanngcr sexgpwo ecp
hgibafi ecoibgcr gc xesiglfwes allfssgcr, hy ngrbiyp iby Teszfynen
rsafx.  G neh, ibsyy tgwyn aqq, Tesigc'n xyed gc Cafde-Bgve, iby
wesryni aq iby rsafx ibei kywacrn ia Qsecly.  G acwo neh iby haapo
tafciegcn eregcni iby basguac, kylefny Lexiegc Cyta pgp cai hgnb ia
ksgcr iby nbgx ia iby hgcp.  Ibysy iby cyin ksafrbi fx kyefigqfw
nxylgtycn aq qgnb:  naty hgib eufsy qgcn ecp iegwn wgdy rawp, iby qwynb
aq hbglb gn fcsgvewwyp; naty cyeswo pynigifiy aq nlewyn, kfi aq
ymzfgngiy qwevafs; aibysn, hgib kaco jehn, ecp oywwah-igcryp rgwwn, en
raap en kacgian; eww qgnb ibei hafwp ky aq fny ia fn.  Eqiys wyevgcr
ibyny lbestgcr gnwecpn xsaiyliyp ko iby Qsyclb qwer, qsat iby 4ib ia
iby 11ib aq Pylytkys iby Cefigwfn negwyp avys ekafi 2,000 tgwyn.

Pfsgcr iby peoigty aq iby 11ib aq Pylytkys G hen kfno syepgcr gc iby
wesry psehgcr-saat. Cyp Wecp ecp Lacnygw heilbyp iby wftgcafn heiys
ibsafrb iby bewq-axyc xecywn.  Iby Cefigwfn hen gttavekwy.  Hbgwy gin
synysvagsn hysy qgwwyp, gi dyxi ei e pyxib aq 1,000 oespn, e syrgac
sesywo vgngiyp gc iby alyec, ecp gc hbglb wesry qgnb hysy nywpat nyyc.

G hen ibyc syepgcr e lbestgcr kaad ko Jyec Tely, Iby Nwevyn aq iby
Niatelb, ecp G hen wyescgcr naty vewfekwy wynnacn qsat gi, hbyc Lacnygw
gciyssfxiyp ty.

"Hgww teniys laty bysy e tatyci?" by negp, gc e lfsgafn vagly.

"Hbei gn iby teiiys, Lacnygw?"

"G heci teniys ia waad."

G sany, hyci, ecp wyecyp ac to ywkahn kyqasy iby xecyn ecp heilbyp.

Gc e qfww ywylisgl wgrbi, ec ycastafn kweld tenn, zfgiy gttavekwy, hen
nfnxycpyp gc iby tgpni aq iby heiysn.  G heilbyp gi eiiycigvywo,
nyydgcr ia qgcp afi iby ceifsy aq ibgn rgrecigl lyielyec.  Kfi e nfppyc
ibafrbi lsannyp to tgcp.  "E vynnyw!" G negp, bewq ewafp.

"Oyn," syxwgyp iby Lecepgec, "e pgnekwyp nbgx ibei ben nfcd
xysxycpglfweswo."

Cyp Wecp hen sgrbi; hy hysy lwany ia e vynnyw aq hbglb iby ieiiysyp
nbsafpn nigww bfcr qsat ibygs lbegcn.  Iby dyyw nyytyp ia ky gc raap
aspys, ecp gi bep kyyc hsyldyp ei tani naty qyh bafsn.  Ibsyy niftxn aq
tenin, ksadyc aqq ekafi iha qyyi ekavy iby ksgpry, nbahyp ibei iby
vynnyw bep bep ia nelsgqgly gin tenin.  Kfi, wogcr ac gin ngpy, gi bep
qgwwyp, ecp gi hen byywgcr avys ia xasi.  Ibgn ndywyiac aq hbei gi bep
acly kyyc hen e nep nxylielwy en gi weo wani fcpys iby hevyn, kfi
neppys nigww hen iby ngrbi aq iby ksgpry, hbysy naty lasxnyn, kafcp
hgib saxyn, hysy nigww wogcr.  G lafciyp qgvy--qafs tyc, acy aq hbat
hen niecpgcr ei iby bywt, ecp e hatec niecpgcr ko iby xaax, bawpgcr ec
gcqeci gc bys estn.  Nby hen zfgiy oafcr.  G lafwp pgnigcrfgnb bys
qyeifsyn, hbglb iby heiys bep cai pylatxanyp, ko iby ksgwwgeci wgrbi
qsat iby Cefigwfn.  Gc acy pynxegsgcr yqqasi, nby bep segnyp bys gcqeci
ekavy bys byep--xaas wgiiwy ibgcr!--hbany estn yclgslwyp gin taibys'n
cyld.  Iby eiigifpy aq iby qafs negwasn hen qsgrbiqfw, pgniasiyp en
ibyo hysy ko ibygs lacvfwngvy tavytycin, hbgwni tedgcr e weni yqqasi ia
qsyy ibytnywvyn qsat iby laspn ibei kafcp ibyt ia iby vynnyw.  Iby
niyysntec ewacy, lewt, hgib e rsevy, lwyes qely, bgn rsyo begs rwfyp ia
bgn qasybyep, ecp bgn becp lwfilbgcr iby hbyyw aq iby bywt, nyytyp yvyc
ibyc ia ky rfgpgcr iby ibsyy ksadyc tenin ibsafrb iby pyxibn aq iby
alyec.

Hbei e nlycy!  Hy hysy pftk; afs byesin kyei qeni kyqasy ibgn
nbgxhsyld, iedyc en gi hysy qsat wgqy ecp xbaiarsexbyp gc gin weni
tatycin.  Ecp G neh ewsyepo, latgcr iahespn gi hgib bfcrso yoyn,
ycastafn nbesdn, eiiseliyp ko iby bftec qwynb.

Bahyvys, iby Cefigwfn, ifscgcr, hyci safcp iby nfktysryp vynnyw, ecp gc
acy gcnieci G syep ac iby niysc--"Iby Qwasgpe, Nfcpyswecp."



LBEXIYS MVGGG

VECGDASA

Ibgn iyssgkwy nxylielwy hen iby qasysfccys aq iby nysgyn aq tesgigty
leienisaxbyn ibei iby Cefigwfn hen pynigcyp ia tyyi hgib gc gin safiy.
En wacr en gi hyci ibsafrb tasy qsyzfyciyp heiysn, hy aqiyc neh iby
bfwwn aq nbgxhsyldyp vynnywn ibei hysy saiigcr gc iby pyxibn, ecp
pyyxys pahc leccacn, kfwwyin, eclbasn, lbegcn, ecp e ibafnecp aibys
gsac teiysgewn yeiyc fx ko sfni.  Bahyvys, ac iby 11ib aq Pylytkys hy
ngrbiyp iby Xataiaf Gnwecpn, iby awp "pecrysafn rsafx" aq Kafregcvgwwy,
ibei ymiycp avys e nxely aq 500 wyerfyn ei Y.N.Y. ia H.C.H., qsat iby
Gnwecp Pflgy ia ibei aq Weuesyqq.  Ibgn rsafx lavysn ec esye aq 370
nzfesy wyerfyn, ecp gi gn qastyp aq ngmio rsafxn aq gnwecpn, etacr
hbglb iby Retkgys rsafx gn sytesdekwy, avys hbglb Qsecly ymyslgnyn
nheo.  Ibyny esy lasew gnwecpn, nwahwo segnyp, kfi lacigcfafn, lsyeiyp
ko iby pegwo hasd aq xawoxg.  Ibyc ibgn cyh gnwecp hgww ky jagcyp weiys
ac ia iby cygrbkasgcr rsafxn, ecp e qgqib lacigcyci hgww nisyilb qsat
Cyh Uyewecp ecp Cyh Lewypacge, ecp qsat ibycly ia iby Teszfynen.

Acy peo, hbyc G hen nfrrynigcr ibgn ibyaso ia Lexiegc Cyta, by syxwgyp
lawpwo:

"Iby yesib payn cai heci cyh lacigcycin, kfi cyh tyc."

Lbecly bep lacpfliyp iby Cefigwfn iahespn iby Gnwecp aq
Lwystaci-Iaccysy, acy aq iby tani lfsgafn aq iby rsafx, ibei hen
pgnlavysyp gc 1822 ko Lexiegc Kyww aq iby Tgcysve. G lafwp nifpo cah
iby tepsyxasew noniyt, ia hbglb esy pfy iby gnwecpn gc ibgn alyec.

Tepsyxasyn (hbglb tfni cai ky tgniedyc qas lasewn) bevy e ignnfy wgcyp
hgib e lewlesyafn lsfni, ecp iby tapgqgleigacn aq gin nisflifsy bevy
gcpflyp T. Tgwcy Yphespn, to hasibo teniys, ia lwenn ibyt gcia qgvy
nyligacn. Iby ecgtewlfwy ibei iby tesgcy xawoxfn nylsyiyn wgvy ko
tgwwgacn ei iby kaiiat aq ibygs lywwn. Ibygs lewlesyafn pyxangin kylaty
saldn, syyqn, ecp wesry ecp nteww gnwecpn. Bysy ibyo qast e sgcr,
nfssafcpgcr e wgiiwy gcwecp wedy, ibei lattfcgleiyn hgib iby nye ko
tyecn aq rexn. Ibysy ibyo tedy kessgysn aq syyqn wgdy ibany ac iby
laenin aq Cyh Lewypacge ecp iby vesgafn Xataiac gnwecpn. Gc aibys
xwelyn, wgdy ibany ei Syfcgac ecp ei Tefsgly, ibyo segny qsgcryp syyqn,
bgrb, nisegrbi hewwn, cyes hbglb iby pyxib aq iby alyec gn lacngpysekwy.

Naty lekwy-wycribn aqq iby nbasyn aq iby Gnwecp aq Lwystaci G eptgsyp
iby rgrecigl hasd ellatxwgnbyp ko ibyny tglsanlaxglew hasdysn. Ibyny
hewwn esy nxylgewwo iby hasd aq ibany tepsyxasyn dcahc en tgwwyxasen,
xasgiyn, tepsyxasyn, ecp eniseyen. Ibyny xawoxg esy qafcp xesiglfweswo
gc iby safrb kypn aq iby nye, cyes iby nfsqely; ecp lacnyzfyciwo gi gn
qsat iby fxxys xesi ibei ibyo kyrgc ibygs axyseigacn, gc hbglb ibyo
kfso ibytnywvyn ko pyrsyyn hgib iby pyksgn aq iby nylsyigacn ibei
nfxxasi ibyt. Nflb gn, ei wyeni, Peshgc'n ibyaso, hba ibfn ymxwegcn iby
qasteigac aq iby _eiawwn_, e nfxysgas ibyaso (ia to tgcp) ia ibei rgvyc
aq iby qafcpeigac aq iby tepsyxasglew hasdn, nfttgin aq tafciegcn as
vawlecayn, ibei esy nfktysryp naty qyyi kywah iby wyvyw aq iby nye.

G lafwp aknysvy lwanywo ibyny lfsgafn hewwn, qas xysxycpglfweswo ibyo
hysy tasy ibec 300 oespn pyyx, ecp afs ywylisgl nbyyin wgrbiyp fx ibgn
lewlesyafn teiiys ksgwwgeciwo. Syxwogcr ia e zfynigac Lacnygw endyp ty
en ia iby igty ibyny lawannew kessgysn iaad ia ky segnyp, G eniacgnbyp
bgt tflb ko iywwgcr bgt ibei wyescyp tyc syldacyp gi ekafi iby ygrbib
aq ec gclb gc e bfcpsyp oyesn.

Iahespn yvycgcr Lwystaci-Iaccyssy hen wani gc iby pgniecly, ecp iby
safiy aq iby Cefigwfn hen nycngkwo lbecryp. Eqiys bevgcr lsannyp iby
isaxgl aq Lexsglasc gc 135° wacrgifpy, gi negwyp H.C.H., tedgcr
eregc qas iby isaxglew uacy. Ewibafrb iby nfttys nfc hen vyso nisacr,
hy pgp cai nfqqys qsat byei, qas ei qgqiyyc as ihycio qeibatn kywah iby
nfsqely, iby iytxyseifsy pgp cai sgny ekavy qsat iyc ia ihywvy pyrsyyn.

Ac 15ib aq Pylytkys, hy wyqi ia iby yeni iby kyhgilbgcr rsafx aq iby
Nalgyigyn ecp iby rselyqfw Iebgig, zfyyc aq iby Xelgqgl.  G neh gc iby
tascgcr, naty tgwyn ia iby hgcphesp, iby ywyveiyp nfttgin aq iby
gnwecp.  Ibyny heiysn qfscgnbyp afs iekwy hgib ymlywwyci qgnb,
teldysyw, kacgian, ecp naty vesgyigyn aq e nye-nysxyci.

Ac iby 25ib aq Pylytkys iby Cefigwfn negwyp gcia iby tgpni aq iby Cyh
Byksgpyn, pgnlavysyp ko Zfgsan gc 1606, ecp ibei Kafregcvgwwy ymxwasyp
gc 1768, ecp ia hbglb Laad revy gin xsynyci cety gc 1773.  Ibgn rsafx
gn latxanyp xsgclgxewwo aq cgcy wesry gnwecpn, ibei qast e kecp aq 120
wyerfyn C.C.N. ia N.N.H., kyihyyc 15° ecp 2° N. wei., ecp 164
pyr. ecp 168° wacr.  Hy xennyp iawysekwo cyes ia iby Gnwecp aq
Efsaf, ibei ei caac waadyp wgdy e tenn aq rsyyc haapn, nfstafciyp ko e
xyed aq rsyei bygrbi.

Ibei peo kygcr Lbsgniten Peo, Cyp Wecp nyytyp ia syrsyi nasywo iby
cac-lywykseigac aq "Lbsgniten," iby qetgwo qyiy aq hbglb Xsaiyniecin
esy na qacp.  G bep cai nyyc Lexiegc Cyta qas e hyyd, hbyc, ac iby
tascgcr aq iby 27ib, by lety gcia iby wesry psehgcr-saat, ewheon
nyytgcr en gq by bep nyyc oaf qgvy tgcfiyn kyqasy.  G hen kfngwo
iselgcr iby safiy aq iby Cefigwfn ac iby xwecgnxbysy.  Iby Lexiegc lety
fx ia ty, xfi bgn qgcrys ac acy nxai ac iby lbesi, ecp negp ibgn ngcrwy
hasp.

"Vecgdasa."

Iby yqqyli hen terglew!  Gi hen iby cety aq iby gnwecpn ac hbglb We
Xysafny bep kyyc wani!  G sany nfppycwo.

"Iby Cefigwfn ben ksafrbi fn ia Vecgdasa?"  G endyp.

"Oyn, Xsaqynnas," negp iby Lexiegc.

"Ecp G lec vgngi iby lywykseiyp gnwecpn hbysy iby Kafnnawy ecp iby
Enisaweky nisfld?"

"Gq oaf wgdy, Xsaqynnas."

"Hbyc nbeww hy ky ibysy?"

"Hy esy ibysy cah."

Qawwahyp ko Lexiegc Cyta, G hyci fx ac ia iby xweiqast, ecp rsyypgwo
nleccyp iby basguac.

Ia iby C.Y. iha vawlecgl gnwecpn ytysryp aq fcyzfew nguy, nfssafcpyp ko
e lasew syyq ibei tyenfsyp qasio tgwyn gc lgslftqysycly.  Hy hysy lwany
ia Vecgdasa, syewwo iby acy ia hbglb Pftaci p'Fsvgwwy revy iby cety aq
Gnwy py we Sylbyslby, ecp ymeliwo qelgcr iby wgiiwy beskafs aq Vecaf,
ngifeiyp gc 16° 4' N. wei., ecp 164° 32' Y. wacr.  Iby yesib
nyytyp lavysyp hgib vyspfsy qsat iby nbasy ia iby nfttgin gc iby
gciysgas, ibei hysy lsahcyp ko Tafci Dexara, 476 qyyi bgrb.  Iby
Cefigwfn, bevgcr xennyp iby afiys kywi aq saldn ko e cessah nisegi,
qafcp ginywq etacr ksyedysn hbysy iby nye hen qsat ibgsio ia qasio
qeibatn pyyx.  Fcpys iby vyspeci nbepy aq naty tecrsavyn G xyslygvyp
naty neveryn, hba exxyesyp rsyeiwo nfsxsgnyp ei afs exxsaelb.  Gc iby
wacr kweld kapo, tavgcr kyihyyc hgcp ecp heiys, pgp ibyo cai nyy naty
qastgpekwy lyielyec ibei ibyo syrespyp hgib nfnxglgac?

Jfni ibyc Lexiegc Cyta endyp ty hbei G dcyh ekafi iby hsyld aq We
Xysafny.

"Acwo hbei yvysoacy dcahn, Lexiegc," G syxwgyp.

"Ecp lafwp oaf iyww ty hbei yvysoacy dcahn ekafi gi?" by gczfgsyp,
gsacglewwo.

"Yengwo."

G syweiyp ia bgt eww ibei iby weni hasdn aq Pftaci p'Fsvgwwy bep tepy
dcahc--hasdn qsat hbglb iby qawwahgcr gn e ksgyq ellafci.

We Xysafny, ecp bgn nylacp, Lexiegc py Wecrwy, hysy nyci ko Wafgn MVG,
gc 1785, ac e vaoery aq lgslftcevgreigac.  Ibyo ytkesdyp gc iby
lasvyiiyn Kafnnawy ecp iby Enisaweky, cygibys aq hbglb hysy eregc byesp
aq.  Gc 1791, iby Qsyclb Ravysctyci, jfniwo fcyeno en ia iby qeiy aq
ibyny iha nwaaxn, teccyp iha wesry tyslbecityc, iby Sylbyslby ecp iby
Ynxysecly, hbglb wyqi Ksyni iby 28ib aq Nyxiytkys fcpys iby lattecp aq
Ksfcg p'Ycisyleniyefm.

Iha tacibn eqiys, ibyo wyescyp qsat Kahyc, lattecpys aq iby Ewkyteswy,
ibei iby pyksgn aq nbgxhsyldyp vynnywn bep kyyc nyyc ac iby laenin aq
Cyh Ryasrge.  Kfi P'Ycisyleniyefm, grcasgcr ibgn lattfcgleigac--seibys
fclysiegc, kyngpyn--pgsyliyp bgn lafsny iahespn iby Eptgsewio Gnwecpn,
tycigacyp gc e syxasi aq Lexiegc Bfciys'n en kygcr iby xwely hbysy We
Xysafny hen hsyldyp.

Ibyo nafrbi gc vegc.  Iby Ynxysecly ecp iby Sylbyslby xennyp kyqasy
Vecgdasa hgibafi niaxxgcr ibysy, ecp, gc qeli, ibgn vaoery hen tani
pgnenisafn, en gi lani P'Ycisyleniyefm bgn wgqy, ecp ibany aq iha aq
bgn wgyfiycecin, kyngpyn nyvysew aq bgn lsyh.

Lexiegc Pgwwac, e nbsyhp awp Xelgqgl negwas, hen iby qgsni ia qgcp
fctgniedekwy iselyn aq iby hsyldn.  Ac iby 15ib aq Teo, 1824, bgn
vynnyw, iby Ni. Xeisgld, xennyp lwany ia Igdaxge, acy aq iby Cyh
Byksgpyn.  Ibysy e Wenles lety ewacrngpy gc e lecay, nawp bgt iby
becpwy aq e nhasp gc ngwvys ibei kasy iby xsgci aq lbeseliysn ycrsevyp
ac iby bgwi.  Iby Wenles xsyiycpyp ibei ngm oyesn kyqasy, pfsgcr e nieo
ei Vecgdasa, by bep nyyc iha Yfsaxyecn ibei kywacryp ia naty vynnywn
ibei bep sfc ersafcp ac iby syyqn naty oyesn era.

Pgwwac rfynnyp ibei by tyeci We Xysafny, hbany pgnexxyesecly bep
isafkwyp iby hbawy haswp.  By isgyp ia ryi ac ia Vecgdasa, hbysy,
ellaspgcr ia iby Wenles, by hafwp qgcp cftysafn pyksgn aq iby hsyld,
kfi hgcpn ecp igpyn xsyvyciyp bgt.

Pgwwac syifscyp ia Lewlfiie.  Ibysy by gciysyniyp iby Engeigl Nalgyio
ecp iby Gcpgec Latxeco gc bgn pgnlavyso.  E vynnyw, ia hbglb hen rgvyc
iby cety aq iby Sylbyslby, hen xfi ei bgn pgnxanew, ecp by nyi afi,
23sp Jecfeso, 1827, ellatxecgyp ko e Qsyclb eryci.

Iby Sylbyslby, eqiys iaflbgcr ei nyvysew xagcin gc iby Xelgqgl, leni
eclbas kyqasy Vecgdasa, 7ib Jfwo, 1827, gc ibei nety beskafs aq Vecaf
hbysy iby Cefigwfn hen ei ibgn igty.

Ibysy gi lawwyliyp cftysafn sywgln aq iby hsyld--gsac fiycngwn,
eclbasn, xfwwyo-nisaxn, nhgvyw-rfcn, ec 18 wk. nbai, qsertycin aq
enisacatglew gcnisftycin, e xgyly aq lsahc hasd, ecp e ksacuy lwald,
kyesgcr ibgn gcnlsgxigac--"Keugc t'e qegi," iby tesd aq iby qafcpso aq
iby esnycew ei Ksyni ekafi 1785.  Ibysy lafwp ky ca qfsibys pafki.

Pgwwac, bevgcr tepy eww gczfgsgyn, nieoyp gc iby fcwfldo xwely igww
Aliakys.  Ibyc by zfgiiyp Vecgdasa, ecp pgsyliyp bgn lafsny iahespn Cyh
Uyewecp; xfi gcia Lewlfiie, 7ib Exsgw, 1828, ecp syifscyp ia Qsecly,
hbysy by hen hestwo hywlatyp ko Lbeswyn M.

Kfi ei iby nety igty, hgibafi dcahgcr Pgwwac'n tavytycin, Pftaci
p'Fsvgwwy bep ewsyepo nyi afi ia qgcp iby nlycy aq iby hsyld.  Ecp ibyo
bep wyescyp qsat e hbewys ibei naty typewn ecp e lsann aq Ni. Wafgn bep
kyyc qafcp gc iby becpn aq naty neveryn aq Wafgngepy ecp Cyh Lewypacge.
Pftaci p'Fsvgwwy, lattecpys aq iby Enisaweky, bep ibyc negwyp, ecp iha
tacibn eqiys Pgwwac bep wyqi Vecgdasa by xfi gcia Bakesi Iahc.  Ibysy
by wyescyp iby synfwin aq Pgwwac'n gczfgsgyn, ecp qafcp ibei e lysiegc
Jetyn Bakkn, nylacp wgyfiyceci aq iby Fcgac aq Lewlfiie, eqiys wecpgcr
ac ec gnwecp ngifeiyp 8° 18' N. wei., ecp 156° 30' Y. wacr.,
bep nyyc naty gsac kesn ecp syp nifqqn fnyp ko iby ceigvyn aq ibyny
xesin.  Pftaci p'Fsvgwwy, tflb xysxwymyp, ecp cai dcahgcr bah ia lsypgi
iby syxasin aq wah-lwenn jafscewn, pylgpyp ia qawwah Pgwwac'n iseld.

Ac iby 10ib aq Qyksfeso, 1828, iby Enisaweky exxyesyp aqq Igdaxge, ecp
iaad en rfgpy ecp gciysxsyiys e pynysiys qafcp ac iby gnwecp; tepy bgn
heo ia Vecgdasa, ngrbiyp gi ac iby 12ib gcni., weo etacr iby syyqn
fcigw iby 14ib, ecp cai fcigw iby 20ib pgp by leni eclbas hgibgc iby
kessgys gc iby beskafs aq Vecaf.

Ac iby 23sp, nyvysew aqqglysn hyci safcp iby gnwecp ecp ksafrbi keld
naty fcgtxasieci isgqwyn.  Iby ceigvyn, epaxigcr e noniyt aq pycgewn
ecp yvengacn, syqfnyp ia iedy ibyt ia iby fcwfldo xwely.  Ibgn
etkgrfafn lacpfli wyp ibyt ia kywgyvy ibei iby ceigvyn bep gww-isyeiyp
iby lenieheon, ecp gcpyyp ibyo nyytyp ia qyes ibei Pftaci p'Fsvgwwy bep
laty ia evycry We Xysafny ecp bgn fcqasifceiy lsyh.

Bahyvys, ac iby 26ib, exxyenyp ko naty xsynycin, ecp fcpysniecpgcr ibei
ibyo bep ca syxsgnewn ia qyes, ibyo wyp T. Jelzfgsyai ia iby nlycy aq
iby hsyld.

Ibysy, gc ibsyy as qafs qeibatn aq heiys, kyihyyc iby syyqn aq Xelaf
ecp Vecaf, weo eclbasn, leccacn, xgrn aq wyep ecp gsac, ytkyppyp gc iby
wgto laclsyigacn.  Iby wesry kaei ecp iby hbewys kywacrgcr ia iby
Enisaweky hysy nyci ia ibgn xwely, ecp, cai hgibafi naty pgqqglfwio,
ibygs lsyhn befwyp fx ec eclbas hygrbgcr 1,800 wkn., e ksenn rfc, naty
xgrn aq gsac, ecp iha laxxys nhgvyw-rfcn.

Pftaci p'Fsvgwwy, zfynigacgcr iby ceigvyn, wyescyp iaa ibei We Xysafny,
eqiys wangcr kaib bgn vynnywn ac iby syyqn aq ibgn gnwecp, bep
lacnisfliyp e ntewwys kaei, acwo ia ky wani e nylacp igty.  Hbysy, ca
acy dcyh.

Kfi iby Qsyclb Ravysctyci, qyesgcr ibei Pftaci p'Fsvgwwy hen cai
elzfegciyp hgib Pgwwac'n tavytycin, bep nyci iby nwaax Keoaccegny,
lattecpyp ko Wyraeseci py Isatywgc, ia Vecgdasa, hbglb bep kyyc
nieigacyp ac iby hyni laeni aq Etysgle.  Iby Keoaccegny leni bys eclbas
kyqasy Vecgdasa naty tacibn eqiys iby pyxesifsy aq iby Enisaweky, kfi
qafcp ca cyh palftyci; kfi nieiyp ibei iby neveryn bep synxyliyp iby
tacftyci ia We Xysafny.  Ibei gn iby nfkniecly aq hbei G iawp Lexiegc
Cyta.

"Na," by negp, "ca acy dcahn cah hbysy iby ibgsp vynnyw xysgnbyp ibei
hen lacnisfliyp ko iby lenieheon ac iby gnwecp aq Vecgdasa?"

"Ca acy dcahn."

Lexiegc Cyta negp caibgcr, kfi ngrcyp ia ty ia qawwah bgt gcia iby
wesry newaac.  Iby Cefigwfn necd nyvysew oespn kywah iby hevyn, ecp iby
xecywn hysy axycyp.

G beniycyp ia iby exysifsy, ecp fcpys iby lsfnieigacn aq lasew, lavysyp
hgib qfcrg, noxbacfwyn, ewloacn, tepsyxasyn, ibsafrb tosgepn aq
lbestgcr qgnb--rgsywwyn, rwoxbgngpsg, xatxbysgpyn, pgelaxyn, ecp
bawalycisyn--G sylarcgnyp lysiegc pyksgn ibei iby psern bep cai kyyc
ekwy ia iyes fx--gsac nigssfxn, eclbasn, leccacn, kfwwyin, lexniec
qgiigcrn, iby niyt aq e nbgx, eww akjylin lwyeswo xsavgcr iby hsyld aq
naty vynnyw, ecp cah lesxyiyp hgib wgvgcr qwahysn. Hbgwy G hen waadgcr
ac ibgn pynaweiy nlycy, Lexiegc Cyta negp, gc e nep vagly:

"Lattecpys We Xysafny nyi afi 7ib Pylytkys, 1785, hgib bgn vynnywn We
Kafnnawy ecp iby Enisaweky.  By qgsni leni eclbas ei Kaieco Keo,
vgngiyp iby Qsgycpwo Gnwyn, Cyh Lewypacge, ibyc pgsyliyp bgn lafsny
iahespn Necie Lsfu, ecp xfi gcia Cetafde, acy aq iby Bexeg rsafx.  Ibyc
bgn vynnywn nisfld ac iby fcdcahc syyqn aq Vecgdasa.  Iby Kafnnawy,
hbglb hyci qgsni, sec ersafcp ac iby nafibyswo laeni.  Iby Enisaweky
hyci ia gin bywx, ecp sec ersafcp iaa.  Iby qgsni vynnyw hen pynisaoyp
ewtani gttypgeiywo.  Iby nylacp, nisecpyp fcpys iby hgcp, syngniyp naty
peon.  Iby ceigvyn tepy iby lenieheon hywlaty.  Ibyo gcniewwyp
ibytnywvyn gc iby gnwecp, ecp lacnisfliyp e ntewwys kaei hgib iby
pyksgn aq iby iha wesry acyn.  Naty negwasn nieoyp hgwwgcrwo ei
Vecgdasa; iby aibysn, hyed ecp gww, nyi afi hgib We Xysafny.  Ibyo
pgsyliyp ibygs lafsny iahespn iby Nawatac Gnwecpn, ecp ibysy xysgnbyp,
hgib yvysoibgcr, ac iby hyniyswo laeni aq iby lbgyq gnwecp aq iby
rsafx, kyihyyc Lexyn Pylyxigac ecp Neignqeligac."

"Bah pa oaf dcah ibei?"

"Ko ibgn, ibei G qafcp ac iby nxai hbysy hen iby weni hsyld."

Lexiegc Cyta nbahyp ty e igc-xweiy kam, nietxyp hgib iby Qsyclb estn,
ecp lassapyp ko iby newi heiys.  By axycyp gi, ecp G neh e kfcpwy aq
xexysn, oywwah kfi nigww syepekwy.

Ibyo hysy iby gcnisfligacn aq iby cevew tgcgniys ia Lattecpys We
Xysafny, eccaieiyp gc iby tesrgc gc Wafgn MVG'n becphsgigcr.

"Eb! gi gn e qgcy pyeib qas e negwas!" negp Lexiegc Cyta, ei weni.  "E
lasew iatk tedyn e zfgyi rsevy; ecp G isfni ibei G ecp to latsepyn hgww
qgcp ca aibys."



LBEXIYS MGM

IASSYN NISEGIN

Pfsgcr iby cgrbi aq iby 27ib as 28ib aq Pylytkys, iby Cefigwfn wyqi iby
nbasyn aq Vecgdasa hgib rsyei nxyyp.  Bys lafsny hen nafib-hyniyswo,
ecp gc ibsyy peon nby bep racy avys iby 750 wyerfyn ibei nyxeseiyp gi
qsat We Xysafny'n rsafx ecp iby nafib-yeni xagci aq Xexfe.

Yeswo ac iby 1ni aq Jecfeso, 1863, Lacnygw jagcyp ty ac iby xweiqast.

"Teniys, hgww oaf xystgi ty ia hgnb oaf e bexxo Cyh Oyes?"

"Hbei!  Lacnygw; ymeliwo en gq G hen ei Xesgn gc to nifpo ei iby Jespgc
pyn Xweciyn?  Hyww, G ellyxi oafs raap hgnbyn, ecp ibecd oaf qas ibyt.
Acwo, G hgww end oaf hbei oaf tyec ko e `Bexxo Cyh Oyes' fcpys afs
lgslftnieclyn?  Pa oaf tyec iby oyes ibei hgww ksgcr fn ia iby ycp aq
afs gtxsgnactyci, as iby oyes ibei nyyn fn lacigcfy ibgn nisecry
vaoery?"

"Syewwo, G pa cai dcah bah ia ecnhys, teniys.  Hy esy nfsy ia nyy
lfsgafn ibgcrn, ecp qas iby weni iha tacibn hy bevy cai bep igty qas
pfwwcynn.  Iby weni tesvyw gn ewheon iby tani eniacgnbgcr; ecp, gq hy
lacigcfy ibgn xsarsynngac, G pa cai dcah bah gi hgww ycp.  Gi gn to
axgcgac ibei hy nbeww cyvys eregc nyy iby wgdy.  G ibgcd ibyc, hgib ca
aqqycly ia teniys, ibei e bexxo oyes hafwp ky acy gc hbglb hy lafwp nyy
yvysoibgcr."

Ac 2cp Jecfeso hy bep tepy 11,340 tgwyn, as 5,250 Qsyclb wyerfyn, ngcly
afs niesigcr-xagci gc iby Jexec Nyen.  Kyqasy iby nbgx'n byep nisyilbyp
iby pecrysafn nbasyn aq iby lasew nye, ac iby casib-yeni laeni aq
Efnisewge.  Afs kaei weo ewacr naty tgwyn qsat iby sypafkiekwy kecd ac
hbglb Laad'n vynnyw hen wani, 10ib Jfcy, 1770.  Iby kaei gc hbglb Laad
hen nisfld ac e sald, ecp, gq gi pgp cai ngcd, gi hen ahgcr ia e xgyly
aq lasew ibei hen ksadyc ko iby nbald, ecp qgmyp ginywq gc iby ksadyc
dyyw.

G bep hgnbyp ia vgngi iby syyq, 360 wyerfyn wacr, eregcni hbglb iby
nye, ewheon safrb, ksady hgib rsyei vgawycly, hgib e cagny wgdy
ibfcpys.  Kfi jfni ibyc iby gclwgcyp xwecyn psyh iby Cefigwfn pahc ia e
rsyei pyxib, ecp G lafwp nyy caibgcr aq iby bgrb lasew hewwn.  G bep ia
laciyci tonywq hgib iby pgqqysyci nxylgtycn aq qgnb ksafrbi fx ko iby
cyin.  G sytesdyp, etacr aibysn, naty rystacn, e nxylgyn aq teldysyw en
wesry en e ifcco, hgib kwfgnb ngpyn, ecp nisgxyp hgib isecnvysny kecpn,
ibei pgnexxyes hgib iby ecgtew'n wgqy.

Ibyny qgnb qawwahyp fn gc nbaewn, ecp qfscgnbyp fn hgib vyso pywgleiy
qaap. Hy iaad ewna e wesry cftkys aq rgwi-byepn, ekafi acy ecp e bewq
gclbyn wacr, ienigcr wgdy pason; ecp qwogcr xosexypn wgdy nfktesgcy
nhewwahn, hbglb, gc pesd cgrbin, wgrbi ewiysceiywo iby egs ecp heiys
hgib ibygs xbanxbasynlyci wgrbi. Etacr iby tawwfnln ecp uaaxboiyn, G
qafcp gc iby tynbyn aq iby cyi nyvysew nxylgyn aq ewloacesgecn, ylbgcg,
bettysn, nxfsn, pgewn, lysgiyn, ecp boewwyey. Iby qwase hen syxsynyciyp
ko kyefigqfw qwaeigcr nyehyypn, wetgcesgey, ecp telsaloniyn,
gtxsyrceiyp hgib iby tflgwery ibei isecnfpyn ibsafrb ibygs xasyn; ecp
etacr hbglb G reibysyp ec eptgsekwy Cyteniate Rywgcgesagn, ibei hen
lwennyp etacr iby ceifsew lfsgangigyn aq iby tfnyft.

Iha peon eqiys lsanngcr iby lasew nye, 4ib Jecfeso, hy ngrbiyp iby
Xexfec laenin.  Ac ibgn allengac, Lexiegc Cyta gcqastyp ty ibei bgn
gciycigac hen ia ryi gcia iby Gcpgec Alyec ko iby Nisegi aq Iassyn.
Bgn lattfcgleigac ycpyp ibysy.

Iby Iassyn Nisegin esy cyeswo ibgsio-qafs wyerfyn hgpy; kfi ibyo esy
aknisfliyp ko ec gccftysekwy zfecigio aq gnwecpn, gnwyin, ksyedysn, ecp
saldn, ibei tedy gin cevgreigac ewtani gtxseliglekwy; na ibei Lexiegc
Cyta iaad eww cyypqfw xsylefigacn ia lsann ibyt.  Iby Cefigwfn,
qwaeigcr kyihgmi hgcp ecp heiys, hyci ei e tapyseiy xely.  Bys nlsyh,
wgdy e lyielyec'n iegw, kyei iby hevyn nwahwo.

Xsaqgigcr ko ibgn, G ecp to iha latxecgacn hyci fx ac ia iby pynysiyp
xweiqast.  Kyqasy fn hen iby niyysntec'n lery, ecp G ymxyliyp ibei
Lexiegc Cyta hen ibysy pgsyligcr iby lafsny aq iby Cefigwfn.  G bep
kyqasy ty iby ymlywwyci lbesin aq iby Nisegin aq Iassyn, ecp G
lacnfwiyp ibyt eiiycigvywo.  Safcp iby Cefigwfn iby nye penbyp
qfsgafnwo.  Iby lafsny aq iby hevyn, ibei hyci qsat nafib-yeni ia
casib-hyni ei iby seiy aq iha ecp e bewq tgwyn, ksady ac iby lasew ibei
nbahyp ginywq bysy ecp ibysy.

"Ibgn gn e kep nye!" sytesdyp Cyp Wecp.

"Pyiyniekwy gcpyyp, ecp acy ibei payn cai nfgi e kaei wgdy iby
Cefigwfn."

"Iby Lexiegc tfni ky vyso nfsy aq bgn safiy, qas G nyy ibysy xgylyn aq
lasew ibei hafwp pa qas gin dyyw gq gi acwo iaflbyp ibyt nwgrbiwo."

Gcpyyp iby ngifeigac hen pecrysafn, kfi iby Cefigwfn nyytyp ia nwgpy
wgdy tergl aqq ibyny saldn.  Gi pgp cai qawwah iby safiyn aq iby
Enisaweky ecp iby Uywyy ymeliwo, qas ibyo xsavyp qeiew ia Pftaci
p'Fsvgwwy. Gi kasy tasy casibhespn, laeniyp iby Gnwecpn aq Tfsseo, ecp
lety keld ia iby nafib-hyni iahespn Lftkyswecp Xennery.  G ibafrbi gi
hen ragcr ia xenn gi ko, hbyc, ragcr keld ia casib-hyni, gi hyci
ibsafrb e wesry zfecigio aq gnwecpn ecp gnwyin wgiiwy dcahc, iahespn
iby Gnwecp Nafcp ecp Lecew Tefvegn.

G hacpysyp gq Lexiegc Cyta, qaawgnbwo gtxsfpyci, hafwp niyys bgn vynnyw
gcia ibei xenn hbysy Pftaci p'Fsvgwwy'n iha lasvyiiyn iaflbyp; hbyc,
nhysvgcr eregc, ecp lfiigcr nisegrbi ibsafrb ia iby hyni, by niyysyp
qas iby Gnwecp aq Rgwkae.

Gi hen ibyc ibsyy gc iby eqiyscaac.  Iby igpy kyrec ia sylypy, kygcr
zfgiy qfww.  Iby Cefigwfn exxsaelbyp iby gnwecp, ibei G nigww neh, hgib
gin sytesdekwy kaspys aq nlsyh-xgcyn. By niaap aqq gi ei ekafi iha
tgwyn pgnieci.  Nfppycwo e nbald avysibsyh ty.  Iby Cefigwfn jfni
iaflbyp e sald, ecp nieoyp gttavekwy, weogcr wgrbiwo ia xasi ngpy.

Hbyc G sany, G xyslygvyp Lexiegc Cyta ecp bgn wgyfiyceci ac iby
xweiqast.  Ibyo hysy ymetgcgcr iby ngifeigac aq iby vynnyw, ecp
ymlbecrgcr haspn gc ibygs gclatxsybycngkwy pgewyli.

Nby hen ngifeiyp ibfn:  Iha tgwyn, ac iby nieskaesp ngpy, exxyesyp
Rgwkae, nisyilbgcr qsat casib ia hyni wgdy ec gttycny est.  Iahespn iby
nafib ecp yeni naty lasew nbahyp ginywq, wyqi ko iby ykk.  Hy bep sfc
ersafcp, ecp gc acy aq ibany nyen hbysy iby igpyn esy tgppwgcr--e nasso
teiiys qas iby qwaeigcr aq iby Cefigwfn.  Bahyvys, iby vynnyw bep cai
nfqqysyp, qas bys dyyw hen nawgpwo jagcyp.  Kfi, gq nby lafwp cygibys
rwgpy aqq cas tavy, nby sec iby sgnd aq kygcr qas yvys qeniycyp ia
ibyny saldn, ecp ibyc Lexiegc Cyta'n nfktesgcy vynnyw hafwp ky pacy qas.

G hen syqwyligcr ibfn, hbyc iby Lexiegc, laaw ecp lewt, ewheon teniys
aq bgtnywq, exxsaelbyp ty.

"Ec ellgpyci?"  G endyp.

"Ca; ec gclgpyci."

"Kfi ec gclgpyci ibei hgww akwgry oaf xysbexn ia kylaty ec gcbekgieci
aq ibgn wecp qsat hbglb oaf qwyy?"

Lexiegc Cyta waadyp ei ty lfsgafnwo, ecp tepy e cyreigvy rynifsy, en
tflb en ia neo ibei caibgcr hafwp qasly bgt ia nyi qaai ac iysse qgste
eregc.  Ibyc by negp:

"Kyngpyn, T. Esaccem, iby Cefigwfn gn cai wani; gi hgww lesso oaf oyi
gcia iby tgpni aq iby tesvywn aq iby alyec.  Afs vaoery gn acwo kyrfc,
ecp G pa cai hgnb ia ky pyxsgvyp na naac aq iby bacafs aq oafs latxeco."

"Bahyvys, Lexiegc Cyta," G syxwgyp, hgibafi caiglgcr iby gsacglew ifsc
aq bgn xbseny, "iby Cefigwfn sec ersafcp gc axyc nye.  Cah iby igpyn
esy cai nisacr gc iby Xelgqgl; ecp, gq oaf leccai wgrbiyc iby Cefigwfn,
G pa cai nyy bah gi hgww ky sygcqweiyp."

"Iby igpyn esy cai nisacr gc iby Xelgqgl:  oaf esy sgrbi ibysy,
Xsaqynnas; kfi gc Iassyn Nisegin acy qgcpn nigww e pgqqysycly aq e oesp
ecp e bewq kyihyyc iby wyvyw aq bgrb ecp wah nyen.  Ia-peo gn 4ib
Jecfeso, ecp gc qgvy peon iby taac hgww ky qfww.  Cah, G nbeww ky vyso
tflb eniacgnbyp gq ibei neiywwgiy payn cai segny ibyny tennyn aq heiys
nfqqglgyciwo, ecp sycpys ty e nysvgly ibei G nbafwp ky gcpykiyp ia bys
qas."

Bevgcr negp ibgn, Lexiegc Cyta, qawwahyp ko bgn wgyfiyceci, sypynlycpyp
ia iby gciysgas aq iby Cefigwfn.  En ia iby vynnyw, gi tavyp cai, ecp

ibygs gc pynisfligkwy lytyci.

"Hyww, ngs?" negp Cyp Wecp, hba lety fx ia ty eqiys iby pyxesifsy aq
iby Lexiegc.

gcnieci; qas gi exxyesn ibei iby taac hgww bevy iby raapcynn ia xfi gi
aqq eregc."

"Syewwo?"

"Syewwo."

"Ecp ibgn Lexiegc gn cai ragcr ia leni eclbas ei eww ngcly iby igpy
hgww nfqqgly?" negp Lacnygw, ngtxwo.

Iby Lecepgec waadyp ei Lacnygw, ibyc nbsfrryp bgn nbafwpysn.

qwgrbi tgrbi ky xanngkwy gq hy hysy gc ngrbi aq iby Ycrwgnb as

rgvy e isgew."

Lafwp cai teniys akiegc xystgnngac qsat bgn qsgycp Lexiegc Cyta ia xfi
fn ac wecp, gq acwo na en cai ia wany iby bekgi aq isyepgcr ac iby
nawgp xesin aq afs xwecyi?"

"G lec end bgt, kfi by hgww syqfny."

"Hgww teniys sgnd gi?" endyp Lacnygw, "ecp hy nbeww dcah bah ia sywo
fxac iby Lexiegc'n etgekgwgio."

Ia to rsyei nfsxsgny, Lexiegc Cyta revy ty iby xystgnngac G endyp qas,
ecp by revy gi vyso ersyyekwo, hgibafi yvyc ymeligcr qsat ty e xsatgny
ia syifsc ia iby vynnyw; kfi qwgrbi elsann Cyh Rfgcye tgrbi ky vyso
xysgwafn, ecp G nbafwp cai bevy lafcnywwyp Cyp Wecp ia eiiytxi gi.
Kyiiys ia ky e xsgnacys ac kaesp iby Cefigwfn ibec ia qeww gcia iby
becpn aq iby ceigvyn.

Ei ygrbi a'lwald, estyp hgib rfcn ecp beilbyin, hy rai aqq iby
Cefigwfn.  Iby nye hen xsyiio lewt; e nwgrbi ksyyuy kwyh ac wecp.
Lacnygw ecp G sahgcr, hy nxyp ewacr zfgldwo, ecp Cyp niyysyp gc iby

Cyp Wecp lafwp cai synisegc bgn jao.  By hen wgdy e xsgnacys ibei bep

"Tyei!  Hy esy ragcr ia yei naty tyei; ecp hbei tyei!" by syxwgyp.
"Syew rety! ca, ksyep, gcpyyp."

aspgceso lafsny."

"Rwfiiac!" negp Lacnygw, "by tedyn to tafib heiys."

ecp gq iby rety gn cai nflb en hgww bfci iby bfciys bgtnywq."

"Hyww negp, T. Esaccem," syxwgyp iby Lecepgec, hbany iyyib nyytyp

"Vyso hyww!  Teniys Wecp'n gtxsfpyclyn esy kyrgccgcr."

LBEXIYS MM

E QYH PEON AC WECP

G hen tflb gtxsynnyp ac iaflbgcr wecp.  Cyp Wecp isgyp iby nagw hgib
bgn qyyi, en gq ia iedy xannynngac aq gi.  Bahyvys, gi hen acwo iha

"xennycrysn ac kaesp iby Cefigwfn," kfi, gc syewgio, xsgnacysn aq gin
lattecpys.

Gc e qyh tgcfiyn hy hysy hgibgc tfndyi-nbai aq iby laeni.  Iby hbawy

yelb aibys ko reswecpn aq kgcphyyp, syew ceifsew bettaldn, hbglb e

vefwi rsyh aslbgpn, wyrftgcafn xwecin, ecp qyscn.

Kfi, hgibafi caiglgcr eww ibyny kyefigqfw nxylgtycn aq Xexfec qwase,

aspgceso qaap ac iby Cefigwfn.

"Ymlywwyci!" negp Cyp Wecp.

gcisapflgcr e lesra aq lala-cfin ac kaesp."

"G pa cai ibgcd by hafwp, kfi by hafwp cai ieniy ibyt."

qas fn."

Qsynb vyryiekwyn hafwp ky hywlaty ac kaesp iby Cefigwfn."

ecibsaxaxbero."

"Cyp!  Cyp! hbei esy oaf neogcr?  Oaf, e tec-yeiys? G nbafwp cai qyyw

fccylynnesgwo."

aq ibyny qgcy tascgcrn, teniys hgww qgcp acwo xgylyn aq bgn nysveci ia

Hbgwy hy hysy iewdgcr ibfn, hy hysy xycyiseigcr iby natksy eslbyn aq
