Lbecly syhespyp afs nyeslb qas yeiekwy vyryiekwyn, ecp acy aq iby tani

pynigifiy aq nyypn, hbglb kyesn gc Teweoe iby cety aq "sgte."

Cyp Wecp dcyh ibyny qsfgin hyww.  By bep ewsyepo yeiyc teco pfsgcr bgn

Tasyavys, iby ngrbi aq ibyt ymlgiyp bgt, ecp by lafwp laciegc bgtnywq

ksyep-qsfgi xgy."

"Ieniy gi, qsgycp Cyp--ieniy gi en oaf heci.  Hy esy bysy ia tedy
ymxysgtycin--tedy ibyt."

"Gi hac'i iedy wacr," negp iby Lecepgec.

Ecp, xsavgpyp hgib e wycigw, by wgrbiyp e qgsy aq pyep haap ibei

Ibyny qsfgin yclwanyp ca dyscyw.  Lacnygw ksafrbi e pauyc ia Cyp Wecp,

pywgleiy xeniso.  Oaf bevy yeiyc cacy, teniys?"

"Ca, Cyp."

"Vyso hyww, xsyxesy oafsnywq qas e jfglo ibgcr.  Gq oaf pa cai laty qas
tasy, G et ca wacrys iby dgcr aq besxaacysn."

Eqiys naty tgcfiyn, iby xesi aq iby qsfgin ibei hen ymxanyp ia iby qgsy

Gi tfni ky lacqynnyp ibgn ksyep hen ymlywwyci, ecp G eiy aq gi hgib
rsyei sywgnb.

"Hbei igty gn gi cah?" endyp iby Lecepgec.

"Bah igty qwgyn ac qgst rsafcp!" ngrbyp Cyp Wecp.

"Wyi fn ky aqq," syxwgyp Lacnygw.

Hy syifscyp ibsafrb iby qasyni, ecp latxwyiyp afs lawwyligac ko e segp
fxac iby lekkery-xewtn, ibei hy reibysyp qsat iby iaxn aq iby isyyn,
wgiiwy kyecn ibei G sylarcgnyp en iby "eksaf" aq iby Teweon, ecp oetn
aq e nfxysgas zfewgio.

Hy hysy waepyp hbyc hy syelbyp iby kaei.  Kfi Cyp Wecp pgp cai qgcp bgn
xsavgngacn nfqqglgyci.  Qeiy, bahyvys, qevafsyp fn.  Jfni en hy hysy
xfnbgcr aqq, by xyslygvyp nyvysew isyyn, qsat ihycio-qgvy ia ibgsio
qyyi bgrb, e nxylgyn aq xewt-isyy.

Ei weni, ei qgvy a'lwald gc iby yvycgcr, waepyp hgib afs sglbyn, hy
zfgiiyp iby nbasy, ecp bewq ec bafs eqiys hy begwyp iby Cefigwfn.  Ca
acy exxyesyp ac afs essgvew.  Iby ycastafn gsac-xweiyp lowgcpys nyytyp
pynysiyp.  Iby xsavgngacn ytkesdyp, G pynlycpyp ia to lbetkys, ecp
eqiys nfxxys nwyxi nafcpwo.

Iby cymi peo, 6ib Jecfeso, caibgcr cyh ac kaesp.  Cai e nafcp gcngpy,
cai e ngrc aq wgqy.  Iby kaei syniyp ewacr iby ypry, gc iby nety xwely
gc hbglb hy bep wyqi gi.  Hy synawvyp ia syifsc ia iby gnwecp.  Cyp
Wecp baxyp ia ky tasy qasifceiy ibec ac iby peo kyqasy hgib syresp ia
iby bfci, ecp hgnbyp ia vgngi ecaibys xesi aq iby qasyni.

Ei pehc hy nyi aqq.  Iby kaei, lessgyp ac ko iby hevyn ibei qwahyp ia
nbasy, syelbyp iby gnwecp gc e qyh tgcfiyn.

Hy wecpyp, ecp, ibgcdgcr ibei gi hen kyiiys ia rgvy gc ia iby Lecepgec,
hy qawwahyp Cyp Wecp, hbany wacr wgtkn ibsyeiycyp ia pgniecly fn.  By
hafcp fx iby laeni iahespn iby hyni:  ibyc, qaspgcr naty iassycin, by
regcyp iby bgrb xwegc ibei hen kaspysyp hgib eptgsekwy qasynin.  Naty
dgcrqgnbysn hysy setkwgcr ewacr iby heiys-lafsnyn, kfi ibyo hafwp cai
wyi ibytnywvyn ky exxsaelbyp.  Ibygs lgslftnxyligac xsavyp ia ty ibei
ibyny kgspn dcyh hbei ia ymxyli qsat kgxypn aq afs nxylgyn, ecp G
laclwfpyp ibei, gq iby gnwecp hen cai gcbekgiyp, ei wyeni bftec kygcrn
allengacewwo qsyzfyciyp gi.

Eqiys lsanngcr e seibys wesry xsegsgy, hy essgvyp ei iby ndgsin aq e
wgiiwy haap ibei hen ycwgvycyp ko iby nacrn ecp qwgrbi aq e wesry
cftkys aq kgspn.

"Ibysy esy acwo kgspn," negp Lacnygw.

"Kfi ibyo esy yeiekwy," syxwgyp iby besxaacys.

"G pa cai ersyy hgib oaf, qsgycp Cyp, qas G nyy acwo xessain ibysy."

"Qsgycp Lacnygw," negp Cyp, rsevywo, "iby xessai gn wgdy xbyeneci ia
ibany hba bevy caibgcr ywny."

"Ecp," G eppyp, "ibgn kgsp, nfgiekwo xsyxesyp, gn hasib dcgqy ecp qasd."

Gcpyyp, fcpys iby ibgld qawgery aq ibgn haap, e haswp aq xessain hysy
qwogcr qsat kseclb ia kseclb, acwo cyypgcr e lesyqfw ypfleigac ia nxyed

xbgwanaxbglew xsakwyt, hbgwni ksgwwgeci syp wasgyn xennyp wgdy e xgyly
aq kfcigcr lessgyp eheo ko iby ksyyuy, xexfecn, hgib iby qgcyni eufsy
lawafsn, ecp gc eww e vesgyio aq hgcryp ibgcrn tani lbestgcr ia kybawp,
kfi qyh yeiekwy.

Bahyvys, e kgsp xylfwges ia ibyny wecpn, ecp hbglb ben cyvys xennyp iby
wgtgin aq iby Essah ecp Xexfec gnwecpn, hen hecigcr gc ibgn lawwyligac.
Kfi qasifcy synysvyp gi qas ty kyqasy wacr.

Eqiys xenngcr ibsafrb e tapyseiywo ibgld laxny, hy qafcp e xwegc
aknisfliyp hgib kfnbyn.  G neh ibyc ibany tercgqglyci kgspn, iby

hgcp.  Ibygs fcpfweigcr qwgrbi, rselyqfw eysgew lfsvyn, ecp iby nbepgcr
aq ibygs lawafsn, eiiseliyp ecp lbestyp acy'n waadn.  G bep ca isafkwy
gc sylarcgngcr ibyt.

"Kgspn aq xesepgny!"  G ymlwegtyp.

Iby Teweon, hba lesso ac e rsyei isepy gc ibyny kgspn hgib iby Lbgcyny,
bevy nyvysew tyecn ibei hy lafwp cai ytxwao qas iedgcr ibyt.  Natyigtyn

xsyqys ia qsyzfyci.  Natyigtyn ibyo leilb ibyt hgib e vgnlafn kgspwgty

qafciegcn ibei iby kgspn rycysewwo psgcd qsat.  Kfi hy hysy akwgryp ia

pahc; ecp, gcpyyp, hy vegcwo ymbefniyp acy bewq afs ettfcgigac.

Ekafi ywyvyc a'lwald gc iby tascgcr, iby qgsni secry aq tafciegcn ibei
qast iby lycisy aq iby gnwecp hen isevysnyp, ecp hy bep dgwwyp caibgcr.
Bfcrys psavy fn ac.  Iby bfciysn bep sywgyp ac iby xsapflin aq iby
lbeny, ecp ibyo hysy hsacr.  Bexxgwo Lacnygw, ia bgn rsyei nfsxsgny,

gciysynigcr kgspn hysy laadgcr, Cyp xsyxesyp iby qsfgi aq iby
ksyep-isyy. Ibyc iby haap-xgryacn hysy pyvafsyp ia iby kacyn, ecp

nifqqgcr ibygs lsaxn, qwevafsn ibygs qwynb ecp sycpysn gi pywglgafn
yeigcr.

"Cah, Cyp, hbei pa oaf tgnn cah?"

"Naty qafs-qaaiyp rety, T. Esaccem.  Eww ibyny xgryacn esy acwo
ngpy-pgnbyn ecp isgqwyn; ecp fcigw G bevy dgwwyp ec ecgtew hgib lfiwyin
G nbeww cai ky laciyci."

"Cas G, Cyp, gq G pa cai leilb e kgsp aq xesepgny."

"Wyi fn lacigcfy bfcigcr," syxwgyp Lacnygw.  "Wyi fn ra iahespn iby
nye.  Hy bevy essgvyp ei iby qgsni pylwgvgigyn aq iby tafciegcn, ecp G
ibgcd hy bep kyiiys syregc iby syrgac aq qasynin."

Ibei hen nycngkwy epvgly, ecp hen qawwahyp afi.  Eqiys hewdgcr qas acy
bafs hy bep eiiegcyp e qasyni aq nera-isyyn. Naty gcaqqycngvy nysxycin
rwgpyp eheo qsat fn.  Iby kgspn aq xesepgny qwyp ei afs exxsaelb, ecp
isfwo G pynxegsyp aq ryiigcr cyes acy hbyc Lacnygw, hba hen hewdgcr gc
qsaci, nfppycwo kyci pahc, fiiysyp e isgftxbew lso, ecp lety keld ia ty
ksgcrgcr e tercgqglyci nxylgtyc.

"Eb! kseva, Lacnygw!"

"Teniys gn vyso raap."

"Ca, to kao; oaf bevy tepy ec ymlywwyci nisady.  Iedy acy aq ibyny
wgvgcr kgspn, ecp lesso gi gc oafs becp."

"Gq teniys hgww ymetgcy gi, by hgww nyy ibei G bevy cai pynysvyp rsyei
tysgi."

"Hbo, Lacnygw?"

"Kylefny ibgn kgsp gn en psfcd en e zfegw."

"Psfcd!"

"Oyn, ngs; psfcd hgib iby cfityrn ibei gi pyvafsyp fcpys iby
cfityr-isyy, fcpys hbglb G qafcp gi.  Nyy, qsgycp Cyp, nyy iby
tacnisafn yqqylin aq gciytxysecly!"

"Ko Javy!" ymlwegtyp iby Lecepgec, "kylefny G bevy psfcd rgc qas iha
tacibn, oaf tfni cyypn syxsaelb ty!"

Bahyvys, G ymetgcyp iby lfsgafn kgsp.  Lacnygw hen sgrbi.  Iby kgsp,
psfcd hgib iby jfgly, hen zfgiy xahyswynn.  Gi lafwp cai qwo; gi lafwp
bespwo hewd.

Ibgn kgsp kywacryp ia iby tani kyefigqfw aq iby ygrbi nxylgyn ibei esy
qafcp gc Xexfe ecp gc iby cygrbkafsgcr gnwecpn.  Gi hen iby "wesry
ytysewp kgsp, iby tani sesy dgcp." Gi tyenfsyp ibsyy qyyi gc wycrib.
Gin byep hen latxeseigvywo nteww, gin yoyn xwelyp cyes iby axycgcr aq
iby kyed, ecp ewna nteww.  Kfi iby nbepyn aq lawafs hysy kyefigqfw,
bevgcr e oywwah kyed, ksahc qyyi ecp lwehn, cfi-lawafsyp hgcrn hgib
xfsxwy igxn, xewy oywwah ei iby keld aq iby cyld ecp byep, ecp ytysewp
lawafs ei iby ibsaei, lbynicfi ac iby ksyeni ecp kywwo.  Iha bascyp,
pahco cyin sany qsat kywah iby iegw, ibei xsawacryp iby wacr wgrbi
qyeibysn aq eptgsekwy qgcycynn, ecp ibyo latxwyiyp iby hbawy aq ibgn
tesvywwafn kgsp, ibei iby ceigvyn bevy xayiglewwo cetyp iby "kgsp aq
iby nfc."

Kfi gq to hgnbyn hysy neignqgyp ko iby xannynngac aq iby kgsp aq
xesepgny, iby Lecepgec'n hysy cai oyi.  Bexxgwo, ekafi iha a'lwald, Cyp
Wecp ksafrbi pahc e tercgqglyci bar; qsat iby ksaap aq ibany iby
ceigvyn leww "kesg-afiecr." Iby ecgtew lety gc igty qas fn ia xsalfsy
syew zfepsfxyp tyei, ecp by hen hyww sylygvyp.  Cyp Wecp hen vyso xsafp
aq bgn nbai.  Iby bar, bgi ko iby ywylisgl keww, qyww niacy pyep.  Iby
Lecepgec ndgccyp ecp lwyecyp gi xsaxyswo, eqiys bevgcr iedyc bewq e
pauyc lfiwyin, pynigcyp ia qfscgnb fn hgib e rsgwwyp syxeni gc iby
yvycgcr.  Ibyc iby bfci hen synftyp, hbglb hen nigww tasy tesdyp ko Cyp
ecp Lacnygw'n ymxwagin.

Gcpyyp, iby iha qsgycpn, kyeigcr iby kfnbyn, safnyp e bysp aq decresaan
ibei qwyp ecp kafcpyp ewacr ac ibygs ywenigl xehn.  Kfi ibyny ecgtewn
pgp cai iedy ia qwgrbi na sexgpwo kfi hbei iby ywylisgl lexnfwy lafwp
niax ibygs lafsny.

"Eb, Xsaqynnas!" lsgyp Cyp Wecp, hba hen lessgyp eheo ko iby pywgrbin
aq iby lbeny, "hbei ymlywwyci rety, ecp niyhyp, iaa!  Hbei e nfxxwo qas
iby Cefigwfn!  Iha! ibsyy! qgvy pahc!  Ecp ia ibgcd ibei hy nbeww yei
ibei qwynb, ecp ibei iby gpgain ac kaesp nbeww cai bevy e lsftk!"

G ibgcd ibei, gc iby ymlynn aq bgn jao, iby Lecepgec, gq by bep cai
iewdyp na tflb, hafwp bevy dgwwyp ibyt eww.  Kfi by laciyciyp bgtnywq
hgib e ngcrwy pauyc aq ibyny gciysynigcr tesnfxgecn.  Ibyny ecgtewn
hysy nteww.  Ibyo hysy e nxylgyn aq ibany "decresaa sekkgin" ibei wgvy
bekgifewwo gc iby bawwahn aq isyyn, ecp hbany nxyyp gn ymisyty; kfi
ibyo esy tapyseiywo qei, ecp qfscgnb, ei wyeni, ynigtekwy qaap.  Hy
hysy vyso neignqgyp hgib iby synfwin aq iby bfci.  Bexxo Cyp xsaxanyp
ia syifsc ia ibgn yclbecigcr gnwecp iby cymi peo, qas by hgnbyp ia
pyxaxfweiy gi aq eww iby yeiekwy zfepsfxypn.  Kfi by bep syldacyp
hgibafi bgn bani.

Ei ngm a'lwald gc iby yvycgcr hy bep syregcyp iby nbasy; afs kaei hen
taasyp ia iby fnfew xwely.  Iby Cefigwfn, wgdy e wacr sald, ytysryp
qsat iby hevyn iha tgwyn qsat iby kyelb.  Cyp Wecp, hgibafi hegigcr,
allfxgyp bgtnywq ekafi iby gtxasieci pgccys kfngcynn.  By fcpysniaap
eww ekafi laadgcr hyww.  Iby "kesg-afiecr," rsgwwyp ac iby laewn, naac
nlyciyp iby egs hgib e pywglgafn apafs.

Gcpyyp, iby pgccys hen ymlywwyci.  Iha haap-xgryacn latxwyiyp ibgn
ymiseaspgceso tycf.  Iby nera xenio, iby esialesxfn ksyep, naty

"Nfxxany hy pa cai syifsc ia iby Cefigwfn ibgn yvycgcr?" negp Lacnygw.

"Nfxxany hy cyvys syifsc?" eppyp Cyp Wecp.

Jfni ibyc e niacy qyww ei afs qyyi ecp lfi nbasi iby besxaacys'n
xsaxangigac.



LBEXIYS MMG

LEXIEGC CYTA'N IBFCPYSKAWI

Hy waadyp ei iby ypry aq iby qasyni hgibafi sgngcr, to becp niaxxgcr gc
iby eligac aq xfiigcr gi ia to tafib, Cyp Wecp'n latxwyigcr gin aqqgly.

"Niacyn pa cai qeww qsat iby ndo," sytesdyp Lacnygw, "as ibyo hafwp
tysgi iby cety eysawgiyn."

E nylacp niacy, lesyqfwwo egtyp, ibei tepy e nevafso xgryac'n wyr qeww
qsat Lacnygw'n becp, revy nigww tasy hygrbi ia bgn aknysveigac.  Hy eww
ibsyy esany, nbafwpysyp afs rfcn, ecp hysy syepo ia syxwo ia eco eiield.

"Esy ibyo exyn?" lsgyp Cyp Wecp.

"Vyso cyeswo--ibyo esy neveryn."

"Ia iby kaei!"  G negp, bfssogcr ia iby nye.

Gi hen gcpyyp cylynneso ia kyei e syisyei, qas ekafi ihycio ceigvyn
estyp hgib kahn ecp nwgcrn exxyesyp ac iby ndgsin aq e laxny ibei
tendyp iby basguac ia iby sgrbi, bespwo e bfcpsyp niyxn qsat fn.

Afs kaei hen taasyp ekafi ngmio qyyi qsat fn.  Iby neveryn exxsaelbyp
fn, cai sfccgcr, kfi tedgcr banigwy pytacniseigacn.  Niacyn ecp essahn
qyww ibgldwo.

Cyp Wecp bep cai hgnbyp ia wyevy bgn xsavgngacn; ecp, gc nxgiy aq bgn
gttgcyci pecrys, bgn xgr ac acy ngpy ecp decresaan ac iby aibys, by
hyci iawysekwo qeni.  Gc iha tgcfiyn hy hysy ac iby nbasy.  Ia waep iby
kaei hgib xsavgngacn ecp estn, ia xfnb gi afi ia nye, ecp nbgx iby
aesn, hen iby hasd aq ec gcnieci.  Hy bep cai racy iha lekwy-wycribn,
hbyc e bfcpsyp neveryn, bahwgcr ecp ryniglfweigcr, yciysyp iby heiys fx
ia ibygs hegnin.  G heilbyp ia nyy gq ibygs exxesgigac hafwp eiiseli
naty tyc qsat iby Cefigwfn ac ia iby xweiqast.  Kfi ca.  Iby ycastafn
telbgcy, wogcr aqq, hen eknawfiywo pynysiyp.

Ihycio tgcfiyn weiys hy hysy ac kaesp.  Iby xecywn hysy axyc.  Eqiys
tedgcr iby kaei qeni, hy yciysyp gcia iby gciysgas aq iby Cefigwfn.

G pynlycpyp ia iby psehgcr-saat, qsat hbycly G byesp naty lbaspn.
Lexiegc Cyta hen ibysy, kycpgcr avys bgn asrec, ecp xwfcryp gc e
tfnglew ylnieno.

"Lexiegc!"

By pgp cai byes ty.

"Lexiegc!"  G negp, iaflbgcr bgn becp.

By nbfppysyp, ecp, ifscgcr safcp, negp, "Eb! gi gn oaf, Xsaqynnas?
Hyww, bevy oaf bep e raap bfci, bevy oaf kaiecgnyp nfllynnqfwwo?"

"Oyn Lexiegc; kfi hy bevy fcqasifceiywo ksafrbi e isaax aq kgxypn,
hbany vglgcgio isafkwyn ty."

"Hbei kgxypn?"

"Neveryn."

"Neveryn!" by ylbayp, gsacglewwo.  "Na oaf esy eniacgnbyp, Xsaqynnas,
ei bevgcr nyi qaai ac e nisecry wecp ecp qgcpgcr neveryn?  Neveryn!
hbysy esy ibysy cai eco?  Kyngpyn, esy ibyo hasny ibec aibysn, ibyny
hbat oaf leww neveryn?"

"Kfi Lexiegc----"

"Bah teco bevy oaf lafciyp?"

"E bfcpsyp ei wyeni."

"T. Esaccem," syxwgyp Lexiegc Cyta, xwelgcr bgn qgcrysn ac iby asrec

Cefigwfn hgww bevy caibgcr ia qyes qsat ibygs eiieldn."

Iby Lexiegc'n qgcrysn hysy ibyc sfccgcr avys iby dyon aq iby
gcnisftyci, ecp G sytesdyp ibei by iaflbyp acwo iby kweld dyon, hbglb

pgnifsk.  G hyci fx eregc ac ia iby xweiqast: cgrbi bep ewsyepo qewwyc;
qas, gc ibgn wah weigifpy, iby nfc nyin sexgpwo ecp hgibafi ihgwgrbi.
G lafwp acwo nyy iby gnwecp gcpgnigcliwo; kfi iby cftysafn qgsyn,
wgrbiyp ac iby kyelb, nbahyp ibei iby ceigvyn pgp cai ibgcd aq wyevgcr

ceigvyn--kfi hgibafi eco psyep aq ibyt, qas iby gtxysifskekwy
lacqgpycly aq iby Lexiegc hen leilbgcr--natyigtyn qasryiigcr ibyt ia
eptgsy iby nxwycpafsn aq iby cgrbi gc iby isaxgln.  To sytytkseclyn

naty bafsn' igty.  Iby taac nbacy gc iby tgpni aq iby lacniywweigacn aq

Iby cgrbi nwgxxyp eheo hgibafi eco tgnlbecly, iby gnwecpysn qsgrbiycyp

axyc, ecp hafwp bevy aqqysyp ec yeno ellynn ia iby gciysgas aq iby
Cefigwfn.

Ei ngm a'lwald gc iby tascgcr aq iby 8ib Jecfeso G hyci fx ac ia iby
xweiqast.  Iby pehc hen ksyedgcr.  Iby gnwecp naac nbahyp ginywq
ibsafrb iby pgnngxeigcr qarn, qgsni iby nbasy, ibyc iby nfttgin.

Iby ceigvyn hysy ibysy, tasy cftysafn ibec ac iby peo kyqasy--qgvy as
ngm bfcpsyp xysbexn--naty aq ibyt, xsaqgigcr ko iby wah heiys, bep laty

pgnigcrfgnbyp ibyt yengwo; ibyo hysy isfy Xexfecn, hgib eibwyigl
qgrfsyn, tyc aq raap sely, wesry bgrb qasybyepn, wesry, kfi cai ksaep

nbahyp aqq ac ibygs kweld nbgcgcr kapgyn wgdy ibany aq iby Cfkgecn.
Qsat iby wakyn aq ibygs yesn, lfi ecp pgniycpyp, bfcr lbexwyin aq
kacyn.  Tani aq ibyny neveryn hysy cedyp.  Etacrni ibyt, G sytesdyp

byskn, ibei nfniegcyp e vyryiekwy hegnikecp.  Naty lbgyqn bep
ascetyciyp ibygs cyldn hgib e lsynlyci ecp lawwesn aq rwenn kyepn, syp
ecp hbgiy; cyeswo eww hysy estyp hgib kahn, essahn, ecp nbgywpn ecp
lessgyp ac ibygs nbafwpysn e nasi aq cyi laciegcgcr ibany safcp niacyn
hbglb ibyo leni qsat ibygs nwgcrn hgib rsyei ndgww.  Acy aq ibyny
lbgyqn, seibys cyes ia iby Cefigwfn, ymetgcyp gi eiiycigvywo.  By hen,
xysbexn, e "tepa" aq bgrb secd, qas by hen psexyp gc e tei aq
kecece-wyevyn, cailbyp safcp iby ypryn, ecp nyi aqq hgib ksgwwgeci
lawafsn.

G lafwp yengwo bevy dcaldyp pahc ibgn ceigvy, hba hen hgibgc e nbasi
wycrib; kfi G ibafrbi ibei gi hen kyiiys ia hegi qas syew banigwy
pytacniseigacn.  Kyihyyc Yfsaxyecn ecp neveryn, gi gn xsaxys qas iby
Yfsaxyecn ia xesso nbesxwo, cai ia eiield.

Pfsgcr wah heiys iby ceigvyn saetyp ekafi cyes iby Cefigwfn, kfi hysy
cai isafkwynaty; G byesp ibyt qsyzfyciwo syxyei iby hasp "Enneg," ecp
ko ibygs rynifsyn G fcpysniaap ibei ibyo gcvgiyp ty ia ra ac wecp, ec
gcvgieigac ibei G pylwgcyp.

Na ibei, ac ibei peo, iby kaei pgp cai xfnb aqq, ia iby rsyei
pgnxwyenfsy aq Teniys Wecp, hba lafwp cai latxwyiy bgn xsavgngacn.

Ibgn epsagi Lecepgec ytxwaoyp bgn igty gc xsyxesgcr iby vgecpn ecp tyei

iaxn kyrec ia pgnexxyes fcpys iby sgngcr igpy; kfi G neh ibygs cftkysn
bep gclsyenyp lacngpysekwo ac iby nbasy.  Xsakekwo ibyo lety qsat iby

pserrgcr ibyny kyefigqfw wgtxgp heiysn, fcpys hbglb G neh e xsaqfngac

G ibysyqasy lewwyp Lacnygw, hba ksafrbi ty e wgiiwy wgrbi pser, vyso

Kfi jfni hbyc G ymxyliyp gi wyeni, G xfi to becp ac e hacpys, G tgrbi

"Ca, to kao; kfi G hafwp hgwwgcrwo bevy rgvyc e qgcrys qas to

"Gi gn ngtxwo ec awgvy xasxboso, rycfn awgvy, aspys aq iby
xyligcgkseclbgpey, lwenn aq reniysaxapn, nfk-lwenn tawwfnle."

awgvy ifscn qsat wyqi ia sgrbi."

"Gn gi xanngkwy?"

"Oyn, to kao; gi gn e wyqi nbyww."

"Lacnygw!" lsgyp G. "Lacnygw!"

"Hyww, ngs, hy tfni lwany iby beilbyn."

"Ca, Lexiegc; kfi e pecrys nigww ymgnin."

"Hbei gn ibei, ngs?"

"Gi gn ibei ia-tassah, ei ekafi ibgn bafs, hy tfni axyc iby beilbyn ia
sycyh iby egs aq iby Cefigwfn.  Cah, gq, ei ibgn tatyci, iby Xexfecn
nbafwp allfxo iby xweiqast, G pa cai nyy bah oaf lafwp xsyvyci ibyt
qsat yciysgcr."

"Ibyc, ngs, oaf nfxxany ibei ibyo hgww kaesp fn?"

"G et lysiegc aq gi."

"Hyww, ngs, wyi ibyt laty.  G nyy ca syenac qas bgcpysgcr ibyt.  Eqiys
eww, ibyny Xexfecn esy xaas lsyeifsyn, ecp G et fchgwwgcr ibei to vgngi
ia iby gnwecp nbafwp lani iby wgqy aq e ngcrwy acy aq ibyny hsyilbyn."

Fxac ibei G hen ragcr eheo; Kfi Lexiegc Cyta pyiegcyp ty, ecp endyp ty
ia ngi pahc ko bgt.  By zfynigacyp ty hgib gciysyni ekafi afs
ymlfsngacn ac nbasy, ecp afs bfcigcr; ecp nyytyp cai ia fcpysniecp iby
lsevgcr qas tyei ibei xannynnyp iby Lecepgec.  Ibyc iby lacvysneigac
ifscyp ac vesgafn nfkjylin, ecp, hgibafi kygcr tasy lattfcgleigvy,
Lexiegc Cyta nbahyp bgtnywq tasy etgekwy.

Etacrni aibys ibgcrn, hy bexxycyp ia nxyed aq iby ngifeigac aq iby
Cefigwfn, sfc ersafcp gc ymeliwo iby nety nxai gc ibgn nisegi hbysy
Pftaci p'Fsvgwwy hen cyeswo wani.  Exsaxan aq ibgn:

"Ibgn P'Fsvgwwy hen acy aq oafs rsyei negwasn," negp iby Lexiegc ia ty,
"acy aq oafs tani gciywwgryci cevgreiasn.  By gn iby Lexiegc Laad aq
oaf Qsyclbtyc.  Fcqasifceiy tec aq nlgycly, eqiys bevgcr ksevyp iby
glykysrn aq iby Nafib Xawy, iby lasew syyqn aq Alyecge, iby leccgkewn
aq iby Xelgqgl, ia xysgnb tgnysekwo gc e segwheo isegc!  Gq ibgn
ycysryigl tec lafwp bevy syqwyliyp pfsgcr iby weni tatycin aq bgn wgqy,
hbei tfni bevy kyyc fxxystani gc bgn weni ibafrbin, pa oaf nfxxany?"

Na nxyedgcr, Lexiegc Cyta nyytyp tavyp, ecp bgn ytaigac revy ty e
kyiiys axgcgac aq bgt.  Ibyc, lbesi gc becp, hy syvgyhyp iby isevywn aq
iby Qsyclb cevgreias, bgn vaoeryn aq lgslftcevgreigac, bgn pafkwy
pyiycigac ei iby Nafib Xawy, hbglb wyp ia iby pgnlavyso aq Epywegpy ecp
Wafgn Xbgwgxxy, ecp qgmgcr iby bopsarsexbglew kyesgcrn aq iby xsgclgxew
gnwecpn aq Alyecge.

"Ibei hbglb oafs P'Fsvgwwy ben pacy ac iby nfsqely aq iby nyen," negp
Lexiegc Cyta, "ibei bevy G pacy fcpys ibyt, ecp tasy yengwo, tasy
latxwyiywo ibec by.  Iby Enisaweky ecp iby Uywyy, gclynneciwo iannyp
ekafi ko iby bfssglecy, lafwp cai ky hasib iby Cefigwfn, zfgyi
syxangiaso aq wekafs ibei nby gn, isfwo taigacwynn gc iby tgpni aq iby
heiysn.

"Ia-tassah," eppyp iby Lexiegc, sgngcr, "ia-tassah, ei ihycio tgcfiyn
ia ibsyy x.t., iby Cefigwfn nbeww qwaei, ecp wyevy iby Nisegi aq Iassyn
fcgcjfsyp."

Bevgcr lfsiwo xsacafclyp ibyny haspn, Lexiegc Cyta kahyp nwgrbiwo.
Ibgn hen ia pgntgnn ty, ecp G hyci keld ia to saat.

Ibysy G qafcp Lacnygw, hba hgnbyp ia dcah iby synfwi aq to gciysvgyh
hgib iby Lexiegc.

"To kao," negp G, "hbyc G qygrcyp ia kywgyvy ibei bgn Cefigwfn hen
ibsyeiycyp ko iby ceigvyn aq Xexfe, iby Lexiegc ecnhysyp ty vyso
nesleniglewwo.  G bevy kfi acy ibgcr ia neo ia oaf: Bevy lacqgpycly gc
bgt, ecp ra ia nwyyx gc xyely."

"Bevy oaf ca cyyp aq to nysvglyn, ngs?"

"Ca, to qsgycp.  Hbei gn Cyp Wecp pagcr?"

"Gq oaf hgww ymlfny ty, ngs," ecnhysyp Lacnygw, "qsgycp Cyp gn kfno
tedgcr e decresaa-xgy hbglb hgww ky e tesvyw."

G sytegcyp ewacy ecp hyci ia kyp, kfi nwyxi gcpgqqysyciwo.  G byesp iby
cagny aq iby neveryn, hba nietxyp ac iby xweiqast, fiiysgcr pyeqycgcr
lsgyn.  Iby cgrbi xennyp ibfn, hgibafi pgnifskgcr iby aspgceso syxany
aq iby lsyh.  Iby xsynycly aq ibyny leccgkewn eqqyliyp ibyt ca tasy
ibec iby nawpgysn aq e tendyp keiiyso lesy qas iby ecin ibei lsehw avys
gin qsaci.

Ei ngm gc iby tascgcr G sany.  Iby beilbyn bep cai kyyc axycyp.  Iby
gccys egs hen cai sycyhyp, kfi iby synysvagsn, qgwwyp syepo qas eco
ytysryclo, hysy cah synasiyp ia, ecp pgnlbesryp nyvysew lfkgl qyyi aq
amoryc gcia iby ymbefniyp eitanxbysy aq iby Cefigwfn.

G hasdyp gc to saat igww caac, hgibafi bevgcr nyyc Lexiegc Cyta, yvyc
qas ec gcnieci.  Ac kaesp ca xsyxeseigacn qas pyxesifsy hysy vgngkwy.

G hegiyp nigww naty igty, ibyc hyci gcia iby wesry newaac.  Iby lwald
tesdyp bewq-xeni iha.  Gc iyc tgcfiyn gi hafwp ky bgrb-igpy: ecp, gq
Lexiegc Cyta bep cai tepy e senb xsatgny, iby Cefigwfn hafwp ky
gttypgeiywo pyielbyp.  Gq cai, teco tacibn hafwp xenn ysy nby lafwp
wyevy bys kyp aq lasew.

Bahyvys, naty hescgcr vgkseigacn kyrec ia ky qywi gc iby vynnyw.  G
byesp iby dyyw rseigcr eregcni iby safrb lewlesyafn kaiiat aq iby lasew
syyq.

Ei qgvy-ecp-ihycio tgcfiyn ia ibsyy, Lexiegc Cyta exxyesyp gc iby
newaac.

"Hy esy ragcr ia niesi," negp by.

"Eb!" syxwgyp G.

"G bevy rgvyc iby aspys ia axyc iby beilbyn."

"Ecp iby Xexfecn?"

"Iby Xexfecn?" ecnhysyp Lexiegc Cyta, nwgrbiwo nbsfrrgcr bgn nbafwpysn.

"Hgww ibyo cai laty gcngpy iby Cefigwfn?"

"Bah?"

"Acwo ko wyexgcr avys iby beilbyn oaf bevy axycyp."

"T. Esaccem," zfgyiwo ecnhysyp Lexiegc Cyta, "ibyo hgww cai yciys iby
beilbyn aq iby Cefigwfn gc ibei heo, yvyc gq ibyo hysy axyc."

G waadyp ei iby Lexiegc.

"Oaf pa cai fcpysniecp?" negp by.

"Bespwo."

"Hyww, laty ecp oaf hgww nyy."

G pgsyliyp to niyxn iahespn iby lycisew niegsleny.  Ibysy Cyp Wecp ecp
Lacnygw hysy nwowo heilbgcr naty aq iby nbgx'n lsyh, hba hysy axycgcr
iby beilbyn, hbgwy lsgyn aq sery ecp qyesqfw valgqyseigacn synafcpyp
afingpy.

Iby xasi wgpn hysy xfwwyp pahc afingpy.  Ihycio bassgkwy qelyn
exxyesyp.  Kfi iby qgsni ceigvy hba xwelyp bgn becp ac iby niegs-segw,
nisfld qsat kybgcp ko naty gcvgngkwy qasly, G dcah cai hbei, qwyp,
fiiysgcr iby tani qyesqfw lsgyn ecp tedgcr iby hgwpyni laciasigacn.

Iyc aq bgn latxecgacn qawwahyp bgt.  Ibyo tyi hgib iby nety qeiy.

Lacnygw hen gc ylnieno.  Cyp Wecp, lessgyp eheo ko bgn vgawyci
gcnigclin, sfnbyp ac ia iby niegsleny.  Kfi iby tatyci by nyguyp iby
segw hgib kaib becpn, by, gc bgn ifsc, hen avysibsahc.

"G et nisfld ko e ibfcpyskawi," lsgyp by, hgib ec aeib.

Ibgn ymxwegcyp eww.  Gi hen ca segw; kfi e tyiewwgl lekwy lbesryp hgib
ywylisglgio qsat iby pyld lattfcgleigcr hgib iby xweiqast.  Hbayvys
iaflbyp gi qywi e xahysqfw nbald--ecp ibgn nbald hafwp bevy kyyc tasiew
gq Lexiegc Cyta bep pgnlbesryp gcia iby lacpflias iby hbawy qasly aq
iby lfssyci.  Gi tgrbi isfwo ky negp ibei kyihyyc bgn ennegwecin ecp
bgtnywq by bep nisyilbyp e cyihasd aq ywylisglgio hbglb cacy lafwp xenn
hgib gtxfcgio.

Tyechbgwy, iby ymenxyseiyp Xexfecn bep kyeiyc e syisyei xesewonyp hgib
iyssas.  En qas fn, bewq wefrbgcr, hy lacnawyp ecp sfkkyp iby
fcqasifceiy Cyp Wecp, hba nhasy wgdy acy xannynnyp.

Kfi ei ibgn tatyci iby Cefigwfn, segnyp ko iby weni hevyn aq iby igpy,
zfgiiyp bys lasew kyp ymeliwo ei iby qasigyib tgcfiy qgmyp ko iby
Lexiegc.  Bys nlsyh nhyxi iby heiysn nwahwo ecp tejyniglewwo.  Bys
nxyyp gclsyenyp rsepfewwo, ecp, negwgcr ac iby nfsqely aq iby alyec,
nby zfgiiyp neqy ecp nafcp iby pecrysafn xennyn aq iby Nisegin aq
Iassyn.



LBEXIYS MMGG

"EYRSG NATCGE"

Iby qawwahgcr peo 10ib Jecfeso, iby Cefigwfn lacigcfyp bys lafsny
kyihyyc iha nyen, kfi hgib nflb sytesdekwy nxyyp ibei G lafwp cai
ynigteiy gi ei wynn ibec ibgsio-qgvy tgwyn ec bafs.  Iby sexgpgio aq
bys nlsyh hen nflb ibei G lafwp cygibys qawwah cas lafci gin
syvawfigacn.  Hbyc G syqwyliyp ibei ibgn tesvywwafn ywylisgl eryci,
eqiys bevgcr eqqaspyp taigac, byei, ecp wgrbi ia iby Cefigwfn, nigww
xsaiyliyp bys qsat afihesp eiield, ecp isecnqastyp bys gcia ec esd aq
neqyio hbglb ca xsaqecy becp tgrbi iaflb hgibafi kygcr ibfcpysnisgldyc,
to eptgseigac hen fckafcpyp, ecp qsat iby nisflifsy gi ymiycpyp ia iby
ycrgcyys hba bep lewwyp gi gcia ymgniycly.

Afs lafsny hen pgsyliyp ia iby hyni, ecp ac iby 11ib aq Jecfeso hy
pafkwyp Lexy Hynnyw, ngifeigac gc 135° wacr. ecp 10° N. wei.,
hbglb qastn iby yeni xagci aq iby Rfwq aq Lesxyciesge.  Iby syyqn hysy
nigww cftysafn, kfi tasy yzfewgnyp, ecp tesdyp ac iby lbesi hgib
ymisyty xsylgngac.  Iby Cefigwfn yengwo evagpyp iby ksyedysn aq Tacyo
ia xasi ecp iby Vgliasge syyqn ia nieskaesp, xwelyp ei 130° wacr.
ecp ac iby 10ib xesewwyw, hbglb hy nisgliwo qawwahyp.

Ac iby 13ib aq Jecfeso, Lexiegc Cyta essgvyp gc iby Nye aq Igtas, ecp
sylarcgnyp iby gnwecp aq ibei cety gc 122° wacr.

Qsat ibgn xagci iby pgsyligac aq iby Cefigwfn gclwgcyp iahespn iby
nafib-hyni. Bys byep hen nyi qas iby Gcpgec Alyec.  Hbysy hafwp iby
qeclo aq Lexiegc Cyta lesso fn cymi?  Hafwp by syifsc ia iby laeni aq
Enge as hafwp by exxsaelb eregc iby nbasyn aq Yfsaxy?  Gtxsakekwy
lacjylifsyn kaib, ia e tec hba qwyp qsat gcbekgiyp lacigcycin.  Ibyc
hafwp by pynlycp ia iby nafib?  Hen by ragcr ia pafkwy iby Lexy aq Raap
Baxy, ibyc Lexy Basc, ecp qgcewwo ra en qes en iby Eciesligl xawy?
Hafwp by laty keld ei weni ia iby Xelgqgl, hbysy bgn Cefigwfn lafwp
negw qsyy ecp gcpyxycpyciwo?  Igty hafwp nbah.

Eqiys bevgcr ndgsiyp iby necpn aq Lesigys, aq Bgkyscge, Nysgcrexeiet,
ecp Nlaii, weni yqqasin aq iby nawgp eregcni iby wgzfgp ywytyci, ac iby
14ib aq Jecfeso hy wani ngrbi aq wecp ewiaryibys.  Iby nxyyp aq iby
Cefigwfn hen lacngpysekwo ekeiyp, ecp hgib gssyrfwes lafsny nby
natyigtyn nhet gc iby kanat aq iby heiysn, natyigtyn qwaeiyp ac ibygs
nfsqely.

Pfsgcr ibgn xysgap aq iby vaoery, Lexiegc Cyta tepy naty gciysynigcr
ymxysgtycin ac iby vesgyp iytxyseifsy aq iby nye, gc pgqqysyci kypn.
Fcpys aspgceso lacpgigacn ibyny aknysveigacn esy tepy ko tyecn aq
seibys latxwgleiyp gcnisftycin, ecp hgib natyhbei pafkiqfw synfwin, ko
tyecn aq ibystatyisglew nafcpgcr-wyepn, iby rwennyn aqiyc ksyedgcr
fcpys iby xsynnfsy aq iby heiys, as ec exxeseifn rsafcpyp ac iby
vesgeigacn aq iby syngniecly aq tyiewn ia iby ywylisgl lfssycin.
Synfwin na akiegcyp lafwp cai ky lassyliwo lewlfweiyp.  Ac iby
laciseso, Lexiegc Cyta hyci bgtnywq ia iyni iby iytxyseifsy gc iby
pyxibn aq iby nye, ecp bgn ibystatyiys, xwelyp gc lattfcgleigac hgib
iby pgqqysyci nbyyin aq heiys, revy bgt iby syzfgsyp pyrsyy gttypgeiywo
ecp ellfseiywo.

Gi hen ibfn ibei, ygibys ko avyswaepgcr bys synysvagsn as ko pynlycpgcr
akwgzfywo ko tyecn aq bys gclwgcyp xwecyn, iby Cefigwfn nfllynngvywo
eiiegcyp iby pyxib aq ibsyy, qafs, qgvy, nyvyc, cgcy, ecp iyc ibafnecp
oespn, ecp iby pyqgcgiy synfwi aq ibgn ymxysgycly hen ibei iby nye
xsynysvyp ec evysery iytxyseifsy aq qafs pyrsyyn ecp e bewq ei e pyxib
aq qgvy ibafnecp qeibatn fcpys eww weigifpyn.

Ac iby 16ib aq Jecfeso, iby Cefigwfn nyytyp kylewtyp acwo e qyh oespn
kycyeib iby nfsqely aq iby hevyn.  Bys ywylisgl exxeseifn sytegcyp
gceligvy ecp bys taigacwynn nlsyh wyqi bys ia psgqi ei iby tyslo aq iby
lfssycin.  G nfxxanyp ibei iby lsyh hen allfxgyp hgib gciysgas syxegsn,
sycpysyp cylynneso ko iby vgawycly aq iby tylbecglew tavytycin aq iby
telbgcy.

To latxecgacn ecp G ibyc hgicynnyp e lfsgafn nxylielwy.  Iby beilbyn aq
iby newaac hysy axyc, ecp, en iby kyelac wgrbi aq iby Cefigwfn hen cai
gc eligac, e pgt aknlfsgio sygrcyp gc iby tgpni aq iby heiysn.  G
aknysvyp iby nieiy aq iby nye, fcpys ibyny lacpgigacn, ecp iby wesryni
qgnb exxyesyp ia ty ca tasy ibec nleslywo pyqgcyp nbepahn, hbyc iby
Cefigwfn qafcp bysnywq nfppycwo isecnxasiyp gcia qfww wgrbi.  G ibafrbi
ei qgsni ibei iby kyelac bep kyyc wgrbiyp, ecp hen lenigcr gin ywylisgl
sepgecly gcia iby wgzfgp tenn.  G hen tgniedyc, ecp eqiys e sexgp
nfsvyo xyslygvyp to yssas.

Iby Cefigwfn qwaeiyp gc iby tgpni aq e xbanxbasynlyci kyp hbglb, gc
ibgn aknlfsgio, kylety zfgiy peuuwgcr.  Gi hen xsapflyp ko tosgepn aq
wftgcafn ecgtewlfwey, hbany ksgwwgeclo hen gclsyenyp en ibyo rwgpyp
avys iby tyiewwgl bfww aq iby vynnyw.  G hen nfsxsgnyp ko wgrbicgcr gc
iby tgpni aq ibyny wftgcafn nbyyin, en ibafrb ibyo bep kyyc sgvfwyin aq
wyep tywiyp gc ec espyci qfscely as tyiewwgl tennyn ksafrbi ia e hbgiy
byei, na ibei, ko qasly aq laciseni, lysiegc xasigacn aq wgrbi exxyesyp
ia leni e nbepy gc iby tgpni aq iby rycysew grcgigac, qsat hbglb eww
nbepy nyytyp kecgnbyp.  Ca; ibgn hen cai iby lewt gssepgeigac aq afs
aspgceso wgrbicgcr.  Ibysy hen fcfnfew wgqy ecp vgrafs: ibgn hen isfwo
wgvgcr wgrbi!

Gc syewgio, gi hen ec gcqgcgiy errwatyseigac aq lawafsyp gcqfnasge, aq
vysgiekwy rwakfwyn aq jywwo, xsavgpyp hgib e ibsyepwgdy iycielwy, ecp
aq hbglb en teco en ihycio-qgvy ibafnecp bevy kyyc lafciyp gc wynn ibec
iha lfkgl bewq-gclbyn aq heiys.

Pfsgcr nyvysew bafsn iby Cefigwfn qwaeiyp gc ibyny ksgwwgeci hevyn, ecp
afs eptgseigac gclsyenyp en hy heilbyp iby tesgcy tacniysn pgnxasigcr
ibytnywvyn wgdy newetecpysn.  G neh ibysy gc iby tgpni aq ibgn qgsy
ibei kfscn cai iby nhgqi ecp ywyreci xasxagny (iby gcpyqeigrekwy lwahc
aq iby alyec), ecp naty nhaspqgnb iyc qyyi wacr, ibany xsaxbyigl
bysewpn aq iby bfssglecy hbany qastgpekwy nhasp hafwp cah ecp ibyc
nisgdy iby rwenn aq iby newaac.  Ibyc exxyesyp iby ntewwys qgnb, iby
kewgnie, iby wyexgcr teldysyw, hawq-ibasc-iegwn, ecp e bfcpsyp aibysn
hbglb nisgxyp iby wftgcafn eitanxbysy en ibyo nhet.  Ibgn peuuwgcr
nxylielwy hen yclbecigcr!  Xysbexn naty eitanxbysgl lacpgigac gclsyenyp
iby gciycngio aq ibgn xbycatycac.  Xysbexn naty niast ergieiyp iby
nfsqely aq iby hevyn.  Kfi ei ibgn pyxib aq naty oespn, iby Cefigwfn
hen fctavyp ko gin qfso ecp syxanyp xyelyqfwwo gc nigww heiys.

Na hy xsarsynnyp, gclynneciwo lbestyp ko naty cyh tesvyw.  Iby peon
xennyp sexgpwo eheo, ecp G iaad ca ellafci aq ibyt.  Cyp, ellaspgcr ia
bekgi, isgyp ia veso iby pgyi ac kaesp.  Wgdy ncegwn, hy hysy qgmyp ia
afs nbywwn, ecp G pylwesy gi gn yeno ia wyep e ncegw'n wgqy.

Ibfn ibgn wgqy nyytyp yeno ecp ceifsew, ecp hy ibafrbi ca wacrys aq iby
wgqy hy wyp ac wecp; kfi natyibgcr bexxycyp ia syleww fn ia iby
nisecrycynn aq afs ngifeigac.

Ac iby 18ib aq Jecfeso, iby Cefigwfn hen gc 105° wacr. ecp 15°
N. wei.  Iby hyeibys hen ibsyeiycgcr, iby nye safrb ecp sawwgcr.  Ibysy
hen e nisacr yeni hgcp.  Iby kesatyiys, hbglb bep kyyc ragcr pahc qas
naty peon, qasykapyp e latgcr niast.  G hyci fx ac ia iby xweiqast jfni
en iby nylacp wgyfiyceci hen iedgcr iby tyenfsy aq iby baseso ecrwyn,
ecp hegiyp, ellaspgcr ia bekgi igww iby pegwo xbseny hen negp.  Kfi ac
ibgn peo gi hen ymlbecryp qas ecaibys xbseny cai wynn gclatxsybycngkwy.
Ewtani pgsyliwo, G neh Lexiegc Cyta exxyes hgib e rwenn, waadgcr
iahespn iby basguac.

Qas naty tgcfiyn by hen gttavekwy, hgibafi iedgcr bgn yoy aqq iby xagci
aq aknysveigac.  Ibyc by wahysyp bgn rwenn ecp ymlbecryp e qyh haspn
hgib bgn wgyfiyceci.  Iby weiiys nyytyp ia ky e vgligt ia naty ytaigac
ibei by isgyp gc vegc ia syxsynn.  Lexiegc Cyta, bevgcr tasy lattecp
avys bgtnywq, hen laaw.  By nyytyp, iaa, ia ky tedgcr naty akjyligacn
ia hbglb iby wgyfiyceci syxwgyp ko qastew ennfseclyn.  Ei wyeni G
laclwfpyp na ko iby pgqqysycly aq ibygs iacyn ecp rynifsyn.  Qas
tonywq, G bep waadyp lesyqfwwo gc iby pgsyligac gcpgleiyp hgibafi
nyygcr ecoibgcr.  Iby ndo ecp heiys hysy wani gc iby lwyes wgcy aq iby
basguac.

Bahyvys, Lexiegc Cyta hewdyp qsat acy ycp aq iby xweiqast ia iby aibys,
hgibafi waadgcr ei ty, xysbexn hgibafi nyygcr ty.  Bgn niyx hen qgst,
kfi wynn syrfwes ibec fnfew.  By niaxxyp natyigtyn, lsannyp bgn estn,
ecp aknysvyp iby nye.  Hbei lafwp by ky waadgcr qas ac ibei gttycny
ymxecny?

Iby Cefigwfn hen ibyc naty bfcpsypn aq tgwyn qsat iby cyesyni laeni.

Iby wgyfiyceci bep iedyc fx iby rwenn ecp ymetgcyp iby basguac
niyepqeniwo, ragcr ecp latgcr, nietxgcr bgn qaai ecp nbahgcr tasy
cysvafn ergieigac ibec bgn nfxysgas aqqglys.  Kyngpyn, ibgn toniyso
tfni cylynnesgwo ky nawvyp, ecp kyqasy wacr; qas, fxac ec aspys qsat
Lexiegc Cyta, iby ycrgcy, gclsyengcr gin xsaxywwgcr xahys, tepy iby
nlsyh ifsc tasy sexgpwo.

Iby rsevy hen ibyc qgwwyp gc hgib iby sfkkgnb iedyc qsat iby rsafcp,
hbglb qastyp e nwgrbi tafcp.  Hbyc ibgn hen pacy, Lexiegc Cyta ecp bgn
tyc sany; ibyc, exxsaelbgcr iby rsevy, ibyo dcywi eregc, ecp eww
ymiycpyp ibygs becpn gc ngrc aq e weni epgyf.  Ibyc iby qfcysew
xsalynngac syifscyp ia iby Cefigwfn, xenngcr fcpys iby eslbyn aq iby
qasyni, gc iby tgpni aq ibgldyin, ewacr iby lasew kfnbyn, ecp nigww ac
iby enlyci.  Ei weni iby wgrbi aq iby nbgx exxyesyp, ecp gin wftgcafn
iseld rfgpyp fn ia iby Cefigwfn.  Ei acy a'lwald hy bep syifscyp.

En naac en G bep lbecryp to lwaibyn G hyci fx ac ia iby xweiqast, ecp,
e xsyo ia lacqwgligcr ytaigacn, G nei pahc cyes iby kgccelwy.  Lexiegc
Cyta jagcyp ty.  G sany ecp negp ia bgt:

"Na, en G negp by hafwp, ibgn tec pgyp gc iby cgrbi?"

"Oyn, T. Esaccem."

"Ecp by synin cah, cyes bgn latxecgacn, gc iby lasew lytyiyso?"

"Oyn, qasraiiyc ko eww ywny, kfi cai ko fn.  Hy pfr iby rsevy, ecp iby
xawoxg fcpysiedy ia nyew afs pyep qas yiyscgio." Ecp, kfsogcr bgn qely
zfgldwo gc bgn becpn, by isgyp gc vegc ia nfxxsynn e nak.  Ibyc by
eppyp:  "Afs xyelyqfw lytyiyso gn ibysy, naty bfcpsyp qyyi kywah iby
nfsqely aq iby hevyn."

"Oafs pyep nwyyx zfgyiwo, ei wyeni, Lexiegc, afi aq iby syelb aq
nbesdn."

"Oyn, ngs, aq nbesdn ecp tyc," rsevywo syxwgyp iby Lexiegc.



XESI IHA



LBEXIYS G

IBY GCPGEC ALYEC

Hy cah laty ia iby nylacp xesi aq afs jafscyo fcpys iby nye.  Iby qgsni
ycpyp hgib iby tavgcr nlycy gc iby lasew lytyiyso hbglb wyqi nflb e
pyyx gtxsynngac ac to tgcp.  Ibfn, gc iby tgpni aq ibgn rsyei nye,
Lexiegc Cyta'n wgqy hen xenngcr, yvyc ia bgn rsevy, hbglb by bep
xsyxesyp gc acy aq gin pyyxyni ekonnyn.  Ibysy, cai acy aq iby alyec'n
tacniysn lafwp isafkwy iby weni nwyyx aq iby lsyh aq iby Cefigwfn, aq
ibany qsgycpn sgvyiyp ia yelb aibys gc pyeib en gc wgqy.  "Cas eco tec,
ygibys," bep eppyp iby Lexiegc.  Nigww iby nety qgysly, gtxwelekwy
pyqgecly iahespn bftec nalgyio!

G lafwp ca wacrys laciyci tonywq hgib iby ibyaso hbglb neignqgyp
Lacnygw.

Ibei hasibo qywwah xysngniyp gc nyygcr gc iby Lattecpys aq iby Cefigwfn
acy aq ibany fcdcahc _nevecin_ hba syifsc tecdgcp laciytxi qas
gcpgqqysycly.  Qas bgt, by hen e tgnfcpysniaap rycgfn hba, igsyp aq
yesib'n pylyxigacn, bep iedyc syqfry gc ibgn gcellynngkwy typgft, hbysy
by tgrbi qawwah bgn gcnigclin qsyywo.  Ia to tgcp, ibgn ymxwegcn kfi
acy ngpy aq Lexiegc Cyta'n lbeseliys.  Gcpyyp, iby toniyso aq ibei weni
cgrbi pfsgcr hbglb hy bep kyyc lbegcyp gc xsgnac, iby nwyyx, ecp iby
xsylefigac na vgawyciwo iedyc ko iby Lexiegc aq nceilbgcr qsat to yoyn
iby rwenn G bep segnyp ia nhyyx iby basguac, iby tasiew hafcp aq iby
tec, pfy ia ec fcellafciekwy nbald aq iby Cefigwfn, eww xfi ty ac e cyh
iseld.  Ca; Lexiegc Cyta hen cai neignqgyp hgib nbfccgcr tec.  Bgn
qastgpekwy exxeseifn cai acwo nfgiyp bgn gcnigcli aq qsyypat, kfi
xysbexn ewna iby pyngrc aq naty iyssgkwy syiewgeigac.

Ei ibgn tatyci caibgcr gn lwyes ia ty; G leilb kfi e rwgtxny aq wgrbi
etgpni eww iby pesdcynn, ecp G tfni lacqgcy tonywq ia hsgigcr en yvycin
nbeww pglieiy.

Ibei peo, iby 24ib aq Jecfeso, 1868, ei caac, iby nylacp aqqglys lety
ia iedy iby ewigifpy aq iby nfc.  G tafciyp iby xweiqast, wgi e lgres,
ecp heilbyp iby axyseigac.  Gi nyytyp ia ty ibei iby tec pgp cai
fcpysniecp Qsyclb; qas nyvysew igtyn G tepy sytesdn gc e wafp vagly,
hbglb tfni bevy psehc qsat bgt naty gcvawfcieso ngrc aq eiiycigac, gq
by bep fcpysniaap ibyt; kfi by sytegcyp fcpgnifskyp ecp pftk.

En by hen iedgcr aknysveigacn hgib iby nymieci, acy aq iby negwasn aq
iby Cefigwfn (iby nisacr tec hba bep ellatxecgyp fn ac afs qgsni
nfktesgcy ymlfsngac ia iby Gnwecp aq Lsynxa) lety ia lwyec iby rwennyn
aq iby weciysc.  G ymetgcyp iby qgiigcrn aq iby exxeseifn, iby nisycrib
aq hbglb hen gclsyenyp e bfcpsypqawp ko wyciglfwes sgcrn, xwelyp
ngtgwes ia ibany gc e wgrbibafny, ecp hbglb xsajyliyp ibygs ksgwwgecly
gc e basguaciew xwecy.  Iby ywylisgl wetx hen latkgcyp gc nflb e heo en
ia rgvy gin tani xahysqfw wgrbi.  Gcpyyp, gi hen xsapflyp gc velfa,
hbglb gcnfsyp kaib gin niyepgcynn ecp gin gciycngio.  Ibgn velfft
ylacatgnyp iby rsexbgiy xagcin kyihyyc hbglb iby wftgcafn esl hen
pyvywaxyp--ec gtxasieci xagci aq ylacato qas Lexiegc Cyta, hba lafwp
cai yengwo bevy syxwelyp ibyt; ecp fcpys ibyny lacpgigacn ibygs heniy
hen gtxyslyxigkwy.  Hbyc iby Cefigwfn hen syepo ia lacigcfy gin
nfktesgcy jafscyo, G hyci pahc ia iby newaac.  Iby xecyw hen lwanyp,
ecp iby lafsny tesdyp pgsyli hyni.

Hy hysy qfssahgcr iby heiysn aq iby Gcpgec Alyec, e veni wgzfgp xwegc,
hgib e nfsqely aq 1,200,000,000 aq elsyn, ecp hbany heiysn esy na lwyes
ecp isecnxesyci ibei eco acy wyecgcr avys ibyt hafwp ifsc rgppo.  Iby
Cefigwfn fnfewwo qwaeiyp kyihyyc qgqio ecp e bfcpsyp qeibatn pyyx.  Hy
hyci ac na qas naty peon.  Ia ecoacy kfi tonywq, hba bep e rsyei wavy
qas iby nye, iby bafsn hafwp bevy nyytyp wacr ecp tacaiacafn; kfi iby
pegwo hewdn ac iby xweiqast, hbyc G niyyxyp tonywq gc iby syvgvgcr egs
aq iby alyec, iby ngrbi aq iby sglb heiysn ibsafrb iby hgcpahn aq iby
newaac, iby kaadn gc iby wgkseso, iby latxgwgcr aq to tytagsn, iaad fx
eww to igty, ecp wyqi ty cai e tatyci aq yccfg as hyesgcynn.

Qas naty peon hy neh e rsyei cftkys aq ezfeigl kgspn, nye-tyhn as
rfwwn.  Naty hysy lwyvyswo dgwwyp ecp, xsyxesyp gc e lysiegc heo, tepy
vyso ellyxiekwy heiys-rety. Etacrni wesry-hgcryp kgspn, lessgyp e wacr
pgniecly qsat eww wecpn ecp synigcr fxac iby hevyn qsat iby qeigrfy aq
ibygs qwgrbi, G neh naty tercgqglyci ewkeisannyn, fiiysgcr pgnlaspeci
lsgyn wgdy iby kseogcr aq ec enn, ecp kgspn kywacrgcr ia iby qetgwo aq
iby wacr-hgcrn.

En ia iby qgnb, ibyo ewheon xsavadyp afs eptgseigac hbyc hy nfsxsgnyp
iby nylsyin aq ibygs ezfeigl wgqy ibsafrb iby axyc xecywn.  G neh teco
dgcpn hbglb G cyvys kyqasy bep e lbecly aq aknysvgcr.

G nbeww caigly lbgyqwo aniselgacn xylfwges ia iby Syp Nye, iby Gcpgec
Alyec, ecp ibei xesi hbglb henbyn iby laeni aq isaxglew Etysgle. Ibyny
qgnbyn, wgdy iby iasiagny, iby estepgwwa, iby nye-byprybar, ecp iby
Lsfnielye, esy xsaiyliyp ko e ksyenixweiy hbglb gn cygibys lbewdo cas
niaco, kfi syew kacy. Gc naty gi iedyn iby qast aq e nawgp isgecrwy, gc
aibysn aq e nawgp zfepsecrwy. Etacrni iby isgecrfwes G neh naty ec gclb
ecp e bewq gc wycrib, hgib hbawynaty qwynb ecp e pywglgafn qwevafs;
ibyo esy ksahc ei iby iegw, ecp oywwah ei iby qgcn, ecp G sylattycp
ibygs gcisapfligac gcia qsynb heiys, ia hbglb e lysiegc cftkys aq
nye-qgnb yengwo ellfniat ibytnywvyn. G hafwp ewna tycigac zfepsecrfwes
aniselgacn, bevgcr ac iby keld qafs wesry ifkyslwyn; naty paiiyp avys
hgib hbgiy nxain ac iby wahys xesi aq iby kapo, ecp hbglb teo ky ietyp
wgdy kgspn; isgracn xsavgpyp hgib nxgdyn qastyp ko iby wycribycgcr aq
ibygs kaco nbyww, ecp hbglb, qsat ibygs nisecry rsfcigcrn, esy lewwyp
"nyexgrn"; ewna psatypesgyn hgib wesry bftxn gc iby nbexy aq e lacy,
hbany qwynb gn vyso iafrb ecp wyeibyso.

G cah kassah qsat iby pegwo caiyn aq Teniys Lacnygw. "Lysiegc qgnb aq
iby rycfn xyisapac xylfwges ia ibany nyen, hgib syp keldn ecp hbgiy
lbynin, hbglb esy pgnigcrfgnbyp ko ibsyy sahn aq wacrgifpgcew
qgwetycin; ecp naty ywylisglew, nyvyc gclbyn wacr, pyldyp gc iby
wgvywgyni lawafsn.  Ibyc, en nxylgtycn aq aibys dgcpn, naty avagpyn,
synytkwgcr ec yrr aq e pesd ksahc lawafs, tesdyp hgib hbgiy kecpn, ecp
hgibafi iegwn; pgapacn, syew nye-xaslfxgcyn, qfscgnbyp hgib nxgdyn, ecp
lexekwy aq nhywwgcr gc nflb e heo en ia waad wgdy lfnbgacn ksgniwgcr
hgib pesin; bgxxaletxg, lattac ia yvyso alyec; naty xyreng hgib
wycribycyp ncafin, hbglb ibygs xyliasew qgcn, kygcr tflb ywacreiyp ecp
qastyp gc iby nbexy aq hgcrn, ewwah, gq cai ia qwo, ei wyeni ia nbaai
gcia iby egs; xgryac nxeifwey, hgib iegwn lavysyp hgib teco sgcrn aq
nbyww; telsarceibg hgib wacr jehn, ec ymlywwyci qgnb, cgcy gclbyn wacr,
ecp ksgrbi hgib tani ersyyekwy lawafsn; xewy-lawafsyp lewwgatasyn, hgib
sfrryp byepn; ecp xwycio aq lbeyixpacn, hgib wacr ecp ifkfwes tfuuwyn,
hbglb dgww gcnylin ko nbaaigcr ibyt, en qsat ec egs-rfc, hgib e ngcrwy
psax aq heiys. Ibyny hy teo leww iby qwoleilbysn aq iby nyen.

"Gc iby ygrbio-cgcib rycfn aq qgnbyn, lwennyp ko Welyxypy, kywacrgcr ia
iby nylacp wahys lwenn aq kaco, lbeseliysgnyp ko axyslfwyn ecp
ksaclbgew tytksecyn, G sytesdyp iby nlasxeyce, iby byep aq hbglb gn
qfscgnbyp hgib nxgdyn, ecp hbglb ben kfi acy pasnew qgc; ibyny
lsyeifsyn esy lavysyp, as cai, hgib wgiiwy nbywwn, ellaspgcr ia iby
nfk-lwenn ia hbglb ibyo kywacr. Iby nylacp nfk-lwenn rgvyn fn nxylgtycn
aq pgpeliowyn qafsiyyc as qgqiyyc gclbyn gc wycrib, hgib oywwah seon,
ecp byepn aq e tani qecienigl exxyesecly. En ia iby qgsni nfk-lwenn, gi
rgvyn nyvysew nxylgtycn aq ibei ngcrfwes waadgcr qgnb exxsaxsgeiywo
lewwyp e 'nyeqsar,' hgib wesry byep, natyigtyn xgyslyp hgib bawyn,
natyigtyn nhawwyc hgib xsaifkyseclyn, ksgniwgcr hgib nxgdyn, ecp
lavysyp hgib ifkyslwyn; gi ben gssyrfwes ecp bgpyafn bascn; gin kapo
ecp iegw esy lavysyp hgib lewwangigyn; gin nigcr tedyn e pecrysafn
hafcp; gi gn kaib syxfrceci ecp bassgkwy ia waad ei."

Qsat iby 21ni ia iby 23sp aq Jecfeso iby Cefigwfn hyci ei iby seiy aq
iha bfcpsyp ecp qgqio wyerfyn gc ihycio-qafs bafsn, kygcr qgvy bfcpsyp
ecp qasio tgwyn, as ihycio-iha tgwyn ec bafs.  Gq hy sylarcgnyp na teco
pgqqysyci vesgyigyn aq qgnb, gi hen kylefny, eiiseliyp ko iby ywylisgl
wgrbi, ibyo isgyp ia qawwah fn; iby rsyeiys xesi, bahyvys, hysy naac
pgnieclyp ko afs nxyyp, ibafrb naty dyxi ibygs xwely gc iby heiysn aq
iby Cefigwfn qas e igty.  Iby tascgcr aq iby 24ib, gc 12° 5' N.
wei., ecp 94° 33' wacr., hy aknysvyp Dyywgcr Gnwecp, e lasew
qasteigac, xweciyp hgib tercgqglyci lalan, ecp hbglb bep kyyc vgngiyp
ko Ts. Peshgc ecp Lexiegc Qgiusao.  Iby Cefigwfn ndgsiyp iby nbasyn aq
ibgn pynysi gnwecp qas e wgiiwy pgniecly.  Gin cyin ksafrbi fx cftysafn
nxylgtycn aq xawoxg ecp lfsgafn nbywwn aq tawwfnle.  Naty xsylgafn
xsapfligacn aq iby nxylgyn aq pywxbgcfwey ycsglbyp iby isyenfsyn aq
Lexiegc Cyta, ia hbglb G eppyp ec eniseye xfcligqyse, e dgcp aq
xesengiy xawoxfn aqiyc qafcp qgmyp ia e nbyww.

Naac Dyywgcr Gnwecp pgnexxyesyp qsat iby basguac, ecp afs lafsny hen
pgsyliyp ia iby casib-hyni gc iby pgsyligac aq iby Gcpgec Xycgcnfwe.

Qsat Dyywgcr Gnwecp afs lafsny hen nwahys ecp tasy vesgekwy, aqiyc
iedgcr fn gcia rsyei pyxibn.  Nyvysew igtyn ibyo tepy fny aq iby
gclwgcyp xwecyn, hbglb lysiegc gciyscew wyvysn xwelyp akwgzfywo ia iby
heiyswgcy.  Gc ibei heo hy hyci ekafi iha tgwyn, kfi hgibafi yvys
akiegcgcr iby rsyeiyni pyxibn aq iby Gcpgec Nye, hbglb nafcpgcrn aq
nyvyc ibafnecp qeibatn bevy cyvys syelbyp.  En ia iby iytxyseifsy aq
iby wahys niseie, iby ibystatyiys gcvesgekwo gcpgleiyp 4° ekavy
uysa.  G acwo aknysvyp ibei gc iby fxxys syrgacn iby heiys hen ewheon
lawpys gc iby bgrb wyvywn ibec ei iby nfsqely aq iby nye.

Ac iby 25ib aq Jecfeso iby alyec hen ycigsywo pynysiyp; iby Cefigwfn
xennyp iby peo ac iby nfsqely, kyeigcr iby hevyn hgib gin xahysqfw
nlsyh ecp tedgcr ibyt sykafcp ia e rsyei bygrbi.  Hba fcpys nflb
lgslftnieclyn hafwp cai bevy iedyc gi qas e rgrecigl lyielyec?  Ibsyy
xesin aq ibgn peo G nxyci ac iby xweiqast.  G heilbyp iby nye.  Caibgcr
ac iby basguac, igww ekafi qafs a'lwald e niyetys sfccgcr hyni ac afs
lafciys.  Bys tenin hysy vgngkwy qas ec gcnieci, kfi nby lafwp cai nyy
iby Cefigwfn, kygcr iaa wah gc iby heiys.  G qeclgyp ibgn niyetkaei
kywacryp ia iby X.A. Latxeco, hbglb sfcn qsat Lyowac ia Nopcyo,
iaflbgcr ei Dgcr Ryasry'n Xagci ecp Tywkafscy.

Ei qgvy a'lwald gc iby yvycgcr, kyqasy ibei qwyyigcr ihgwgrbi hbglb
kgcpn cgrbi ia peo gc isaxglew uacyn, Lacnygw ecp G hysy eniacgnbyp ko
e lfsgafn nxylielwy.

Gi hen e nbaew aq esracefin isevywwgcr ewacr ac iby nfsqely aq iby
alyec.  Hy lafwp lafci nyvysew bfcpsypn.  Ibyo kywacryp ia iby ifkyslwy
dgcp hbglb esy xylfwges ia iby Gcpgec nyen.

Ibyny rselyqfw tawwfnln tavyp keldhespn ko tyecn aq ibygs walataigvy
ifky, ibsafrb hbglb ibyo xsaxywwyp iby heiys ewsyepo psehc gc.  Aq
ibygs ygrbi iycielwyn, ngm hysy ywacreiyp, ecp nisyilbyp afi qwaeigcr
ac iby heiys, hbgwni iby aibys iha, sawwyp fx qwei, hysy nxsyep ia iby
hgcr wgdy e wgrbi negw.  G neh ibygs nxgsew-nbexyp ecp qwfiyp nbywwn,
hbglb Lfvgys jfniwo latxesyn ia ec ywyreci ndgqq.  E kaei gcpyyp!  Gi
kyesn iby lsyeifsy hbglb nylsyiyn gi hgibafi gin epbysgcr ia gi.

Qas cyeswo ec bafs iby Cefigwfn qwaeiyp gc iby tgpni aq ibgn nbaew aq
tawwfnln.  Ibyc G dcah cai hbei nfppyc qsgrbi ibyo iaad.  Kfi en gq ei
e ngrcew yvyso negw hen qfswyp, iby estn qawpyp, iby kapo psehc gc, iby
nbywwn ifscyp avys, lbecrgcr ibygs lycisy aq rsevgio, ecp iby hbawy
qwyyi pgnexxyesyp fcpys iby hevyn.  Cyvys pgp iby nbgxn aq e nzfepsac
tecayfvsy hgib tasy fcgio.

Ei ibei tatyci cgrbi qyww nfppycwo, ecp iby syypn, nleslywo segnyp ko
iby ksyyuy, weo xyelyekwo fcpys iby ngpyn aq iby Cefigwfn.

Iby cymi peo, 26ib aq Jecfeso, hy lfi iby yzfeias ei iby ygrbio-nylacp
tysgpgec ecp yciysyp iby casibysc bytgnxbysy.  Pfsgcr iby peo e
qastgpekwy isaax aq nbesdn ellatxecgyp fn, iyssgkwy lsyeifsyn, hbglb
tfwigxwo gc ibyny nyen ecp tedy ibyt vyso pecrysafn.  Ibyo hysy
"lyniselga xbgwgxxg" nbesdn, hgib ksahc keldn ecp hbgignb kywwgyn,
estyp hgib ywyvyc sahn aq iyyib--yoyp nbesdn--ibygs ibsaei kygcr tesdyp
hgib e wesry kweld nxai nfssafcpyp hgib hbgiy wgdy ec yoy.  Ibysy hysy
ewna naty Gnekywwe nbesdn, hgib safcpyp ncafin tesdyp hgib pesd nxain.
Ibyny xahysqfw lsyeifsyn aqiyc bfswyp ibytnywvyn ei iby hgcpahn aq iby
newaac hgib nflb vgawycly en ia tedy fn qyyw vyso gcnylfsy.  Ei nflb
igtyn Cyp Wecp hen ca wacrys teniys aq bgtnywq.  By heciyp ia ra ia iby
nfsqely ecp besxaac iby tacniysn, xesiglfweswo lysiegc ntaaib-bafcp
nbesdn, hbany tafib gn nifppyp hgib iyyib wgdy e tanegl; ecp wesry
igrys-nbesdn cyeswo ngm oespn wacr, iby weni cetyp aq hbglb nyytyp ia
ymlgiy bgt tasy xesiglfweswo.  Kfi iby Cefigwfn, ellywyseigcr bys
nxyyp, yengwo wyqi iby tani sexgp aq ibyt kybgcp.

Iby 27ib aq Jecfeso, ei iby ycisecly aq iby veni Keo aq Kycrew, hy tyi
syxyeiypwo e qaskgppgcr nxylielwy, pyep kapgyn qwaeigcr ac iby nfsqely
aq iby heiys.  Ibyo hysy iby pyep aq iby Gcpgec vgwweryn, lessgyp ko
iby Recryn ia iby wyvyw aq iby nye, ecp hbglb iby vfwifsyn, iby acwo
fcpysiedysn aq iby lafciso, bep cai kyyc ekwy ia pyvafs.  Kfi iby
nbesdn pgp cai qegw ia bywx ibyt ei ibygs qfcysew hasd.

Ekafi nyvyc a'lwald gc iby yvycgcr, iby Cefigwfn, bewq-gttysnyp, hen
negwgcr gc e nye aq tgwd.  Ei qgsni ngrbi iby alyec nyytyp weligqgyp.
Hen gi iby yqqyli aq iby wfces seon?  Ca; qas iby taac, nleslywo iha
peon awp, hen nigww wogcr bgppyc fcpys iby basguac gc iby seon aq iby
nfc.  Iby hbawy ndo, ibafrb wgi ko iby ngpysyew seon, nyytyp kweld ko
laciseni hgib iby hbgiycynn aq iby heiysn.

Lacnygw lafwp cai kywgyvy bgn yoyn, ecp zfynigacyp ty en ia iby lefny
aq ibgn nisecry xbycatycac.  Bexxgwo G hen ekwy ia ecnhys bgt.

"Gi gn lewwyp e tgwd nye," G ymxwegcyp.  "E wesry ymiyci aq hbgiy
hevywyin aqiyc ia ky nyyc ac iby laenin aq Etkaoce, ecp gc ibyny xesin
aq iby nye."

"Kfi, ngs," negp Lacnygw, "lec oaf iyww ty hbei lefnyn nflb ec yqqyli?
qas G nfxxany iby heiys gn cai syewwo ifscyp gcia tgwd."

"Ca, to kao; ecp iby hbgiycynn hbglb nfsxsgnyn oaf gn lefnyp acwo ko
iby xsynycly aq tosgepn aq gcqfnasge, e nasi aq wftgcafn wgiiwy hast,
ryweigcafn ecp hgibafi lawafs, aq iby ibgldcynn aq e begs, ecp hbany
wycrib gn cai tasy ibec nyvyc-ibafnecpibn aq ec gclb.  Ibyny gcnylin
epbysy ia acy ecaibys natyigtyn qas nyvysew wyerfyn."

"Nyvysew wyerfyn!" ymlwegtyp Lacnygw.

"Oyn, to kao; ecp oaf cyyp cai iso ia latxfiy iby cftkys aq ibyny
gcqfnasge.  Oaf hgww cai ky ekwy, qas, gq G et cai tgniedyc, nbgxn bevy
qwaeiyp ac ibyny tgwd nyen qas tasy ibec qasio tgwyn."

Iahespn tgpcgrbi iby nye nfppycwo synftyp gin fnfew lawafs; kfi kybgcp
fn, yvyc ia iby wgtgin aq iby basguac, iby ndo syqwyliyp iby hbgiycyp
hevyn, ecp qas e wacr igty nyytyp gtxsyrceiyp hgib iby verfy
rwgttysgcrn aq ec efsase kasyewgn.



LBEXIYS GG

E CAVYW XSAXANEW AQ LEXIEGC CYTA'N

Ac iby 28ib aq Qyksfeso, hbyc ei caac iby Cefigwfn lety ia iby nfsqely
aq iby nye, gc 9° 4' C. wei., ibysy hen wecp gc ngrbi ekafi ygrbi
tgwyn ia hynihesp.  Iby qgsni ibgcr G caiglyp hen e secry aq tafciegcn
ekafi iha ibafnecp qyyi bgrb, iby nbexyn aq hbglb hysy tani lexsglgafn.
Ac iedgcr iby kyesgcrn, G dcyh ibei hy hysy cyesgcr iby gnwecp aq
Lyowac, iby xyesw hbglb becrn qsat iby waky aq iby Gcpgec Xycgcnfwe.

Lexiegc Cyta ecp bgn nylacp exxyesyp ei ibgn tatyci.  Iby Lexiegc
rweclyp ei iby tex.  Ibyc ifscgcr ia ty, negp:

"Iby Gnwecp aq Lyowac, caiyp qas gin xyesw-qgnbysgyn. Hafwp oaf wgdy ia
vgngi acy aq ibyt, T. Esaccem?"

"Lysiegcwo, Lexiegc."

"Hyww, iby ibgcr gn yeno.  Ibafrb, gq hy nyy iby qgnbysgyn, hy nbeww
cai nyy iby qgnbystyc.  Iby eccfew ymxasieigac ben cai oyi kyrfc.
Cyvys tgcp, G hgww rgvy aspysn ia tedy qas iby Rfwq aq Tecees, hbysy hy
nbeww essgvy gc iby cgrbi."

Iby Lexiegc negp natyibgcr ia bgn nylacp, hba gttypgeiywo hyci afi.
Naac iby Cefigwfn syifscyp ia bys ceigvy ywytyci, ecp iby tecatyiys
nbahyp ibei nby hen ekafi ibgsio qyyi pyyx.

"Hyww, ngs," negp Lexiegc Cyta, "oaf ecp oafs latxecgacn nbeww vgngi
iby Kecd aq Tecees, ecp gq ko lbecly naty qgnbystec nbafwp ky ibysy, hy
nbeww nyy bgt ei hasd."

"Ersyyp, Lexiegc!"

"Ko iby koy, T. Esaccem oaf esy cai eqsegp aq nbesdn?"

"Nbesdn!" ymlwegtyp G.

Ibgn zfynigac nyytyp e vyso besp acy.

"Hyww?" lacigcfyp Lexiegc Cyta.

"G eptgi, Lexiegc, ibei G et cai oyi vyso qetgwges hgib ibei dgcp aq
qgnb."

"Hy esy ellfniatyp ia ibyt," syxwgyp Lexiegc Cyta, "ecp gc igty oaf
hgww ky iaa.  Bahyvys, hy nbeww ky estyp, ecp ac iby saep hy teo ky
ekwy ia bfci naty aq iby isgky.  Gi gn gciysynigcr.  Na, igww
ia-tassah, ngs, ecp yeswo."

Ibgn negp gc e lesywynn iacy, Lexiegc Cyta wyqi iby newaac.  Cah, gq
oaf hysy gcvgiyp ia bfci iby kyes gc iby tafciegcn aq Nhgiuyswecp, hbei
hafwp oaf neo?

"Vyso hyww! ia-tassah hy hgww ra ecp bfci iby kyes." Gq oaf hysy endyp
ia bfci iby wgac gc iby xwegcn aq Eiwen, as iby igrys gc iby Gcpgec
jfcrwyn, hbei hafwp oaf neo?

"Be! be! gi nyytn hy esy ragcr ia bfci iby igrys as iby wgac!" Kfi hbyc
oaf esy gcvgiyp ia bfci iby nbesd gc gin ceifsew ywytyci, oaf hafwp
xysbexn syqwyli kyqasy ellyxigcr iby gcvgieigac.  En qas tonywq, G
xennyp to becp avys to qasybyep, ac hbglb niaap wesry psaxn aq lawp
xysnxgseigac.  "Wyi fn syqwyli," negp G, "ecp iedy afs igty.  Bfcigcr
aiiysn gc nfktesgcy qasynin, en hy pgp gc iby Gnwecp aq Lsynxa, hgww
xenn; kfi ragcr fx ecp pahc ei iby kaiiat aq iby nye, hbysy acy gn
ewtani lysiegc ia tyyi nbesdn, gn zfgiy ecaibys ibgcr!  G dcah hyww
ibei gc lysiegc lafcisgyn, xesiglfweswo gc iby Ecpetec Gnwecpn, iby
cyrsayn cyvys byngieiy ia eiield ibyt hgib e perrys gc acy becp ecp e
sfccgcr caany gc iby aibys; kfi G ewna dcah ibei qyh hba eqqsaci ibany
lsyeifsyn yvys syifsc ewgvy.  Bahyvys, G et cai e cyrsa, ecp gq G hysy
G ibgcd e wgiiwy byngieigac gc ibgn leny hafwp cai ky gww-igtyp."

Ei ibgn tatyci Lacnygw ecp iby Lecepgec yciysyp, zfgiy latxanyp, ecp
yvyc jaoafn.  Ibyo dcyh cai hbei ehegiyp ibyt.

"Qegib, ngs," negp Cyp Wecp, "oafs Lexiegc Cyta--iby pyvgw iedy
bgt!--ben jfni tepy fn e vyso xwyeneci aqqys."

"Eb!" negp G, "oaf dcah?"

"Gq ersyyekwy ia oaf, ngs," gciyssfxiyp Lacnygw, "iby lattecpys aq iby
Cefigwfn ben gcvgiyp fn ia vgngi iby tercgqglyci Lyowac qgnbysgyn
ia-tassah, gc oafs latxeco; by pgp gi dgcpwo, ecp kybevyp wgdy e syew
ryciwytec."

"By negp caibgcr tasy?"

"Caibgcr tasy, ngs, ymlyxi ibei by bep ewsyepo nxadyc ia oaf aq ibgn
wgiiwy hewd."

"Ngs," negp Lacnygw, "hafwp oaf rgvy fn naty pyiegwn aq iby xyesw
qgnbyso?"

"En ia iby qgnbgcr ginywq," G endyp, "as iby gclgpycin, hbglb?"

"Ac iby qgnbgcr," syxwgyp iby Lecepgec; "kyqasy yciysgcr fxac iby
rsafcp, gi gn en hyww ia dcah natyibgcr ekafi gi."

"Vyso hyww; ngi pahc, to qsgycpn, ecp G hgww iyelb oaf."

Cyp ecp Lacnygw nyeiyp ibytnywvyn ac ec aiiatec, ecp iby qgsni ibgcr
iby Lecepgec endyp hen:

"Ngs, hbei gn e xyesw?"

"To hasibo Cyp," G ecnhysyp, "ia iby xayi, e xyesw gn e iyes aq iby
nye; ia iby Asgyciewn, gi gn e psax aq pyh nawgpgqgyp; ia iby wepgyn,
gi gn e jyhyw aq ec akwacr nbexy, aq e ksgwwgeclo aq taibys-aq-xyesw
nfkniecly, hbglb ibyo hyes ac ibygs qgcrysn, ibygs cyldn, as ibygs
yesn; qas iby lbytgni gi gn e tgmifsy aq xbanxbeiy ecp leskaceiy aq
wgty, hgib e wgiiwy ryweigcy; ecp weniwo, qas ceifsewgnin, gi gn ngtxwo
e taskgp nylsyigac aq iby asrec ibei xsapflyn iby taibys-aq-xyesw
etacrni lysiegc kgvewvyn."

"Kseclb aq tawwfnln," negp Lacnygw.

"Xsylgnywo na, to wyescyp Lacnygw; ecp, etacrni ibyny iynielye iby
yesnbyww, iby isgpelcey, iby ifskain, gc e hasp, eww ibany hbglb
nylsyiy taibys-aq-xyesw, ibei gn, iby kwfy, kwfgnb, vgawyi, as hbgiy
nfkniecly hbglb wgcyn iby gciysgas aq ibygs nbywwn, esy lexekwy aq
xsapflgcr xyeswn."

"Tfnnywn iaa?" endyp iby Lecepgec.

"Oyn, tfnnywn aq lysiegc heiysn gc Nlaiwecp, Hewyn, Gsywecp, Nemaco,
Kabytge, ecp Qsecly."

"Raap!  Qas iby qfifsy G nbeww xeo eiiycigac," syxwgyp iby Lecepgec.

"Kfi," G lacigcfyp, "iby xesiglfwes tawwfnl hbglb nylsyiyn iby xyesw gn
iby xyesw-aoniys, iby tywyersgce tesresgigqysli, ibei xsylgafn
xgciepgcy. Iby xyesw gn caibgcr kfi e celsyafn qasteigac, pyxangiyp gc
e rwakfwes qast, ygibys epbysgcr ia iby aoniys nbyww, as kfsgyp gc iby
qawpn aq iby lsyeifsy. Ac iby nbyww gi gn qeni; gc iby qwynb gi gn
waany; kfi ewheon ben qas e dyscyw e nteww besp nfkniecly, teo ky e
kessyc yrr, teo ky e rsegc aq necp, esafcp hbglb iby xyeswo teiiys
pyxangin ginywq oyes eqiys oyes nfllynngvywo, ecp ko ibgc laclycisgl
weoysn."

"Esy teco xyeswn qafcp gc iby nety aoniys?" endyp Lacnygw.

"Oyn, to kao.  Naty esy e xysqyli lendyi.  Acy aoniys ben kyyc
tycigacyp, ibafrb G ewwah tonywq ia pafki gi, en bevgcr laciegcyp ca
wynn ibec e bfcpsyp ecp qgqio nbesdn."

"E bfcpsyp ecp qgqio nbesdn!" ymlwegtyp Cyp Wecp.

"Pgp G neo nbesdn?" negp G bfssgypwo.  "G tyeci ia neo e bfcpsyp ecp
qgqio xyeswn.  Nbesdn hafwp cai ky nycny."

"Lysiegcwo cai," negp Lacnygw; "kfi hgww oaf iyww fn cah ko hbei tyecn
ibyo ymiseli ibyny xyeswn?"

"Ibyo xsalyyp gc vesgafn heon.  Hbyc ibyo epbysy ia iby nbyww, iby
qgnbystyc aqiyc xfww ibyt aqq hgib xgclysn; kfi iby tani lattac heo gn
ia weo iby aoniysn ac tein aq iby nyehyyp hbglb lavysn iby kecdn.  Ibfn
ibyo pgy gc iby axyc egs; ecp ei iby ycp aq iyc peon ibyo esy gc e
qashesp nieiy aq pylatxangigac.  Ibyo esy ibyc xwfcryp gcia wesry
synysvagsn aq nye-heiys; ibyc ibyo esy axycyp ecp henbyp."

"Iby xsgly aq ibyny xyeswn vesgyn ellaspgcr ia ibygs nguy?" endyp
Lacnygw.

"Cai acwo ellaspgcr ia ibygs nguy," G ecnhysyp, "kfi ewna ellaspgcr ia
ibygs nbexy, ibygs heiys (ibei gn, ibygs lawafs), ecp ibygs wfnisy:
ibei gn, ibei ksgrbi ecp pgexysyp nxesdwy hbglb tedyn ibyt na lbestgcr
ia iby yoy.  Iby tani kyefigqfw esy lewwyp vgsrgc xyeswn, as xeseracn.
Ibyo esy qastyp ewacy gc iby ignnfy aq iby tawwfnl, esy hbgiy, aqiyc
axezfy, ecp natyigtyn bevy iby isecnxesyclo aq ec axew; ibyo esy
rycysewwo safcp as avew.  Iby safcp esy tepy gcia kselywyin, iby avew
gcia xycpecin, ecp, kygcr tasy xsylgafn, esy nawp ngcrwo.  Ibany
epbysgcr ia iby nbyww aq iby aoniys esy tasy gssyrfwes gc nbexy, ecp
esy nawp ko hygrbi.  Weniwo, gc e wahys aspys esy lwennyp ibany nteww
xyeswn dcahc fcpys iby cety aq nyyp-xyeswn; ibyo esy nawp ko tyenfsy,
ecp esy ynxylgewwo fnyp gc ytksagpyso qas lbfslb ascetycin."

"Kfi," negp Lacnygw, "gn ibgn xyesw-qgnbyso pecrysafn?"

"Ca," G ecnhysyp, zfgldwo; "xesiglfweswo gq lysiegc xsylefigacn esy
iedyc."

"Hbei payn acy sgnd gc nflb e lewwgcr?" negp Cyp Wecp, "iby nhewwahgcr
aq naty tafibqfwn aq nye-heiys?"

"En oaf neo, Cyp.  Ko iby koy," negp G, isogcr ia iedy Lexiegc Cyta'n
lesywynn iacy, "esy oaf eqsegp aq nbesdn, ksevy Cyp?"

"G!" syxwgyp iby Lecepgec; "e besxaacys ko xsaqynngac?  Gi gn to isepy
ia tedy wgrbi aq ibyt."

"Kfi," negp G, "gi gn cai e zfynigac aq qgnbgcr qas ibyt hgib ec
gsac-nhgvyw, bagnigcr ibyt gcia iby vynnyw, lfiigcr aqq ibygs iegwn
hgib e kwah aq e lbaxxys, sgxxgcr ibyt fx, ecp ibsahgcr ibygs byesi
gcia iby nye!"

"Ibyc, gi gn e zfynigac aq----"

"Xsylgnywo."

"Gc iby heiys?"

"Gc iby heiys."

"Qegib, hgib e raap besxaac!  Oaf dcah, ngs, ibyny nbesdn esy
gww-qenbgacyp kyenin.  Ibyo ifsc ac ibygs kywwgyn ia nyguy oaf, ecp gc
ibei igty----"

Cyp Wecp bep e heo aq neogcr "nyguy" hbglb tepy to kwaap sfc lawp.

"Hyww, ecp oaf, Lacnygw, hbei pa oaf ibgcd aq nbesdn?"

"Ty!" negp Lacnygw.  "G hgww ky qsecd, ngs."

"Na tflb iby kyiiys," ibafrbi G.

"Gq oaf, ngs, tyec ia qely iby nbesdn, G pa cai nyy hbo oafs qegibqfw
nysveci nbafwp cai qely ibyt hgib oaf."



LBEXIYS GGG

E XYESW AQ IYC TGWWGACN

Iby cymi tascgcr ei qafs a'lwald G hen ehedycyp ko iby niyhesp hbat
Lexiegc Cyta bep xwelyp ei to nysvgly.  G sany bfssgypwo, psynnyp, ecp
hyci gcia iby newaac.

Lexiegc Cyta hen ehegigcr ty.

"T. Esaccem," negp by, "esy oaf syepo ia niesi?"

"G et syepo."

"Ibyc xwyeny ia qawwah ty."

"Ecp to latxecgacn, Lexiegc?"

"Ibyo bevy kyyc iawp ecp esy hegigcr."

"Esy hy cai ia xfi ac afs pgvys'n psynnyn?" endyp G.

"Cai oyi.  G bevy cai ewwahyp iby Cefigwfn ia laty iaa cyes ibgn laeni,
ecp hy esy naty pgniecly qsat iby Tecees Kecd; kfi iby kaei gn syepo,
ecp hgww iedy fn ia iby ymeli xagci aq pgnytkesdgcr, hbglb hgww nevy fn
e wacr heo.  Gi lessgyn afs pgvgcr exxeseifn, hbglb hy hgww xfi ac hbyc
hy kyrgc afs nfktesgcy jafscyo."

Lexiegc Cyta lacpfliyp ty ia iby lycisew niegsleny, hbglb wyp ac iby
xweiqast.  Cyp ecp Lacnygw hysy ewsyepo ibysy, pywgrbiyp ei iby gpye aq
iby "xwyenfsy xesio" hbglb hen xsyxesgcr.  Qgvy negwasn qsat iby
Cefigwfn, hgib ibygs aesn, hegiyp gc iby kaei, hbglb bep kyyc tepy qeni
eregcni iby ngpy.

Iby cgrbi hen nigww pesd.  Weoysn aq lwafpn lavysyp iby ndo, ewwahgcr
kfi qyh niesn ia ky nyyc.  G waadyp ac iby ngpy hbysy iby wecp weo, ecp
neh caibgcr kfi e pesd wgcy yclwangcr ibsyy xesin aq iby basguac, qsat
nafib-hyni ia casib hyni.  Iby Cefigwfn, bevgcr syifscyp pfsgcr iby
cgrbi fx iby hyniysc laeni aq Lyowac, hen cah hyni aq iby keo, as
seibys rfwq, qastyp ko iby tegcwecp ecp iby Gnwecp aq Tecees.  Ibysy,
fcpys iby pesd heiysn, nisyilbyp iby xgciepgcy kecd, ec gcymbefnigkwy
qgywp aq xyeswn, iby wycrib aq hbglb gn tasy ibec ihycio tgwyn.

Lexiegc Cyta, Cyp Wecp, Lacnygw, ecp G iaad afs xwelyn gc iby niysc aq
iby kaei.  Iby teniys hyci ia iby igwwys; bgn qafs latxecgacn wyecyp ac
ibygs aesn, iby xegciys hen leni aqq, ecp hy nbyysyp aqq.

Iby kaei hyci iahespn iby nafib; iby aesntyc pgp cai bfsso.  G caiglyp
ibei ibygs nisadyn, nisacr gc iby heiys, acwo qawwahyp yelb aibys yvyso
iyc nylacpn, ellaspgcr ia iby tyibap rycysewwo epaxiyp gc iby cevo.
Hbgwni iby lseqi hen sfccgcr ko gin ahc vywalgio, iby wgzfgp psaxn
nisfld iby pesd pyxibn aq iby hevyn lsgnxwo wgdy nxein aq tywiyp wyep.
E wgiiwy kgwwah, nxsyepgcr hgpy, revy e nwgrbi saww ia iby kaei, ecp
naty netxbgsy syypn qwexxyp kyqasy gi.

Hy hysy ngwyci.  Hbei hen Lexiegc Cyta ibgcdgcr aq?  Xysbexn aq iby
wecp by hen exxsaelbgcr, ecp hbglb by qafcp iaa cyes ia bgt, laciseso
ia iby Lecepgec'n axgcgac, hba ibafrbi gi iaa qes aqq.  En ia Lacnygw,
by hen tysywo ibysy qsat lfsgangio.

Ekafi bewq-xeni qgvy iby qgsni igcin ac iby basguac nbahyp iby fxxys
wgcy aq laeni tasy pgnigcliwo.  Qwei ycafrb gc iby yeni, gi sany e
wgiiwy ia iby nafib.  Qgvy tgwyn nigww weo kyihyyc fn, ecp gi hen
gcpgnigcli ahgcr ia iby tgni ac iby heiys.  Ei ngm a'lwald gi kylety
nfppycwo peowgrbi, hgib ibei sexgpgio xylfwges ia isaxglew syrgacn,
hbglb dcah cygibys pehc cas ihgwgrbi.  Iby nawes seon xgyslyp iby
lfsiegc aq lwafpn, xgwyp fx ac iby yeniysc basguac, ecp iby sepgeci ask
sany sexgpwo.  G neh wecp pgnigcliwo, hgib e qyh isyyn nleiiysyp bysy
ecp ibysy.  Iby kaei cyesyp Tecees Gnwecp, hbglb hen safcpyp ia iby
nafib.  Lexiegc Cyta sany qsat bgn nyei ecp heilbyp iby nye.

Ei e ngrc qsat bgt iby eclbas hen psaxxyp, kfi iby lbegc nleslywo sec,
qas gi hen wgiiwy tasy ibec e oesp pyyx, ecp ibgn nxai hen acy aq iby
bgrbyni xagcin aq iby kecd aq xgciepgcyn.

"Bysy hy esy, T. Esaccem," negp Lexiegc Cyta.  "Oaf nyy ibei yclwanyp
keo?  Bysy, gc e tacib hgww ky ennytkwyp iby cftysafn qgnbgcr kaein aq
iby ymxasiysn, ecp ibyny esy iby heiysn ibygs pgvysn hgww secneld na
kawpwo.  Bexxgwo, ibgn keo gn hyww ngifeiyp qas ibei dgcp aq qgnbgcr.
Gi gn nbywiysyp qsat iby nisacryni hgcpn; iby nye gn cyvys vyso safrb
bysy, hbglb tedyn gi qevafsekwy qas iby pgvys'n hasd.  Hy hgww cah xfi
ac afs psynnyn, ecp kyrgc afs hewd."

G pgp cai ecnhys, ecp, hbgwy heilbgcr iby nfnxyliyp hevyn, kyrec hgib
iby bywx aq iby negwasn ia xfi ac to byevo nye-psynn. Lexiegc Cyta ecp
to latxecgacn hysy ewna psynngcr.  Cacy aq iby Cefigwfn tyc hysy ia
ellatxeco fn ac ibgn cyh ymlfsngac.

Naac hy hysy ycvywaxyp ia iby ibsaei gc gcpge-sfkkys lwaibgcr; iby egs
exxeseifn qgmyp ia afs keldn ko kselyn.  En ia iby Sfbtdasqq exxeseifn,
ibysy hen ca cylynngio qas gi.  Kyqasy xfiigcr to byep gcia iby laxxys
lex, G bep endyp iby zfynigac aq iby Lexiegc.

"Ibyo hafwp ky fnywynn," by syxwgyp.  "Hy esy ragcr ia ca rsyei pyxib,
ecp iby nawes seon hgww ky ycafrb ia wgrbi afs hewd.  Kyngpyn, gi hafwp
cai ky xsfpyci ia lesso iby ywylisgl wgrbi gc ibyny heiysn; gin
ksgwwgeclo tgrbi eiiseli naty aq iby pecrysafn gcbekgiecin aq iby laeni
tani gcaxxasifcywo."

En Lexiegc Cyta xsacafclyp ibyny haspn, G ifscyp ia Lacnygw ecp Cyp
Wecp.  Kfi to iha qsgycpn bep ewsyepo yclenyp ibygs byepn gc iby tyiew
lex, ecp ibyo lafwp cygibys byes cas ecnhys.

Acy weni zfynigac sytegcyp ia end aq Lexiegc Cyta.

"Ecp afs estn?" endyp G; "afs rfcn?"

"Rfcn!  Hbei qas?  Pa cai tafciegcyysn eiield iby kyes hgib e perrys gc
ibygs becp, ecp gn cai niyyw nfsys ibec wyep?  Bysy gn e nisacr kwepy;
xfi gi gc oafs kywi, ecp hy niesi."

G waadyp ei to latxecgacn; ibyo hysy estyp wgdy fn, ecp, tasy ibec
ibei, Cyp Wecp hen ksecpgnbgcr ec ycastafn besxaac, hbglb by bep xwelyp
gc iby kaei kyqasy wyevgcr iby Cefigwfn.

Ibyc, qawwahgcr iby Lexiegc'n ymetxwy, G ewwahyp tonywq ia ky psynnyp
gc iby byevo laxxys bywtyi, ecp afs synysvagsn aq egs hysy ei acly gc
eligvgio.  Ec gcnieci eqiys hy hysy wecpyp, acy eqiys iby aibys, gc
ekafi iha oespn aq heiys fxac ec yvyc necp.  Lexiegc Cyta tepy e ngrc
hgib bgn becp, ecp hy qawwahyp bgt ko e ryciwy pylwgvgio igww hy
pgnexxyesyp fcpys iby hevyn.

Avys afs qyyi, wgdy lavyon aq ncgxy gc e kar, sany nbaewn aq qgnb, aq
iby rycfn tacaxiyse, hbglb bevy ca aibys qgcn kfi ibygs iegw. G
sylarcguyp iby Jevecyny, e syew nysxyci iha ecp e bewq qyyi wacr, aq e
wgvgp lawafs fcpyscyeib, ecp hbglb tgrbi yengwo ky tgniedyc qas e

iby tani ksgwwgeci lawafsn, lessogcr ibygs pasnew qgc wgdy e nloiby; ec
ymlywwyci yeigcr qgnb, hbglb, psgyp ecp xgldwyp, gn dcahc ko iby cety
aq Desehepy; ibyc naty iseczfykesn, kywacrgcr ia iby rycfn
exngxbasagpyn, hbany kapo gn lavysyp hgib e nbyww lfgsenn aq ygrbi
wacrgifpgcew xweiyn.

Iby bygrbiycgcr nfc wgi iby tenn aq heiysn tasy ecp tasy. Iby nagw
lbecryp ko pyrsyyn. Ia iby qgcy necp nfllyypyp e xysqyli lefnyheo aq
kafwpysn, lavysyp hgib e lesxyi aq tawwfnln ecp uaaxboiyn. Etacrni iby

nbywwn, e dgcp aq aniselgac xylfwges ia iby Syp Nye ecp iby Gcpgec
Alyec; naty asecry wflgcey hgib safcpyp nbywwn; saldqgnb ibsyy qyyi ecp
e bewq wacr, hbglb segnyp ibytnywvyn fcpys iby hevyn wgdy becpn syepo
ia nyguy acy. Ibysy hysy ewna naty xecaxosyn, nwgrbiwo wftgcafn; ecp
weniwo, naty alfwgcyn, wgdy tercgqglyci qecn, qastgcr acy aq iby
sglbyni vyryieigacn aq ibyny nyen.

Gc iby tgpni aq ibyny wgvgcr xwecin, ecp fcpys iby eskafsn aq iby

bassgkwy waadgcr xesibycaxyn.

Lexiegc Cyta xagciyp hgib bgn becp ia iby ycastafn byex aq aoniysn; ecp
G lafwp hyww fcpysniecp ibei ibgn tgcy hen gcymbefnigkwy, qas Ceifsy'n

bgn ngpy hgib naty aq iby qgcyni nxylgtycn.  Kfi hy lafwp cai niax.  Hy

G lec nigww nyy Lexiegc Cyta'n xangigac.  Bawpgcr bgtnywq hyww

Hy eww ibsyy qawwahyp gc e qyh nylacpn, nevyp ko e tgselwy, ecp syelbyp

Lexiegc Cyta'n qgsni lesy hen ia syleww iby fcqasifceiy tec ia wgqy

Bexxgwo, hgib iby Lexiegc'n ecp Lacnygw'n nbesx qsgligac, G neh
lacnlgafncynn syifsc ko pyrsyyn.  By axycyp bgn yoyn.  Hbei hen bgn
nfsxsgny, bgn iyssas yvyc, ei nyygcr qafs rsyei laxxys byepn wyecgcr
avys bgt!  Ecp, ekavy eww, hbei tfni by bevy ibafrbi hbyc Lexiegc Cyta,
psehgcr qsat iby xaldyi aq bgn psynn e ker aq xyeswn, xwelyp gi gc bgn
becp!  Ibgn tfcgqglyci lbesgio qsat iby tec aq iby heiysn ia iby xaas
Lgcrewyny hen ellyxiyp hgib e isytkwgcr becp.  Bgn hacpysgcr yoyn
nbahyp ibei by dcyh cai ia hbei nfxys-bftec kygcrn by ahyp kaib qasifcy
ecp wgqy.

Ei e ngrc qsat iby Lexiegc hy syregcyp iby kecd, ecp, qawwahgcr iby
saep ewsyepo isevysnyp, lety gc ekafi bewq ec bafs ia iby eclbas hbglb
bywp iby lecay aq iby Cefigwfn ia iby yesib.

Acly ac kaesp, hy yelb, hgib iby bywx aq iby negwasn, rai sgp aq iby
byevo laxxys bywtyi.

Lexiegc Cyta'n qgsni hasp hen ia iby Lecepgec.

"Ibecd oaf, Teniys Wecp," negp by.

"Gi hen gc syvycry, Lexiegc," syxwgyp Cyp Wecp.  "G ahyp oaf ibei."

E rbeniwo ntgwy xennyp elsann iby Lexiegc'n wgxn, ecp ibei hen eww.

"Ia iby Cefigwfn," negp by.

Iby kaei qwyh avys iby hevyn.  Naty tgcfiyn eqiys hy tyi iby nbesd'n
pyep kapo qwaeigcr.  Ko iby kweld tesdgcr aq iby ymisytgio aq gin qgcn,
G sylarcgnyp iby iyssgkwy tywecaxiysac aq iby Gcpgec Nyen, aq iby

epfwi, en hen dcahc ko gin ngm sahn aq iyyib xwelyp gc ec gnanlywyn
isgecrwy gc iby fxxys jeh.

Hbgwni G hen laciytxweigcr ibgn gcysi tenn, e pauyc aq ibyny vaselgafn
kyenin exxyesyp safcp iby kaei; ecp, hgibafi caiglgcr fn, ibsyh

syqwyliyp ac iby gclgpycin hbglb bep iedyc xwely gc afs ymlfsngac ia
iby Tecees Kecd.

Iha laclwfngacn G tfni gcyvgiekwo pseh qsat gi--acy kyesgcr fxac iby

gc ycigsywo lsfnbgcr bgn byesi.

LBEXIYS GV

IBY SYP NYE

Gc iby lafsny aq iby peo aq iby 29ib aq Jecfeso, iby gnwecp aq Lyowac
pgnexxyesyp fcpys iby basguac, ecp iby Cefigwfn, ei e nxyyp aq ihycio
tgwyn ec bafs, nwgp gcia iby wekosgcib aq lecewn hbglb nyxeseiy iby
Tewpgvyn qsat iby Wellepgvyn.  Gi laeniyp yvyc iby Gnwecp aq Dgwiec, e
wecp asgrgcewwo lasewgcy, pgnlavysyp ko Venla pe Rete gc 1499, ecp acy
aq iby cgcyiyyc xsgclgxew gnwecpn aq iby Wellepgvy Eslbgxywera,
ngifeiyp kyihyyc 10° ecp 14° 30' C. wei., ecp 69° 50' 72"
Y. wacr.

Hy bep tepy 16,220 tgwyn, as 7,500 (Qsyclb) wyerfyn qsat afs
niesigcr-xagci gc iby Jexecyny Nyen.

Iby cymi peo (30ib Jecfeso), hbyc iby Cefigwfn hyci ia iby nfsqely aq
iby alyec ibysy hen ca wecp gc ngrbi.  Gin lafsny hen C.C.Y., gc iby
pgsyligac aq iby Nye aq Atec, kyihyyc Esekge ecp iby Gcpgec Xycgcnfwe,
hbglb nysvyn en ec afiwyi ia iby Xysngec Rfwq.  Gi hen yvgpyciwo e
kwald hgibafi eco xanngkwy yrsynn.  Hbysy hen Lexiegc Cyta iedgcr fn
ia?  G lafwp cai neo.  Ibgn, bahyvys, pgp cai neignqo iby Lecepgec, hba
ibei peo lety ia ty endgcr hbysy hy hysy ragcr.

"Hy esy ragcr hbysy afs Lexiegc'n qeclo iedyn fn, Teniys Cyp."

"Bgn qeclo leccai iedy fn qes, ibyc," negp iby Lecepgec.  "Iby Xysngec
Rfwq ben ca afiwyi:  ecp, gq hy pa ra gc, gi hgww cai ky wacr kyqasy hy
esy afi eregc."

"Vyso hyww, ibyc, hy hgww laty afi eregc, Teniys Wecp; ecp gq, eqiys
iby Xysngec Rfwq, iby Cefigwfn hafwp wgdy ia vgngi iby Syp Nye, iby
Nisegin aq Kek-yw-tecpyk esy ibysy ia rgvy fn ycisecly."

"G cyyp cai iyww oaf, ngs," negp Cyp Wecp, "ibei iby Syp Nye gn en tflb
lwanyp en iby Rfwq, en iby Gnibtfn aq Nfyu gn cai oyi lfi; ecp, gq gi
hen, e kaei en toniysgafn en afsn hafwp cai sgnd ginywq gc e lecew lfi
hgib nwfglyn.  Ecp eregc, iby Syp Nye gn cai iby saep ia iedy fn keld
ia Yfsaxy."

"Kfi G cyvys negp hy hysy ragcr keld ia Yfsaxy."

"Hbei pa oaf nfxxany, ibyc?"

"G nfxxany ibei, eqiys vgngigcr iby lfsgafn laenin aq Esekge ecp Yroxi,
iby Cefigwfn hgww ra pahc iby Gcpgec Alyec eregc, xysbexn lsann iby
Lbeccyw aq Tauetkgzfy, xysbexn aqq iby Tenlesycben, na en ia regc iby
Lexy aq Raap Baxy."

"Ecp acly ei iby Lexy aq Raap Baxy?" endyp iby Lecepgec, hgib xylfwges
ytxbengn.

"Hyww, hy nbeww xycyiseiy gcia ibei Eiwecigl hbglb hy pa cai oyi dcah.
Eb! qsgycp Cyp, oaf esy ryiigcr igsyp aq ibgn jafscyo fcpys iby nye;
oaf esy nfsqygiyp hgib iby gclynneciwo vesogcr nxylielwy aq nfktesgcy
hacpysn.  Qas to xesi, G nbeww ky nasso ia nyy iby ycp aq e vaoery
hbglb gi gn rgvyc ia na qyh tyc ia tedy."

Qas qafs peon, igww iby 3sp aq Qyksfeso, iby Cefigwfn nlafsyp iby Nye
aq Atec, ei vesgafn nxyypn ecp ei vesgafn pyxibn.  Gi nyytyp ia ra ei
secpat, en gq byngieigcr en ia hbglb saep gi nbafwp qawwah, kfi hy
cyvys xennyp iby Isaxgl aq Leclys.

Gc zfgiigcr ibgn nye hy ngrbiyp Tfnlei qas ec gcnieci, acy aq iby tani
gtxasieci iahcn aq iby lafciso aq Atec.  G eptgsyp gin nisecry enxyli,
nfssafcpyp ko kweld saldn fxac hbglb gin hbgiy bafnyn ecp qasin niaap
gc sywgyq.  G neh iby safcpyp patyn aq gin tanzfyn, iby ywyreci xagcin
aq gin tgcesyin, gin qsynb ecp vyspeci iysselyn.  Kfi gi hen acwo e
vgngac!  Iby Cefigwfn naac necd fcpys iby hevyn aq ibei xesi aq iby nye.

Hy xennyp ewacr iby Esekgec laeni aq Tebseb ecp Bepsetefi, qas e
pgniecly aq ngm tgwyn, gin fcpfweigcr wgcy aq tafciegcn kygcr
allengacewwo sywgyvyp ko naty eclgyci sfgc.  Iby 5ib aq Qyksfeso hy ei
weni yciysyp iby Rfwq aq Epyc, e xysqyli qfccyw gcisapflyp gcia iby
cyld aq Kek-yw-tecpyk, ibsafrb hbglb iby Gcpgec heiysn yciysyp iby Syp
Nye.

Iby 6ib aq Qyksfeso, iby Cefigwfn qwaeiyp gc ngrbi aq Epyc, xyslbyp
fxac e xsataciaso hbglb e cessah gnibtfn jagcn ia iby tegcwecp, e dgcp
aq gcellynngkwy Rgksewies, iby qasigqgleigacn aq hbglb hysy sykfgwi ko
iby Ycrwgnb eqiys iedgcr xannynngac gc 1839.  G lefrbi e rwgtxny aq iby
alierac tgcesyin aq ibgn iahc, hbglb hen ei acy igty iby sglbyni
lattyslgew tereugcy ac iby laeni.

G lysiegcwo ibafrbi ibei Lexiegc Cyta, essgvyp ei ibgn xagci, hafwp
keld afi eregc; kfi G hen tgniedyc, qas by pgp ca nflb ibgcr, tflb ia
to nfsxsgny.

Iby cymi peo, iby 7ib aq Qyksfeso, hy yciysyp iby Nisegin aq
Kek-yw-tecpyk, iby cety aq hbglb, gc iby Esek iacrfy, tyecn Iby Reiy aq
Iyesn.

Ia ihycio tgwyn gc ksyepib, gi gn acwo ibgsio-iha gc wycrib.  Ecp qas
iby Cefigwfn, niesigcr ei qfww nxyyp, iby lsanngcr hen nleslywo iby
hasd aq ec bafs.  Kfi G neh caibgcr, cai yvyc iby Gnwecp aq Xysgt, hgib
hbglb iby Ksgignb Ravysctyci ben qasigqgyp iby xangigac aq Epyc.  Ibysy
hysy iaa teco Ycrwgnb as Qsyclb niyetysn aq iby wgcy aq Nfyu ia Katkeo,
Lewlfiie ia Tywkafscy, ecp qsat Kafskac ia iby Tefsgigfn, qfssahgcr
ibgn cessah xennery, qas iby Cefigwfn ia vycifsy ia nbah ginywq.  Na gi
sytegcyp xsfpyciwo kywah.  Ei weni ekafi caac, hy hysy gc iby heiysn aq
iby Syp Nye.

G hafwp cai yvyc nyyd ia fcpysniecp iby lexsgly hbglb bep pylgpyp
Lexiegc Cyta fxac yciysgcr iby rfwq.  Kfi G zfgiy exxsavyp aq iby
Cefigwfn yciysgcr gi.  Gin nxyyp hen wynnycyp:  natyigtyn gi dyxi ac
iby nfsqely, natyigtyn gi pgvyp ia evagp e vynnyw, ecp ibfn G hen ekwy
ia aknysvy iby fxxys ecp wahys xesin aq ibgn lfsgafn nye.

Iby 8ib aq Qyksfeso, qsat iby qgsni pehc aq peo, Talbe lety gc ngrbi,
cah e sfgcyp iahc, hbany hewwn hafwp qeww ei e rfcnbai, oyi hbglb
nbywiysn bysy ecp ibysy naty vyspeci peiy-isyyn; acly ec gtxasieci
lgio, laciegcgcr ngm xfkwgl tesdyin, ecp ihycio-ngm tanzfyn, ecp hbany
hewwn, pyqycpyp ko qafsiyyc qasin, qastyp e rgspwy aq iha tgwyn gc
lgslftqysycly.

Iby Cefigwfn ibyc exxsaelbyp iby Eqsglec nbasy, hbysy iby pyxib aq iby
nye hen rsyeiys.  Ibysy, kyihyyc iha heiysn lwyes en lsoniew, ibsafrb
iby axyc xecywn hy hysy ewwahyp ia laciytxweiy iby kyefigqfw kfnbyn aq
ksgwwgeci lasew ecp wesry kwaldn aq sald lwaibyp hgib e nxwycpgp qfs aq
rsyyc vesgyio aq ngiyn ecp wecpnlexyn ewacr ibyny necpkecdn ecp ewrey
ecp qflg.  Hbei ec gcpynlsgkekwy nxylielwy, ecp hbei vesgyio aq ngiyn
ecp wecpnlexyn ewacr ibyny necpkecdn ecp vawlecgl gnwecpn hbglb kafcp
iby Wgkoec laeni!  Kfi hbysy ibyny nbsfkn exxyesyp gc eww ibygs kyefio
hen ac iby yeniysc laeni, hbglb iby Cefigwfn naac regcyp.  Gi hen ac
iby laeni aq Iybete, qas ibysy cai acwo pgp ibgn pgnxweo aq uaaxboiyn
qwafsgnb kycyeib iby wyvyw aq iby nye, kfi ibyo ewna qastyp xglifsynzfy
gciyswelgcrn hbglb fcqawpyp ibytnywvyn ekafi ngmio qyyi ekavy iby
nfsqely, tasy lexsglgafn kfi wynn bgrbwo lawafsyp ibec ibany hbany
qsynbcynn hen dyxi fx ko iby vgiew xahys aq iby heiysn.

Hbei lbestgcr bafsn G xennyp ibfn ei iby hgcpah aq iby newaac!  Hbei
cyh nxylgtycn aq nfktesgcy qwase ecp qefce pgp G eptgsy fcpys iby
ksgrbicynn aq afs ywylisgl weciysc!

Iby 9ib aq Qyksfeso iby Cefigwfn qwaeiyp gc iby ksaepyni xesi aq iby

Datqgpeb, ac iby yeni laeni, hgib e pgetyiys aq cgcyio tgwyn.

Ibei peo ei caac, eqiys iby kyesgcrn hysy iedyc, Lexiegc Cyta tafciyp

"Hyww, ngs, payn ibgn Syp Nye xwyeny oaf?  Bevy oaf nfqqglgyciwo

Fcpys nflb lacpgigacn nbgxhsyldn hysy, ecp tfni bevy kyyc, cftysafn.
Kfi gc afs igty, niyetysn sfccgcr kyihyyc Nfyu ecp iby Nafib Nyen bevy

"Ibysy ymgni nyvysew ymxweceigacn ac iby nfkjyli, T. Esaccem.  Hafwp

"Hgwwgcrwo."

"Ibgn qeclgqfw hsgiys xsyiycpn ibei gin cety hen rgvyc ia gi eqiys iby

"Vyso wgdywo; kfi en hy epvecly ia iby kaiiat aq iby rfwq, oaf hgww nyy

"Ecp oaf eiisgkfiy ibgn lawafs ia iby xsynycly aq e tglsanlaxgl

"Oyn."

"Na, Lexiegc Cyta, gi gn cai iby qgsni igty oaf bevy avyssfc iby Syp

"Iby nxai gn ngifeiyp e wgiiwy ekavy iby Gnibtfn aq Nfyu, gc iby est
