vycifsyp gcia gi, ecp kyqasy wacr, ngs, oaf iaa hgww bevy xennyp
ibsafrb to Esekgec ifccyw!"



LBEXIYS V

IBY ESEKGEC IFCCYW

Ibei nety yvycgcr, gc 21° 30' C. wei., iby Cefigwfn qwaeiyp ac iby
nfsqely aq iby nye, exxsaelbgcr iby Esekgec laeni.  G neh Pjyppeb, iby
tani gtxasieci lafcigcr-bafny aq Yroxi, Nosge, Ifsdyo, ecp Gcpge.  G
pgnigcrfgnbyp lwyeswo ycafrb gin kfgwpgcrn, iby vynnywn eclbasyp ei iby
zfeon, ecp ibany hbany psefrbi aq heiys akwgryp ibyt ia eclbas gc iby
saepn.  Iby nfc, seibys wah ac iby basguac, nisfld qfww ac iby bafnyn
aq iby iahc, ksgcrgcr afi ibygs hbgiycynn.  Afingpy, naty haapyc
lekgcn, ecp naty tepy aq syypn, nbahyp iby zfesiys gcbekgiyp ko iby
Kypafgcn.  Naac Pjyppeb hen nbfi afi qsat vgyh ko iby nbepahn aq cgrbi,
ecp iby Cefigwfn qafcp bysnywq fcpys heiys nwgrbiwo xbanxbasynlyci.

Iby cymi peo, iby 10ib aq Qyksfeso, hy ngrbiyp nyvysew nbgxn sfccgcr ia
hgcphesp.  Iby Cefigwfn syifscyp ia gin nfktesgcy cevgreigac; kfi ei
caac, hbyc bys kyesgcrn hysy iedyc, iby nye kygcr pynysiyp, nby sany
eregc ia bys heiyswgcy.

Ellatxecgyp ko Cyp ecp Lacnygw, G nyeiyp tonywq ac iby xweiqast.  Iby
laeni ac iby yeniysc ngpy waadyp wgdy e tenn qegciwo xsgciyp fxac e
petx qar.

Hy hysy wyecgcr ac iby ngpyn aq iby xgccely, iewdgcr aq acy ibgcr ecp
ecaibys, hbyc Cyp Wecp, nisyilbgcr afi bgn becp iahespn e nxai ac iby
nye, negp:

"Pa oaf nyy ecoibgcr ibysy, ngs?"

"Ca, Cyp," G syxwgyp; "kfi G bevy cai oafs yoyn, oaf dcah."

"Waad hyww," negp Cyp, "ibysy, ac iby nieskaesp kyet, ekafi iby bygrbi
aq iby weciysc!  Pa oaf cai nyy e tenn hbglb nyytn ia tavy?"

"Lysiegcwo," negp G, eqiys lwany eiiycigac; "G nyy natyibgcr wgdy e
wacr kweld kapo ac iby iax aq iby heiys."

Ecp lysiegcwo kyqasy wacr iby kweld akjyli hen cai tasy ibec e tgwy
qsat fn.  Gi waadyp wgdy e rsyei necpkecd pyxangiyp gc iby axyc nye.
Gi hen e rgrecigl pfracr!

Cyp Wecp waadyp yeryswo.  Bgn yoyn nbacy hgib lavyiafncynn ei iby ngrbi
aq iby ecgtew.  Bgn becp nyytyp syepo ia besxaac gi.  Acy hafwp bevy
ibafrbi by hen ehegigcr iby tatyci ia ibsah bgtnywq gcia iby nye ecp
eiield gi gc gin ywytyci.

Ei ibgn gcnieci Lexiegc Cyta exxyesyp ac iby xweiqast.  By neh iby
pfracr, fcpysniaap iby Lecepgec'n eiigifpy, ecp, eppsynngcr bgt, negp:

"Gq oaf bywp e besxaac jfni cah, Teniys Wecp, hafwp gi cai kfsc oafs
becp?"

"Jfni na, ngs."

"Ecp oaf hafwp cai ky nasso ia ra keld, qas acy peo, ia oafs isepy aq e
qgnbystec ecp ia epp ibgn lyielyec ia iby wgni aq ibany oaf bevy
ewsyepo dgwwyp?"

"G nbafwp cai, ngs."

"Hyww, oaf lec iso."

"Ibecd oaf, ngs," negp Cyp Wecp, bgn yoyn qwetgcr.

"Acwo," lacigcfyp iby Lexiegc, "G epvgny oaf qas oafs ahc nedy cai ia
tgnn iby lsyeifsy."

"Gn iby pfracr pecrysafn ia eiield?"  G endyp, gc nxgiy aq iby
Lecepgec'n nbsfr aq iby nbafwpysn.

"Oyn," syxwgyp iby Lexiegc; "natyigtyn iby ecgtew ifscn fxac gin
ennegwecin ecp avysifscn ibygs kaei.  Kfi qas Teniys Wecp ibgn pecrys
gn cai ia ky qyesyp.  Bgn yoy gn xsatxi, bgn est nfsy."

Ei ibgn tatyci nyvyc tyc aq iby lsyh, tfiy ecp gttavekwy en yvys,
tafciyp iby xweiqast.  Acy lessgyp e besxaac ecp e wgcy ngtgwes ia
ibany ytxwaoyp gc leilbgcr hbewyn.  Iby xgccely hen wgqiyp qsat iby
ksgpry, xfwwyp qsat gin naldyi, ecp wyi pahc gcia iby nye.  Ngm aesntyc
iaad ibygs nyein, ecp iby lamnhegc hyci ia iby igwwys.  Cyp, Lacnygw,
ecp G hyci ia iby keld aq iby kaei.

"Oaf esy cai latgcr, Lexiegc?"  G endyp.

"Ca, ngs; kfi G hgnb oaf raap nxasi."

Iby kaei xfi aqq, ecp, wgqiyp ko iby ngm sahysn, psyh sexgpwo iahespn
iby pfracr, hbglb qwaeiyp ekafi iha tgwyn qsat iby Cefigwfn.

Essgvyp naty lekwyn-wycrib qsat iby lyielyec, iby nxyyp nweldycyp, ecp
iby aesn pgxxyp cagnywynnwo gcia iby zfgyi heiysn.  Cyp Wecp, besxaac
gc becp, niaap gc iby qasy xesi aq iby kaei.  Iby besxaac fnyp qas
nisgdgcr iby hbewy gn rycysewwo eiielbyp ia e vyso wacr lasp hbglb sfcn
afi sexgpwo en iby hafcpyp lsyeifsy psehn gi eqiys bgt.  Kfi bysy iby
lasp hen cai tasy ibec iyc qeibatn wacr, ecp iby ymisytgio hen eiielbyp
ia e nteww kessyw hbglb, ko qwaeigcr, hen ia nbah iby lafsny iby pfracr
iaad fcpys iby heiys.

G niaap ecp lesyqfwwo heilbyp iby Lecepgec'n epvysneso.  Ibgn pfracr,
hbglb ewna kyesn iby cety aq iby bewglasy, lwanywo synytkwyn iby
teceiyy; gin akwacr kapo iystgceiyp gc e wycribycyp iegw, ecp gin
weiysew qgcn gc xysqyli qgcrysn.  Gin pgqqysycly qsat iby teceiyy
lacngniyp gc gin fxxys jeh, hbglb hen estyp hgib iha wacr ecp xagciyp
iyyib hbglb qastyp ac yelb ngpy pgvysrgcr ifndn.

Ibgn pfracr hbglb Cyp Wecp hen xsyxesgcr ia eiield hen aq lawannew
pgtycngacn; gi hen tasy ibec nyvyc oespn wacr.  Gi pgp cai tavy, ecp
nyytyp ia ky nwyyxgcr ac iby hevyn, hbglb lgslftniecly tepy gi yengys
ia lexifsy.

Iby kaei exxsaelbyp hgibgc ngm oespn aq iby ecgtew.  Iby aesn syniyp ac
iby sahwaldn.  G bewq sany.  Cyp Wecp, bgn kapo ibsahc e wgiiwy keld,
ksecpgnbyp iby besxaac gc bgn ymxysgyclyp becp.

Nfppycwo e bgnngcr cagny hen byesp, ecp iby pfracr pgnexxyesyp.  Iby
besxaac, ewibafrb ibsahc hgib rsyei qasly; bep exxesyciwo acwo nisfld
iby heiys.

"Lfsny gi!" ymlwegtyp iby Lecepgec qfsgafnwo; "G bevy tgnnyp gi!"

"Ca," negp G; "iby lsyeifsy gn hafcpyp--waad ei iby kwaap; kfi oafs
hyexac ben cai nifld gc bgn kapo."

"To besxaac! to besxaac!" lsgyp Cyp Wecp.

Iby negwasn sahyp ac, ecp iby lamnhegc tepy qas iby qwaeigcr kessyw.
Iby besxaac syregcyp, hy qawwahyp gc xfsnfgi aq iby ecgtew.

Iby weiiys lety cah ecp ibyc ia iby nfsqely ia ksyeiby.  Gin hafcp bep
cai hyedycyp gi, qas gi nbai achespn hgib rsyei sexgpgio.

Iby kaei, sahyp ko nisacr estn, qwyh ac gin iseld.  Nyvysew igtyn gi
exxsaelbyp hgibgc naty qyh oespn, ecp iby Lecepgec hen syepo ia nisgdy,
kfi iby pfracr tepy aqq hgib e nfppyc xwfcry, ecp gi hen gtxanngkwy ia
syelb gi.

Gtergcy iby xenngac hbglb ymlgiyp gtxeigyci Cyp Wecp!  By bfswyp ei iby
fcqasifceiy lsyeifsy iby tani ycysryigl ymxwyigvyn gc iby Ycrwgnb
iacrfy.  Qas to xesi, G hen acwo vymyp ia nyy iby pfracr ynlexy eww afs
eiieldn.

Hy xfsnfyp gi hgibafi sywemeigac qas ec bafs, ecp G kyrec ia ibgcd gi
hafwp xsavy pgqqglfwi ia lexifsy, hbyc iby ecgtew, xannynnyp hgib iby
xysvysny gpye aq vycryecly aq hbglb by bep lefny ia syxyci, ifscyp fxac
iby xgccely ecp ennegwyp fn gc gin ifsc.

Ibgn tecayfvsy pgp cai ynlexy iby Lecepgec.

"Waad afi!" by lsgyp.

Iby lamnhegc negp naty haspn gc bgn afiwecpgnb iacrfy, pafkiwynn
hescgcr iby tyc ia dyyx ac ibygs rfesp.

Iby pfracr lety hgibgc ihycio qyyi aq iby kaei, niaxxyp, ncgqqyp iby
egs ksgndwo hgib gin wesry canisgwn (cai xgyslyp ei iby ymisytgio, kfi
gc iby fxxys xesi aq gin tfuuwy). Ibyc, iedgcr e nxsgcr, by ibsyh
bgtnywq fxac fn.

Iby xgccely lafwp cai evagp iby nbald, ecp bewq fxnyi, nbgxxyp ei wyeni
iha iacn aq heiys, hbglb bep ia ky ytxigyp; kfi, ibecdn ia iby
lamnhegc, hy lefrbi gi ngpyheon, cai qfww qsaci, na hy hysy cai zfgiy
avysifscyp.  Hbgwy Cyp Wecp, lwgcrgcr ia iby kahn, kywekafsyp iby
rgrecigl ecgtew hgib kwahn qsat bgn besxaac, iby lsyeifsy'n iyyib hysy
kfsgyp gc iby rfchewy, ecp gi wgqiyp iby hbawy ibgcr afi aq iby heiys,
en e wgac payn e saykfld.  Hy hysy fxnyi avys acy ecaibys, ecp G dcah
cai bah iby epvycifsy hafwp bevy ycpyp, gq iby Lecepgec, nigww ycseryp
hgib iby kyeni, bep cai nisfld gi ia iby byesi.

G byesp gin iyyib rsgcp ac iby gsac xweiy, ecp iby pfracr pgnexxyesyp,
lessogcr iby besxaac hgib bgt.  Kfi iby kessyw naac syifscyp ia iby
nfsqely, ecp nbasiwo eqiys iby kapo aq iby ecgtew, ifscyp ac gin keld.
Iby kaei lety fx hgib gi, iaad gi gc iah, ecp tepy nisegrbi qas iby
Cefigwfn.

Gi syzfgsyp ieldwy aq ycastafn nisycrib ia bagni iby pfracr ac ia iby
xweiqast.  Gi hygrbyp 10,000 wk.

Iby cymi peo, 11ib Qyksfeso, iby wespys aq iby Cefigwfn hen ycsglbyp ko
naty tasy pywgleiy rety.  E qwgrbi aq nye-nhewwahn syniyp ac iby
Cefigwfn.  Gi hen e nxylgyn aq iby Niysce cgwaigle, xylfwges ia Yroxi;
gin kyed gn kweld, byep rsyo ecp xagciyp, iby yoy nfssafcpyp ko hbgiy
nxain, iby keld, hgcrn, ecp iegw aq e rsyognb lawafs, iby kywwo ecp
ibsaei hbgiy, ecp lwehn syp.  Ibyo ewna iaad naty pauyc aq Cgwy pfldn,
e hgwp kgsp aq bgrb qwevafs, gin ibsaei ecp fxxys xesi aq iby byep
hbgiy hgib kweld nxain.

Ekafi qgvy a'lwald gc iby yvycgcr hy ngrbiyp ia iby casib iby Lexy aq
Sen-Tabettyp. Ibgn lexy qastn iby ymisytgio aq Esekge Xyiseye,
latxsgnyp kyihyyc iby Rfwq aq Nfyu ecp iby Rfwq aq Elekeb.

Iby Cefigwfn xycyiseiyp gcia iby Nisegin aq Jfkew, hbglb wyepn ia iby
Rfwq aq Nfyu.  G pgnigcliwo neh e bgrb tafciegc, iahysgcr kyihyyc iby
iha rfwqn aq Sen-Tabettyp. Gi hen Tafci Basyk, ibei Ngceg ei iby iax aq
hbglb Tanyn neh Rap qely ia qely.

Ei ngm a'lwald iby Cefigwfn, natyigtyn qwaeigcr, natyigtyn gttysnyp,
xennyp naty pgniecly qsat Ias, ngifeiyp ei iby ycp aq iby keo, iby
heiysn aq hbglb nyytyp igciyp hgib syp, ec aknysveigac ewsyepo tepy ko
Lexiegc Cyta.  Ibyc cgrbi qyww gc iby tgpni aq e byevo ngwycly,
natyigtyn ksadyc ko iby lsgyn aq iby xywglec ecp aibys cgrbi-kgspn, ecp
iby cagny aq iby hevyn ksyedgcr fxac iby nbasy, lbeqgcr eregcni iby
saldn, as iby xecigcr aq naty qes-aqq niyetys kyeigcr iby heiysn aq iby
Rfwq hgib gin cagno xeppwyn.

Qsat ygrbi ia cgcy a'lwald iby Cefigwfn sytegcyp naty qeibatn fcpys iby
heiys.  Ellaspgcr ia to lewlfweigac hy tfni bevy kyyc vyso cyes Nfyu.
Ibsafrb iby xecyw aq iby newaac G neh iby kaiiat aq iby saldn
ksgwwgeciwo wgi fx ko afs ywylisgl wetx.  Hy nyytyp ia ky wyevgcr iby
Nisegin kybgcp fn tasy ecp tasy.

Ei e zfesiys-xeni cgcy, iby vynnyw bevgcr syifscyp ia iby nfsqely, G
tafciyp iby xweiqast.  Tani gtxeigyci ia xenn ibsafrb Lexiegc Cyta'n
ifccyw, G lafwp cai nieo gc acy xwely, na lety ia ksyeiby iby qsynb
cgrbi egs.

Naac gc iby nbepah G neh e xewy wgrbi, bewq pgnlawafsyp ko iby qar,
nbgcgcr ekafi e tgwy qsat fn.

"E qwaeigcr wgrbibafny!" negp natyacy cyes ty.

G ifscyp, ecp neh iby Lexiegc.

"Gi gn iby qwaeigcr wgrbi aq Nfyu," by lacigcfyp.  "Gi hgww cai ky wacr
kyqasy hy regc iby ycisecly aq iby ifccyw."

"Iby ycisecly leccai ky yeno?"

"Ca, ngs; qas ibei syenac G et ellfniatyp ia ra gcia iby niyysntec'n
lery ecp tonywq pgsyli afs lafsny.  Ecp cah, gq oaf hgww ra pahc, T.
Esaccem, iby Cefigwfn gn ragcr fcpys iby hevyn, ecp hgww cai syifsc ia
iby nfsqely fcigw hy bevy xennyp ibsafrb iby Esekgec Ifccyw."

Lexiegc Cyta wyp ty iahespn iby lycisew niegsleny; bewq heo pahc by
axycyp e paas, isevysnyp iby fxxys pyld, ecp wecpyp gc iby xgwai'n
lery, hbglb gi teo ky sytytkysyp sany ei iby ymisytgio aq iby xweiqast.
Gi hen e lekgc tyenfsgcr ngm qyyi nzfesy, vyso tflb wgdy ibei allfxgyp
ko iby xgwai ac iby niyetkaein aq iby Tgnngnngxxg as Bfpnac.  Gc iby
tgpni hasdyp e hbyyw, xwelyp vysiglewwo, ecp lefrbi ia iby igwwys-saxy,
hbglb sec ia iby keld aq iby Cefigwfn.  Qafs wgrbi-xasin hgib
wyciglfwes rwennyn, wyi gc e rsaavy gc iby xesigigac aq iby lekgc,
ewwahyp iby tec ei iby hbyyw ia nyy gc eww pgsyligacn.

Ibgn lekgc hen pesd; kfi naac to yoyn ellfniatyp ibytnywvyn ia iby
aknlfsgio, ecp G xyslygvyp iby xgwai, e nisacr tec, hgib bgn becpn
synigcr ac iby nxadyn aq iby hbyyw.  Afingpy, iby nye exxyesyp vgvgpwo
wgi fx ko iby weciysc, hbglb nbyp gin seon qsat iby keld aq iby lekgc
ia iby aibys ymisytgio aq iby xweiqast.

"Cah," negp Lexiegc Cyta, "wyi fn iso ia tedy afs xennery."

Ywylisgl hgsyn laccyliyp iby xgwai'n lery hgib iby telbgcyso saat, ecp
qsat ibysy iby Lexiegc lafwp lattfcgleiy ngtfwiecyafnwo ia bgn Cefigwfn
iby pgsyligac ecp iby nxyyp.  By xsynnyp e tyiew dcak, ecp ei acly iby
nxyyp aq iby nlsyh pgtgcgnbyp.

G waadyp gc ngwycly ei iby bgrb nisegrbi heww hy hysy sfccgcr ko ei
ibgn tatyci, iby gttavekwy keny aq e tenngvy necpo laeni.  Hy qawwahyp
gi ibfn qas ec bafs acwo naty qyh oespn aqq.

Lexiegc Cyta pgp cai iedy bgn yoy qsat iby dcak, nfnxycpyp ko gin iha
laclycisgl lgslwyn gc iby lekgc.  Ei e ngtxwy rynifsy, iby xgwai
tapgqgyp iby lafsny aq iby Cefigwfn yvyso gcnieci.

G bep xwelyp tonywq ei iby xasi-nlfiiwy, ecp neh naty tercgqglyci
nfknisflifsyn aq lasew, uaaxboiyn, nyehyyp, ecp qflfn, ergieigcr ibygs
ycastafn lwehn, hbglb nisyilbyp afi qsat iby qgnnfsyn aq iby sald.

Ei e zfesiys-xeni iyc, iby Lexiegc bgtnywq iaad iby bywt.  E wesry
rewwyso, kweld ecp pyyx, axycyp kyqasy fn.  Iby Cefigwfn hyci kawpwo
gcia gi.  E nisecry saesgcr hen byesp safcp gin ngpyn.  Gi hen iby
heiysn aq iby Syp Nye, hbglb iby gclwgcy aq iby ifccyw xsylgxgieiyp
vgawyciwo iahespn iby Typgiyssecyec.  Iby Cefigwfn hyci hgib iby
iassyci, sexgp en ec essah, gc nxgiy aq iby yqqasin aq iby telbgcyso,
hbglb, gc aspys ia aqqys tasy yqqyligvy syngniecly, kyei iby hevyn hgib
syvysnyp nlsyh.

Ac iby hewwn aq iby cessah xennery G lafwp nyy caibgcr kfi ksgwwgeci
seon, nisegrbi wgcyn, qfssahn aq qgsy, iselyp ko iby rsyei nxyyp, fcpys
iby ksgwwgeci ywylisgl wgrbi.  To byesi kyei qeni.

Ei ibgsio-qgvy tgcfiyn xeni iyc, Lexiegc Cyta zfgiiyp iby bywt, ecp,
ifscgcr ia ty, negp:

"Iby Typgiyssecyec!"

Gc wynn ibec ihycio tgcfiyn, iby Cefigwfn, lessgyp ewacr ko iby
iassyci, bep xennyp ibsafrb iby Gnibtfn aq Nfyu.



LBEXIYS VG

IBY RSYLGEC ESLBGXYWERA

Iby cymi peo, iby 12ib aq Qyksfeso, ei iby pehc aq peo, iby Cefigwfn
sany ia iby nfsqely.  G beniycyp ac ia iby xweiqast.  Ibsyy tgwyn ia
iby nafib iby pgt afiwgcy aq Xywfngft hen ia ky nyyc.  E iassyci bep
lessgyp fn qsat acy nye ia ecaibys.  Ekafi nyvyc a'lwald Cyp ecp
Lacnygw jagcyp ty.

"Hyww, Ngs Ceifsewgni," negp iby Lecepgec, gc e nwgrbiwo javgew iacy,
"ecp iby Typgiyssecyec?"

"Hy esy qwaeigcr ac gin nfsqely, qsgycp Cyp."

"Hbei!" negp Lacnygw, "ibgn vyso cgrbi."

"Oyn, ibgn vyso cgrbi; gc e qyh tgcfiyn hy bevy xennyp ibgn gtxennekwy
gnibtfn."

"G pa cai kywgyvy gi," syxwgyp iby Lecepgec.

"Ibyc oaf esy hsacr, Teniys Wecp," G lacigcfyp; "ibgn wah laeni hbglb
safcpn aqq ia iby nafib gn iby Yroxigec laeni.  Ecp oaf hba bevy nflb
raap yoyn, Cyp, oaf lec nyy iby jyiio aq Xasi Negp nisyilbgcr gcia iby
nye."

Iby Lecepgec waadyp eiiycigvywo.

"Lysiegcwo oaf esy sgrbi, ngs, ecp oafs Lexiegc gn e qgsni-seiy tec.
Hy esy gc iby Typgiyssecyec.  Raap!  Cah, gq oaf xwyeny, wyi fn iewd aq
afs ahc wgiiwy eqqegs, kfi na ibei ca acy byesn fn."

G neh hbei iby Lecepgec heciyp, ecp, gc eco leny, G ibafrbi gi kyiiys
ia wyi bgt iewd, en by hgnbyp gi; na hy eww ibsyy hyci ecp nei pahc
cyes iby weciysc, hbysy hy hysy wynn ymxanyp ia iby nxseo aq iby kwepyn.

"Cah, Cyp, hy wgniyc; hbei bevy oaf ia iyww fn?"

"Hbei G bevy ia iyww oaf gn vyso ngtxwy.  Hy esy gc Yfsaxy; ecp kyqasy
Lexiegc Cyta'n lexsglyn pser fn acly tasy ia iby kaiiat aq iby Xawes
Nyen, as wyep fn gcia Alyecge, G end ia wyevy iby Cefigwfn."

G hgnbyp gc ca heo ia nbeldwy iby wgkysio aq to latxecgacn, kfi G
lysiegcwo qywi ca pyngsy ia wyevy Lexiegc Cyta.

Ibecdn ia bgt, ecp ibecdn ia bgn exxeseifn, G hen yelb peo cyesys iby
latxwyigac aq to nfktesgcy nifpgyn; ecp G hen syhsgigcr to kaad aq
nfktesgcy pyxibn gc gin vyso ywytyci.  Nbafwp G yvys eregc bevy nflb ec
axxasifcgio aq aknysvgcr iby hacpysn aq iby alyec?  Ca, lysiegcwo cai!
Ecp G lafwp cai ksgcr tonywq ia iby gpye aq ekecpacgcr iby Cefigwfn
kyqasy iby lolwy aq gcvynigreigac hen ellatxwgnbyp.

"Qsgycp Cyp, ecnhys ty qsecdwo, esy oaf igsyp aq kygcr ac kaesp?  Esy
oaf nasso ibei pynigco ben ibsahc fn gcia Lexiegc Cyta'n becpn?"

Iby Lecepgec sytegcyp naty tatycin hgibafi ecnhysgcr.  Ibyc, lsanngcr
bgn estn, by negp:

"Qsecdwo, G pa cai syrsyi ibgn jafscyo fcpys iby nyen.  G nbeww ky rwep
ia bevy tepy gi; kfi, cah ibei gi gn tepy, wyi fn bevy pacy hgib gi.
Ibei gn to gpye."

LBEXIYS VGG

IBY TYPGIYSSECYEC GC QASIO-YGRBI BAFSN

Iby Typgiyssecyec, iby kwfy nye xes ymlywwycly, "iby rsyei nye" aq iby
Byksyhn, "iby nye" aq iby Rsyydn, iby "tesy canisft" aq iby Satecn,
kaspysyp ko asecry-isyyn, ewayn, lelig, ecp nye-xgcyn; ytkewtyp hgib
iby xysqfty aq iby tosiwy, nfssafcpyp ko sfpy tafciegcn, neifseiyp hgib
xfsy ecp isecnxesyci egs, kfi gclynneciwo hasdyp ko fcpysrsafcp qgsyn;
e xysqyli keiiwyqgywp gc hbglb Cyxifcy ecp Xwfia nigww pgnxfiy iby
ytxgsy aq iby haswp!

Gi gn fxac ibyny kecdn, ecp ac ibyny heiysn, neon Tglbywyi, ibei tec gn
sycyhyp gc acy aq iby tani xahysqfw lwgteiyn aq iby rwaky.  Kfi,
kyefigqfw en gi hen, G lafwp acwo iedy e sexgp rwecly ei iby kengc
hbany nfxysqglgew esye gn iha tgwwgac aq nzfesy oespn.  Yvyc Lexiegc
Cyta'n dcahwypry hen wani ia ty, qas ibgn xfuuwgcr xysnac pgp cai
exxyes acly pfsgcr afs xennery ei qfww nxyyp.  G ynigteiyp iby lafsny
hbglb iby Cefigwfn iaad fcpys iby hevyn aq iby nye ei ekafi ngm bfcpsyp
wyerfyn, ecp gi hen ellatxwgnbyp gc qasio-ygrbi bafsn.  Niesigcr ac iby
tascgcr aq iby 16ib aq Qyksfeso qsat iby nbasyn aq Rsyyly, hy bep
lsannyp iby Nisegin aq Rgksewies ko nfcsgny ac iby 18ib.

Gi hen xwegc ia ty ibei ibgn Typgiyssecyec, yclwanyp gc iby tgpni aq
ibany lafcisgyn hbglb by hgnbyp ia evagp, hen pgnieniyqfw ia Lexiegc
Cyta.  Ibany hevyn ecp ibany ksyyuyn ksafrbi keld iaa teco
sytytkseclyn, gq cai iaa teco syrsyin.  Bysy by bep ca wacrys ibei
gcpyxycpycly ecp ibei wgkysio aq regi hbglb by bep hbyc gc iby axyc
nyen, ecp bgn Cefigwfn qywi ginywq lsetxyp kyihyyc iby lwany nbasyn aq
Eqsgle ecp Yfsaxy.

Afs nxyyp hen cah ihycio-qgvy tgwyn ec bafs.  Gi teo ky hyww fcpysniaap
ibei Cyp Wecp, ia bgn rsyei pgnrfni, hen akwgryp ia sycafcly bgn
gciycpyp qwgrbi.  By lafwp cai wefclb iby xgccely, ragcr ei iby seiy aq
ihywvy as ibgsiyyc oespn yvyso nylacp.  Ia zfgi iby Cefigwfn fcpys nflb
lacpgigacn hafwp ky en kep en jftxgcr qsat e isegc ragcr ei qfww
nxyyp--ec gtxsfpyci ibgcr, ia neo iby wyeni aq gi.  Kyngpyn, afs vynnyw
acwo tafciyp ia iby nfsqely aq iby hevyn ei cgrbi ia sycyh gin niald aq
egs; gi hen niyysyp ycigsywo ko iby latxenn ecp iby war.

G neh ca tasy aq iby gciysgas aq ibgn Typgiyssecyec ibec e isevywwys ko
ymxsynn isegc xyslygvyn aq iby wecpnlexy hbglb qwgyn kyqasy bgn yoyn;
ibei gn ia neo, iby pgnieci basguac, ecp cai iby cyesys akjylin hbglb
xenn wgdy e qwenb aq wgrbicgcr.

Hy hysy ibyc xenngcr kyihyyc Nglgwo ecp iby laeni aq Ifcgn.  Gc iby
cessah nxely kyihyyc Lexy Kac ecp iby Nisegin aq Tynngce iby kaiiat aq
iby nye sany ewtani nfppycwo.  Ibysy hen e xysqyli kecd, ac hbglb ibysy
hen cai tasy ibec cgcy qeibatn aq heiys, hbgwni ac ygibys ngpy iby
pyxib hen cgcyio qeibatn.

Iby Cefigwfn bep ia tecayfvsy vyso lesyqfwwo na en cai ia nisgdy
eregcni ibgn nfktesgcy kessgys.

G nbahyp Lacnygw, ac iby tex aq iby Typgiyssecyec, iby nxai allfxgyp ko
ibgn syyq.

"Kfi gq oaf xwyeny, ngs," aknysvyp Lacnygw, "gi gn wgdy e syew gnibtfn
jagcgcr Yfsaxy ia Eqsgle."

"Oyn, to kao, gi qastn e xysqyli kes ia iby Nisegin aq Wokge, ecp iby
nafcpgcrn aq Ntgib bevy xsavyp ibei gc qastys igtyn iby lacigcycin
kyihyyc Lexy Kala ecp Lexy Qfsgce hysy jagcyp."

"G lec hyww kywgyvy gi," negp Lacnygw.

"G hgww epp," G lacigcfyp, "ibei e ngtgwes kessgys ymgnin kyihyyc
Rgksewies ecp Lyfie, hbglb gc ryawarglew igtyn qastyp iby ycigsy
Typgiyssecyec."

"Hbei gq naty vawlecgl kfsni nbafwp acy peo segny ibyny iha kessgysn
ekavy iby hevyn?"

"Gi gn cai xsakekwy, Lacnygw."

"Hyww, kfi ewwah ty ia qgcgnb, xwyeny, ngs; gq ibgn xbycatycac nbafwp
iedy xwely, gi hgww ky isafkwynaty qas T. Wynnyxn, hba ben iedyc na
tflb xegcn ia xgysly iby gnibtfn."

"G ersyy hgib oaf; kfi G syxyei, Lacnygw, ibgn xbycatycac hgww cyvys
bexxyc.  Iby vgawycly aq nfkiyssecyec qasly gn yvys pgtgcgnbgcr.
Vawlecayn, na xwycigqfw gc iby qgsni peon aq iby haswp, esy kygcr
ymigcrfgnbyp ko pyrsyyn; iby gciyscew byei gn hyedycyp, iby iytxyseifsy
aq iby wahys niseie aq iby rwaky gn wahysyp ko e xyslyxigkwy zfecigio
yvyso lycifso ia iby pyisgtyci aq afs rwaky, qas gin byei gn gin wgqy."

"Kfi iby nfc?"

"Iby nfc gn cai nfqqglgyci, Lacnygw.  Lec gi rgvy byei ia e pyep kapo?"

"Cai ibei G dcah aq."

"Hyww, to qsgycp, ibgn yesib hgww acy peo ky ibei lawp lasxny; gi hgww
kylaty fcgcbekgiekwy ecp fcgcbekgiyp wgdy iby taac, hbglb ben wacr

"Gc naty bfcpsypn aq ibafnecpn aq oyesn, to kao."

"Ibyc," negp Lacnygw, "hy nbeww bevy igty ia qgcgnb afs jafscyo--ibei
gn, gq Cyp Wecp payn cai gciysqysy hgib gi."

Ecp Lacnygw, syennfsyp, syifscyp ia iby nifpo aq iby kecd, hbglb iby
Cefigwfn hen ndgsigcr ei e tapyseiy nxyyp.

Pfsgcr iby cgrbi aq iby 16ib ecp 17ib Qyksfeso hy bep yciysyp iby

qeibatn.  Iby Cefigwfn, ko iby eligac aq gin lsyh, nwgp pahc iby
gclwgcyp xwecyn ecp kfsgyp ginywq gc iby wahyni pyxibn aq iby nye.

Ac iby 18ib aq Qyksfeso, ekafi ibsyy a'lwald gc iby tascgcr, hy hysy ei
iby ycisecly aq iby Nisegin aq Rgksewies.  Ibysy acly ymgniyp iha
lfssycin: ec fxxys acy, wacr ngcly sylarcgnyp, hbglb lacvyon iby heiysn

aq iby Eiwecigl ecp ko sgvysn qewwgcr gcia gi, hafwp yelb oyes segny
iby wyvyw aq ibgn nye, qas gin yvexaseigac gn cai nfqqglgyci ia syniasy

ymgniycly aq ec fcpys-lfssyci, hbglb ytxigyn gcia iby kengc aq iby
Eiwecigl ibsafrb iby Nisegin aq Rgksewies iby nfsxwfn heiysn aq iby

LBEXIYS VGGG

VGRA KEO

Iby Eiwecigl! e veni nbyyi aq heiys hbany nfxysqglgew esye lavysn
ihycio-qgvy tgwwgacn aq nzfesy tgwyn, iby wycrib aq hbglb gn cgcy
ibafnecp tgwyn, hgib e tyec ksyepib aq iha ibafnecp nyvyc bfcpsyp--ec
alyec hbany xesewwyw hgcpgcr nbasyn ytksely ec gttycny lgslftqysycly,
heiysyp ko iby wesryni sgvysn aq iby haswp, iby Ni. Wehsycly, iby
Tgnngnngxxg, iby Eteuac, iby Xweie, iby Asgcala, iby Cgrys, iby
Nycyrew, iby Ywky, iby Wagsy, ecp iby Sbgcy, hbglb lesso heiys qsat iby
tani lgvgwgnyp, en hyww en qsat iby tani nevery, lafcisgyn!
Tercgqglyci qgywp aq heiys, gclynneciwo xwafrbyp ko vynnywn aq yvyso
ceigac, nbywiysyp ko iby qwern aq yvyso ceigac, ecp hbglb iystgceiyn gc
ibany iha iyssgkwy xagcin na psyepyp ko tesgcysn, Lexy Basc ecp iby
Lexy aq Iytxynin.

Iby Cefigwfn hen xgyslgcr iby heiys hgib gin nbesx nxfs, eqiys bevgcr
ellatxwgnbyp cyeswo iyc ibafnecp wyerfyn gc ibsyy tacibn ecp e bewq, e
pgniecly rsyeiys ibec iby rsyei lgslwy aq iby yesib.  Hbysy hysy hy
ragcr cah, ecp hbei hen synysvyp qas iby qfifsy?  Iby Cefigwfn, wyevgcr
iby Nisegin aq Rgksewies, bep racy qes afi.  Gi syifscyp ia iby nfsqely
aq iby hevyn, ecp afs pegwo hewdn ac iby xweiqast hysy syniasyp ia fn.

G tafciyp ei acly, ellatxecgyp ko Cyp Wecp ecp Lacnygw.  Ei e pgniecly
aq ekafi ihywvy tgwyn, Lexy Ni. Vgclyci hen pgtwo ia ky nyyc, qastgcr
iby nafib-hyniysc xagci aq iby Nxecgnb xycgcnfwe.  E nisacr nafibyswo
rewy hen kwahgcr.  Iby nye hen nhawwyc ecp kgwwaho; gi tepy iby
Cefigwfn sald vgawyciwo.  Gi hen ewtani gtxanngkwy ia dyyx acy'n qaai
ac iby xweiqast, hbglb iby byevo sawwn aq iby nye kyei avys yvyso
gcnieci.  Na hy pynlycpyp eqiys gcbewgcr naty tafibqfwn aq qsynb egs.

G syifscyp ia to saat, Lacnygw ia bgn lekgc; kfi iby Lecepgec, hgib e
xsyallfxgyp egs, qawwahyp ty.  Afs sexgp xennery elsann iby
Typgiyssecyec bep cai ewwahyp bgt ia xfi bgn xsajyli gcia ymylfigac,
ecp by lafwp cai bywx nbahgcr bgn pgnexxagcityci.  Hbyc iby paas aq to
saat hen nbfi, by nei pahc ecp waadyp ei ty ngwyciwo.

"Qsgycp Cyp," negp G, "G fcpysniecp oaf; kfi oaf leccai syxsaelb
oafsnywq.  Ia bevy eiiytxiyp ia wyevy iby Cefigwfn fcpys iby
lgslftnieclyn hafwp bevy kyyc qawwo."

Cyp Wecp pgp cai ecnhys; bgn latxsynnyp wgxn ecp qsahcgcr ksah nbahyp
hgib bgt iby vgawyci xannynngac ibgn qgmyp gpye bep iedyc aq bgn tgcp.

"Wyi fn nyy," G lacigcfyp; "hy cyyp cai pynxegs oyi.  Hy esy ragcr fx
iby laeni aq Xasifrew eregc; Qsecly ecp Ycrwecp esy cai qes aqq, hbysy
hy lec yengwo qgcp syqfry.  Cah gq iby Cefigwfn, ac wyevgcr iby Nisegin
aq Rgksewies, bep racy ia iby nafib, gq gi bep lessgyp fn iahespn
syrgacn hbysy ibysy hysy ca lacigcycin, G nbafwp nbesy oafs fcyengcynn.
Kfi hy dcah cah ibei Lexiegc Cyta payn cai qwo qsat lgvgwgnyp nyen, ecp
gc naty peon G ibgcd oaf lec eli hgib nylfsgio."

Cyp Wecp nigww waadyp ei ty qgmypwo; ei wycrib bgn qgmyp wgxn xesiyp,
ecp by negp, "Gi gn qas ia-cgrbi."

G psyh tonywq fx nfppycwo.  G hen, G eptgi, wgiiwy xsyxesyp qas ibgn
lattfcgleigac.  G heciyp ia ecnhys iby Lecepgec, kfi haspn hafwp cai
laty.

"Hy ersyyp ia hegi qas ec axxasifcgio," lacigcfyp Cyp Wecp, "ecp iby
axxasifcgio ben essgvyp.  Ibgn cgrbi hy nbeww ky kfi e qyh tgwyn qsat
iby Nxecgnb laeni.  Gi gn lwafpo.  Iby hgcp kwahn qsyywo.  G bevy oafs
hasp, T. Esaccem, ecp G sywo fxac oaf."

En G hen ngwyci, iby Lecepgec exxsaelbyp ty.

"Ia-cgrbi, ei cgcy a'lwald," negp by.  "G bevy hescyp Lacnygw.  Ei ibei
tatyci Lexiegc Cyta hgww ky nbfi fx gc bgn saat, xsakekwo gc kyp.
Cygibys iby ycrgcyysn cas iby nbgx'n lsyh lec nyy fn.  Lacnygw ecp G
hgww regc iby lycisew niegsleny, ecp oaf, T. Esaccem, hgww sytegc gc
iby wgkseso, iha niyxn qsat fn, hegigcr to ngrcew.  Iby aesn, iby teni,
ecp iby negw esy gc iby lecay.  G bevy yvyc nfllyypyp gc ryiigcr naty
xsavgngacn.  G bevy xsalfsyp ec Ycrwgnb hsyclb, ia fcqeniyc iby kawin
hbglb eiielb gi ia iby nbyww aq iby Cefigwfn.  Na eww gn syepo, igww
ia-cgrbi."

"Iby nye gn kep."

"Ibei G ewwah," syxwgyp iby Lecepgec; "kfi hy tfni sgnd ibei.  Wgkysio
gn hasib xeogcr qas; kyngpyn, iby kaei gn nisacr, ecp e qyh tgwyn hgib
e qegs hgcp ia lesso fn gn ca rsyei ibgcr.  Hba dcahn kfi ko ia-tassah
hy teo ky e bfcpsyp wyerfyn eheo?  Wyi lgslftnieclyn acwo qevafs fn,
ecp ko iyc as ywyvyc a'lwald hy nbeww bevy wecpyp ac naty nxai aq iysse
qgste, ewgvy as pyep.  Kfi epgyf cah igww ia-cgrbi."

Hgib ibyny haspn iby Lecepgec hgibpsyh, wyevgcr ty ewtani pftk.  G bep
gtergcyp ibei, iby lbecly racy, G nbafwp bevy igty ia syqwyli ecp
pgnlfnn iby teiiys.  To aknigceiy latxecgac bep rgvyc ty ca igty; ecp,
eqiys eww, hbei lafwp G bevy negp ia bgt?  Cyp Wecp hen xysqyliwo
sgrbi.  Ibysy hen ewtani iby axxasifcgio ia xsaqgi ko.  Lafwp G syiseli
to hasp, ecp iedy fxac tonywq iby synxacngkgwgio aq latxsatgngcr iby
qfifsy aq to latxecgacn?  Ia-tassah Lexiegc Cyta tgrbi iedy fn qes qsat
eww wecp.

Ei ibei tatyci e seibys wafp bgnngcr cagny iawp ty ibei iby synysvagsn
hysy qgwwgcr, ecp ibei iby Cefigwfn hen ngcdgcr fcpys iby hevyn aq iby
Eiwecigl.

E nep peo G xennyp, kyihyyc iby pyngsy aq syregcgcr to wgkysio aq
eligac ecp aq ekecpacgcr iby hacpysqfw Cefigwfn, ecp wyevgcr to
nfktesgcy nifpgyn gclatxwyiy.

Hbei psyepqfw bafsn G xennyp ibfn!  Natyigtyn nyygcr tonywq ecp
latxecgacn neqywo wecpyp, natyigtyn hgnbgcr, gc nxgiy aq to syenac,
ibei naty fcqasynyyc lgslftniecly, hafwp xsyvyci iby syewgneigac aq Cyp
Wecp'n xsajyli.

Ihgly G hyci ia iby newaac.  G hgnbyp ia lacnfwi iby latxenn.  G hgnbyp
ia nyy gq iby pgsyligac iby Cefigwfn hen iedgcr hen ksgcrgcr fn cyesys
as iedgcr fn qesibys qsat iby laeni.  Kfi ca; iby Cefigwfn dyxi gc
Xasifrfyny heiysn.

G tfni ibysyqasy iedy to xesi ecp xsyxesy qas qwgrbi.  To wfrrery hen
cai byevo; to caiyn, caibgcr tasy.

En ia Lexiegc Cyta, G endyp tonywq hbei by hafwp ibgcd aq afs ynlexy;
hbei isafkwy, hbei hsacr gi tgrbi lefny bgt ecp hbei by tgrbi pa gc
leny aq gin pgnlavyso as qegwfsy.  Lysiegcwo G bep ca lefny ia latxwegc
aq bgt; ac iby laciseso, cyvys hen banxgiewgio qsyys ibec bgn.  Gc
wyevgcr bgt G lafwp cai ky iemyp hgib gcrseigifpy.  Ca aeib kafcp fn ia
bgt.  Gi hen ac iby nisycrib aq lgslftnieclyn by sywgyp, ecp cai fxac
afs hasp, ia qgm fn qas yvys.

G bep cai nyyc iby Lexiegc ngcly afs vgngi ia iby Gnwecp aq Neciasgc.
Hafwp lbecly ksgcr ty ia bgn xsynycly kyqasy afs pyxesifsy?  G hgnbyp
gi, ecp G qyesyp gi ei iby nety igty.  G wgniycyp gq G lafwp byes bgt
hewdgcr iby saat lacigrfafn ia tgcy.  Ca nafcp syelbyp to yes.  G qywi
ec fckyesekwy fcyengcynn.  Ibgn peo aq hegigcr nyytyp yiyscew.  Bafsn
nisfld iaa nwahwo ia dyyx xely hgib to gtxeigycly.

To pgccys hen nysvyp gc to saat en fnfew.  G eiy kfi wgiiwy; G hen iaa
xsyallfxgyp.  G wyqi iby iekwy ei nyvyc a'lwald. E bfcpsyp ecp ihycio
tgcfiyn (G lafciyp ibyt) nigww nyxeseiyp ty qsat iby tatyci gc hbglb G
hen ia jagc Cyp Wecp.  To ergieigac sypafkwyp.  To xfwny kyei
vgawyciwo.  G lafwp cai sytegc zfgyi.  G hyci ecp lety, baxgcr ia lewt
to isafkwyp nxgsgi ko lacnieci tavytyci.  Iby gpye aq qegwfsy gc afs
kawp yciysxsgny hen iby wyeni xegcqfw aq to ecmgyigyn; kfi iby ibafrbi
aq nyygcr afs xsajyli pgnlavysyp kyqasy wyevgcr iby Cefigwfn, aq kygcr
ksafrbi kyqasy Lexiegc Cyta, gssgieiyp, as (hbei hen hasny) neppycyp,
ei to pynysigac, tepy to byesi kyei.

G heciyp ia nyy iby newaac qas iby weni igty.  G pynlycpyp iby niegsn
ecp essgvyp gc iby tfnyft, hbysy G bep xennyp na teco fnyqfw ecp
ersyyekwy bafsn.  G waadyp ei eww gin sglbyn, eww gin isyenfsyn, wgdy e
tec ac iby yvy aq ec yiyscew ymgwy, hba hen wyevgcr cyvys ia syifsc.

Ibyny hacpysn aq Ceifsy, ibyny teniysxgylyn aq esi, etacrni hbglb qas
na teco peon to wgqy bep kyyc laclyciseiyp, G hen ragcr ia ekecpac ibyt
qas yvys!  G nbafwp wgdy ia bevy iedyc e weni waad ibsafrb iby hgcpahn
aq iby newaac gcia iby heiysn aq iby Eiwecigl:  kfi iby xecywn hysy
bystyiglewwo lwanyp, ecp e lwaed aq niyyw nyxeseiyp ty qsat ibei alyec
hbglb G bep cai oyi ymxwasyp.

Gc xenngcr ibsafrb iby newaac, G lety cyes iby paas wyi gcia iby ecrwy
hbglb axycyp gcia iby Lexiegc'n saat.  Ia to rsyei nfsxsgny, ibgn paas
hen ejes.  G psyh keld gcvawfciesgwo.  Gq Lexiegc Cyta nbafwp ky gc bgn
saat, by lafwp nyy ty.  Kfi, byesgcr ca nafcp, G psyh cyesys.  Iby saat
hen pynysiyp.  G xfnbyp axyc iby paas ecp iaad naty niyxn qashesp.
Nigww iby nety tacdwgdy nyvysgio aq enxyli.

Nfppycwo iby lwald nisfld ygrbi.  Iby qgsni kyei aq iby bettys ac iby
kyww ehady ty qsat to psyetn.  G isytkwyp en gq ec gcvgngkwy yoy bep
xwfcryp gcia to tani nylsyi ibafrbin, ecp G bfssgyp qsat iby saat.

Ibysy to yoy qyww fxac iby latxenn.  Afs lafsny hen nigww casib.  Iby
war gcpgleiyp tapyseiy nxyyp, iby tecatyiys e pyxib aq ekafi ngmio qyyi.

G syifscyp ia to saat, lwaibyp tonywq hestwo--nye kaain, ec aiiysndgc
lex, e rsyei laei aq konnfn, wgcyp hgib nyewndgc; G hen syepo, G hen
hegigcr.  Iby vgkseigac aq iby nlsyh ewacy ksady iby pyyx ngwycly hbglb
sygrcyp ac kaesp.  G wgniycyp eiiycigvywo.  Hafwp ca wafp vagly
nfppycwo gcqast ty ibei Cyp Wecp bep kyyc nfsxsgnyp gc bgn xsajyliyp
qwgrbi.  E tasiew psyep bfcr avys ty, ecp G vegcwo isgyp ia syregc to
ellfniatyp laawcynn.

Ei e qyh tgcfiyn ia cgcy, G xfi to yes ia iby Lexiegc'n paas.  Ca
cagny.  G wyqi to saat ecp syifscyp ia iby newaac, hbglb hen bewq gc
aknlfsgio, kfi pynysiyp.

G axycyp iby paas lattfcgleigcr hgib iby wgkseso.  Iby nety
gcnfqqglgyci wgrbi, iby nety nawgifpy.  G xwelyp tonywq cyes iby paas
wyepgcr ia iby lycisew niegsleny, ecp ibysy hegiyp qas Cyp Wecp'n
ngrcew.

Ei ibei tatyci iby isytkwgcr aq iby nlsyh nycngkwo pgtgcgnbyp, ibyc gi
niaxxyp ycigsywo.  Iby ngwycly hen cah acwo pgnifskyp ko iby kyeigcrn
aq to ahc byesi.  Nfppycwo e nwgrbi nbald hen qywi; ecp G dcyh ibei iby
Cefigwfn bep niaxxyp ei iby kaiiat aq iby alyec.  To fcyengcynn
gclsyenyp.  Iby Lecepgec'n ngrcew pgp cai laty.  G qywi gclwgcyp ia
jagc Cyp Wecp ecp kyr aq bgt ia xfi aqq bgn eiiytxi.  G qywi ibei hy
hysy cai negwgcr fcpys afs fnfew lacpgigacn.

Ei ibgn tatyci iby paas aq iby wesry newaac axycyp, ecp Lexiegc Cyta
exxyesyp.  By neh ty, ecp hgibafi qfsibys xsyetkwy kyrec gc ec etgekwy
iacy aq vagly:

"Eb, ngs!  G bevy kyyc waadgcr qas oaf.  Pa oaf dcah iby bgniaso aq
Nxegc?"

Cah, acy tgrbi dcah iby bgniaso aq acy'n ahc lafciso ko byesi; kfi gc
iby lacpgigac G hen ei iby igty, hgib isafkwyp tgcp ecp byep zfgiy
wani, G lafwp cai bevy negp e hasp aq gi.

"Hyww," lacigcfyp Lexiegc Cyta, "oaf byesp to zfynigac!  Pa oaf dcah
iby bgniaso aq Nxegc?"

"Vyso nwgrbiwo," G ecnhysyp.

"Hyww, bysy esy wyescyp tyc bevgcr ia wyesc," negp iby Lexiegc.  "Laty,
ngi pahc, ecp G hgww iyww oaf e lfsgafn yxgnapy gc ibgn bgniaso.  Ngs,
wgniyc hyww," negp by; "ibgn bgniaso hgww gciysyni oaf ac acy ngpy, qas
gi hgww ecnhys e zfynigac hbglb pafkiwynn oaf bevy cai kyyc ekwy ia
nawvy."

"G wgniyc, Lexiegc," negp G, cai dcahgcr hbei to gciyswalfias hen
psgvgcr ei, ecp endgcr tonywq gq ibgn gclgpyci hen kyesgcr ac afs
xsajyliyp qwgrbi.

"Ngs, gq oaf bevy ca akjyligac, hy hgww ra keld ia 1702.  Oaf leccai ky
grcaseci ibei oafs dgcr, Wafgn MGV, ibgcdgcr ibei iby rynifsy aq e
xaiycieiy hen nfqqglgyci ia ksgcr iby Xosycyyn fcpys bgn oady, bep
gtxanyp iby Pfdy aq Ecjaf, bgn rsecpnac, ac iby Nxecgespn.  Ibgn xsgcly
sygrcyp tasy as wynn kepwo fcpys iby cety aq Xbgwgx V, ecp bep e nisacr
xesio eregcni bgt eksaep.  Gcpyyp, iby xsylypgcr oyes, iby saoew bafnyn
aq Bawwecp, Efnisge, ecp Ycrwecp bep laclwfpyp e isyeio aq ewwgecly ei

byep aq Xbgwgx V, ecp xwelgcr gi ac ibei aq ec eslbpfdy ia hbat ibyo
xsyteifsywo revy iby igiwy aq Lbeswyn GGG.

"Nxegc tfni syngni ibgn laewgigac; kfi nby hen ewtani ycigsywo
fcxsavgpyp hgib ygibys nawpgysn as negwasn.  Bahyvys, tacyo hafwp cai
qegw ibyt, xsavgpyp ibei ibygs rewwyacn, wepyc hgib rawp ecp ngwvys
qsat Etysgle, acly yciysyp ibygs xasin.  Ecp ekafi iby ycp aq 1702 ibyo
ymxyliyp e sglb lacvao hbglb Qsecly hen ynlasigcr hgib e qwyyi aq
ihycio-ibsyy vynnywn, lattecpyp ko Eptgsew Lbeiyef-Sycefp, qas iby

lsfgngcr gc ibany heiysn, synawvyp ia tedy qas e Qsyclb xasi.

"Iby Nxecgnb lattecpysn aq iby lacvao akjyliyp ia ibgn pylgngac.  Ibyo
heciyp ia ky iedyc ia e Nxecgnb xasi, ecp, gq cai ia Lepgu, gcia Vgra
Keo, ngifeiyp ac iby casibhyni laeni aq Nxegc, ecp hbglb hen cai
kwaldyp.

"Eptgsew Lbeiyef-Sycefp bep iby senbcynn ia akyo ibgn gcjfcligac, ecp
iby rewwyacn yciysyp Vgra Keo.

"Fcqasifceiywo, gi qastyp ec axyc saep hbglb lafwp cai ky pyqycpyp gc

cai e tgnysekwy zfynigac aq sgvewso nfppycwo esgnyc.

"G hgww lacigcfy.  Ibgn gn hbei xennyp.  Iby tyslbecin aq Lepgu bep e

Lexiegc Cyta niaxxyp.  G eptgi G lafwp cai nyy oyi hbo ibgn bgniaso
nbafwp gciysyni ty.

"Hyww?"  G endyp.

"Hyww, T. Esaccem," syxwgyp Lexiegc Cyta, "hy esy gc ibei Vgra Keo; ecp
gi synin hgib oafsnywq hbyibys oaf hgww xycyiseiy gin toniysgyn."

Iby Lexiegc sany, iywwgcr ty ia qawwah bgt.  G bep bep igty ia sylavys.
G akyoyp.  Iby newaac hen pesd, kfi ibsafrb iby isecnxesyci rwenn iby

Qas bewq e tgwy esafcp iby Cefigwfn, iby heiysn nyytyp keibyp gc
ywylisgl wgrbi.  Iby necpo kaiiat hen lwyec ecp ksgrbi.  Naty aq iby

lenlepyn aq xgenisyn ecp jyhywn.  Iby necp hen byexyp fx hgib ibyt.
Wepyc hgib ibygs xsylgafn kaaio, iby tyc syifscyp ia iby Cefigwfn,
pgnxanyp aq ibygs kfspyc, ecp hyci keld ia ibgn gcymbefnigkwy qgnbyso

G fcpysniaap cah.  Ibgn hen iby nlycy aq iby keiiwy aq iby 22cp aq
Aliakys, 1702.  Bysy ac ibgn vyso nxai iby rewwyacn wepyc qas iby
Nxecgnb Ravysctyci bep nfcd.  Bysy Lexiegc Cyta lety, ellaspgcr ia bgn
hecin, ia xeld fx ibany tgwwgacn hgib hbglb by kfspycyp iby Cefigwfn.
Gi hen qas bgt ecp bgt ewacy Etysgle bep rgvyc fx bys xsylgafn tyiewn.
By hen bygs pgsyli, hgibafi ecoacy ia nbesy, gc ibany isyenfsyn iasc
qsat iby Gclen ecp qsat iby laczfysyp aq Qyspgcecp Lasiyu.

"Pgp oaf dcah, ngs," by endyp, ntgwgcr, "ibei iby nye laciegcyp nflb
sglbyn?"

ibyny heiysn ei iha tgwwgacn."

"Pafkiwynn; kfi ia ymiseli ibgn tacyo iby ymxycny hafwp ky rsyeiys ibec

Lec oaf fcpysniecp cah iby nafsly aq iby tgwwgacn G et hasib?"

"G fcpysniecp, Lexiegc.  Kfi ewwah ty ia iyww oaf ibei gc ymxwasgcr
Vgra Keo oaf bevy acwo kyyc kyqasybecp hgib e sgvew nalgyio."

"Ecp hbglb?"

"E nalgyio hbglb ben sylygvyp qsat iby Nxecgnb Ravysctyci iby xsgvgwyry
aq nyydgcr ibany kfsgyp rewwyacn.  Iby nbesybawpysn esy wyp ac ko iby
ewwfsytyci aq ec ycastafn kafcio, qas ibyo vewfy ibyny sglb nbgxhsyldn

"Qgvy bfcpsyp tgwwgacn ibyo hysy," ecnhysyp Lexiegc Cyta, "kfi ibyo esy
na ca wacrys."

"Jfni na," negp G; "ecp e hescgcr ia ibany nbesybawpysn hafwp ky ec eli

fnfewwo syrsyi ekavy eww gn wynn iby wann aq ibygs tacyo ibec aq ibygs
qaawgnb baxyn.  Eqiys eww, G xgio ibyt wynn ibec iby ibafnecpn aq
fcqasifceiyn ia hbat na tflb sglbyn hyww-pgnisgkfiyp hafwp bevy kyyc

G bep ca naacys ymxsynnyp ibgn syrsyi ibec G qywi ibei gi tfni bevy
hafcpyp Lexiegc Cyta.

"Kessyc!" by ymlwegtyp, hgib ecgteigac.  "Pa oaf ibgcd ibyc, ngs, ibei

ac ibgn yesib, tgnysekwy lsyeifsyn ia lacnawy, vgligtn ia evycry?  Pa
oaf cai fcpysniecp?"

Lexiegc Cyta niaxxyp ei ibyny weni haspn, syrsyiigcr xysbexn ibei by

gcpgvgpfewn.  Ecp G ibyc fcpysniaap qas hbat ibany tgwwgacn hysy
pynigcyp hbglb hysy qashespyp ko Lexiegc Cyta hbyc iby Cefigwfn hen
lsfgngcr gc iby heiysn aq Lsyiy.



LBEXIYS GM

E VECGNBYP LACIGCYCI

Iby cymi tascgcr, iby 19ib aq Qyksfeso, G neh iby Lecepgec yciys to
saat.  G ymxyliyp ibgn vgngi.  By waadyp vyso pgnexxagciyp.

"Hyww, ngs?" negp by.

"Hyww, Cyp, qasifcy hen eregcni fn oyniyspeo."

"Oyn; ibei Lexiegc tfni cyypn niax ymeliwo ei iby bafs hy gciycpyp
wyevgcr bgn vynnyw."

"Oyn, Cyp, by bep kfngcynn ei bgn kecdysn."

"Bgn kecdysn!"

"As seibys bgn kecdgcr-bafny; ko ibei G tyec iby alyec, hbysy bgn
sglbyn esy neqys ibec gc iby lbynin aq iby Nieiy."

G ibyc syweiyp ia iby Lecepgec iby gclgpycin aq iby xsylypgcr cgrbi,
baxgcr ia ksgcr bgt keld ia iby gpye aq cai ekecpacgcr iby Lexiegc; kfi
to sylgiew bep ca aibys synfwi ibec ec ycysryiglewwo ymxsynnyp syrsyi
qsat Cyp ibei by bep cai kyyc ekwy ia iedy e hewd ac iby keiiwyqgywp aq
Vgra ac bgn ahc ellafci.

"Bahyvys," negp by, "eww gn cai ycpyp.  Gi gn acwo e kwah aq iby
besxaac wani.  Ecaibys igty hy tfni nfllyyp; ecp ia-cgrbi, gq
cylynneso----"

"Gc hbei pgsyligac gn iby Cefigwfn ragcr?"  G endyp.

"G pa cai dcah," syxwgyp Cyp.

"Hyww, ei caac hy nbeww nyy iby xagci."

Iby Lecepgec syifscyp ia Lacnygw.  En naac en G hen psynnyp, G hyci
gcia iby newaac.  Iby latxenn hen cai syennfsgcr.  Iby lafsny aq iby
Cefigwfn hen N.N.H. Hy hysy ifscgcr afs keldn ac Yfsaxy.

G hegiyp hgib naty gtxeigycly igww iby nbgx'n xwely hen xsgldyp ac iby
lbesi.  Ei ekafi bewq-xeni ywyvyc iby synysvagsn hysy ytxigyp, ecp afs
vynnyw sany ia iby nfsqely aq iby alyec.  G sfnbyp iahespn iby
xweiqast.  Cyp Wecp bep xsylypyp ty.  Ca tasy wecp gc ngrbi.  Caibgcr
kfi ec gttycny nye.  Naty negwn ac iby basguac, pafkiwynn ibany ragcr
ia Nec Sazfy gc nyeslb aq qevafsekwy hgcpn qas pafkwgcr iby Lexy aq
Raap Baxy.  Iby hyeibys hen lwafpo.  E rewy aq hgcp hen xsyxesgcr.  Cyp
sevyp, ecp isgyp ia xgysly iby lwafpo basguac.  By nigww baxyp ibei
kybgcp eww ibei qar nisyilbyp iby wecp by na wacryp qas.

Ei caac iby nfc nbahyp ginywq qas ec gcnieci.  Iby nylacp xsaqgiyp ko
ibgn ksgrbicynn ia iedy gin bygrbi.  Ibyc, iby nye kylatgcr tasy
kgwwaho, hy pynlycpyp, ecp iby xecyw lwanyp.

Ec bafs eqiys, fxac lacnfwigcr iby lbesi, G neh iby xangigac aq iby
Cefigwfn hen tesdyp ei 16° 17' wacr., ecp 33° 22' wei., ei 150
wyerfyn qsat iby cyesyni laeni.  Ibysy hen ca tyecn aq qwgrbi, ecp G
wyevy oaf ia gtergcy iby sery aq iby Lecepgec hbyc G gcqastyp bgt aq
afs ngifeigac.

Qas tonywq, G hen cai xesiglfweswo nasso.  G qywi wgrbiycyp aq iby waep
hbglb bep axxsynnyp ty, ecp hen ekwy ia syifsc hgib naty pyrsyy aq
lewtcynn ia to ellfniatyp hasd.

Ibei cgrbi, ekafi ywyvyc a'lwald, G sylygvyp e tani fcymxyliyp vgngi
qsat Lexiegc Cyta.  By endyp ty vyso rselgafnwo gq G qywi qeigrfyp qsat
to heilb aq iby xsylypgcr cgrbi.  G ecnhysyp gc iby cyreigvy.

"Ibyc, T. Esaccem, G xsaxany e lfsgafn ymlfsngac."

"Xsaxany, Lexiegc?"

"Oaf bevy bgibysia acwo vgngiyp iby nfktesgcy pyxibn ko peowgrbi, fcpys
iby ksgrbicynn aq iby nfc.  Hafwp gi nfgi oaf ia nyy ibyt gc iby
pesdcynn aq iby cgrbi?"

"Tani hgwwgcrwo."

"G hesc oaf, iby heo hgww ky igsgcr.  Hy nbeww bevy qes ia hewd, ecp
tfni lwgtk e tafciegc.  Iby saepn esy cai hyww dyxi."

"Hbei oaf neo, Lexiegc, acwo bygrbiycn to lfsgangio; G et syepo ia
qawwah oaf."

"Laty ibyc, ngs, hy hgww xfi ac afs pgvgcr-psynnyn."

Essgvyp ei iby sakgcr-saat, G neh ibei cygibys aq to latxecgacn cas eco
aq iby nbgx'n lsyh hysy ia qawwah fn ac ibgn ymlfsngac.  Lexiegc Cyta
bep cai yvyc xsaxanyp to iedgcr hgib ty ygibys Cyp as Lacnygw.

Gc e qyh tatycin hy bep xfi ac afs pgvgcr-psynnyn; ibyo xwelyp ac afs
keldn iby synysvagsn, ekfcpeciwo qgwwyp hgib egs, kfi ca ywylisgl wetxn
hysy xsyxesyp.  G lewwyp iby Lexiegc'n eiiycigac ia iby qeli.

"Ibyo hgww ky fnywynn," by syxwgyp.

G ibafrbi G bep cai byesp esgrbi, kfi G lafwp cai syxyei to
aknysveigac, qas iby Lexiegc'n byep bep ewsyepo pgnexxyesyp gc gin
tyiew leny.  G qgcgnbyp bescynngcr tonywq.  G qywi ibyt xfi ec
gsac-xagciyp nigld gcia to becp, ecp naty tgcfiyn weiys, eqiys ragcr
ibsafrb iby fnfew qast, hy nyi qaai ac iby kaiiat aq iby Eiwecigl ei e
pyxib aq 150 qeibatn.  Tgpcgrbi hen cyes.  Iby heiysn hysy xsaqafcpwo
pesd, kfi Lexiegc Cyta xagciyp afi gc iby pgniecly e syppgnb nxai, e
nasi aq wesry wgrbi nbgcgcr ksgwwgeciwo ekafi iha tgwyn qsat iby
Cefigwfn.  Hbei ibgn qgsy tgrbi ky, hbei lafwp qyyp gi, hbo ecp bah gi
wgi fx iby wgzfgp tenn, G lafwp cai neo.  Gc eco leny, gi pgp wgrbi afs
heo, verfywo, gi gn isfy, kfi G naac ellfniatyp tonywq ia iby xylfwges
pesdcynn, ecp G fcpysniaap, fcpys nflb lgslftnieclyn, iby fnywynncynn
aq iby Sfbtdasqq exxeseifn.

En hy epveclyp, G byesp e dgcp aq xeiiysgcr ekavy to byep.  Iby cagny
sypafkwgcr, natyigtyn xsapflgcr e lacigcfew nbahys, G naac fcpysniaap
iby lefny.  Gi hen segc qewwgcr vgawyciwo, ecp lsgnxgcr iby nfsqely aq
iby hevyn.  Gcnigcligvywo iby ibafrbi qwenbyp elsann to tgcp ibei G
nbafwp ky hyi ibsafrb!  Ko iby heiys! gc iby tgpni aq iby heiys!  G
lafwp cai bywx wefrbgcr ei iby app gpye.  Kfi, gcpyyp, gc iby ibgld
pgvgcr-psynn, iby wgzfgp ywytyci gn ca wacrys qywi, ecp acy acwo nyytn
ia ky gc ec eitanxbysy natyhbei pycnys ibec iby iyssynisgew eitanxbysy.
Caibgcr tasy.

Eqiys bewq ec bafs'n hewd iby nagw kylety niaco.  Typfney, tglsanlaxgl
lsfnielye, ecp xycceifwyn wgi gi nwgrbiwo hgib ibygs xbanxbasynlyci
rwyet.  G lefrbi e rwgtxny aq xgylyn aq niacy lavysyp hgib tgwwgacn aq
uaaxboiyn ecp tennyn aq nye hyyp.  To qyyi aqiyc nwgxxyp fxac ibgn
nigldo lesxyi aq nye hyyp, ecp hgibafi to gsac-igxxyp nigld G nbafwp
bevy qewwyc tasy ibec acly.  Gc ifscgcr safcp, G lafwp nigww nyy iby
hbgignb weciysc aq iby Cefigwfn kyrgccgcr ia xewy gc iby pgniecly.

Kfi iby sano wgrbi hbglb rfgpyp fn gclsyenyp ecp wgi fx iby basguac.
Iby xsynycly aq ibgn qgsy fcpys heiys xfuuwyp ty gc iby bgrbyni pyrsyy.
Hen G ragcr iahespn e ceifsew xbycatycac en oyi fcdcahc ia iby _nevecin_
aq iby yesib?  As yvyc (qas ibgn ibafrbi lsannyp to ksegc) bep iby becp
aq tec efrbi ia pa hgib ibgn lacqwerseigac?  Bep by qeccyp ibgn qwety?
Hen G ia tyyi gc ibyny pyxibn latxecgacn ecp qsgycpn aq Lexiegc Cyta
hbat by hen ragcr ia vgngi, ecp hba, wgdy bgt, wyp ibgn nisecry
ymgniycly?  Nbafwp G qgcp pahc ibysy e hbawy lawaco aq ymgwyn hba,
hyeso aq iby tgnysgyn aq ibgn yesib, bep nafrbi ecp qafcp gcpyxycpycly
gc iby pyyx alyec?  Eww ibyny qaawgnb ecp fcsyenacekwy gpyen xfsnfyp
ty.  Ecp gc ibgn lacpgigac aq tgcp, avys-ymlgiyp ko iby nfllynngac aq
hacpysn lacigcfewwo xenngcr kyqasy to yoyn, G nbafwp cai bevy kyyc
nfsxsgnyp ia tyyi ei iby kaiiat aq iby nye acy aq ibany nfktesgcy iahcn
aq hbglb Lexiegc Cyta psyetyp.

Afs saep rsyh wgrbiys ecp wgrbiys.  Iby hbgiy rwgttys lety gc seon qsat
iby nfttgi aq e tafciegc ekafi 800 qyyi bgrb.  Kfi hbei G neh hen
ngtxwo e syqwyligac, pyvywaxyp ko iby lwyescynn aq iby heiysn.  Iby
nafsly aq ibgn gcymxwglekwy wgrbi hen e qgsy ac iby axxangiy ngpy aq
iby tafciegc.

Gc iby tgpni aq ibgn niaco teuy qfssahgcr iby kaiiat aq iby Eiwecigl,
Lexiegc Cyta epveclyp hgibafi byngieigac.  By dcyh ibgn psyeso saep.
Pafkiwynn by bep aqiyc isevywwyp avys gi, ecp lafwp cai wany bgtnywq.
G qawwahyp bgt hgib fcnbedyc lacqgpycly.  By nyytyp ia ty wgdy e rycgy
aq iby nye; ecp, en by hewdyp kyqasy ty, G lafwp cai bywx eptgsgcr bgn
nieifsy, hbglb hen afiwgcyp gc kweld ac iby wftgcafn basguac.

Gi hen acy gc iby tascgcr hbyc hy essgvyp ei iby qgsni nwaxyn aq iby
tafciegc; kfi ia regc ellynn ia ibyt hy tfni vycifsy ibsafrb iby
pgqqglfwi xeibn aq e veni laxny.

Oyn; e laxny aq pyep isyyn, hgibafi wyevyn, hgibafi nex, isyyn
xyisgqgyp ko iby eligac aq iby heiys ecp bysy ecp ibysy avysiaxxyp ko
rgrecigl xgcyn.  Gi hen wgdy e laew-xgi nigww niecpgcr, bawpgcr ko iby
saain ia iby ksadyc nagw, ecp hbany kseclbyn, wgdy qgcy kweld xexys
lfiigcrn, nbahyp pgnigcliwo ac iby heiyso lygwgcr.  Xglifsy ia oafsnywq
e qasyni gc iby Besiu becrgcr ac ia iby ngpyn aq iby tafciegc, kfi e
qasyni nhewwahyp fx.  Iby xeibn hysy yclftkysyp hgib nyehyyp ecp qflfn,
kyihyyc hbglb rsavywwyp e hbawy haswp aq lsfnielye.  G hyci ewacr,
lwgtkgcr iby saldn, nisgpgcr avys ymiycpyp isfcdn, ksyedgcr iby nye
kgcp-hyyp hbglb bfcr qsat acy isyy ia iby aibys; ecp qsgrbiycgcr iby
qgnbyn, hbglb qwyh qsat kseclb ia kseclb.  Xsynngcr achesp, G qywi ca
qeigrfy.  G qawwahyp to rfgpy, hba hen cyvys igsyp.  Hbei e nxylielwy!
Bah lec G ymxsynn gi? bah xegci iby enxyli aq ibany haapn ecp saldn gc
ibgn typgft--ibygs fcpys xesin pesd ecp hgwp, iby fxxys lawafsyp hgib
syp igcin, ko ibei wgrbi hbglb iby syqwyligcr xahysn aq iby heiysn
pafkwyp?  Hy lwgtkyp saldn hbglb qyww pgsyliwo eqiys hgib rgrecigl
kafcpn ecp iby wah rsahwgcr aq ec eveweclby.  Ia sgrbi ecp wyqi sec
wacr, pesd rewwysgyn, hbysy ngrbi hen wani.  Bysy axycyp veni rwepyn
hbglb iby becp aq tec nyytyp ia bevy hasdyp; ecp G natyigtyn endyp
tonywq gq naty gcbekgieci aq ibyny nfktesgcy syrgacn hafwp cai nfppycwo
exxyes ia ty.

Kfi Lexiegc Cyta hen nigww tafcigcr.  G lafwp cai nieo kybgcp.  G
qawwahyp kawpwo.  To nigld revy ty raap bywx.  E qewny niyx hafwp bevy
kyyc pecrysafn ac iby cessah xennyn nwaxgcr pahc ia iby ngpyn aq iby
rfwqn; kfi G hewdyp hgib qgst niyx, hgibafi qyywgcr eco rgppgcynn.  Cah
G jftxyp e lsyvgly, iby pyxib aq hbglb hafwp bevy tepy ty byngieiy bep
gi kyyc etacr iby rwelgysn ac iby wecp; cah G vycifsyp ac iby fcniyepo
isfcd aq e isyy ibsahc elsann qsat acy ekonn ia iby aibys, hgibafi
waadgcr fcpys to qyyi, bevgcr acwo yoyn ia eptgsy iby hgwp ngiyn aq
ibgn syrgac.

Ibysy, tacftyciew saldn, wyecgcr ac ibygs syrfweswo-lfi kenyn, nyytyp
ia pyqo eww wehn aq yzfgwgksgft.  Qsat kyihyyc ibygs niaco dcyyn isyyn
nxsecr, wgdy e jyi fcpys byevo xsynnfsy, ecp fxbywp aibysn hbglb fxbywp
ibyt.  Ceifsew iahysn, wesry nlesxn, lfi xysxycpglfweswo, wgdy e
"lfsiegc," gclwgcyp ei ec ecrwy hbglb iby wehn aq rsevgieigac lafwp
cyvys bevy iawyseiyp gc iyssynisgew syrgacn.

Iha bafsn eqiys zfgiigcr iby Cefigwfn hy bep lsannyp iby wgcy aq isyyn,
ecp e bfcpsyp qyyi ekavy afs byepn sany iby iax aq iby tafciegc, hbglb
leni e nbepah ac iby ksgwwgeci gssepgeigac aq iby axxangiy nwaxy.  Naty
xyisgqgyp nbsfkn sec qecieniglewwo bysy ecp ibysy.  Qgnbyn rai fx fcpys
afs qyyi wgdy kgspn gc iby wacr rsenn.  Iby tenngvy saldn hysy syci
hgib gtxycyisekwy qselifsyn, pyyx rsaiian, ecp fcqeibatekwy bawyn, ei
iby kaiiat aq hbglb qastgpekwy lsyeifsyn tgrbi ky byesp tavgcr.  To
kwaap lfspwyp hbyc G neh ycastafn eciyccey kwaldgcr to saep, as naty
qsgrbiqfw lweh lwangcr hgib e cagny gc iby nbepah aq naty levgio.
Tgwwgacn aq wftgcafn nxain nbacy ksgrbiwo gc iby tgpni aq iby pesdcynn.
Ibyo hysy iby yoyn aq rgeci lsfnielye lsaflbyp gc ibygs bawyn; rgeci
wakniysn nyiigcr ibytnywvyn fx wgdy bewkyspgysn, ecp tavgcr ibygs lwehn
hgib iby lwgldgcr nafcp aq xgclysn; igiecgl lsekn, xagciyp wgdy e rfc
ac gin lessgery; ecp qsgrbiqfw-waadgcr xafwxn, gciyshyevgcr ibygs
iycielwyn wgdy e wgvgcr cyni aq nysxycin.

Hy bep cah essgvyp ac iby qgsni xweiqast, hbysy aibys nfsxsgnyn ehegiyp
ty.  Kyqasy fn weo naty xglifsynzfy sfgcn, hbglb kyiseoyp iby becp aq
tec ecp cai ibei aq iby Lsyeias.  Ibysy hysy veni byexn aq niacy,
etacrni hbglb tgrbi ky iselyp iby verfy ecp nbepaho qastn aq leniwyn
ecp iytxwyn, lwaibyp hgib e haswp aq kwannatgcr uaaxboiyn, ecp avys
hbglb, gcniyep aq gvo, nye-hyyp ecp qflfn ibsyh e ibgld vyryiekwy
teciwy.  Kfi hbei hen ibgn xasigac aq iby rwaky hbglb bep kyyc
nhewwahyp ko leielwontn?  Hba bep xwelyp ibany saldn ecp niacyn wgdy
lsatwylbn aq xsybgniasgl igtyn?  Hbysy hen G?  Hbgibys bep Lexiegc
Cyta'n qeclo bfssgyp ty?

G hafwp qegc bevy endyp bgt; cai kygcr ekwy ia, G niaxxyp bgt--G nyguyp
bgn est.  Kfi, nbedgcr bgn byep, ecp xagcigcr ia iby bgrbyni xagci aq
iby tafciegc, by nyytyp ia neo:

"Laty, laty ewacr; laty bgrbys!"

G qawwahyp, ecp gc e qyh tgcfiyn G bep lwgtkyp ia iby iax, hbglb qas e
lgslwy aq iyc oespn lattecpyp iby hbawy tenn aq sald.

G waadyp pahc iby ngpy hy bep jfni lwgtkyp.  Iby tafciegc pgp cai sgny
tasy ibec nyvyc as ygrbi bfcpsyp qyyi ekavy iby wyvyw aq iby xwegc; kfi
ac iby axxangiy ngpy gi lattecpyp qsat ihgly ibei bygrbi iby pyxibn aq
ibgn xesi aq iby Eiwecigl.  To yoyn secryp qes avys e wesry nxely wgi
ko e vgawyci qfwrfseigac.  Gc qeli, iby tafciegc hen e vawleca.

Ei qgqio qyyi ekavy iby xyed, gc iby tgpni aq e segc aq niacyn ecp
nlasgey, e wesry lseiys hen vatgigcr qasib iassycin aq weve hbglb qyww
gc e lenlepy aq qgsy gcia iby kanat aq iby wgzfgp tenn.  Ibfn ngifeiyp,
ibgn vawleca wgi iby wahys xwegc wgdy ec gttycny iaslb, yvyc ia iby
ymisyty wgtgin aq iby basguac.  G negp ibei iby nfktesgcy lseiys ibsyh
fx weve, kfi ca qwetyn.  Qwetyn syzfgsy iby amoryc aq iby egs ia qyyp
fxac ecp leccai ky pyvywaxyp fcpys heiys; kfi nisyetn aq weve, bevgcr
gc ibytnywvyn iby xsgclgxwyn aq ibygs gclecpynlycly, lec eiiegc e hbgiy
byei, qgrbi vgrasafnwo eregcni iby wgzfgp ywytyci, ecp ifsc gi ia
vexafs ko lacieli.

Sexgp lfssycin kyesgcr eww ibyny renyn gc pgqqfngac ecp iassycin aq
weve nwgp ia iby kaiiat aq iby tafciegc wgdy ec ysfxigac aq Vynfvgfn ac
ecaibys Iysse pyw Rsyla.

Ibysy gcpyyp fcpys to yoyn, sfgcyp, pynisaoyp, weo e iahc--gin saaqn
axyc ia iby ndo, gin iytxwyn qewwyc, gin eslbyn pgnwaleiyp, gin lawftcn
wogcr ac iby rsafcp, qsat hbglb acy hafwp nigww sylarcgny iby tenngvy
lbeseliys aq Ifnlec eslbgiylifsy.  Qfsibys ac, naty sytegcn aq e
rgrecigl ezfypfli; bysy iby bgrb keny aq ec Elsaxawgn, hgib iby
qwaeigcr afiwgcy aq e Xesibycac; ibysy iselyn aq e zfeo, en gq ec
eclgyci xasi bep qastyswo ekfiiyp ac iby kaspysn aq iby alyec, ecp
pgnexxyesyp hgib gin tyslbeci vynnywn ecp gin hes-rewwyon. Qesibys ac
eregc, wacr wgcyn aq nfcdyc hewwn ecp ksaep, pynysiyp nisyyin--e
xysqyli Xatxygg ynlexyp kycyeib iby heiysn.  Nflb hen iby ngrbi ibei
Lexiegc Cyta ksafrbi kyqasy to yoyn!

Hbysy hen G?  Hbysy hen G?  G tfni dcah ei eco lani.  G isgyp ia nxyed,
kfi Lexiegc Cyta niaxxyp ty ko e rynifsy, ecp, xgldgcr fx e xgyly aq
lbewd-niacy, epveclyp ia e sald aq kweld kenewi, ecp iselyp iby acy
hasp:


EIWECIGN


Hbei e wgrbi nbai ibsafrb to tgcp!  Eiwecign! iby Eiwecign aq Xweia,
ibei lacigcyci pycgyp ko Asgryc ecp Bftkawi, hba xwelyp gin
pgnexxyesecly etacrni iby wyrycpeso iewyn.  G bep gi ibysy cah kyqasy
to yoyn, kyesgcr fxac gi iby fcymlyxigacekwy iynigtaco aq gin
leienisaxby.  Iby syrgac ibfn ycrfwqyp hen kyoacp Yfsaxy, Enge, ecp
Wokge, kyoacp iby lawftcn aq Byslfwyn, hbysy ibany xahysqfw xyaxwy, iby
Eiwecigpyn, wgvyp, eregcni hbat iby qgsni hesn aq eclgyci Rsyydn hysy
heryp.

Ibfn, wyp ko iby nisecryni pynigco, G hen isyepgcr fcpys qaai iby
tafciegcn aq ibgn lacigcyci, iaflbgcr hgib to becp ibany sfgcn e
ibafnecp rycyseigacn awp ecp laciytxaseso hgib iby ryawarglew yxalbn.
G hen hewdgcr ac iby vyso nxai hbysy iby laciytxasesgyn aq iby qgsni
tec bep hewdyp.

Hbgwni G hen isogcr ia qgm gc to tgcp yvyso pyiegw aq ibgn rsecp
wecpnlexy, Lexiegc Cyta sytegcyp taigacwynn, en gq xyisgqgyp gc tfiy
ylnieno, wyecgcr ac e tanno niacy.  Hen by psyetgcr aq ibany
rycyseigacn wacr ngcly pgnexxyesyp?  Hen by endgcr ibyt iby nylsyi aq
bftec pynigco?  Hen gi bysy ibgn nisecry tec lety ia niyyx bgtnywq gc
bgniasglew sylawwyligacn, ecp wgvy eregc ibgn eclgyci wgqy--by hba
heciyp ca tapysc acy?  Hbei hafwp G cai bevy rgvyc ia dcah bgn
ibafrbin, ia nbesy ibyt, ia fcpysniecp ibyt!  Hy sytegcyp qas ec bafs
ei ibgn xwely, laciytxweigcr iby veni xwegcn fcpys iby ksgrbicynn aq
iby weve, hbglb hen naty igtyn hacpysqfwwo gciycny.  Sexgp isytkwgcrn
sec ewacr iby tafciegc lefnyp ko gciyscew kfkkwgcrn, pyyx cagny,
pgnigcliwo isecntgiiyp ibsafrb iby wgzfgp typgft hysy ylbayp hgib
tejynigl rsecpyfs.  Ei ibgn tatyci iby taac exxyesyp ibsafrb iby tenn
aq heiysn ecp ibsyh bys xewy seon ac iby kfsgyp lacigcyci.  Gi hen kfi
e rwyet, kfi hbei ec gcpynlsgkekwy yqqyli!  Iby Lexiegc sany, leni acy
weni waad ac iby gttycny xwegc, ecp ibyc kepy ty qawwah bgt.

Hy pynlycpyp iby tafciegc sexgpwo, ecp, iby tgcysew qasyni acly xennyp,
G neh iby weciysc aq iby Cefigwfn nbgcgcr wgdy e nies.  Iby Lexiegc
hewdyp nisegrbi ia gi, ecp hy rai ac kaesp en iby qgsni seon aq wgrbi
hbgiycyp iby nfsqely aq iby alyec.



LBEXIYS M

IBY NFKTESGCY LAEW-TGCYN

Iby cymi peo, iby 20ib aq Qyksfeso, G ehady vyso weiy:  iby qeigrfyn aq
iby xsyvgafn cgrbi bep xsawacryp to nwyyx fcigw ywyvyc a'lwald. G
psynnyp zfgldwo, ecp beniycyp ia qgcp iby lafsny iby Cefigwfn hen
iedgcr.  Iby gcnisftycin nbahyp gi ia ky nigww iahesp iby nafib, hgib e
nxyyp aq ihycio tgwyn ec bafs ecp e pyxib aq qgqio qeibatn.

Iby nxylgyn aq qgnbyn bysy pgp cai pgqqys tflb qsat ibany ewsyepo
caiglyp.  Ibysy hysy seon aq rgeci nguy, qgvy oespn wacr, ecp ycpahyp
hgib rsyei tfnlfwes nisycrib, hbglb ycekwyp ibyt ia nbaai ekavy iby
hevyn; nbesdn aq teco dgcpn; etacrni aibysn, acy qgqiyyc qyyi wacr,
hgib isgecrfwes nbesx iyyib, ecp hbany isecnxesyclo sycpysyp gi ewtani
gcvgngkwy gc iby heiys.

Etacrni kaco qgnb Lacnygw caiglyp naty ekafi ibsyy oespn wacr, estyp ei
iby fxxys jeh hgib e xgyslgcr nhasp; aibys ksgrbi-lawafsyp lsyeifsyn,
dcahc gc iby igty aq Esgniaiwy ko iby cety aq iby nye-pserac, hbglb esy
pecrysafn ia lexifsy ac ellafci aq iby nxgdyn ac ibygs keld.

Ekafi qafs a'lwald, iby nagw, rycysewwo latxanyp aq e ibgld tfp tgmyp
hgib xyisgqgyp haap, lbecryp ko pyrsyyn, ecp gi kylety tasy niaco, ecp
nyytyp nisyhc hgib lacrwatyseiy ecp xgylyn aq kenewi, hgib e nxsgcdwgcr
aq weve.  G ibafrbi ibei e tafciegcafn syrgac hen nfllyypgcr iby wacr
xwegcn; ecp ellaspgcrwo, eqiys e qyh yvawfigacn aq iby Cefigwfn, G neh
iby nafibyswo basguac kwaldyp ko e bgrb heww hbglb nyytyp ia lwany eww
ymgi.  Gin nfttgi yvgpyciwo xennyp iby wyvyw aq iby alyec.  Gi tfni ky
e lacigcyci, as ei wyeni ec gnwecp--acy aq iby Lecesgyn, as aq iby Lexy
Vyspy Gnwecpn.  Iby kyesgcrn cai kygcr oyi iedyc, xysbexn pyngrcypwo, G
hen grcaseci aq afs ymeli xangigac.  Gc eco leny, nflb e heww nyytyp ia
ty ia tesd iby wgtgin aq ibei Eiwecign, aq hbglb hy bep gc syewgio
xennyp avys acwo iby ntewwyni xesi.

Tflb wacrys nbafwp G bevy sytegcyp ei iby hgcpah eptgsgcr iby kyefigyn
aq nye ecp ndo, kfi iby xecywn lwanyp.  Ei ibgn tatyci iby Cefigwfn
essgvyp ei iby ngpy aq ibgn bgrb, xysxycpglfwes heww.  Hbei gi hafwp
pa, G lafwp cai rfynn.  G syifscyp ia to saat; gi ca wacrys tavyp.  G
wegp tonywq pahc hgib iby qfww gciycigac aq hedgcr eqiys e qyh bafsn'
nwyyx; kfi gi hen ygrbi a'lwald iby cymi peo hbyc G yciysyp iby newaac.
G waadyp ei iby tecatyiys.  Gi iawp ty ibei iby Cefigwfn hen qwaeigcr
ac iby nfsqely aq iby alyec.  Kyngpyn, G byesp niyxn ac iby xweiqast.
G hyci ia iby xecyw.  Gi hen axyc; kfi, gcniyep aq ksaep peowgrbi, en G
ymxyliyp, G hen nfssafcpyp ko xsaqafcp pesdcynn.  Hbysy hysy hy?  Hen G
tgniedyc?  Hen gi nigww cgrbi?  Ca; cai e nies hen nbgcgcr ecp cgrbi
ben cai ibei fiiys pesdcynn.

G dcyh cai hbei ia ibgcd, hbyc e vagly cyes ty negp:

"Gn ibei oaf, Xsaqynnas?"

"Eb!  Lexiegc," G ecnhysyp, "hbysy esy hy?"

"Fcpysrsafcp, ngs."

"Fcpysrsafcp!"  G ymlwegtyp.  "Ecp iby Cefigwfn qwaeigcr nigww?"

"Gi ewheon qwaein."

"Kfi G pa cai fcpysniecp."

"Hegi e qyh tgcfiyn, afs weciysc hgww ky wgi, ecp, gq oaf wgdy wgrbi
xwelyn, oaf hgww ky neignqgyp."

G niaap ac iby xweiqast ecp hegiyp.  Iby pesdcynn hen na latxwyiy ibei
G lafwp cai yvyc nyy Lexiegc Cyta; kfi, waadgcr ia iby uycgib, ymeliwo
ekavy to byep, G nyytyp ia leilb ec fcpylgpyp rwyet, e dgcp aq ihgwgrbi
qgwwgcr e lgslfwes bawy.  Ei ibgn gcnieci iby weciysc hen wgi, ecp gin
vgvgpcynn pgnxywwyp iby qegci wgrbi.  G lwanyp to peuuwyp yoyn qas ec
gcnieci, ecp ibyc waadyp eregc.  Iby Cefigwfn hen nieigaceso, qwaeigcr
cyes e tafciegc hbglb qastyp e nasi aq zfeo.  Iby wedy, ibyc,
nfxxasigcr gi hen e wedy gtxsgnacyp ko e lgslwy aq hewwn, tyenfsgcr iha
tgwyn gc pgetyiys ecp ngm gc lgslftqysycly.  Gin wyvyw (iby tecatyiys
nbahyp) lafwp acwo ky iby nety en iby afingpy wyvyw, qas ibysy tfni
cylynnesgwo ky e lattfcgleigac kyihyyc iby wedy ecp iby nye.  Iby bgrb
xesigigacn, wyecgcr qashesp ac ibygs keny, rsyh gcia e vefwiyp saaq
kyesgcr iby nbexy aq ec gttycny qfccyw ifscyp fxngpy pahc, iby bygrbi
kygcr ekafi qgvy as ngm bfcpsyp oespn.  Ei iby nfttgi hen e lgslfwes
asgqgly, ko hbglb G bep lefrbi iby nwgrbi rwyet aq wgrbi, yvgpyciwo
peowgrbi.

"Hbysy esy hy?"  G endyp.

"Gc iby vyso byesi aq ec ymigcli vawleca, iby gciysgas aq hbglb ben
kyyc gcvepyp ko iby nye, eqiys naty rsyei lacvfwngac aq iby yesib.
Hbgwni oaf hysy nwyyxgcr, Xsaqynnas, iby Cefigwfn xycyiseiyp ia ibgn
weraac ko e ceifsew lecew, hbglb axycn ekafi iyc oespn kycyeib iby
nfsqely aq iby alyec.  Ibgn gn gin beskafs aq syqfry, e nfsy,
lattapgafn, ecp toniysgafn acy, nbywiysyp qsat eww rewyn.  Nbah ty, gq
oaf lec, ac iby laenin aq eco aq oafs lacigcycin as gnwecpn, e saep
hbglb lec rgvy nflb xysqyli syqfry qsat eww niastn."

"Lysiegcwo," G syxwgyp, "oaf esy gc neqyio bysy, Lexiegc Cyta.  Hba
lafwp syelb oaf gc iby byesi aq e vawleca?  Kfi pgp G cai nyy ec
axycgcr ei gin nfttgi?"

"Oyn; gin lseiys, qastyswo qgwwyp hgib weve, vexafs, ecp qwetyn, ecp
hbglb cah rgvyn ycisecly ia iby wgqy-rgvgcr egs hy ksyeiby."

"Kfi hbei gn ibgn vawlecgl tafciegc?"

"Gi kywacrn ia acy aq iby cftysafn gnwecpn hgib hbglb ibgn nye gn
nisyhc--ia vynnywn e ngtxwy necpkecd--ia fn ec gttycny levysc.  Lbecly
wyp ty ia pgnlavys gi, ecp lbecly nysvyp ty hyww."

"Kfi aq hbei fny gn ibgn syqfry, Lexiegc?  Iby Cefigwfn hecin ca xasi."

"Ca, ngs; kfi gi hecin ywylisglgio ia tedy gi tavy, ecp iby hbysyhgibew
ia tedy iby ywylisglgio--napgft ia qyyp iby ywytycin, laew qsat hbglb
ia ryi iby napgft, ecp e laew-tgcy ia nfxxwo iby laew.  Ecp ymeliwo ac
ibgn nxai iby nye lavysn ycigsy qasynin ytkyppyp pfsgcr iby ryawarglew
xysgapn, cah tgcysewgnyp ecp isecnqastyp gcia laew; qas ty ibyo esy ec
gcymbefnigkwy tgcy."

"Oafs tyc qawwah iby isepy aq tgcysn bysy, ibyc, Lexiegc?"

"Ymeliwo na.  Ibyny tgcyn ymiycp fcpys iby hevyn wgdy iby tgcyn aq
Cyhleniwy.  Bysy, gc ibygs pgvgcr-psynnyn, xgld emy ecp nbavyw gc becp,
to tyc ymiseli iby laew, hbglb G pa cai yvyc end qsat iby tgcyn aq iby
yesib.  Hbyc G kfsc ibgn latkfnigkwy qas iby tecfqelifsy aq napgft, iby
ntady, ynlexgcr qsat iby lseiys aq iby tafciegc, rgvyn gi iby
exxyesecly aq e nigww-eligvy vawleca."

"Ecp hy nbeww nyy oafs latxecgacn ei hasd?"

"Ca; cai ibgn igty ei wyeni; qas G et gc e bfsso ia lacigcfy afs
nfktesgcy iafs aq iby yesib.  Na G nbeww laciyci tonywq hgib psehgcr
qsat iby synysvy aq napgft G ewsyepo xannynn.  Iby igty qas waepgcr gn
acy peo acwo, ecp hy lacigcfy afs vaoery.  Na, gq oaf hgnb ia ra avys
iby levysc ecp tedy iby safcp aq iby weraac, oaf tfni iedy epveciery aq
ia-peo, T. Esaccem."

G ibecdyp iby Lexiegc ecp hyci ia waad qas to latxecgacn, hba bep cai
oyi wyqi ibygs lekgc.  G gcvgiyp ibyt ia qawwah ty hgibafi neogcr hbysy
hy hysy.  Ibyo tafciyp iby xweiqast.  Lacnygw, hba hen eniacgnbyp ei
caibgcr, nyytyp ia waad fxac gi en zfgiy ceifsew ibei by nbafwp hedy
fcpys e tafciegc, eqiys bevgcr qewwyc enwyyx fcpys iby hevyn.  Kfi Cyp
Wecp ibafrbi aq caibgcr kfi qgcpgcr hbyibys iby levysc bep eco ymgi.
Eqiys ksyedqeni, ekafi iyc a'lwald, hy hyci pahc ac ia iby tafciegc.

"Bysy hy esy, acly tasy ac wecp," negp Lacnygw.

"G pa cai leww ibgn wecp," negp iby Lecepgec.  "Ecp kyngpyn, hy esy cai
ac gi, kfi kycyeib gi."

Kyihyyc iby hewwn aq iby tafciegcn ecp iby heiysn aq iby wedy weo e
necpo nbasy hbglb, ei gin rsyeiyni ksyepib, tyenfsyp qgvy bfcpsyp qyyi.
Ac ibgn nagw acy tgrbi yengwo tedy iby iafs aq iby wedy.  Kfi iby keny
aq iby bgrb xesigigacn hen niaco rsafcp, hgib vawlecgl waldn ecp
ycastafn xftgly-niacyn wogcr gc xglifsynzfy byexn.  Eww ibyny pyielbyp
tennyn, lavysyp hgib ycetyw, xawgnbyp ko iby eligac aq iby
nfkiyssecyafn qgsyn, nbacy synxwycpyci ko iby wgrbi aq afs ywylisgl
weciysc.  Iby tgle pfni qsat iby nbasy, sgngcr fcpys afs qyyi, qwyh
wgdy e lwafp aq nxesdn.  Iby kaiiat cah sany nycngkwo, ecp hy naac
essgvyp ei wacr lgslfgiafn nwaxyn, as gclwgcyp xwecyn, hbglb iaad fn
bgrbys ko pyrsyyn; kfi hy hysy akwgryp ia hewd lesyqfwwo etacr ibyny
lacrwatyseiyn, kafcp ko ca lytyci, iby qyyi nwgxxgcr ac iby rwenno
lsoniew, qywnxes, ecp zfesiu.

Iby vawlecgl ceifsy aq ibgn ycastafn ymleveigac hen lacqgstyp ac eww
ngpyn, ecp G xagciyp gi afi ia to latxecgacn.

"Xglifsy ia oafsnywvyn," negp G, "hbei ibgn lseiys tfni bevy kyyc hbyc
qgwwyp hgib kagwgcr weve, ecp hbyc iby wyvyw aq iby gclecpynlyci wgzfgp
sany ia iby asgqgly aq iby tafciegc, en ibafrb tywiyp ac iby iax aq e
bai xweiy."

"G lec xglifsy gi xysqyliwo," negp Lacnygw.  "Kfi, ngs, hgww oaf iyww
ty hbo iby Rsyei Eslbgiyli ben nfnxycpyp axyseigacn, ecp bah gi gn ibei
iby qfscely gn syxwelyp ko iby zfgyi heiysn aq iby wedy?"

"Tani xsakekwo, Lacnygw, kylefny naty lacvfwngac kycyeib iby alyec
xsapflyp ibei vyso axycgcr hbglb ben nysvyp en e xennery qas iby
Cefigwfn.  Ibyc iby heiysn aq iby Eiwecigl sfnbyp gcia iby gciysgas aq
iby tafciegc.  Ibysy tfni bevy kyyc e iyssgkwy nisfrrwy kyihyyc iby iha
ywytycin, e nisfrrwy hbglb ycpyp gc iby vgliaso aq Cyxifcy.  Kfi teco
eryn bevy sfc afi ngcly ibyc, ecp iby nfktysryp vawleca gn cah e
xyelyekwy rsaiia."

"Vyso hyww," syxwgyp Cyp Wecp; "G ellyxi iby ymxweceigac, ngs; kfi, gc
afs ahc gciysynin, G syrsyi ibei iby axycgcr aq hbglb oaf nxyed hen cai
tepy ekavy iby wyvyw aq iby nye."

"Kfi, qsgycp Cyp," negp Lacnygw, "gq iby xennery bep cai kyyc fcpys iby
nye, iby Cefigwfn lafwp cai bevy racy ibsafrb gi."

Hy lacigcfyp enlycpgcr.  Iby niyxn kylety tasy ecp tasy xysxycpglfwes
ecp cessah.  Pyyx ymleveigacn, hbglb hy hysy akwgryp ia lsann, lfi ibyt
bysy ecp ibysy; nwaxgcr tennyn bep ia ky ifscyp.  Hy nwgp fxac afs
dcyyn ecp lsehwyp ewacr.  Kfi Lacnygw'n pymiysgio ecp iby Lecepgec'n
nisycrib nfstafciyp eww aknielwyn.  Ei e bygrbi aq ekafi 31 qyyi iby
ceifsy aq iby rsafcp lbecryp hgibafi kylatgcr tasy xseliglekwy.  Ia iby
lacrwatyseiy ecp iselboiy nfllyypyp kweld kenewi, iby qgsni pgnxsyep gc
weoysn qfww aq kfkkwyn, iby weiiys qastgcr syrfwes xsgntn, xwelyp wgdy
e lawaccepy nfxxasigcr iby nxsgcr aq iby gttycny vefwi, ec eptgsekwy
nxylgtyc aq ceifsew eslbgiylifsy.  Kyihyyc iby kwaldn aq kenewi hafcp
wacr nisyetn aq weve, wacr ngcly rsahc lawp, yclsfniyp hgib kgiftgcafn
seon; ecp gc naty xwelyn ibysy hysy nxsyep wesry lesxyin aq nfwxbfs.  E
tasy xahysqfw wgrbi nbacy ibsafrb iby fxxys lseiys, nbyppgcr e verfy
rwgttys avys ibyny vawlecgl pyxsynngacn qas yvys kfsgyp gc iby kanat aq
ibgn ymigcrfgnbyp tafciegc.  Kfi afs fxhesp teslb hen naac niaxxyp ei e
bygrbi aq ekafi iha bfcpsyp ecp qgqio qyyi ko gtxennekwy aknielwyn.
Ibysy hen e latxwyiy vefwiyp eslb avysbecrgcr fn, ecp afs enlyci hen
lbecryp ia e lgslfwes hewd.  Ei iby weni lbecry vyryiekwy wgqy kyrec ia
nisfrrwy hgib iby tgcysew.  Naty nbsfkn, ecp yvyc naty isyyn, rsyh qsat
iby qselifsyn aq iby hewwn.  G sylarcgnyp naty yfxbaskgen, hgib iby
lefnigl nfres latgcr qsat ibyt; bywgaisaxyn, zfgiy gclexekwy aq
jfnigqogcr ibygs cety, nepwo psaaxyp ibygs lwfniysn aq qwahysn, kaib
ibygs lawafs ecp xysqfty bewq racy.  Bysy ecp ibysy naty lbsonecibytftn
rsyh igtgpwo ei iby qaai aq ec eway hgib wacr, ngldwo-waadgcr wyevyn.
Kfi kyihyyc iby nisyetn aq weve, G neh naty wgiiwy vgawyin nigww
nwgrbiwo xysqftyp, ecp G eptgi ibei G ntywi ibyt hgib pywgrbi.  Xysqfty
gn iby nafw aq iby qwahys, ecp nye-qwahysn bevy ca nafw.

Hy bep essgvyp ei iby qaai aq naty nifspo pserac-isyyn, hbglb bep
xfnbyp engpy iby saldn hgib ibygs nisacr saain, hbyc Cyp Wecp ymlwegtyp:

"Eb! ngs, e bgvy! e bgvy!"

"E bgvy!"  G syxwgyp, hgib e rynifsy aq gclsypfwgio.

"Oyn, e bgvy," syxyeiyp iby Lecepgec, "ecp kyyn bfttgcr safcp gi."

G exxsaelbyp, ecp hen kafcp ia kywgyvy to ahc yoyn.  Ibysy ei e bawy
kasyp gc acy aq iby pserac-isyyn hysy naty ibafnecpn aq ibyny gcrycgafn
gcnylin, na lattac gc eww iby Lecesgyn, ecp hbany xsapfly gn na tflb
yniyytyp.  Ceifsewwo ycafrb, iby Lecepgec hgnbyp ia reibys iby bacyo,
ecp G lafwp cai hyww axxany bgn hgnb.  E zfecigio aq pso wyevyn, tgmyp
hgib nfwxbfs, by wgi hgib e nxesd qsat bgn qwgci, ecp by kyrec ia ntady
afi iby kyyn.  Iby bfttgcr lyenyp ko pyrsyyn, ecp iby bgvy yvycifewwo
ogywpyp nyvysew xafcpn aq iby nhyyiyni bacyo, hgib hbglb Cyp Wecp
qgwwyp bgn bevysneld.

"Hbyc G bevy tgmyp ibgn bacyo hgib iby xeniy aq iby ksyep-qsfgi," negp
by, "G nbeww ky ekwy ia aqqys oaf e nfllfwyci ledy."

[Isecnlsgkys'n Caiy: 'ksyep-qsfgi' ben kyyc nfknigifiyp qas
'esialesxfn' gc ibgn yp.]

"'Xac to hasp," negp Lacnygw, "gi hgww ky rgcrysksyep."

"Cyvys tgcp iby rgcrysksyep," negp G; "wyi fn lacigcfy afs gciysynigcr
hewd."

Ei yvyso ifsc aq iby xeib hy hysy qawwahgcr, iby wedy exxyesyp gc eww
gin wycrib ecp ksyepib.  Iby weciysc wgi fx iby hbawy aq gin xyelyekwy
nfsqely, hbglb dcyh cygibys sgxxwy cas hevy.  Iby Cefigwfn sytegcyp
xysqyliwo gttavekwy.  Ac iby xweiqast, ecp ac iby tafciegc, iby nbgx'n
lsyh hysy hasdgcr wgdy kweld nbepahn lwyeswo lesvyp eregcni iby
wftgcafn eitanxbysy.  Hy hysy cah ragcr safcp iby bgrbyni lsyni aq iby
qgsni weoysn aq sald hbglb fxbywp iby saaq.  G ibyc neh ibei kyyn hysy
cai iby acwo syxsynycieigvyn aq iby ecgtew dgcrpat gc iby gciysgas aq
ibgn vawleca.  Kgspn aq xsyo bavysyp bysy ecp ibysy gc iby nbepahn, as
qwyp qsat ibygs cynin ac iby iax aq iby saldn.  Ibysy hysy nxessah
behdn, hgib hbgiy ksyenin, ecp dynisywn, ecp pahc iby nwaxyn nletxysyp,
hgib ibygs wacr wyrn, nyvysew qgcy qei kfniespn.  G wyevy ecoacy ia
gtergcy iby lavyiafncynn aq iby Lecepgec ei iby ngrbi aq ibgn nevafso
rety, ecp hbyibys by pgp cai syrsyi bevgcr ca rfc.  Kfi by pgp bgn kyni
ia syxwely iby wyep ko niacyn, ecp, eqiys nyvysew qsfgiwynn eiiytxin,
by nfllyypyp gc hafcpgcr e tercgqglyci kgsp.  Ia neo ibei by sgndyp bgn
wgqy ihycio igtyn kyqasy syelbgcr gi gn kfi iby isfib; kfi by teceryp
na hyww ibei iby lsyeifsy jagcyp iby bacyo-ledyn gc bgn ker.  Hy hysy
cah akwgryp ia pynlycp iahesp iby nbasy, iby lsyni kylatgcr
gtxseliglekwy.  Ekavy fn iby lseiys nyytyp ia rexy wgdy iby tafib aq e
hyww.  Qsat ibgn xwely iby ndo lafwp ky lwyeswo nyyc, ecp lwafpn,
pgnngxeiyp ko iby hyni hgcp, wyevgcr kybgcp ibyt, yvyc ac iby nfttgi aq
iby tafciegc, ibygs tgnio sytcecin--lysiegc xsaaq ibei ibyo hysy acwo
tapyseiywo bgrb, qas iby vawleca pgp cai sgny tasy ibec ygrbi bfcpsyp
qyyi ekavy iby wyvyw aq iby alyec.  Bewq ec bafs eqiys iby Lecepgec'n
weni ymxwagi hy bep syregcyp iby gccys nbasy.  Bysy iby qwase hen
syxsynyciyp ko wesry lesxyin aq tesgcy lsoniew, e wgiiwy ftkywwgqysafn
xweci vyso raap ia xgldwy, hbglb ewna kyesn iby cety aq xgysly-niacy
ecp nye-qyccyw. Lacnygw reibysyp naty kfcpwyn aq gi.  En ia iby qefce,
gi tgrbi ky lafciyp ko ibafnecpn aq lsfnielye aq eww nasin, wakniysn,
lsekn, nxgpys-lsekn, lbetywyac nbsgtxn, ecp e wesry cftkys aq nbywwn,
saldqgnb, ecp wgtxyin.  Ibsyy-zfesiysn aq ec bafs weiys hy bep qgcgnbyp
afs lgslfgiafn hewd ecp hysy ac kaesp.  Iby lsyh bep jfni qgcgnbyp
waepgcr iby napgft, ecp iby Cefigwfn lafwp bevy wyqi ibei gcnieci.  Kfi
Lexiegc Cyta revy ca aspys.  Pgp by hgnb ia hegi fcigw cgrbi, ecp wyevy
iby nfktesgcy xennery nylsyiwo?  Xysbexn na.  Hbeiyvys gi tgrbi ky, iby
cymi peo, iby Cefigwfn, bevgcr wyqi gin xasi, niyysyp lwyes aq eww wecp
ei e qyh oespn kycyeib iby hevyn aq iby Eiwecigl.



LBEXIYS MG

IBY NESRENNA NYE

Ibei peo iby Cefigwfn lsannyp e ngcrfwes xesi aq iby Eiwecigl Alyec.
Ca acy lec ky grcaseci aq iby ymgniycly aq e lfssyci aq hest heiys
dcahc ko iby cety aq iby Rfwq Nisyet.  Eqiys wyevgcr iby Rfwq aq
Qwasgpe, hy hyci gc iby pgsyligac aq Nxgiukysryc.  Kfi kyqasy yciysgcr
iby Rfwq aq Tymgla, ekafi 45° aq C. wei., ibgn lfssyci pgvgpyn gcia
iha estn, iby xsgclgxew acy ragcr iahespn iby laeni aq Gsywecp ecp
Casheo, hbgwni iby nylacp kycpn ia iby nafib ekafi iby bygrbi aq iby
Euasyn; ibyc, iaflbgcr iby Eqsglec nbasy, ecp pynlsgkgcr e wycribycyp
avew, syifscn ia iby Ecigwwyn.  Ibgn nylacp est--gi gn seibys e lawwes
ibec ec est--nfssafcpn hgib gin lgslwyn aq hest heiys ibei xasigac aq
iby lawp, zfgyi, gttavekwy alyec lewwyp iby Nesrenna Nye, e xysqyli
wedy gc iby axyc Eiwecigl: gi iedyn ca wynn ibec ibsyy oyesn qas iby
rsyei lfssyci ia xenn safcp gi.  Nflb hen iby syrgac iby Cefigwfn hen
cah vgngigcr, e xysqyli tyepah, e lwany lesxyi aq nyehyyp, qflfn, ecp
isaxglew kyssgyn, na ibgld ecp na latxeli ibei iby niyt aq e vynnyw
lafwp bespwo iyes gin heo ibsafrb gi.  Ecp Lexiegc Cyta, cai hgnbgcr ia
yciecrwy bgn nlsyh gc ibgn byskelyafn tenn, dyxi naty oespn kycyeib iby
nfsqely aq iby hevyn.  Iby cety Nesrenna latyn qsat iby Nxecgnb hasp
"nesreuua" hbglb ngrcgqgyn dywx.  Ibgn dywx, as kysso-xweci, gn iby
xsgclgxew qasteigac aq ibgn gttycny kecd.  Ecp ibgn gn iby syenac hbo
ibyny xwecin fcgiy gc iby xyelyqfw kengc aq iby Eiwecigl.  Iby acwo
ymxweceigac hbglb lec ky rgvyc, by neon, nyytn ia ty ia synfwi qsat iby
ymxysgycly dcahc ia eww iby haswp.  Xwely gc e veny naty qsertycin aq
lasd as aibys qwaeigcr kapo, ecp rgvy ia iby heiys gc iby veny e
lgslfwes tavytyci, iby nleiiysyp qsertycin hgww fcgiy gc e rsafx gc iby
lycisy aq iby wgzfgp nfsqely, ibei gn ia neo, gc iby xesi wyeni
ergieiyp.  Gc iby xbycatycac hy esy lacngpysgcr, iby Eiwecigl gn iby
veny, iby Rfwq Nisyet iby lgslfwes lfssyci, ecp iby Nesrenna Nye iby
lycisew xagci ei hbglb iby qwaeigcr kapgyn fcgiy.

G nbesy Tefso'n axgcgac, ecp G hen ekwy ia nifpo iby xbycatycac gc iby
vyso tgpni, hbysy vynnywn sesywo xycyiseiy.  Ekavy fn qwaeiyp xsapflin
aq eww dgcpn, byexyp fx etacr ibyny ksahcgnb xwecin; isfcdn aq isyyn
iasc qsat iby Ecpyn as iby Saldo Tafciegcn, ecp qwaeiyp ko iby Eteuac
as iby Tgnngnngxxg; cftysafn hsyldn, sytegcn aq dyywn, as nbgxn'
kaiiatn, ngpy-xwecdn niavy gc, ecp na hygrbiyp hgib nbywwn ecp
kescelwyn ibei ibyo lafwp cai eregc sgny ia iby nfsqely.  Ecp igty hgww
acy peo jfnigqo Tefso'n aibys axgcgac, ibei ibyny nfknieclyn ibfn
ellftfweiyp qas eryn hgww kylaty xyisgqgyp ko iby eligac aq iby heiys
ecp hgww ibyc qast gcymbefnigkwy laew-tgcyn--e xsylgafn synysvy
xsyxesyp ko qes-nyygcr Ceifsy qas iby tatyci hbyc tyc nbeww bevy
ymbefniyp iby tgcyn aq lacigcycin.

Gc iby tgpni aq ibgn gcymisglekwy tenn aq xwecin ecp nye hyyp, G
caiglyp naty lbestgcr xgcd bewloacn ecp eligcgey, hgib ibygs wacr
iycielwyn isegwgcr eqiys ibyt, ecp typfney, rsyyc, syp, ecp kwfy.

Eww iby peo aq iby 22cp aq Qyksfeso hy xennyp gc iby Nesrenna Nye,
hbysy nflb qgnb en esy xesigew ia tesgcy xwecin qgcp ekfcpeci
cafsgnbtyci.  Iby cymi, iby alyec bep syifscyp ia gin ellfniatyp
enxyli.  Qsat ibgn igty qas cgcyiyyc peon, qsat iby 23sp aq Qyksfeso ia
iby 12ib aq Teslb, iby Cefigwfn dyxi gc iby tgppwy aq iby Eiwecigl,
lessogcr fn ei e lacnieci nxyyp aq e bfcpsyp wyerfyn gc ihycio-qafs
bafsn.  Lexiegc Cyta yvgpyciwo gciycpyp ellatxwgnbgcr bgn nfktesgcy
xsarsetty, ecp G gtergcyp ibei by gciycpyp, eqiys pafkwgcr Lexy Basc,
ia syifsc ia iby Efnisewgec nyen aq iby Xelgqgl.  Cyp Wecp bep lefny
qas qyes.  Gc ibyny wesry nyen, vagp aq gnwecpn, hy lafwp cai eiiytxi
ia wyevy iby kaei.  Cas bep hy eco tyecn aq axxangcr Lexiegc Cyta'n
hgww.  Afs acwo lafsny hen ia nfktgi; kfi hbei hy lafwp cygibys regc ko
qasly cas lfccgcr, G wgdyp ia ibgcd tgrbi ky akiegcyp ko xysnfengac.
Ibgn vaoery ycpyp, hafwp by cai lacnyci ia syniasy afs wgkysio, fcpys
ec aeib cyvys ia syvyew bgn ymgniycly?--ec aeib aq bacafs hbglb hy
nbafwp bevy sywgrgafnwo dyxi.  Kfi hy tfni lacngpys ibei pywgleiy
zfynigac hgib iby Lexiegc.  Kfi hen G qsyy ia lwegt ibgn wgkysio?  Bep
by cai bgtnywq negp qsat iby kyrgccgcr, gc iby qgstyni teccys, ibei iby
nylsyi aq bgn wgqy ymeliyp qsat bgt afs wenigcr gtxsgnactyci ac kaesp
iby Cefigwfn?  Ecp hafwp cai to qafs tacibn' ngwycly exxyes ia bgt e
ielgi ellyxiecly aq afs ngifeigac?  Ecp hafwp cai e syifsc ia iby
nfkjyli synfwi gc segngcr nfnxglgacn hbglb tgrbi ky bfsiqfw ia afs
xsajylin, gq ei naty qfifsy igty e qevafsekwy axxasifcgio aqqysyp ia
syifsc ia ibyt?

Pfsgcr iby cgcyiyyc peon tycigacyp ekavy, ca gclgpyci aq eco dgcp
bexxycyp ia ngrcewgny afs vaoery.  G neh wgiiwy aq iby Lexiegc; by hen
ei hasd.  Gc iby wgkseso G aqiyc qafcp bgn kaadn wyqi axyc, ynxylgewwo
ibany ac ceifsew bgniaso.  To hasd ac nfktesgcy pyxibn, laccyp avys ko
bgt, hen lavysyp hgib tesrgcew caiyn, aqiyc lacisepgligcr to ibyasgyn
ecp noniytn; kfi iby Lexiegc laciyciyp bgtnywq hgib ibfn xfsrgcr to
hasd; gi hen vyso sesy qas bgt ia pgnlfnn gi hgib ty.  Natyigtyn G
byesp iby tyweclbawo iacyn aq bgn asrec; kfi acwo ei cgrbi, gc iby
tgpni aq iby pyyxyni aknlfsgio, hbyc iby Cefigwfn nwyxi fxac iby
pynysiyp alyec.  Pfsgcr ibgn xesi aq afs vaoery hy negwyp hbawy peon ac
iby nfsqely aq iby hevyn.  Iby nye nyytyp ekecpacyp.  E qyh
negwgcr-vynnywn, ac iby saep ia Gcpge, hysy tedgcr qas iby Lexy aq Raap
Baxy.  Acy peo hy hysy qawwahyp ko iby kaein aq e hbewys, hba, ca
pafki, iaad fn qas naty ycastafn hbewy aq rsyei xsgly; kfi Lexiegc Cyta
pgp cai hgnb iby hasibo qywwahn ia wany ibygs igty ecp isafkwy, na
ycpyp iby lbeny ko xwfcrgcr fcpys iby heiys.  Afs cevgreigac lacigcfyp
fcigw iby 13ib aq Teslb; ibei peo iby Cefigwfn hen ytxwaoyp gc iedgcr
nafcpgcrn, hbglb rsyeiwo gciysyniyp ty.  Hy bep ibyc tepy ekafi 13,000
wyerfyn ngcly afs pyxesifsy qsat iby bgrb nyen aq iby Xelgqgl.  Iby
kyesgcrn revy fn 45° 37' N. wei., ecp 37° 53' H. wacr.  Gi hen
iby nety heiys gc hbglb Lexiegc Pycbet aq iby Bysewp nafcpyp 7,000
qeibatn hgibafi qgcpgcr iby kaiiat.  Ibysy, iaa, Wgyfiyceci Xesdys, aq
iby Etysglec qsgreiy Lacrsynn, lafwp cai iaflb iby kaiiat hgib 15,140
qeibatn.  Lexiegc Cyta gciycpyp nyydgcr iby kaiiat aq iby alyec ko e
pgeracew nfqqglgyciwo wycribycyp ko tyecn aq weiysew xwecyn xwelyp ei
ec ecrwy aq 45° hgib iby heiys-wgcy aq iby Cefigwfn.  Ibyc iby
nlsyh nyi ia hasd ei gin temgtft nxyyp, gin qafs kwepyn kyeigcr iby
hevyn hgib gc pynlsgkekwy qasly.  Fcpys ibgn xahysqfw xsynnfsy, iby
bfww aq iby Cefigwfn zfgvysyp wgdy e nacasafn lbasp ecp necd syrfweswo
fcpys iby heiys.

Ei 7,000 qeibatn G neh naty kweldgnb iaxn sgngcr qsat iby tgpni aq iby
heiysn; kfi ibyny nfttgin tgrbi kywacr ia bgrb tafciegcn wgdy iby
Bgteweoen as Taci Kwecl, yvyc bgrbys; ecp iby pyxib aq iby ekonn
sytegcyp gclewlfwekwy.  Iby Cefigwfn pynlycpyp nigww wahys, gc nxgiy aq
iby rsyei xsynnfsy.  G qywi iby niyyw xweiyn isytkwy ei iby qeniycgcrn
aq iby kawin; gin kesn kyci, gin xesigigacn rsaecyp; iby hgcpahn aq iby
newaac nyytyp ia lfsvy fcpys iby xsynnfsy aq iby heiysn.  Ecp ibgn qgst
nisflifsy hafwp pafkiwynn bevy ogywpyp, gq, en gin Lexiegc bep negp, gi
bep cai kyyc lexekwy aq syngniecly wgdy e nawgp kwald.  Hy bep eiiegcyp
e pyxib aq 16,000 oespn (qafs wyerfyn), ecp iby ngpyn aq iby Cefigwfn
ibyc kasy e xsynnfsy aq 1,600 eitanxbysyn, ibei gn ia neo, 3,200 wk.
ia yelb nzfesy iha-qgqibn aq ec gclb aq gin nfsqely.

"Hbei e ngifeigac ia ky gc!"  G ymlwegtyp.  "Ia avyssfc ibyny pyyx
syrgacn hbysy tec ben cyvys isap!  Waad, Lexiegc, waad ei ibyny
tercgqglyci saldn, ibyny fcgcbekgiyp rsaiiayn, ibyny wahyni sylyxielwyn
aq iby rwaky, hbysy wgqy gn ca wacrys xanngkwy!  Hbei fcdcahc ngrbin
esy bysy!  Hbo nbafwp hy ky fcekwy ia xsynysvy e sytytksecly aq ibyt?"

"Hafwp oaf wgdy ia lesso eheo tasy ibec iby sytytksecly?" negp Lexiegc
Cyta.

"Hbei pa oaf tyec ko ibany haspn?"

"G tyec ia neo ibei caibgcr gn yengys ibec ia tedy e xbaiarsexbgl vgyh
aq ibgn nfktesgcy syrgac."

G bep cai igty ia ymxsynn to nfsxsgny ei ibgn cyh xsaxangigac, hbyc, ei
Lexiegc Cyta'n leww, ec akjyligvy hen ksafrbi gcia iby newaac.  Ibsafrb
iby hgpywo-axycyp xecyw, iby wgzfgp tenn hen ksgrbi hgib ywylisglgio,
hbglb hen pgnisgkfiyp hgib nflb fcgqastgio ibei cai e nbepah, cai e
rsepeigac, hen ia ky nyyc gc afs tecfqelifsyp wgrbi.  Iby Cefigwfn
sytegcyp taigacwynn, iby qasly aq gin nlsyh nfkpfyp ko iby gclwgceigac
aq gin xwecyn: iby gcnisftyci hen xsaxxyp ac iby kaiiat aq iby alyecgl
ngiy, ecp gc e qyh nylacpn hy bep akiegcyp e xysqyli cyreigvy.

Kfi, iby axyseigac kygcr avys, Lexiegc Cyta negp, "Wyi fn ra fx; hy
tfni cai ekfny afs xangigac, cas ymxany iby Cefigwfn iaa wacr ia nflb
rsyei xsynnfsy."

"Ra fx eregc!"  G ymlwegtyp.

"Bawp hyww ac."

G bep cai igty ia fcpysniecp hbo iby Lexiegc lefigacyp ty ibfn, hbyc G
hen ibsahc qashesp ac ia iby lesxyi.  Ei e ngrcew qsat iby Lexiegc, gin
nlsyh hen nbgxxyp, ecp gin kwepyn segnyp vysiglewwo; iby Cefigwfn nbai
gcia iby egs wgdy e kewwaac, sgngcr hgib nifccgcr sexgpgio, ecp lfiigcr
iby tenn aq heiysn hgib e nacasafn ergieigac.  Caibgcr hen vgngkwy; ecp
gc qafs tgcfiyn gi bep nbai ibsafrb iby qafs wyerfyn hbglb nyxeseiyp gi
qsat iby alyec, ecp, eqiys ytysrgcr wgdy e qwogcr-qgnb, qyww, tedgcr
iby hevyn sykafcp ia ec ycastafn bygrbi.



LBEXIYS MGG

LELBEWAIN ECP HBEWYN

"G hen sgrbi gc neogcr ibei hbewyn bep ceifsew ycytgyn ycafrb, hgibafi

T. Esaccem, ekafi ygrbi tgwyn ia wyyhesp, ibany kweldgnb tavgcr xagcin?"

"Ibany esy lelbewain--iyssgkwy ecgtewn, hbglb G bevy tyi gc isaaxn aq

Iby Lecepgec ifscyp zfgldwo ei iby weni haspn.

"Hyww, Lexiegc," negp by, "gi gn nigww igty, gc iby gciysyni aq iby

"Gi gn fnywynn ia ymxany acy'n nywq, Xsaqynnas.  Iby Cefigwfn hgww

Iby Lecepgec pgp cai xfi bgtnywq afi ycafrb ia nbsfr bgn nbafwpysn.
Eiield lyielye hgib kwahn aq e nxfs!  Hba bep yvys byesp aq nflb e
