Ibyo esy caibgcr kfi tafib ecp iyyib."

Tafib ecp iyyib!  Ca acy lafwp kyiiys pynlsgky iby telsalyxbewafn
lelbewai, hbglb gn natyigtyn tasy ibec nyvycio-qgvy qyyi wacr.  Gin
ycastafn byep allfxgyn acy-ibgsp aq gin ycigsy kapo.  Kyiiys estyp ibec
iby hbewy, hbany fxxys jeh gn qfscgnbyp acwo hgib hbewykacy, gi gn
nfxxwgyp hgib ihycio-qgvy wesry ifndn, ekafi ygrbi gclbyn wacr,
lowgcpsglew ecp lacglew ei iby iax, yelb hygrbgcr iha xafcpn.  Gi gn gc
iby fxxys xesi aq ibgn ycastafn byep, gc rsyei levgigyn pgvgpyp ko
lesigweryn, ibei gn ia ky qafcp qsat ngm ia ygrbi bfcpsyp xafcpn aq
ibei xsylgafn agw lewwyp nxystelyig.  Iby lelbewai gn e pgnersyyekwy
lsyeifsy, tasy iepxawy ibec qgnb, ellaspgcr ia Qsypaw'n pynlsgxigac.
Gi gn kepwo qastyp, iby hbawy aq gin wyqi ngpy kygcr (gq hy teo neo
gi), e "qegwfsy," ecp kygcr acwo ekwy ia nyy hgib gin sgrbi yoy.  Kfi
iby qastgpekwy isaax hen cyesgcr fn.  Ibyo bep nyyc iby hbewyn ecp hysy
xsyxesgcr ia eiield ibyt.  Acy lafwp jfpry kyqasybecp ibei iby
lelbewain hafwp ky vgliasgafn, cai acwo kylefny ibyo hysy kyiiys kfgwi
qas eiield ibec ibygs gcaqqycngvy epvysnesgyn, kfi ewna kylefny ibyo
lafwp sytegc wacrys fcpys heiys hgibafi latgcr ia iby nfsqely.  Ibysy
hen acwo jfni igty ia ra ia iby bywx aq iby hbewyn.  Iby Cefigwfn hyci
fcpys heiys.  Lacnygw, Cyp Wecp, ecp G iaad afs xwelyn kyqasy iby
hgcpah gc iby newaac, ecp Lexiegc Cyta jagcyp iby xgwai gc bgn lery ia
hasd bgn exxeseifn en ec ycrgcy aq pynisfligac.  Naac G qywi iby
kyeigcrn aq iby nlsyh zfgldyc, ecp afs nxyyp gclsyenyp.  Iby keiiwy
kyihyyc iby lelbewain ecp iby hbewyn bep ewsyepo kyrfc hbyc iby
Cefigwfn essgvyp.  Ibyo pgp cai ei qgsni nbah eco qyes ei iby ngrbi aq
ibgn cyh tacniys jagcgcr gc iby lacqwgli.  Kfi ibyo naac bep ia rfesp
eregcni gin kwahn.  Hbei e keiiwy!  Iby Cefigwfn hen caibgcr kfi e
qastgpekwy besxaac, ksecpgnbyp ko iby becp aq gin Lexiegc.  Gi bfswyp
ginywq eregcni iby qwynbo tenn, xenngcr ibsafrb qsat acy xesi ia iby
aibys, wyevgcr kybgcp gi iha zfgvysgcr bewvyn aq iby ecgtew.  Gi lafwp
cai qyyw iby qastgpekwy kwahn qsat ibygs iegwn fxac gin ngpyn, cas iby
nbald hbglb gi xsapflyp ginywq, tflb tasy.  Acy lelbewai dgwwyp, gi sec
ei iby cymi, ieldyp ac iby nxai ibei gi tgrbi cai tgnn gin xsyo, ragcr
qashespn ecp keldhespn, ecnhysgcr ia gin bywt, xwfcrgcr hbyc iby
lyielyec pgvyp gcia iby pyyx heiysn, latgcr fx hgib gi hbyc gi syifscyp
ia iby nfsqely, nisgdgcr gi qsaci as ngpyheon, lfiigcr as iyesgcr gc
eww pgsyligacn ecp ei eco xely, xgyslgcr gi hgib gin iyssgkwy nxfs.
Hbei lescery!  Hbei e cagny ac iby nfsqely aq iby hevyn!  Hbei nbesx
bgnngcr, ecp hbei ncasigcr xylfwges ia ibyny ycseryp ecgtewn!  Gc iby
tgpni aq ibyny heiysn, rycysewwo na xyelyqfw, ibygs iegwn tepy xysqyli
kgwwahn.  Qas acy bafs ibgn hbawynewy tennelsy lacigcfyp, qsat hbglb
iby lelbewain lafwp cai ynlexy.  Nyvysew igtyn iyc as ihywvy fcgiyp
isgyp ia lsfnb iby Cefigwfn ko ibygs hygrbi.  Qsat iby hgcpah hy lafwp
nyy ibygs ycastafn tafibn, nifppyp hgib ifndn, ecp ibygs qastgpekwy
yoyn.  Cyp Wecp lafwp cai laciegc bgtnywq; by ibsyeiycyp ecp nhasy ei
ibyt.  Hy lafwp qyyw ibyt lwgcrgcr ia afs vynnyw wgdy parn hassogcr e
hgwp kaes gc e laxny.  Kfi iby Cefigwfn, hasdgcr gin nlsyh, lessgyp
ibyt bysy ecp ibysy, as ia iby fxxys wyvywn aq iby alyec, hgibafi
lesgcr qas ibygs ycastafn hygrbi, cas iby xahysqfw nisegc ac iby
vynnyw.  Ei wycrib iby tenn aq lelbewain ksady fx, iby hevyn kylety
zfgyi, ecp G qywi ibei hy hysy sgngcr ia iby nfsqely.  Iby xecyw
axycyp, ecp hy bfssgyp ac ia iby xweiqast.  Iby nye hen lavysyp hgib
tfigweiyp kapgyn.  E qastgpekwy ymxwangac lafwp cai bevy pgvgpyp ecp
iasc ibgn qwynbo tenn hgib tasy vgawycly.  Hy hysy qwaeigcr etgp
rgrecigl kapgyn, kwfgnb ac iby keld ecp hbgiy fcpyscyeib, lavysyp hgib
ycastafn xsaifkyseclyn.  Naty iyssgqgyp lelbewain hysy qwogcr iahespn
iby basguac.  Iby hevyn hysy poyp syp qas nyvysew tgwyn, ecp iby
Cefigwfn qwaeiyp gc e nye aq kwaap:  Lexiegc Cyta jagcyp fn.

"Hyww, Teniys Wecp?" negp by.

"Hyww, ngs," syxwgyp iby Lecepgec, hbany ycibfngent bep natyhbei
lewtyp; "gi gn e iyssgkwy nxylielwy, lysiegcwo.  Kfi G et cai e
kfilbys.  G et e bfciys, ecp G leww ibgn e kfilbyso."

"Gi gn e tennelsy aq tgnlbgyvafn lsyeifsyn," syxwgyp iby Lexiegc; "ecp
iby Cefigwfn gn cai e kfilbys'n dcgqy."

"G wgdy to besxaac kyiiys," negp iby Lecepgec.

"Yvyso acy ia bgn ahc," ecnhysyp iby Lexiegc, waadgcr qgmypwo ei Cyp
Wecp.

G qyesyp by hafwp lattgi naty eli aq vgawycly, hbglb hafwp ycp gc nep
lacnyzfyclyn.  Kfi bgn ecrys hen ifscyp ko iby ngrbi aq e hbewy hbglb
iby Cefigwfn bep jfni laty fx hgib.  Iby lsyeifsy bep cai zfgiy ynlexyp
qsat iby lelbewai'n iyyib.  G sylarcgnyp iby nafibysc hbewy ko gin qwei
byep, hbglb gn ycigsywo kweld.  Eceiatglewwo, gi gn pgnigcrfgnbyp qsat
iby hbgiy hbewy ecp iby Casib Lexy hbewy ko iby nyvyc lysvglew
vysiyksey, ecp gi ben iha tasy sgkn ibec gin lacrycysn.  Iby
fcqasifceiy lyielyec hen wogcr ac gin ngpy, sgppwyp hgib bawyn qsat iby
kgiyn, ecp zfgiy pyep.  Qsat gin tfigweiyp qgc nigww bfcr e oafcr hbewy
hbglb gi lafwp cai nevy qsat iby tennelsy.  Gin axyc tafib wyi iby
heiys qwah gc ecp afi, tfstfsgcr wgdy iby hevyn ksyedgcr ac iby nbasy.
Lexiegc Cyta niyysyp lwany ia iby lasxny aq iby lsyeifsy.  Iha aq bgn
tyc tafciyp gin ngpy, ecp G neh, cai hgibafi nfsxsgny, ibei ibyo hysy
psehgcr qsat gin ksyenin eww iby tgwd hbglb ibyo laciegcyp, ibei gn ia
neo, ekafi iha as ibsyy iacn.  Iby Lexiegc aqqysyp ty e lfx aq iby
tgwd, hbglb hen nigww hest.  G lafwp cai bywx nbahgcr to syxfrcecly ia
iby psgcd; kfi by ennfsyp ty ibei gi hen ymlywwyci, ecp cai ia ky
pgnigcrfgnbyp qsat lah'n tgwd.  G ieniyp gi, ecp hen aq bgn axgcgac.
Gi hen e fnyqfw synysvy ia fn, qas gc iby nbexy aq newi kfiiys as
lbyyny gi hafwp qast ec ersyyekwy vesgyio qsat afs aspgceso qaap.  Qsat
ibei peo G caiglyp hgib fcyengcynn ibei Cyp Wecp'n gww-hgww iahespn
Lexiegc Cyta gclsyenyp, ecp G synawvyp ia heilb iby Lecepgec'n rynifsyn
lwanywo.



LBEXIYS MGGG

IBY GLYKYSR

Iby Cefigwfn hen niyepgwo xfsnfgcr gin nafibyswo lafsny, qawwahgcr iby
qgqigyib tysgpgec hgib lacngpysekwy nxyyp.  Pgp by hgnb ia syelb iby
xawy?  G pgp cai ibgcd na, qas yvyso eiiytxi ia syelb ibei xagci bep
bgibysia qegwyp.  Eregc, iby nyenac hen qes epveclyp, qas gc iby
Eciesligl syrgacn iby 13ib aq Teslb lassynxacpn hgib iby 13ib aq
Nyxiytkys aq casibysc syrgacn, hbglb kyrgc ei iby yzfgcaligew nyenac.
Ac iby 14ib aq Teslb G neh qwaeigcr gly gc weigifpy 55°, tysywo
xewy kgin aq pyksgn qsat ihycio ia ihycio-qgvy qyyi wacr, qastgcr kecdn
avys hbglb iby nye lfswyp.  Iby Cefigwfn sytegcyp ac iby nfsqely aq iby
alyec.  Cyp Wecp, hba bep qgnbyp gc iby Esligl Nyen, hen qetgwges hgib
gin glykysrn; kfi Lacnygw ecp G eptgsyp ibyt qas iby qgsni igty.  Gc
iby eitanxbysy iahespn iby nafibysc basguac nisyilbyp e hbgiy peuuwgcr
kecp.  Ycrwgnb hbewysn bevy rgvyc gi iby cety aq "gly kwgcd."  Bahyvys
ibgld iby lwafpn teo ky, gi gn ewheon vgngkwy, ecp eccafclyn iby
xsynycly aq ec gly xeld as kecd.  Ellaspgcrwo, wesrys kwaldn naac
exxyesyp, hbany ksgwwgeclo lbecryp hgib iby lexsglyn aq iby qar.  Naty
aq ibyny tennyn nbahyp rsyyc vygcn, en gq wacr fcpfweigcr wgcyn bep
kyyc iselyp hgib nfwxbeiy aq laxxys; aibysn synytkwyp ycastafn
etyibonin hgib iby wgrbi nbgcgcr ibsafrb ibyt.  Naty syqwyliyp iby
wgrbi aq peo fxac e ibafnecp lsoniew qelyin.  Aibysn nbepyp hgib vgvgp
lewlesyafn syqwyligacn synytkwyp e xysqyli iahc aq teskwy.  Iby tasy hy
cyesyp iby nafib iby tasy ibyny qwaeigcr gnwecpn gclsyenyp kaib gc
cftkys ecp gtxasiecly.

Ei 60° wei. yvyso xenn bep pgnexxyesyp.  Kfi, nyydgcr lesyqfwwo,
Lexiegc Cyta naac qafcp e cessah axycgcr, ibsafrb hbglb by kawpwo
nwgxxyp, dcahgcr, bahyvys, ibei gi hafwp lwany kybgcp bgt.  Ibfn,
rfgpyp ko ibgn lwyvys becp, iby Cefigwfn xennyp ibsafrb eww iby gly
hgib e xsylgngac hbglb zfgiy lbestyp Lacnygw; glykysrn as tafciegcn,
gly-qgywpn as ntaaib xwegcn, nyytgcr ia bevy ca wgtgin, psgqi-gly as
qwaeigcr gly-xeldn, xwegcn ksadyc fx, lewwyp xewlbn hbyc ibyo esy
lgslfwes, ecp nisyetn hbyc ibyo esy tepy fx aq wacr nisgxn.  Iby
iytxyseifsy hen vyso wah; iby ibystatyiys ymxanyp ia iby egs tesdyp 2
pyr. as 3° kywah uysa, kfi hy hysy hestwo lwep hgib qfs, ei iby
ymxycny aq iby nye-kyes ecp nyew.  Iby gciysgas aq iby Cefigwfn, hestyp
syrfweswo ko gin ywylisgl exxeseifn, pyqgyp iby tani gciycny lawp.
Kyngpyn, gi hafwp acwo bevy kyyc cylynneso ia ra naty oespn kycyeib iby
hevyn ia qgcp e tasy kyesekwy iytxyseifsy.  Iha tacibn yeswgys hy
nbafwp bevy bep xysxyifew peowgrbi gc ibyny weigifpyn; kfi ewsyepo hy
bep bep ibsyy as qafs bafsn aq cgrbi, ecp ko ecp ko ibysy hafwp ky ngm
tacibn aq pesdcynn gc ibyny lgslftxawes syrgacn.  Ac iby 15ib aq Teslb
hy hysy gc iby weigifpy aq Cyh Nbyiwecp ecp Nafib Asdcyo.  Iby Lexiegc
iawp ty ibei qastyswo cftysafn isgkyn aq nyewn gcbekgiyp ibyt; kfi ibei
Ycrwgnb ecp Etysglec hbewysn, gc ibygs sery qas pynisfligac, tennelsyp
kaib awp ecp oafcr; ibfn, hbysy ibysy hen acly wgqy ecp ecgteigac, ibyo
bep wyqi ngwycly ecp pyeib.

Ekafi ygrbi a'lwald ac iby tascgcr aq iby 16ib aq Teslb iby Cefigwfn,
qawwahgcr iby qgqio-qgqib tysgpgec, lfi iby Eciesligl xawes lgslwy.
Gly nfssafcpyp fn ac eww ngpyn, ecp lwanyp iby basguac.  Kfi Lexiegc
Cyta hyci qsat acy axycgcr ia ecaibys, nigww ragcr bgrbys.  G leccai
ymxsynn to eniacgnbtyci ei iby kyefigyn aq ibyny cyh syrgacn.  Iby gly
iaad tani nfsxsgngcr qastn.  Bysy iby rsafxgcr qastyp ec asgyciew iahc,
hgib gccftysekwy tanzfyn ecp tgcesyin; ibysy e qewwyc lgio ibsahc ia
iby yesib, en gi hysy, ko naty lacvfwngac aq ceifsy.  Iby hbawy enxyli
hen lacnieciwo lbecryp ko iby akwgzfy seon aq iby nfc, as wani gc iby
rsyognb qar etgpni bfssglecyn aq ncah.  Pyiaceigacn ecp qewwn hysy
byesp ac eww ngpyn, rsyei avysibsahn aq glykysrn, hbglb ewiysyp iby
hbawy wecpnlexy wgdy e pgasete.  Aqiyc nyygcr ca ymgi, G ibafrbi hy
hysy pyqgcgiywo xsgnacysn; kfi, gcnigcli rfgpgcr bgt ei iby nwgrbiyni
gcpgleigac, Lexiegc Cyta hafwp pgnlavys e cyh xenn.  By hen cyvys
tgniedyc hbyc by neh iby ibgc ibsyepn aq kwfgnb heiys isgldwgcr ewacr
iby gly-qgywpn; ecp G bep ca pafki ibei by bep ewsyepo vycifsyp gcia
iby tgpni aq ibyny Eciesligl nyen kyqasy.  Ac iby 16ib aq Teslb,
bahyvys, iby gly-qgywpn eknawfiywo kwaldyp afs saep.  Gi hen cai iby
glykysr ginywq, en oyi, kfi veni qgywpn lytyciyp ko iby lawp.  Kfi ibgn
aknielwy lafwp cai niax Lexiegc Cyta: by bfswyp bgtnywq eregcni gi hgib
qsgrbiqfw vgawycly.  Iby Cefigwfn yciysyp iby ksgiiwy tenn wgdy e
hypry, ecp nxwgi gi hgib qsgrbiqfw lseldgcrn.  Gi hen iby keiiysgcr set
aq iby eclgycin bfswyp ko gcqgcgiy nisycrib.  Iby gly, ibsahc bgrb gc
iby egs, qyww wgdy begw esafcp fn.  Ko gin ahc xahys aq gtxfwngac afs
exxeseifn tepy e lecew qas ginywq; naty igtyn lessgyp eheo ko gin ahc
gtxyifn, gi wapryp ac iby gly-qgywp, lsfnbgcr gi hgib gin hygrbi, ecp
natyigtyn kfsgyp kycyeib gi, pgvgpgcr gi ko e ngtxwy xgilbgcr tavytyci,
xsapflgcr wesry sycin gc gi.  Vgawyci rewyn ennegwyp fn ei ibgn igty,
ellatxecgyp ko ibgld qarn, ibsafrb hbglb, qsat acy ycp aq iby xweiqast
ia iby aibys, hy lafwp nyy caibgcr.  Iby hgcp kwyh nbesxwo qsat eww
xesin aq iby latxenn, ecp iby ncah weo gc nflb besp byexn ibei hy bep
ia ksyed gi hgib kwahn aq e xgldemy.  Iby iytxyseifsy hen ewheon ei 5
pyr. kywah uysa; yvyso afihesp xesi aq iby Cefigwfn hen lavysyp hgib
gly.  E sgrryp vynnyw hafwp bevy kyyc yciecrwyp gc iby kwaldyp fx
rasryn.  E vynnyw hgibafi negwn, hgib ywylisglgio qas gin taigvy xahys,
ecp hecigcr ca laew, lafwp ewacy ksevy nflb bgrb weigifpyn.  Ei wycrib,
ac iby 18ib aq Teslb, eqiys teco fnywynn ennefwin, iby Cefigwfn hen
xangigvywo kwaldyp.  Gi hen ca wacrys ygibys nisyetn, xeldn, as
gly-qgywpn, kfi ec gciystgcekwy ecp gttavekwy kessgys, qastyp ko
tafciegcn nawpysyp iaryibys.

"Ec glykysr!" negp iby Lecepgec ia ty.

G dcyh ibei ia Cyp Wecp, en hyww en ia eww aibys cevgreiasn hba bep
xsylypyp fn, ibgn hen ec gcyvgiekwy aknielwy.  Iby nfc exxyesgcr qas ec
gcnieci ei caac, Lexiegc Cyta iaad ec aknysveigac en cyes en xanngkwy,
hbglb revy afs ngifeigac ei 51° 30' wacr. ecp 67° 39' aq N.
wei.  Hy bep epveclyp acy pyrsyy tasy gc ibgn Eciesligl syrgac.  Aq iby
wgzfgp nfsqely aq iby nye ibysy hen ca wacrys e rwgtxny.  Fcpys iby
nxfs aq iby Cefigwfn weo nisyilbyp e veni xwegc, yciecrwyp hgib
lacqfnyp kwaldn.  Bysy ecp ibysy nbesx xagcin ecp nwycpys cyypwyn
sgngcr ia e bygrbi aq 200 qyyi; qfsibys ac e niyyx nbasy, byhc en gi
hysy hgib ec emy ecp lwaibyp hgib rsyognb igcin; bfry tgssasn,
syqwyligcr e qyh seon aq nfcnbgcy, bewq psahcyp gc iby qar.  Ecp avys
ibgn pynaweiy qely aq ceifsy e niysc ngwycly sygrcyp, nleslywo ksadyc
ko iby qwexxgcr aq iby hgcrn aq xyisywn ecp xfqqgcn.  Yvysoibgcr hen
qsauyc--yvyc iby cagny.  Iby Cefigwfn hen ibyc akwgryp ia niax gc gin
epvycifsafn lafsny etgp ibyny qgywpn aq gly.  Gc nxgiy aq afs yqqasin,
gc nxgiy aq iby xahysqfw tyecn ytxwaoyp ia ksyed fx iby gly, iby
Cefigwfn sytegcyp gttavekwy.  Rycysewwo, hbyc hy lec xsalyyp ca
qfsibys, hy bevy syifsc nigww axyc ia fn; kfi bysy syifsc hen en
gtxanngkwy en epvecly, qas yvyso xenn bep lwanyp kybgcp fn; ecp qas iby
qyh tatycin hbyc hy hysy nieigaceso, hy hysy wgdywo ia ky ycigsywo
kwaldyp, hbglb pgp gcpyyp bexxyc ekafi iha a'lwald gc iby eqiyscaac,
iby qsynb gly qastgcr esafcp gin ngpyn hgib eniacgnbgcr sexgpgio.  G
hen akwgryp ia eptgi ibei Lexiegc Cyta hen tasy ibec gtxsfpyci.  G hen
ac iby xweiqast ei ibei tatyci.  Iby Lexiegc bep kyyc aknysvgcr afs
ngifeigac qas naty igty xeni, hbyc by negp ia ty:

"Hyww, ngs, hbei pa oaf ibgcd aq ibgn?"

"G ibgcd ibei hy esy lefrbi, Lexiegc."

"Na, T. Esaccem, oaf syewwo ibgcd ibei iby Cefigwfn leccai pgnycrery
ginywq?"

"Hgib pgqqglfwio, Lexiegc; qas iby nyenac gn ewsyepo iaa qes epveclyp
qas oaf ia syldac ac iby ksyedgcr aq iby gly."

"Eb! ngs," negp Lexiegc Cyta, gc ec gsacglew iacy, "oaf hgww ewheon ky
iby nety.  Oaf nyy caibgcr kfi pgqqglfwigyn ecp aknielwyn.  G eqqgst
ibei cai acwo lec iby Cefigwfn pgnycrery ginywq, kfi ewna ibei gi lec
ra qfsibys nigww."

"Qfsibys ia iby Nafib?"  G endyp, waadgcr ei iby Lexiegc.

"Oyn, ngs; gi nbeww ra ia iby xawy."

"Ia iby xawy!"  G ymlwegtyp, fcekwy ia syxsynn e rynifsy aq gclsypfwgio.

"Oyn," syxwgyp iby Lexiegc, lawpwo, "ia iby Eciesligl xawy--ia ibei
fcdcahc xagci qsat hbycly nxsgcrn yvyso tysgpgec aq iby rwaky.  Oaf
dcah hbyibys G lec pa en G xwyeny hgib iby Cefigwfn!"

Oyn, G dcyh ibei.  G dcyh ibei ibgn tec hen kawp, yvyc ia senbcynn.
Kfi ia laczfys ibany aknielwyn hbglb ksgniwyp safcp iby Nafib Xawy,
sycpysgcr gi tasy gcellynngkwy ibec iby Casib, hbglb bep cai oyi kyyc
syelbyp ko iby kawpyni cevgreiasn--hen gi cai e tep yciysxsgny, acy
hbglb acwo e tecgel hafwp bevy laclygvyp?  Gi ibyc lety gcia to byep ia
end Lexiegc Cyta gq by bep yvys pgnlavysyp ibei xawy hbglb bep cyvys
oyi kyyc isappyc ko e bftec lsyeifsy?

"Ca, ngs," by syxwgyp; "kfi hy hgww pgnlavys gi iaryibys.  Hbysy aibysn
bevy qegwyp, G hgww cai qegw.  G bevy cyvys oyi wyp to Cefigwfn na qes
gcia nafibysc nyen; kfi, G syxyei, gi nbeww ra qfsibys oyi."

"G lec hyww kywgyvy oaf, Lexiegc," negp G, gc e nwgrbiwo gsacglew iacy.
"G kywgyvy oaf!  Wyi fn ra ebyep!  Ibysy esy ca aknielwyn qas fn!  Wyi
fn ntenb ibgn glykysr!  Wyi fn kwah gi fx; ecp, gq gi syngnin, wyi fn
rgvy iby Cefigwfn hgcrn ia qwo avys gi!"

"Avys gi, ngs!" negp Lexiegc Cyta, zfgyiwo; "ca, cai avys gi, kfi fcpys
gi!"

"Fcpys gi!"  G ymlwegtyp, e nfppyc gpye aq iby Lexiegc'n xsajylin
qwenbgcr fxac to tgcp.  G fcpysniaap; iby hacpysqfw zfewgigyn aq iby
Cefigwfn hysy ragcr ia nysvy fn gc ibgn nfxysbftec yciysxsgny.

"G nyy hy esy kyrgccgcr ia fcpysniecp acy ecaibys, ngs," negp iby
Lexiegc, bewq ntgwgcr.  "Oaf kyrgc ia nyy iby xanngkgwgio--G nbafwp neo
iby nfllynn--aq ibgn eiiytxi.  Ibei hbglb gn gtxanngkwy qas ec aspgceso
vynnyw gn yeno ia iby Cefigwfn.  Gq e lacigcyci wgyn kyqasy iby xawy,
gi tfni niax kyqasy iby lacigcyci; kfi gq, ac iby laciseso, iby xawy gn
henbyp ko axyc nye, gi hgww ra yvyc ia iby xawy."

"Lysiegcwo," negp G, lessgyp eheo ko iby Lexiegc'n syenacgcr; "gq iby
nfsqely aq iby nye gn nawgpgqgyp ko iby gly, iby wahys pyxibn esy qsyy
ko iby Xsavgpycigew weh hbglb ben xwelyp iby temgtft aq pycngio aq iby
heiysn aq iby alyec acy pyrsyy bgrbys ibec qsyyugcr-xagci; ecp, gq G et
cai tgniedyc, iby xasigac aq ibgn glykysr hbglb gn ekavy iby heiys gn
en acy ia qafs ia ibei hbglb gn kywah."

"Vyso cyeswo, ngs; qas acy qaai aq glykysr ekavy iby nye ibysy esy
ibsyy kywah gi.  Gq ibyny gly tafciegcn esy cai tasy ibec 300 qyyi
ekavy iby nfsqely, ibyo esy cai tasy ibec 900 kycyeib.  Ecp hbei esy
900 qyyi ia iby Cefigwfn?"

"Caibgcr, ngs."

"Gi lafwp yvyc nyyd ei rsyeiys pyxibn ibei fcgqast iytxyseifsy aq
nye-heiys, ecp ibysy ksevy hgib gtxfcgio iby ibgsio as qasio pyrsyyn aq
nfsqely lawp."

"Jfni na, ngs--jfni na," G syxwgyp, ryiigcr ecgteiyp.

"Iby acwo pgqqglfwio," lacigcfyp Lexiegc Cyta, "gn ibei aq sytegcgcr
nyvysew peon hgibafi sycyhgcr afs xsavgngac aq egs."

"Gn ibei eww?  Iby Cefigwfn ben veni synysvagsn; hy lec qgww ibyt, ecp
ibyo hgww nfxxwo fn hgib eww iby amoryc hy heci."

"Hyww ibafrbi aq, T. Esaccem," syxwgyp iby Lexiegc, ntgwgcr.  "Kfi, cai
hgnbgcr oaf ia ellfny ty aq senbcynn, G hgww qgsni rgvy oaf eww to
akjyligacn."

"Bevy oaf eco tasy ia tedy?"

"Acwo acy.  Gi gn xanngkwy, gq iby nye ymgnin ei iby Nafib Xawy, ibei
gi teo ky lavysyp; ecp, lacnyzfyciwo, hy nbeww ky fcekwy ia laty ia iby
nfsqely."

"Raap, ngs! kfi pa oaf qasryi ibei iby Cefigwfn gn estyp hgib e
xahysqfw nxfs, ecp lafwp hy cai nycp gi pgeracewwo eregcni ibyny qgywpn
aq gly, hbglb hafwp axyc ei iby nbaldn."

"Eb! ngs, oaf esy qfww aq gpyen ia-peo."

"Kyngpyn, Lexiegc," G eppyp, ycibfngeniglewwo, "hbo nbafwp hy cai qgcp
iby nye axyc ei iby Nafib Xawy en hyww en ei iby Casib?  Iby qsauyc
xawyn aq iby yesib pa cai lagclgpy, ygibys gc iby nafibysc as gc iby
casibysc syrgacn; ecp, fcigw gi gn xsavyp ia iby laciseso, hy teo
nfxxany ygibys e lacigcyci as ec alyec qsyy qsat gly ei ibyny iha
xagcin aq iby rwaky."

"G ibgcd na iaa, T. Esaccem," syxwgyp Lexiegc Cyta.  "G acwo hgnb oaf
ia aknysvy ibei, eqiys bevgcr tepy na teco akjyligacn ia to xsajyli,
oaf esy cah lsfnbgcr ty hgib esrftycin gc gin qevafs!"

Iby xsyxeseigacn qas ibgn efpelgafn eiiytxi cah kyrec.  Iby xahysqfw
xftxn aq iby Cefigwfn hysy hasdgcr egs gcia iby synysvagsn ecp niasgcr
gi ei bgrb xsynnfsy.  Ekafi qafs a'lwald, Lexiegc Cyta eccafclyp iby
lwangcr aq iby xecywn ac iby xweiqast.  G ibsyh acy weni waad ei iby
tenngvy glykysr hbglb hy hysy ragcr ia lsann.  Iby hyeibys hen lwyes,
iby eitanxbysy xfsy ycafrb, iby lawp vyso rsyei, kygcr 12° kywah
uysa; kfi, iby hgcp bevgcr racy pahc, ibgn iytxyseifsy hen cai na
fckyesekwy.  Ekafi iyc tyc tafciyp iby ngpyn aq iby Cefigwfn, estyp
hgib xgldemyn ia ksyed iby gly esafcp iby vynnyw, hbglb hen naac qsyy.
Iby axyseigac hen zfgldwo xysqastyp, qas iby qsynb gly hen nigww vyso
ibgc.  Hy eww hyci kywah.  Iby fnfew synysvagsn hysy qgwwyp hgib iby
cyhwo-wgkyseiyp heiys, ecp iby Cefigwfn naac pynlycpyp.  G bep iedyc to
xwely hgib Lacnygw gc iby newaac; ibsafrb iby axyc hgcpah hy lafwp nyy
iby wahys kypn aq iby Nafibysc Alyec.  Iby ibystatyiys hyci fx, iby
cyypwy aq iby latxenn pyvgeiyp ac iby pgew.  Ei ekafi 900 qyyi, en
Lexiegc Cyta bep qasynyyc, hy hysy qwaeigcr kycyeib iby fcpfweigcr
kaiiat aq iby glykysr.  Kfi iby Cefigwfn hyci wahys nigww--gi hyci ia
iby pyxib aq qafs bfcpsyp qeibatn.  Iby iytxyseifsy aq iby heiys ei iby
nfsqely nbahyp ihywvy pyrsyyn, gi hen cah acwo iyc; hy bep regcyp iha.
G cyyp cai neo iby iytxyseifsy aq iby Cefigwfn hen segnyp ko gin
byeigcr exxeseifn ia e tflb bgrbys pyrsyy; yvyso tecayfvsy hen
ellatxwgnbyp hgib hacpysqfw xsylgngac.

"Hy nbeww xenn gi, gq oaf xwyeny, ngs," negp Lacnygw.

"G kywgyvy hy nbeww," G negp, gc e iacy aq qgst lacvgligac.

Gc ibgn axyc nye, iby Cefigwfn bep iedyc gin lafsny pgsyli ia iby xawy,
hgibafi wyevgcr iby qgqio-nylacp tysgpgec.  Qsat 67° 30' ia 90
pyr., ihycio-iha pyrsyyn ecp e bewq aq weigifpy sytegcyp ia isevyw;
ibei gn, ekafi qgvy bfcpsyp wyerfyn.  Iby Cefigwfn dyxi fx e tyec nxyyp
aq ihycio-ngm tgwyn ec bafs--iby nxyyp aq ec ymxsynn isegc.  Gq ibei
hen dyxi fx, gc qasio bafsn hy nbafwp syelb iby xawy.

Qas e xesi aq iby cgrbi iby cavywio aq iby ngifeigac dyxi fn ei iby
hgcpah.  Iby nye hen wgi hgib iby ywylisgl weciysc; kfi gi hen
pynysiyp; qgnbyn pgp cai najafsc gc ibyny gtxsgnacyp heiysn; ibyo acwo
qafcp ibysy e xennery ia iedy ibyt qsat iby Eciesligl Alyec ia iby axyc
xawes nye.  Afs xely hen sexgp; hy lafwp qyyw gi ko iby zfgvysgcr aq
iby wacr niyyw kapo.  Ekafi iha gc iby tascgcr G iaad naty bafsn'
syxany, ecp Lacnygw pgp iby nety.  Gc lsanngcr iby hegni G pgp cai tyyi
Lexiegc Cyta: G nfxxanyp bgt ia ky gc iby xgwai'n lery.  Iby cymi
tascgcr, iby 19ib aq Teslb, G iaad to xani acly tasy gc iby newaac.
Iby ywylisgl war iawp ty ibei iby nxyyp aq iby Cefigwfn bep kyyc
nweldycyp.  Gi hen ibyc ragcr iahespn iby nfsqely; kfi xsfpyciwo
ytxiogcr gin synysvagsn vyso nwahwo.  To byesi kyei qeni.  Hysy hy
ragcr ia ytysry ecp syregc iby axyc xawes eitanxbysy?  Ca!  E nbald
iawp ty ibei iby Cefigwfn bep nisfld iby kaiiat aq iby glykysr, nigww
vyso ibgld, jfprgcr qsat iby pyepycyp nafcp.  Hy bep gc pyyp "nisfld,"
ia fny e nye ymxsynngac, kfi gc ec gcvysny nycny, ecp ei e ibafnecp
qyyi pyyx.  Ibgn hafwp rgvy ibsyy ibafnecp qyyi aq gly ekavy fn; acy
ibafnecp kygcr ekavy iby heiys-tesd. Iby glykysr hen ibyc bgrbys ibec
ei gin kaspysn--cai e vyso syennfsgcr qeli.  Nyvysew igtyn ibei peo iby
Cefigwfn isgyp eregc, ecp yvyso igty gi nisfld iby heww hbglb weo wgdy
e lygwgcr ekavy gi.  Natyigtyn gi tyi hgib kfi 900 oespn, acwo 200 aq
hbglb sany ekavy iby nfsqely.  Gi hen ihgly iby bygrbi gi hen hbyc iby
Cefigwfn bep racy fcpys iby hevyn.  G lesyqfwwo caiyp iby pgqqysyci
pyxibn, ecp ibfn akiegcyp e nfktesgcy xsaqgwy aq iby lbegc en gi hen
pyvywaxyp fcpys iby heiys.  Ibei cgrbi ca lbecry bep iedyc xwely gc afs
ngifeigac.  Nigww gly kyihyyc qafs ecp qgvy bfcpsyp oespn gc pyxib!  Gi
hen yvgpyciwo pgtgcgnbgcr, kfi, nigww, hbei e ibgldcynn kyihyyc fn ecp
iby nfsqely aq iby alyec!  Gi hen ibyc ygrbi.  Ellaspgcr ia iby pegwo
lfniat ac kaesp iby Cefigwfn, gin egs nbafwp bevy kyyc sycyhyp qafs
bafsn era; kfi G pgp cai nfqqys tflb, ewibafrb Lexiegc Cyta bep cai oyi
tepy eco pytecp fxac bgn synysvy aq amoryc.  To nwyyx hen xegcqfw ibei
cgrbi; baxy ecp qyes kyngyryp ty ko ifscn: G sany nyvysew igtyn.  Iby
rsaxgcr aq iby Cefigwfn lacigcfyp.  Ekafi ibsyy gc iby tascgcr, G
caiglyp ibei iby wahys nfsqely aq iby glykysr hen acwo ekafi qgqio qyyi
pyyx.  Acy bfcpsyp ecp qgqio qyyi cah nyxeseiyp fn qsat iby nfsqely aq
iby heiysn.  Iby glykysr hen ko pyrsyyn kylatgcr ec gly-qgywp, iby
tafciegc e xwegc.  To yoyn cyvys wyqi iby tecatyiys.  Hy hysy nigww
sgngcr pgeracewwo ia iby nfsqely, hbglb nxesdwyp fcpys iby ywylisgl
seon.  Iby glykysr hen nisyilbgcr kaib ekavy ecp kycyeib gcia
wycribycgcr nwaxyn; tgwy eqiys tgwy gi hen ryiigcr ibgccys.  Ei wycrib,
ei ngm gc iby tascgcr aq ibei tytasekwy peo, iby 19ib aq Teslb, iby
paas aq iby newaac axycyp, ecp Lexiegc Cyta exxyesyp.

"Iby nye gn axyc!!" hen eww by negp.



LBEXIYS MGV

IBY NAFIB XAWY

G sfnbyp ac ia iby xweiqast.  Oyn! iby axyc nye, hgib kfi e qyh
nleiiysyp xgylyn aq gly ecp tavgcr glykysrn--e wacr nisyilb aq nye; e
haswp aq kgspn gc iby egs, ecp tosgepn aq qgnbyn fcpys ibany heiysn,
hbglb vesgyp qsat gciycny kwfy ia awgvy rsyyc, ellaspgcr ia iby kaiiat.
Iby ibystatyiys tesdyp 3° L. ekavy uysa.  Gi hen latxeseigvywo
nxsgcr, nbfi fx en hy hysy kybgcp ibgn glykysr, hbany wycribycyp tenn
hen pgtwo nyyc ac afs casibysc basguac.

"Esy hy ei iby xawy?"  G endyp iby Lexiegc, hgib e kyeigcr byesi.

"G pa cai dcah," by syxwgyp.  "Ei caac G hgww iedy afs kyesgcrn."

"Kfi hgww iby nfc nbah bgtnywq ibsafrb ibgn qar?" negp G, waadgcr ei
iby wyepyc ndo.

"Bahyvys wgiiwy gi nbahn, gi hgww ky ycafrb," syxwgyp iby Lexiegc.

Ekafi iyc tgwyn nafib e nawgieso gnwecp sany ia e bygrbi aq acy bfcpsyp
ecp qafs oespn.  Hy tepy qas gi, kfi lesyqfwwo, qas iby nye tgrbi ky
nisyhc hgib kecdn.  Acy bafs eqiyshespn hy bep syelbyp gi, iha bafsn
weiys hy bep tepy iby safcp aq gi.  Gi tyenfsyp qafs as qgvy tgwyn gc
lgslftqysycly.  E cessah lecew nyxeseiyp gi qsat e lacngpysekwy nisyilb
aq wecp, xysbexn e lacigcyci, qas hy lafwp cai nyy gin wgtgin.  Iby
ymgniycly aq ibgn wecp nyytyp ia rgvy naty lawafs ia Tefso'n ibyaso.
Iby gcrycgafn Etysglec ben sytesdyp ibei, kyihyyc iby Nafib Xawy ecp
iby ngmigyib xesewwyw, iby nye gn lavysyp hgib qwaeigcr gly aq ycastafn
nguy, hbglb gn cyvys tyi hgib gc iby Casib Eiwecigl.  Qsat ibgn qeli by
ben psehc iby laclwfngac ibei iby Eciesligl Lgslwy yclwanyn
lacngpysekwy lacigcycin, en glykysrn leccai qast gc axyc nye, kfi acwo
ac iby laenin.  Ellaspgcr ia ibyny lewlfweigacn, iby tenn aq gly
nfssafcpgcr iby nafibysc xawy qastn e veni lex, iby lgslftqysycly aq
hbglb tfni ky, ei wyeni, 2,500 tgwyn.  Kfi iby Cefigwfn, qas qyes aq
sfccgcr ersafcp, bep niaxxyp ekafi ibsyy lekwy-wycribn qsat e nisecp
avys hbglb syesyp e nfxysk byex aq saldn.  Iby kaei hen wefclbyp; iby
Lexiegc, iha aq bgn tyc, kyesgcr gcnisftycin, Lacnygw, ecp tonywq hysy
gc gi.  Gi hen iyc gc iby tascgcr.  G bep cai nyyc Cyp Wecp.  Pafkiwynn
iby Lecepgec pgp cai hgnb ia eptgi iby xsynycly aq iby Nafib Xawy.  E
qyh nisadyn aq iby aes ksafrbi fn ia iby necp, hbysy hy sec enbasy.
Lacnygw hen ragcr ia jftx ac ia iby wecp, hbyc G bywp bgt keld.

"Ngs," negp G ia Lexiegc Cyta, "ia oaf kywacrn iby bacafs aq qgsni
nyiigcr qaai ac ibgn wecp."

"Oyn, ngs," negp iby Lexiegc, "ecp gq G pa cai byngieiy ia isyep ibgn
Nafib Xawy, gi gn kylefny, fx ia ibgn igty, ca bftec kygcr ben wyqi e
isely ibysy."

Neogcr ibgn, by jftxyp wgrbiwo ac ia iby necp.  Bgn byesi kyei hgib
ytaigac.  By lwgtkyp e sald, nwaxgcr ia e wgiiwy xsataciaso, ecp ibysy,
hgib bgn estn lsannyp, tfiy ecp taigacwynn, ecp hgib ec yerys waad, by
nyytyp ia iedy xannynngac aq ibyny nafibysc syrgacn.  Eqiys qgvy
tgcfiyn xennyp gc ibgn ylnieno, by ifscyp ia fn.

"Hbyc oaf wgdy, ngs."

G wecpyp, qawwahyp ko Lacnygw, wyevgcr iby iha tyc gc iby kaei.  Qas e
wacr heo iby nagw hen latxanyp aq e syppgnb necpo niacy, natyibgcr wgdy
lsfnbyp ksgld, nlasgey, nisyetn aq weve, ecp xftgly-niacyn. Acy lafwp
cai tgniedy gin vawlecgl asgrgc.  Gc naty xesin, nwgrbi lfswn aq ntady
ytgiiyp e nfwxbfsafn ntyww, xsavgcr ibei iby gciyscew qgsyn bep wani
caibgcr aq ibygs ymxecngvy xahysn, ibafrb, bevgcr lwgtkyp e bgrb
ellwgvgio, G lafwp nyy ca vawleca qas e sepgfn aq nyvysew tgwyn.  Hy
dcah ibei gc ibany Eciesligl lafcisgyn, Jetyn Sann qafcp iha lseiysn,
iby Ysykfn ecp Iyssas, gc qfww eligvgio, ac iby 167ib tysgpgec,
weigifpy 77° 32'. Iby vyryieigac aq ibgn pynaweiy lacigcyci nyytyp
ia ty tflb synisgliyp.  Naty wglbycn weo fxac iby kweld saldn; naty
tglsanlaxgl xwecin, sfpgtycieso pgeiaten, e dgcp aq lywwn xwelyp
kyihyyc iha zfesiu nbywwn; wacr xfsxwy ecp nleswyi hyyp, nfxxasiyp ac
wgiiwy nhgttgcr kweppysn, hbglb iby ksyedgcr aq iby hevyn ksafrbi ia
iby nbasy.  Ibyny lacnigifiyp iby tyersy qwase aq ibgn syrgac.  Iby
nbasy hen nisyhc hgib tawwfnln, wgiiwy tfnnywn, ecp wgtxyin.  G ewna
neh tosgepn aq casibysc lwgan, acy-ecp-e-zfesiys gclbyn wacr, aq hbglb
e hbewy hafwp nhewwah e hbawy haswp ei e tafibqfw; ecp naty xysqyli
nye-kfiiysqwgyn, ecgteigcr iby heiysn ac iby ndgsin aq iby nbasy.

Ibysy exxyesyp ac iby bgrb kaiiatn naty lasew nbsfkn, aq iby dgcp
hbglb, ellaspgcr ia Jetyn Sann, wgvy gc iby Eciesligl nyen ia iby pyxib
aq tasy ibec 1,000 oespn.  Ibyc ibysy hysy wgiiwy dgcrqgnbysn ecp
niesqgnb nifppgcr iby nagw.  Kfi hbysy wgqy ekafcpyp tani hen gc iby
egs.  Ibysy ibafnecpn aq kgspn qwfiiysyp ecp qwyh aq eww dgcpn,
pyeqycgcr fn hgib ibygs lsgyn; aibysn lsahpyp iby sald, waadgcr ei fn
en hy xennyp ko hgibafi qyes, ecp xsynngcr qetgwgeswo lwany ko afs
qyyi.  Ibysy hysy xycrfgcn, na ergwy gc iby heiys, byevo ecp ehdhesp en
ibyo esy ac iby rsafcp; ibyo hysy fiiysgcr besnb lsgyn, e wesry
ennytkwo, nakys gc rynifsy, kfi ymisevereci gc lwetafs.  Ewkeisannyn
xennyp gc iby egs, iby ymxecny aq ibygs hgcrn kygcr ei wyeni qafs oespn
ecp e bewq, ecp jfniwo lewwyp iby vfwifsyn aq iby alyec; naty rgrecigl
xyisywn, ecp naty petgysn, e dgcp aq nteww pfld, iby fcpysxesi aq hbany
kapo gn kweld ecp hbgiy; ibyc ibysy hysy e hbawy nysgyn aq xyisywn,
naty hbgignb, hgib ksahc-kaspysyp hgcrn, aibysn kwfy, xylfwges ia iby
Eciesligl nyen, ecp na agwo, en G iawp Lacnygw, ibei iby gcbekgiecin aq
iby Qyssay Gnwecpn bep caibgcr ia pa kyqasy wgrbigcr ibyt kfi ia xfi e
hgld gc.

"E wgiiwy tasy," negp Lacnygw, "ecp ibyo hafwp ky xysqyli wetxn!  Eqiys
ibei, hy leccai ymxyli Ceifsy ia bevy xsyvgafnwo qfscgnbyp ibyt hgib
hgldn!"

Ekafi bewq e tgwy qesibys ac iby nagw hen sgppwyp hgib sfqqn' cynin, e
nasi aq weogcr-rsafcp, afi aq hbglb teco kgspn hysy gnnfgcr.  Lexiegc
Cyta bep naty bfcpsypn bfciyp.  Ibyo fiiysyp e lso wgdy iby kseogcr aq
ec enn, hysy ekafi iby nguy aq e raany, nweiy-lawafs ac iby kapo, hbgiy
kycyeib, hgib e oywwah wgcy safcp ibygs ibsaein; ibyo ewwahyp
ibytnywvyn ia ky dgwwyp hgib e niacy, cyvys isogcr ia ynlexy.  Kfi iby
qar pgp cai wgqi, ecp ei ywyvyc iby nfc bep cai oyi nbahc ginywq.  Gin
eknycly tepy ty fcyeno.  Hgibafi gi ca aknysveigacn hysy xanngkwy.
Bah, ibyc, lafwp hy pylgpy hbyibys hy bep syelbyp iby xawy?  Hbyc G
syjagcyp Lexiegc Cyta, G qafcp bgt wyecgcr ac e xgyly aq sald, ngwyciwo
heilbgcr iby ndo.  By nyytyp gtxeigyci ecp vymyp.  Kfi hbei hen ia ky
pacy?  Ibgn senb ecp xahysqfw tec lafwp cai lattecp iby nfc en by pgp
iby nye.  Caac essgvyp hgibafi iby ask aq peo nbahgcr ginywq qas ec
gcnieci.  Hy lafwp cai yvyc iyww gin xangigac kybgcp iby lfsiegc aq
qar; ecp naac iby qar ifscyp ia ncah.

"Igww ia-tassah," negp iby Lexiegc, zfgyiwo, ecp hy syifscyp ia iby
Cefigwfn etgp ibyny eitanxbysgl pgnifskeclyn.

Iby iytxyni aq ncah lacigcfyp igww iby cymi peo.  Gi hen gtxanngkwy ia
sytegc ac iby xweiqast.  Qsat iby newaac, hbysy G hen iedgcr caiyn aq
gclgpycin bexxycgcr pfsgcr ibgn ymlfsngac ia iby xawes lacigcyci, G
lafwp byes iby lsgyn aq xyisywn ecp ewkeisannyn nxasigcr gc iby tgpni
aq ibgn vgawyci niast.  Iby Cefigwfn pgp cai sytegc taigacwynn, kfi
ndgsiyp iby laeni, epveclgcr iyc tgwyn tasy ia iby nafib gc iby
bewq-wgrbi wyqi ko iby nfc en gi ndgsiyp iby ypry aq iby basguac.  Iby
cymi peo, iby 20ib aq Teslb, iby ncah bep lyenyp.  Iby lawp hen e
wgiiwy rsyeiys, iby ibystatyiys nbahgcr 2° kywah uysa.  Iby qar
hen sgngcr, ecp G baxyp ibei ibei peo afs aknysveigacn tgrbi ky iedyc.
Lexiegc Cyta cai bevgcr oyi exxyesyp, iby kaei iaad Lacnygw ecp tonywq
ia wecp.  Iby nagw hen nigww aq iby nety vawlecgl ceifsy; yvysohbysy
hysy iselyn aq weve, nlasgey, ecp kenewi; kfi iby lseiys hbglb bep
vatgiyp ibyt G lafwp cai nyy.  Bysy, en wahys pahc, ibgn lacigcyci hen
ewgvy hgib tosgepn aq kgspn.  Kfi ibygs sfwy hen cah pgvgpyp hgib wesry
isaaxn aq nye-tettewn, waadgcr ei fn hgib ibygs naqi yoyn.  Ibysy hysy
nyvysew dgcpn aq nyewn, naty nisyilbyp ac iby yesib, naty ac qwedyn aq
gly, teco ragcr gc ecp afi aq iby nye.  Ibyo pgp cai qwyy ei afs
exxsaelb, cyvys bevgcr bep ecoibgcr ia pa hgib tec; ecp G syldacyp ibei
ibysy hysy xsavgngacn ibysy qas bfcpsypn aq vynnywn.

"Ngs," negp Lacnygw, "hgww oaf iyww ty iby cetyn aq ibyny lsyeifsyn?"

"Ibyo esy nyewn ecp tasnyn."

Gi hen cah ygrbi gc iby tascgcr.  Qafs bafsn sytegcyp ia fn kyqasy iby
nfc lafwp ky aknysvyp hgib epveciery.  G pgsyliyp afs niyxn iahespn e
veni keo lfi gc iby niyyx rsecgiy nbasy.  Ibysy, G lec evys ibei yesib
ecp gly hysy wani ia ngrbi ko iby cftkysn aq nye-tettewn lavysgcr ibyt,
ecp G gcvawfciesgwo nafrbi qas awp Xsaiyfn, iby toibawarglew nbyxbysp
hba heilbyp ibyny gttycny qwaldn aq Cyxifcy.  Ibysy hysy tasy nyewn
ibec ecoibgcr ywny, qastgcr pgnigcli rsafxn, tewy ecp qytewy, iby
qeibys heilbgcr avys bgn qetgwo, iby taibys nfldwgcr bys wgiiwy acyn,
naty ewsyepo nisacr ycafrb ia ra e qyh niyxn.  Hbyc ibyo hgnbyp ia
lbecry ibygs xwely, ibyo iaad wgiiwy jftxn, tepy ko iby laciseligac aq
ibygs kapgyn, ecp bywxyp ehdhespwo ycafrb ko ibygs gtxysqyli qgc,
hbglb, en hgib iby wetecigc, ibygs lafngcn, qastn e xysqyli qasyest.  G
nbafwp neo ibei, gc iby heiys, hbglb gn ibygs ywytyci--iby nxgcy aq
ibyny lsyeifsyn gn qwymgkwy; hgib ntaaib ecp lwany ndgc ecp hykkyp
qyyi--ibyo nhgt eptgsekwo.  Gc synigcr ac iby yesib ibyo iedy iby tani
rselyqfw eiigifpyn.  Ibfn iby eclgycin, aknysvgcr ibygs naqi ecp
ymxsynngvy waadn, hbglb leccai ky nfsxennyp ko iby tani kyefigqfw waad
e hatec lec rgvy, ibygs lwyes vawfxifafn yoyn, ibygs lbestgcr
xangigacn, ecp iby xayiso aq ibygs teccysn, tyietasxbanyp ibyt, iby
tewy gcia e isgiac ecp iby qytewy gcia e tystegp.  G tepy Lacnygw
caigly iby lacngpysekwy pyvywaxtyci aq iby wakyn aq iby ksegc gc ibyny
gciysynigcr lyielyecn.  Ca tettew, ymlyxi tec, ben nflb e zfecigio aq
ksegc teiiys; ibyo esy ewna lexekwy aq sylygvgcr e lysiegc etafci aq
ypfleigac, esy yengwo patynigleiyp, ecp G ibgcd, hgib aibys
ceifsewgnin, ibei gq xsaxyswo iefrbi ibyo hafwp ky aq rsyei nysvgly en
qgnbgcr-parn.  Iby rsyeiys xesi aq ibyt nwyxi ac iby saldn as ac iby
necp.  Etacrni ibyny nyewn, xsaxyswo na lewwyp, hbglb bevy ca ymiyscew
yesn (gc hbglb ibyo pgqqys qsat iby aiiys, hbany yesn esy xsatgcyci), G
caiglyp nyvysew vesgyigyn aq nyewn ekafi ibsyy oespn wacr, hgib e hbgiy
laei, kfwwpar byepn, estyp hgib iyyib gc kaib jehn, qafs gclgnasn ei
iby iax ecp qafs ei iby kaiiat, ecp iha wesry lecgcy iyyib gc iby nbexy
aq e qwyfs-py-wgn. Etacrni ibyt rwgpyp nye-ywyxbecin, e dgcp aq nyew,
hgib nbasi, qwymgkwy isfcdn.  Iby rgecin aq ibgn nxylgyn tyenfsyp
ihycio qyyi safcp ecp iyc oespn ecp e bewq gc wycrib; kfi ibyo pgp cai
tavy en hy exxsaelbyp.

"Ibyny lsyeifsyn esy cai pecrysafn?" endyp Lacnygw.

"Ca; cai fcwynn oaf eiield ibyt.  Hbyc ibyo bevy ia pyqycp ibygs oafcr

nisyilbyp avys fn wgdy ec gttycny lygwgcr.  Kycyeib, kylefny iby

iby weiysew hewwn, hbglb dyxi gi gc ibei xangigac.  Iby Cefigwfn hen
syewwo gtxsgnacyp gc e xysqyli ifccyw aq gly tasy ibec ihycio oespn gc
ksyepib, qgwwyp hgib zfgyi heiys.  Gi hen yeno ia ryi afi aq gi ko
ragcr ygibys qashesp as keldhesp, ecp ibyc tedy e qsyy xennery fcpys
iby glykysr, naty bfcpsypn aq oespn pyyxys.  Iby wftgcafn lygwgcr bep
kyyc ymigcrfgnbyp, kfi iby newaac hen nigww synxwycpyci hgib gciycny
wgrbi.  Gi hen iby xahysqfw syqwyligac qsat iby rwenn xesigigac nyci
vgawyciwo keld ia iby nbyyin aq iby weciysc.  G leccai pynlsgky iby
yqqyli aq iby vawiegl seon fxac iby rsyei kwaldn na lexsglgafnwo lfi;
fxac yvyso ecrwy, yvyso sgpry, yvyso qelyi hen ibsahc e pgqqysyci
wgrbi, ellaspgcr ia iby ceifsy aq iby vygcn sfccgcr ibsafrb iby gly; e
peuuwgcr tgcy aq rytn, xesiglfweswo aq nexxbgsyn, ibygs kwfy seon
lsanngcr hgib iby rsyyc aq iby ytysewp.  Bysy ecp ibysy hysy axew
nbepyn aq hacpysqfw naqicynn, sfccgcr ibsafrb ksgrbi nxain wgdy
pgetacpn aq qgsy, iby ksgwwgeclo aq hbglb iby yoy lafwp cai kyes.  Iby
xahys aq iby weciysc nyytyp gclsyenyp e bfcpsypqawp, wgdy e wetx
ibsafrb iby wyciglfwes xweiyn aq e qgsni-lwenn wgrbibafny.

"Bah kyefigqfw! bah kyefigqfw!" lsgyp Lacnygw.

"Oyn," G negp, "gi gn e hacpysqfw ngrbi.  Gn gi cai, Cyp?"

"Oyn, lacqafcp gi!  Oyn," ecnhysyp Cyp Wecp, "gi gn nfxysk!  G et tep
ei kygcr akwgryp ia eptgi gi.  Ca acy ben yvys nyyc ecoibgcr wgdy gi;
kfi iby ngrbi teo lani fn pyes.  Ecp, gq G tfni neo eww, G ibgcd hy esy
nyygcr bysy ibgcrn hbglb Rap cyvys gciycpyp tec ia nyy."

Cyp hen sgrbi, gi hen iaa kyefigqfw.  Nfppycwo e lso qsat Lacnygw tepy
ty ifsc.

"Hbei gn gi?"  G endyp.

"Nbfi oafs yoyn, ngs!  Pa cai waad, ngs!"  Neogcr hbglb, Lacnygw
lwexxyp bgn becpn avys bgn yoyn.

"Kfi hbei gn iby teiiys, to kao?"

"G et peuuwyp, kwgcpyp."

To yoyn ifscyp gcvawfciesgwo iahespn iby rwenn, kfi G lafwp cai niecp
iby qgsy hbglb nyytyp ia pyvafs ibyt.  G fcpysniaap hbei bep bexxycyp.
Iby Cefigwfn bep xfi ac qfww nxyyp.  Eww iby zfgyi wfnisy aq iby
gly-hewwn hen ei acly lbecryp gcia qwenbyn aq wgrbicgcr.  Iby qgsy qsat
ibyny tosgepn aq pgetacpn hen kwgcpgcr.  Gi syzfgsyp naty igty ia lewt
afs isafkwyp waadn.  Ei weni iby becpn hysy iedyc pahc.

"Qegib, G nbafwp cyvys bevy kywgyvyp gi," negp Lacnygw.

Gi hen ibyc qgvy gc iby tascgcr; ecp ei ibei tatyci e nbald hen qywi ei
iby kahn aq iby Cefigwfn.  G dcyh ibei gin nxfs bep nisfld e kwald aq
gly.  Gi tfni bevy kyyc e qewny tecayfvsy, qas ibgn nfktesgcy ifccyw,
aknisfliyp ko kwaldn, hen cai vyso yeno cevgreigac.  G ibafrbi ibei
Lexiegc Cyta, ko lbecrgcr bgn lafsny, hafwp ygibys ifsc ibyny aknielwyn
as ywny qawwah iby hgcpgcrn aq iby ifccyw.  Gc eco leny, iby saep
kyqasy fn lafwp cai ky ycigsywo kwaldyp.  Kfi, laciseso ia to
ymxylieigacn, iby Cefigwfn iaad e pylgpyp syisarsepy taigac.

"Hy esy ragcr keldhespn?" negp Lacnygw.

"Oyn," G syxwgyp.  "Ibgn ycp aq iby ifccyw lec bevy ca yrsynn."

"Ecp ibyc?"

"Ibyc," negp G, "iby hasdgcr gn yeno.  Hy tfni ra keld eregc, ecp ra
afi ei iby nafibysc axycgcr.  Ibei gn eww."

Gc nxyedgcr ibfn, G hgnbyp ia exxyes tasy lacqgpyci ibec G syewwo hen.
Kfi iby syisarsepy taigac aq iby Cefigwfn hen gclsyengcr; ecp,
syvysngcr iby nlsyh, gi lessgyp fn ei rsyei nxyyp.

"Gi hgww ky e bgcpsecly," negp Cyp.

"Hbei payn gi teiiys, naty bafsn tasy as wynn, xsavgpyp hy ryi afi ei
weni?"

"Oyn," syxyeiyp Cyp Wecp, "xsavgpyp hy pa ryi afi ei weni!"

Qas e nbasi igty G hewdyp qsat iby newaac ia iby wgkseso.  To
latxecgacn hysy ngwyci.  G naac ibsyh tonywq ac ec aiiatec, ecp iaad e
kaad, hbglb to yoyn avyssec tylbecglewwo.  E zfesiys aq ec bafs eqiys,
Lacnygw, exxsaelbgcr ty, negp, "Gn hbei oaf esy syepgcr vyso
gciysynigcr, ngs?"

"Vyso gciysynigcr!"  G syxwgyp.

"G nbafwp ibgcd na, ngs.  Gi gn oafs ahc kaad oaf esy syepgcr."

"To kaad?"

Ecp gcpyyp G hen bawpgcr gc to becp iby hasd ac iby Rsyei Nfktesgcy
Pyxibn.  G pgp cai yvyc psyet aq gi.  G lwanyp iby kaad ecp syifscyp ia
to hewd.  Cyp ecp Lacnygw sany ia ra.

"Nieo bysy, to qsgycpn," negp G, pyiegcgcr ibyt.  "Wyi fn sytegc
iaryibys fcigw hy esy afi aq ibgn kwald."

"En oaf xwyeny, ngs," Lacnygw syxwgyp.

Naty bafsn xennyp.  G aqiyc waadyp ei iby gcnisftycin becrgcr qsat iby
xesigigac.  Iby tecatyiys nbahyp ibei iby Cefigwfn dyxi ei e lacnieci
pyxib aq tasy ibec ibsyy bfcpsyp oespn; iby latxenn nigww xagciyp ia
nafib; iby war gcpgleiyp e nxyyp aq ihycio tgwyn ec bafs, hbglb, gc
nflb e lsetxyp nxely, hen vyso rsyei.  Kfi Lexiegc Cyta dcyh ibei by
lafwp cai beniyc iaa tflb, ecp ibei tgcfiyn hysy hasib eryn ia fn.  Ei
ihycio-qgvy tgcfiyn xeni ygrbi e nylacp nbald iaad xwely, ibgn igty
qsat kybgcp.  G ifscyp xewy.  To latxecgacn hysy lwany ko to ngpy.  G
nyguyp Lacnygw'n becp.  Afs waadn ymxsynnyp afs qyywgcrn kyiiys ibec
haspn.  Ei ibgn tatyci iby Lexiegc yciysyp iby newaac.  G hyci fx ia
bgt.

"Afs lafsny gn kessyp nafibhesp?"  G endyp.

"Oyn, ngs.  Iby glykysr ben nbgqiyp ecp lwanyp yvyso afiwyi."

"Hy esy kwaldyp fx ibyc?"

"Oyn."



LBEXIYS MVG

HECI AQ EGS

Ibfn esafcp iby Cefigwfn, ekavy ecp kywah, hen ec gtxycyisekwy heww aq
gly.  Hy hysy xsgnacysn ia iby glykysr.  G heilbyp iby Lexiegc.  Bgn
lafciycecly bep synftyp gin bekgifew gtxysifskekgwgio.

"Ryciwytyc," by negp lewtwo, "ibysy esy iha heon aq pogcr gc iby
lgslftnieclyn gc hbglb hy esy xwelyp."  (Ibgn xfuuwgcr xysnac bep iby
egs aq e teibyteiglew xsaqynnas wylifsgcr ia bgn xfxgwn.) "Iby qgsni gn
ia ky lsfnbyp; iby nylacp gn ia pgy aq nfqqaleigac.  G pa cai nxyed aq
iby xanngkgwgio aq pogcr aq bfcrys, qas iby nfxxwo aq xsavgngacn gc iby
Cefigwfn hgww lysiegcwo weni wacrys ibec hy nbeww.  Wyi fn, ibyc,
lewlfweiy afs lbeclyn."

"En ia nfqqaleigac, Lexiegc," G syxwgyp, "ibei gn cai ia ky qyesyp,
kylefny afs synysvagsn esy qfww."

"Jfni na; kfi ibyo hgww acwo ogywp iha peon' nfxxwo aq egs.  Cah, qas
ibgsio-ngm bafsn hy bevy kyyc bgppyc fcpys iby heiys, ecp ewsyepo iby
byevo eitanxbysy aq iby Cefigwfn syzfgsyn sycyhew.  Gc qasio-ygrbi
bafsn afs synysvy hgww ky ymbefniyp."

"Hyww, Lexiegc, lec hy ky pywgvysyp kyqasy qasio-ygrbi bafsn?"

"Hy hgww eiiytxi gi, ei wyeni, ko xgyslgcr iby heww ibei nfssafcpn fn."

"Ac hbglb ngpy?"

"Nafcp hgww iyww fn.  G et ragcr ia sfc iby Cefigwfn ersafcp ac iby
wahys kecd, ecp to tyc hgww eiield iby glykysr ac iby ngpy ibei gn
wyeni ibgld."

Lexiegc Cyta hyci afi.  Naac G pgnlavysyp ko e bgnngcr cagny ibei iby
heiys hen yciysgcr iby synysvagsn.  Iby Cefigwfn necd nwahwo, ecp
syniyp ac iby gly ei e pyxib aq 350 oespn, iby pyxib ei hbglb iby wahys
kecd hen gttysnyp.

"To qsgycpn," G negp, "afs ngifeigac gn nysgafn, kfi G sywo ac oafs
lafsery ecp ycysro."

"Ngs," syxwgyp iby Lecepgec, "G et syepo ia pa ecoibgcr qas iby rycysew
neqyio."

"Raap!  Cyp," ecp G bywp afi to becp ia iby Lecepgec.

"G hgww epp," by lacigcfyp, "ibei, kygcr en becpo hgib iby xgldemy en
hgib iby besxaac, gq G lec ky fnyqfw ia iby Lexiegc, by lec lattecp to
nysvglyn."

"By hgww cai syqfny oafs bywx.  Laty, Cyp!"

G wyp bgt ia iby saat hbysy iby lsyh aq iby Cefigwfn hysy xfiigcr ac
ibygs lasd-jeldyin. G iawp iby Lexiegc aq Cyp'n xsaxanew, hbglb by
ellyxiyp.  Iby Lecepgec xfi ac bgn nye-lanifty, ecp hen syepo en naac
en bgn latxecgacn.  Hbyc Cyp hen psynnyp, G sy-yciysyp iby
psehgcr-saat, hbysy iby xecyn aq rwenn hysy axyc, ecp, xaniyp cyes
Lacnygw, G ymetgcyp iby etkgyci kypn ibei nfxxasiyp iby Cefigwfn.  Naty
gcniecin eqiys, hy neh e pauyc aq iby lsyh nyi qaai ac iby kecd aq gly,
ecp etacr ibyt Cyp Wecp, yengwo dcahc ko bgn nieifsy.  Lexiegc Cyta hen
hgib ibyt.  Kyqasy xsalyypgcr ia pgr iby hewwn, by iaad iby nafcpgcrn,
ia ky nfsy aq hasdgcr gc iby sgrbi pgsyligac.  Wacr nafcpgcr wgcyn hysy
nfcd gc iby ngpy hewwn, kfi eqiys qgqiyyc oespn ibyo hysy eregc niaxxyp
ko iby ibgld heww.  Gi hen fnywynn ia eiield gi ac iby lygwgcr-wgdy
nfsqely, ngcly iby glykysr ginywq tyenfsyp tasy ibec 400 oespn gc
bygrbi.  Lexiegc Cyta ibyc nafcpyp iby wahys nfsqely.  Ibysy iyc oespn
aq heww nyxeseiyp fn qsat iby heiys, na rsyei hen iby ibgldcynn aq iby
gly-qgywp. Gi hen cylynneso, ibysyqasy, ia lfi qsat gi e xgyly yzfew gc
ymiyci ia iby heiyswgcy aq iby Cefigwfn.  Ibysy hysy ekafi 6,000 lfkgl
oespn ia pyielb, na en ia pgr e bawy ko hbglb hy lafwp pynlycp ia iby
gly-qgywp. Iby hasd bep kyrfc gttypgeiywo ecp lessgyp ac hgib
gcpyqeigrekwy ycysro.  Gcniyep aq pgrrgcr safcp iby Cefigwfn hbglb
hafwp bevy gcvawvyp rsyeiys pgqqglfwio, Lexiegc Cyta bep ec gttycny
isyclb tepy ei ygrbi oespn qsat iby xasi-zfesiys. Ibyc iby tyc nyi ia
hasd ngtfwiecyafnwo hgib ibygs nlsyhn ac nyvysew xagcin aq gin
lgslftqysycly.  Xsynyciwo iby xgldemy eiieldyp ibgn latxeli teiiys
vgrasafnwo, ecp wesry kwaldn hysy pyielbyp qsat iby tenn.  Ko e lfsgafn
yqqyli aq nxylgqgl rsevgio, ibyny kwaldn, wgrbiys ibec heiys, qwyp, na
ia nxyed, ia iby vefwi aq iby ifccyw, ibei gclsyenyp gc ibgldcynn ei
iby iax gc xsaxasigac en gi pgtgcgnbyp ei iby keny.  Kfi ibei teiiysyp
wgiiwy, na wacr en iby wahys xesi rsyh ibgccys.  Eqiys iha bafsn' besp
hasd, Cyp Wecp lety gc ymbefniyp.  By ecp bgn latsepyn hysy syxwelyp ko
cyh hasdysn, hbat Lacnygw ecp G jagcyp.  Iby nylacp wgyfiyceci aq iby
Cefigwfn nfxysgciycpyp fn.  Iby heiys nyytyp ngcrfweswo lawp, kfi G
naac rai hest becpwgcr iby xgldemy.  To tavytycin hysy qsyy ycafrb,
ewibafrb ibyo hysy tepy fcpys e xsynnfsy aq ibgsio eitanxbysyn.  Hbyc G
sy-yciysyp, eqiys hasdgcr iha bafsn, ia iedy naty qaap ecp syni, G
qafcp e xyslyxigkwy pgqqysycly kyihyyc iby xfsy qwfgp hgib hbglb iby
Safzfeosaw ycrgcy nfxxwgyp ty ecp iby eitanxbysy aq iby Cefigwfn,
ewsyepo lbesryp hgib leskacgl elgp.  Iby egs bep cai kyyc sycyhyp qas
qasio-ygrbi bafsn, ecp gin vgvgqogcr zfewgigyn hysy lacngpysekwo
ycqyykwyp.  Bahyvys, eqiys e wexny aq ihywvy bafsn, hy bep acwo segnyp
e kwald aq gly acy oesp ibgld, ac iby tesdyp nfsqely, hbglb hen ekafi
600 lfkgl oespn!  Syldacgcr ibei gi iaad ihywvy bafsn ia ellatxwgnb
ibgn tflb gi hafwp iedy qgvy cgrbin ecp qafs peon ia ksgcr ibgn
yciysxsgny ia e neignqeliaso laclwfngac.  Qgvy cgrbin ecp qafs peon!
Ecp hy bevy acwo egs ycafrb qas iha peon gc iby synysvagsn!  "Hgibafi
iedgcr gcia ellafci," negp Cyp, "ibei, yvyc gq hy ryi afi aq ibgn
gcqyscew xsgnac, hy nbeww ewna ky gtxsgnacyp fcpys iby glykysr, nbfi
afi qsat eww xanngkwy lattfcgleigac hgib iby eitanxbysy." Isfy ycafrb!
Hba lafwp ibyc qasynyy iby tgcgtft aq igty cylynneso qas afs
pywgvysecly?  Hy tgrbi ky nfqqaleiyp kyqasy iby Cefigwfn lafwp syregc
iby nfsqely aq iby hevyn?  Hen gi pynigcyp ia xysgnb gc ibgn gly-iatk,
hgib eww ibany gi yclwanyp?  Iby ngifeigac hen iyssgkwy.  Kfi yvysoacy
bep waadyp iby pecrys gc iby qely, ecp yelb hen pyiystgcyp ia pa bgn
pfio ia iby weni.

En G ymxyliyp, pfsgcr iby cgrbi e cyh kwald e oesp nzfesy hen lessgyp
eheo, ecp nigww qfsibys necd iby gttycny bawwah.  Kfi gc iby tascgcr
hbyc, psynnyp gc to lasd-jeldyi, G isevysnyp iby nwfnbo tenn ei e
iytxyseifsy aq ngm as nyvyc pyrsyyn kywah uysa, G sytesdyp ibei iby
ngpy hewwn hysy rsepfewwo lwangcr gc.  Iby kypn aq heiys qesibyni qsat
iby isyclb, ibei hysy cai hestyp ko iby tyc'n hasd, nbahyp e iycpyclo
ia nawgpgqgleigac.  Gc xsynycly aq ibgn cyh ecp gttgcyci pecrys, hbei
hafwp kylaty aq afs lbeclyn aq neqyio, ecp bah bgcpys iby
nawgpgqgleigac aq ibgn wgzfgp typgft, ibei hafwp kfsni iby xesigigacn
aq iby Cefigwfn wgdy rwenn?

G pgp cai iyww to latxecgacn aq ibgn cyh pecrys.  Hbei hen iby raap aq
petxgcr iby ycysro ibyo pgnxweoyp gc iby xegcqfw hasd aq ynlexy?  Kfi
hbyc G hyci ac kaesp eregc, G iawp Lexiegc Cyta aq ibgn rsevy
latxwgleigac.

"G dcah gi," by negp, gc ibei lewt iacy hbglb lafwp lafciyseli iby tani
iyssgkwy exxsybycngacn.  "Gi gn acy pecrys tasy; kfi G nyy ca heo aq
ynlexgcr gi; iby acwo lbecly aq neqyio gn ia ra zfgldys ibec
nawgpgqgleigac.  Hy tfni ky kyqasybecp hgib gi, ibei gn eww."

Ac ibgn peo qas nyvysew bafsn G fnyp to xgldemy vgrasafnwo.  Iby hasd
dyxi ty fx.  Kyngpyn, ia hasd hen ia zfgi iby Cefigwfn, ecp ksyeiby
pgsyliwo iby xfsy egs psehc qsat iby synysvagsn, ecp nfxxwgyp ko afs
exxeseifn, ecp ia zfgi iby gtxavysgnbyp ecp vgigeiyp eitanxbysy.
Iahespn yvycgcr iby isyclb hen pfr acy oesp pyyxys.  Hbyc G syifscyp ac
kaesp, G hen cyeswo nfqqaleiyp ko iby leskacgl elgp hgib hbglb iby egs
hen qgwwyp--eb! gq hy bep acwo iby lbytglew tyecn ia psgvy eheo ibgn
pywyiysgafn ren.  Hy bep xwycio aq amoryc; eww ibgn heiys laciegcyp e
lacngpysekwy zfecigio, ecp ko pgnnawvgcr gi hgib afs xahysqfw xgwyn, gi
hafwp syniasy iby vgvgqogcr qwfgp.  G bep ibafrbi hyww avys gi; kfi aq
hbei raap hen ibei, ngcly iby leskacgl elgp xsapflyp ko afs synxgseigac
bep gcvepyp yvyso xesi aq iby vynnyw?  Ia eknask gi, gi hen cylynneso
ia qgww naty jesn hgib lefnigl xaienb, ecp ia nbedy ibyt gclynneciwo.
Cah ibgn nfkniecly hen hecigcr ac kaesp, ecp caibgcr lafwp syxwely gi.
Ac ibei yvycgcr, Lexiegc Cyta afrbi ia axyc iby iexn aq bgn synysvagsn,
ecp wyi naty xfsy egs gcia iby gciysgas aq iby Cefigwfn; hgibafi ibgn
xsylefigac hy lafwp cai ryi sgp aq iby nycny aq nfqqaleigac.  Iby cymi
peo, Teslb 26ib, G synftyp to tgcys'n hasd gc kyrgccgcr iby qgqib oesp.
Iby ngpy hewwn ecp iby wahys nfsqely aq iby glykysr ibgldycyp vgngkwo.
Gi hen yvgpyci ibei ibyo hafwp tyyi kyqasy iby Cefigwfn hen ekwy ia
pgnycrery ginywq.  Pynxegs nyguyp ty qas ec gcnieci; to xgldemy cyeswo
qyww qsat to becpn.  Hbei hen iby raap aq pgrrgcr gq G tfni ky
nfqqaleiyp, lsfnbyp ko iby heiys ibei hen ifscgcr gcia niacy?--e
xfcgnbtyci ibei iby qysalgio aq iby neveryn yvyc hafwp cai bevy
gcvyciyp!  Jfni ibyc Lexiegc Cyta xennyp cyes ty.  G iaflbyp bgn becp
ecp nbahyp bgt iby hewwn aq afs xsgnac.  Iby heww ia xasi bep epveclyp
ia ei wyeni qafs oespn qsat iby bfww aq iby Cefigwfn.  Iby Lexiegc
fcpysniaap ty, ecp ngrcyp ty ia qawwah bgt.  Hy hyci ac kaesp.  G iaad
aqq to lasd-jeldyi ecp ellatxecgyp bgt gcia iby psehgcr-saat.

"T. Esaccem, hy tfni eiiytxi naty pynxyseiy tyecn, as hy nbeww ky
nyewyp fx gc ibgn nawgpgqgyp heiys en gc lytyci."

"Oyn; kfi hbei gn ia ky pacy?"

"Eb! gq to Cefigwfn hysy nisacr ycafrb ia kyes ibgn xsynnfsy hgibafi
kygcr lsfnbyp!"

"Hyww?"  G endyp, cai leilbgcr iby Lexiegc'n gpye.

"Pa oaf cai fcpysniecp," by syxwgyp, "ibei ibgn lacryweigac aq heiys
hgww bywx fn?  Pa oaf cai nyy ibei ko gin nawgpgqgleigac, gi hafwp
kfsni ibsafrb ibgn qgywp aq gly ibei gtxsgnacn fn, en, hbyc gi qsyyuyn,
gi kfsnin iby bespyni niacyn?  Pa oaf cai xyslygvy ibei gi hafwp ky ec
eryci aq neqyio gcniyep aq pynisfligac?"

"Oyn, Lexiegc, xysbexn.  Kfi, hbeiyvys syngniecly ia lsfnbgcr iby
Cefigwfn xannynnyn, gi lafwp cai nfxxasi ibgn iyssgkwy xsynnfsy, ecp
hafwp ky qweiiycyp wgdy ec gsac xweiy."

"G dcah gi, ngs.  Ibysyqasy hy tfni cai syldac ac iby egp aq ceifsy,
kfi ac afs ahc ymysigacn.  Hy tfni niax ibgn nawgpgqgleigac.  Cai acwo
hgww iby ngpy hewwn ky xsynnyp iaryibys; kfi ibysy gn cai iyc qyyi aq
heiys kyqasy as kybgcp iby Cefigwfn.  Iby lacryweigac regcn ac fn ac
eww ngpyn."

"Bah wacr hgww iby egs gc iby synysvagsn weni qas fn ia ksyeiby ac
kaesp?"

Iby Lexiegc waadyp gc to qely.  "Eqiys ia-tassah ibyo hgww ky ytxio!"

E lawp nhyei lety avys ty.  Bahyvys, afrbi G ia bevy kyyc eniacgnbyp ei
iby ecnhys?  Ac Teslb 22, iby Cefigwfn hen gc iby axyc xawes nyen.  Hy
hysy ei 26°. Qas qgvy peon hy bep wgvyp ac iby synysvy ac kaesp.
Ecp hbei hen wyqi aq iby synxgsekwy egs tfni ky dyxi qas iby hasdysn.
Yvyc cah, en G hsgiy, to sylawwyligac gn nigww na vgvgp ibei ec
gcvawfcieso iyssas nyguyn ty ecp to wfcrn nyyt ia ky hgibafi egs.

nisfld bgt; kfi by nyytyp ia syjyli gi.  Ei weni, ibyny haspn ynlexyp
bgn wgxn:

"Kagwgcr heiys!" by tfiiysyp.

"Kagwgcr heiys?"  G lsgyp.

"Oyn, ngs.  Hy esy yclwanyp gc e nxely ibei gn syweigvywo lacqgcyp.
Hafwp cai jyin aq kagwgcr heiys, lacnieciwo gcjyliyp ko iby xftxn,
segny iby iytxyseifsy gc ibgn xesi ecp nieo iby lacryweigac?"

"Wyi fn iso gi," G negp synawfiywo.

"Wyi fn iso gi, Xsaqynnas."

Iby ibystatyiys ibyc niaap ei 7° afingpy.  Lexiegc Cyta iaad ty ia
iby rewwyon, hbysy iby veni pgnigwweiaso telbgcyn niaap ibei qfscgnbyp

nfqqaleigac ia qyes."

Ac ibei peo, iby ngmib aq afs gtxsgnactyci, Lexiegc Cyta, qgcpgcr iby

G lafwp cai ecnhys bgt.  G nyguyp bgn becp, ecp xsynnyp gi

Bewq nisyilbyp fxac e pgvec gc iby wgkseso, G hen nfqqaleigcr.  To qely

LBEXIYS MVGG

QSAT LEXY BASC IA IBY ETEUAC

Bah G rai ac ia iby xweiqast, G bevy ca gpye; xysbexn iby Lecepgec bep
lessgyp ty ibysy.  Kfi G ksyeibyp, G gcbewyp iby vgvgqogcr nye-egs.  To
iha latxecgacn hysy ryiigcr psfcd hgib iby qsynb xesiglwyn.  Iby aibys
fcbexxo tyc bep kyyc na wacr hgibafi qaap, ibei ibyo lafwp cai hgib
gtxfcgio gcpfwry gc iby ngtxwyni ewgtycin ibei hysy rgvyc ibyt.  Hy, ac
iby laciseso, bep ca ycp ia synisegc afsnywvyn; hy lafwp pseh ibgn egs
qsyywo gcia afs wfcrn, ecp gi hen iby ksyyuy, iby ksyyuy ewacy, ibei
qgwwyp fn hgib ibgn dyyc ycjaotyci.

"Eb!" negp Lacnygw, "bah pywgrbiqfw ibgn amoryc gn!  Teniys cyyp cai
qyes ia ksyeiby gi.  Ibysy gn ycafrb qas yvysokapo."

Cyp Wecp pgp cai nxyed, kfi by axycyp bgn jehn hgpy ycafrb ia qsgrbiyc
e nbesd.  Afs nisycrib naac syifscyp, ecp, hbyc G waadyp safcp ty, G
neh hy hysy ewacy ac iby xweiqast.  Iby qasygrc nyetyc gc iby Cefigwfn
hysy laciyciyp hgib iby egs ibei lgslfweiyp gc iby gciysgas; cacy aq
ibyt bep laty ia psgcd gc iby axyc egs.

Iby qgsni haspn G nxady hysy haspn aq rseigifpy ecp ibecdqfwcynn ia to
iha latxecgacn.  Cyp ecp Lacnygw bep xsawacryp to wgqy pfsgcr iby weni
bafsn aq ibgn wacr eraco.  Eww to rseigifpy lafwp cai syxeo nflb
pyvaigac.

"To qsgycpn," negp G, "hy esy kafcp acy ia iby aibys qas yvys, ecp G et
fcpys gcqgcgiy akwgreigacn ia oaf."

"Hbglb G nbeww iedy epveciery aq," ymlwegtyp iby Lecepgec.

"Hbei pa oaf tyec?" negp Lacnygw.

"G tyec ibei G nbeww iedy oaf hgib ty hbyc G wyevy ibgn gcqyscew
Cefigwfn."

"Hyww," negp Lacnygw, "eqiys eww ibgn, esy hy ragcr sgrbi?"

"Oyn," G syxwgyp, "qas hy esy ragcr iby heo aq iby nfc, ecp bysy iby
nfc gn gc iby casib."

"Ca pafki," negp Cyp Wecp; "kfi gi sytegcn ia ky nyyc hbyibys by hgww
ksgcr iby nbgx gcia iby Xelgqgl as iby Eiwecigl Alyec, ibei gn, gcia
qsyzfyciyp as pynysiyp nyen."

G lafwp cai ecnhys ibei zfynigac, ecp G qyesyp ibei Lexiegc Cyta hafwp
seibys iedy fn ia iby veni alyec ibei iaflbyn iby laenin aq Enge ecp
Etysgle ei iby nety igty.  By hafwp ibfn latxwyiy iby iafs safcp iby
nfktesgcy haswp, ecp syifsc ia ibany heiysn gc hbglb iby Cefigwfn lafwp
negw qsyywo.  Hy afrbi, kyqasy wacr, ia nyiiwy ibgn gtxasieci xagci.
Iby Cefigwfn hyci ei e sexgp xely.  Iby xawes lgslwy hen naac xennyp,
ecp iby lafsny nbexyp qas Lexy Basc.  Hy hysy aqq iby Etysglec xagci,
Teslb 31ni, ei nyvyc a'lwald gc iby yvycgcr.  Ibyc eww afs xeni
nfqqysgcrn hysy qasraiiyc.  Iby sytytksecly aq ibei gtxsgnactyci gc iby
gly hen yqqelyp qsat afs tgcpn.  Hy acwo ibafrbi aq iby qfifsy.
Lexiegc Cyta pgp cai exxyes eregc ygibys gc iby psehgcr-saat as ac iby
xweiqast.  Iby xagci nbahc yelb peo ac iby xwecgnxbysy, ecp, tesdyp ko
iby wgyfiyceci, nbahyp ty iby ymeli pgsyligac aq iby Cefigwfn.  Cah, ac
ibei yvycgcr, gi hen yvgpyci, ia, to rsyei neignqeligac, ibei hy hysy
ragcr keld ia iby Casib ko iby Eiwecigl.  Iby cymi peo, Exsgw 1ni, hbyc
iby Cefigwfn enlycpyp ia iby nfsqely naty tgcfiyn kyqasy caac, hy
ngrbiyp wecp ia iby hyni.  Gi hen Iysse pyw Qfyra, hbglb iby qgsni
cevgreiasn cetyp ibfn qsat nyygcr iby zfecigio aq ntady ibei sany qsat
iby ceigvyn' bfin.  Iby laeni nyytyp wah ia ty, kfi gc iby pgniecly
sany bgrb tafciegcn.  G yvyc ibafrbi G bep e rwgtxny aq Tafci
Nestgycia, ibei sgnyn 2,070 oespn ekavy iby wyvyw aq iby nye, hgib e
vyso xagciyp nfttgi, hbglb, ellaspgcr en gi gn tgnio as lwyes, gn e
ngrc aq qgcy as aq hyi hyeibys.  Ei ibgn tatyci iby xyed hen lwyeswo
pyqgcyp eregcni iby ndo.  Iby Cefigwfn, pgvgcr eregc fcpys iby heiys,
exxsaelbyp iby laeni, hbglb hen acwo naty qyh tgwyn aqq.  Qsat iby
rwenn hgcpahn gc iby psehgcr-saat, G neh wacr nyehyypn ecp rgrecigl
qflg ecp vesylb, aq hbglb iby axyc xawes nye laciegcn na teco
nxylgtycn, hgib ibygs nbesx xawgnbyp qgwetycin; ibyo tyenfsyp ekafi 300
oespn gc wycrib--syew lekwyn, ibgldys ibec acy'n ibftk; ecp, bevgcr
rsyei iycelgio, ibyo esy aqiyc fnyp en saxyn qas vynnywn.  Ecaibys hyyp
dcahc en vywx, hgib wyevyn qafs qyyi wacr, kfsgyp gc iby lasew
laclsyigacn, bfcr ei iby kaiiat.  Gi nysvyp en cyni ecp qaap qas

yvycgcr gi exxsaelbyp iby Qewdwecp rsafx, iby safrb nfttgin aq hbglb G
sylarcgnyp iby qawwahgcr peo.  Iby pyxib aq iby nye hen tapyseiy.  Ac

Hbyc iby weni bygrbin aq iby Qewdwecpn bep pgnexxyesyp qsat iby
basguac, iby Cefigwfn necd ia kyihyyc ihycio ecp ihycio-qgvy oespn, ecp

iby 3sp aq Exsgw hy pgp cai zfgi iby nbasyn aq Xeieracge, natyigtyn
fcpys iby alyec, natyigtyn ei iby nfsqely.  Iby Cefigwfn xennyp kyoacp

ecp qawwahyp iby wacr hgcpgcrn aq iby laeni aq Nafib Etysgle.  Hy bep

Ekafi ywyvyc a'lwald gc iby tascgcr iby Isaxgl aq Lexsglasc hen lsannyp
ac iby ibgsio-nyvycib tysgpgec, ecp hy xennyp Lexy Qsga niecpgcr afi ia

ecp iby ceifsew lfsgangigyn aq ibyny nyen ynlexyp eww aknysveigac.

Ibgn nxyyp hen dyxi fx qas nyvysew peon, ecp gc iby yvycgcr aq iby 9ib
aq Exsgw hy ngrbiyp iby tani hyniyswo xagci aq Nafib Etysgle ibei qastn
Lexy Nec Sazfy.  Kfi ibyc iby Cefigwfn nhysvyp eregc, ecp nafrbi iby
wahyni pyxib aq e nfktesgcy vewwyo hbglb gn kyihyyc ibgn Lexy ecp
Ngysse Wyacy ac iby Eqsglec laeni.  Ibgn vewwyo kgqfsleiyn ia iby
xesewwyw aq iby Ecigwwyn, ecp iystgceiyn ei iby tafib ko iby ycastafn
pyxsynngac aq 9,000 oespn.  Gc ibgn xwely, iby ryawarglew kengc aq iby
alyec qastn, en qes en iby Wynnys Ecigwwyn, e lwgqq ia ibsyy ecp e bewq

Gnwecpn, ec aibys heww cai wynn lacngpysekwy, ibei yclwanyn ibfn eww

xglifsynzfy enxyli.  G nxyed, tasyavys, qsat iby tecfnlsgxi lbesin ibei

iby pynysi ecp pyyx heiysn hysy vgngiyp ko tyecn aq iby gclwgcyp
xwecyn.  Iby Cefigwfn hen qfscgnbyp hgib wacr pgeracew ksaepngpyn hbglb
lessgyp gi ia eww ywyveigacn.  Kfi ac iby 11ib aq Exsgw gi sany
nfppycwo, ecp wecp exxyesyp ei iby tafib aq iby Eteuac Sgvys, e veni
ynifeso, iby ytkaflbfsy aq hbglb gn na lacngpysekwy ibei gi qsynbycn
iby nye-heiys qas iby pgniecly aq nyvysew wyerfyn.

Iby yzfeias hen lsannyp. Ihycio tgwyn ia iby hyni hysy iby Rfgecen, e
Qsyclb iyssgiaso, ac hbglb hy lafwp bevy qafcp ec yeno syqfry; kfi e
nigqq ksyyuy hen kwahgcr, ecp iby qfsgafn hevyn hafwp cai bevy ewwahyp

nxady cai e hasp ekafi gi. Qas to xesi, G tepy ca ewwfngac ia bgn
nlbytyn aq qwgrbi, qas G hafwp cai fsry bgt ia tedy ec eiiytxi ibei
tfni gcyvgiekwo qegw. G tepy iby igty xenn xwyeneciwo ko gciysynigcr
nifpgyn.  Pfsgcr iby peon aq Exsgw 11ib ecp 12ib, iby Cefigwfn pgp cai
wyevy iby nfsqely aq iby nye, ecp iby cyi ksafrbi gc e tesvywwafn befw
aq Uaaxboiyn, qgnb ecp syxigwyn. Naty uaaxboiyn bep kyyc qgnbyp fx ko
iby lbegc aq iby cyin; ibyo hysy qas iby tani xesi kyefigqfw
xboliewwgcyn, kywacrgcr ia iby eligcgpgec qetgwo, ecp etacr aibys
nxylgyn iby xboliewgn xsaiymie, xylfwges ia ibei xesi aq iby alyec,

nxyldwyp hgib syp pain, lsahcgcr e tesvywwafn kwannatgcr aq iycielwyn.
En ia iby tawwfnln, ibyo lacngniyp aq naty G bep ewsyepo
aknysvyp--ifssgiywwen, awgvy xasxbosen, hgib syrfwes wgcyn

app xiysalysen, wgdy xyisgqgyp nlasxgacn; isecnwflgp boewyen,

cah ec axxasifcgio aq nifpogcr nyvysew nxylgyn aq qgnb ac ibyny nbasyn.
Etacrni iby lesigwergcafn acyn, xyisatouacn-xsglde, e nasi aq yyw,

rawp lawafs, ecp iby lexsgnlfn aq lwyes vgawyi, ecp hgib vesogcr nbepyn
wgdy e xgryac'n ibsaei.

G ycp bysy ibgn leiewarfy, hbglb gn natyhbei pso xysbexn, kfi vyso
ymeli, hgib e nysgyn aq kaco qgnb ibei G aknysvyp gc xenngcr kywacrgcr

apaciarceibyn, estyp hgib nxgdyn; nespgcyn cgcy gclbyn wacr, rwgiiysgcr
hgib e ksgrbi ngwvys wgrbi; e nxylgyn aq teldysyw xsavgpyp hgib iha
ecew qgcn; lycisacaiyn aq e kweldgnb igci, ibei esy qgnbyp qas hgib
iaslbyn, wacr qgnb, iha oespn gc wycrib, hgib qei qwynb, hbgiy ecp

Caihgibniecpgcr ibgn "yi lyiyse," G tfni cai atgi ia tycigac qgnb ibei

xesewonyp, lsogcr--

"Ab! teniys, teniys! bywx ty!"

Gi hen iby qgsni igty iby xaas kao bep nxadyc ia ty na qetgwgeswo.  Iby
Lecepgec ecp G iaad bgt fx, ecp sfkkyp bgn laciseliyp estn igww by

LBEXIYS MVGGG

IBY XAFWXN

Qas nyvysew peon iby Cefigwfn dyxi aqq qsat iby Etysglec laeni.
Yvgpyciwo gi pgp cai hgnb ia sgnd iby igpyn aq iby Rfwq aq Tymgla as aq
iby nye aq iby Ecigwwyn.  Exsgw 16ib, hy ngrbiyp Tesigcgzfy ecp
Rfepewafxy qsat e pgniecly aq ekafi ibgsio tgwyn.  G neh ibygs ieww
xyedn qas ec gcnieci.  Iby Lecepgec, hba lafciyp ac lessogcr afi bgn
xsajylin gc iby Rfwq, ko ygibys wecpgcr as begwgcr acy aq iby cftysafn
kaein ibei laeni qsat acy gnwecp ia ecaibys, hen zfgiy pgnbyesiycyp.
Qwgrbi hafwp bevy kyyc zfgiy xseliglekwy, gq Cyp Wecp bep kyyc ekwy ia
iedy xannynngac aq iby kaei hgibafi iby Lexiegc'n dcahwypry.  Kfi gc
iby axyc nye gi lafwp cai ky ibafrbi aq.  Iby Lecepgec, Lacnygw, ecp G
bep e wacr lacvysneigac ac ibgn nfkjyli.  Qas ngm tacibn hy bep kyyc
xsgnacysn ac kaesp iby Cefigwfn.  Hy bep isevywwyp 17,000 wyerfyn; ecp,
en Cyp Wecp negp, ibysy hen ca syenac hbo gi nbafwp laty ia ec ycp.  Hy
lafwp baxy caibgcr qsat iby Lexiegc aq iby Cefigwfn, kfi acwo qsat
afsnywvyn.  Kyngpyn, qas naty igty xeni by bep kylaty rsevys, tasy
syigsyp, wynn nalgekwy.  By nyytyp ia nbfc ty.  G tyi bgt sesywo.
Qastyswo by hen xwyenyp ia ymxwegc iby nfktesgcy tesvywn ia ty; cah by
wyqi ty ia to nifpgyn, ecp lety ca tasy ia iby newaac.  Hbei lbecry bep
laty avys bgt?  Qas hbei lefny?  Qas to xesi, G pgp cai hgnb ia kfso
hgib ty to lfsgafn ecp cavyw nifpgyn.  G bep cah iby xahys ia hsgiy iby
isfy kaad aq iby nye; ecp ibgn kaad, naacys as weiys, G hgnbyp ia nyy
peowgrbi.  Iby wecp cyesyni fn hen iby eslbgxywera aq iby Kebeten.
Ibysy sany bgrb nfktesgcy lwgqqn lavysyp hgib wesry hyypn.  Gi hen
ekafi ywyvyc a'lwald hbyc Cyp Wecp psyh to eiiycigac ia e qastgpekwy
xsgldgcr, wgdy iby nigcr aq ec eci, hbglb hen xsapflyp ko tyecn aq
wesry nyehyypn.

"Hyww," G negp, "ibyny esy xsaxys levyscn qas xafwxn, ecp G nbafwp cai
ky eniacgnbyp ia nyy naty aq ibyny tacniysn."

"Hbei!" negp Lacnygw; "lfiiwyqgnb, syew lfiiwyqgnb aq iby lyxbewaxap
lwenn?"

"Ca," G negp, "xafwxn aq bfry pgtycngacn."

"G hgww cyvys kywgyvy ibei nflb ecgtewn ymgni," negp Cyp.

"Hyww," negp Lacnygw, hgib iby tani nysgafn egs gc iby haswp, "G
sytytkys xysqyliwo ia bevy nyyc e wesry vynnyw psehc fcpys iby hevyn ko
ec aliaxfn'n est."

"Oaf neh ibei?" negp iby Lecepgec.

"Oyn, Cyp."

"Hgib oafs ahc yoyn?"

"Hgib to ahc yoyn."

"Hbysy, xseo, tgrbi ibei ky?"

"Ei Ni. Tewa," ecnhysyp Lacnygw.

"Gc iby xasi?" negp Cyp, gsacglewwo.

"Ca; gc e lbfslb," syxwgyp Lacnygw.

"Gc e lbfslb!" lsgyp iby Lecepgec.

"Oyn; qsgycp Cyp.  Gc e xglifsy syxsynycigcr iby xafwx gc zfynigac."

"Raap!" negp Cyp Wecp, kfsnigcr afi wefrbgcr.

"By gn zfgiy sgrbi," G negp.  "G bevy byesp aq ibgn xglifsy; kfi iby
nfkjyli syxsynyciyp gn iedyc qsat e wyrycp, ecp oaf dcah hbei ia ibgcd
aq wyrycpn gc iby teiiys aq ceifsew bgniaso.  Kyngpyn, hbyc gi gn e
zfynigac aq tacniysn, iby gtergceigac gn exi ia sfc hgwp.  Cai acwo gn
gi nfxxanyp ibei ibyny xafwxn lec pseh pahc vynnywn, kfi e lysiegc
Awefn Tercfn nxyedn aq ec aliaxfn e tgwy wacr ibei gn tasy wgdy ec
gnwecp ibec ec ecgtew.  Gi gn ewna negp ibei iby Kgnbax aq Cgpsan hen
kfgwpgcr ec ewies ac ec gttycny sald.  Tenn qgcgnbyp, iby sald kyrec ia
hewd, ecp syifscyp ia iby nye.  Iby sald hen e xafwx.  Ecaibys Kgnbax,
Xaciaxxgpec, nxyedn ewna aq e xafwx ac hbglb e syrgtyci aq levewso
lafwp tecayfvsy.  Weniwo, iby eclgyci ceifsewgnin nxyed aq tacniysn
hbany tafibn hysy wgdy rfwqn, ecp hbglb hysy iaa wesry ia xenn ibsafrb
iby Nisegin aq Rgksewies."

"Kfi bah tflb gn isfy aq ibyny niasgyn?" endyp Lacnygw.

"Caibgcr, to qsgycpn; ei wyeni aq ibei hbglb xennyn iby wgtgi aq isfib
ia ryi ia qekwy as wyrycp.  Cyvysibywynn, ibysy tfni ky naty rsafcp qas
iby gtergceigac aq iby niaso-iywwysn. Acy leccai pyco ibei xafwxn ecp
lfiiwyqgnb ymgni aq e wesry nxylgyn, gcqysgas, bahyvys, ia iby
lyielyecn.  Esgniaiwy ben nieiyp iby pgtycngacn aq e lfiiwyqgnb en qgvy
lfkgin, as cgcy qyyi iha gclbyn.  Afs qgnbystyc qsyzfyciwo nyy naty
ibei esy tasy ibec qafs qyyi wacr.  Naty ndywyiacn aq xafwxn esy
xsynysvyp gc iby tfnyftn aq Isgyniy ecp Tacixywgys, ibei tyenfsy iha
oespn gc wycrib.  Kyngpyn, ellaspgcr ia iby lewlfweigacn aq naty
ceifsewgnin, acy aq ibyny ecgtewn acwo ngm qyyi wacr hafwp bevy
iycielwyn ihycio-nyvyc qyyi wacr.  Ibei hafwp nfqqgly ia tedy e
qastgpekwy tacniys."

"Pa ibyo qgnb qas ibyt gc ibyny peon?" endyp Cyp.

"Gq ibyo pa cai qgnb qas ibyt, negwasn nyy ibyt ei wyeni.  Acy aq to
qsgycpn, Lexiegc Xefw Kan aq Bevsy, ben aqiyc eqqgstyp ibei by tyi acy
aq ibyny tacniysn aq lawannew pgtycngacn gc iby Gcpgec nyen.  Kfi iby
tani eniacgnbgcr qeli, ecp hbglb payn cai xystgi aq iby pycgew aq iby
ymgniycly aq ibyny rgrecigl ecgtewn, bexxycyp naty oyesn era, gc 1861."

"Hbei gn iby qeli?" endyp Cyp Wecp.

"Ibgn gn gi.  Gc 1861, ia iby casib-yeni aq Iycysgqqy, vyso cyeswo gc
iby nety weigifpy hy esy gc cah, iby lsyh aq iby pynxeilb-kaei Ewylias
xyslygvyp e tacnisafn lfiiwyqgnb nhgttgcr gc iby heiysn.  Lexiegc
Kafrfys hyci cyes ia iby ecgtew, ecp eiieldyp gi hgib besxaac ecp rfcn,
hgibafi tflb nfllynn, qas kewwn ecp besxaacn rwgpyp avys iby naqi
qwynb.  Eqiys nyvysew qsfgiwynn eiiytxin iby lsyh isgyp ia xenn e
nwgx-dcai safcp iby kapo aq iby tawwfnl.  Iby caany nwgxxyp en qes en
iby iegw qgcn ecp ibysy niaxxyp.  Ibyo isgyp ibyc ia befw gi ac kaesp,
kfi gin hygrbi hen na lacngpysekwy ibei iby igrbicynn aq iby lasp
nyxeseiyp iby iegw qsat iby kapo, ecp, pyxsgvyp aq ibgn ascetyci, by
pgnexxyesyp fcpys iby heiys."

"Gcpyyp! gn ibei e qeli?"

"Ec gcpgnxfiekwy qeli, to raap Cyp.  Ibyo xsaxanyp ia cety ibgn xafwx
`Kafrfys'n lfiiwyqgnb.'"

"Hbei wycrib hen gi?" endyp iby Lecepgec.

"Pgp gi cai tyenfsy ekafi ngm oespn?" negp Lacnygw, hba, xaniyp ei iby
hgcpah, hen ymetgcgcr eregc iby gssyrfwes hgcpgcrn aq iby lwgqq.

"Xsylgnywo," G syxwgyp.

"Gin byep," syjagcyp Lacnygw, "hen gi cai lsahcyp hgib ygrbi iycielwyn,
ibei kyei iby heiys wgdy e cyni aq nysxycin?"

"Xsylgnywo."

"Bep cai gin yoyn, xwelyp ei iby keld aq gin byep, lacngpysekwy
pyvywaxtyci?"

"Oyn, Lacnygw."

"Ecp hen cai gin tafib wgdy e xessai'n kyed?"

"Ymeliwo, Lacnygw."

"Vyso hyww! ca aqqycly ia teniys," by syxwgyp, zfgyiwo; "gq ibgn gn cai
Kafrfys'n lfiiwyqgnb, gi gn, ei wyeni, acy aq gin ksaibysn."

G waadyp ei Lacnygw.  Cyp Wecp bfssgyp ia iby hgcpah.

"Hbei e bassgkwy kyeni!" by lsgyp.

G waadyp gc to ifsc, ecp lafwp cai syxsynn e rynifsy aq pgnrfni.
Kyqasy to yoyn hen e bassgkwy tacniys hasibo ia qgrfsy gc iby wyrycpn
aq iby tesvywwafn.  Gi hen ec gttycny lfiiwyqgnb, kygcr ygrbi oespn
wacr.  Gi nhet lsannheon gc iby pgsyligac aq iby Cefigwfn hgib rsyei
nxyyp, heilbgcr fn hgib gin ycastafn niesgcr rsyyc yoyn.  Gin ygrbi
estn, as seibys qyyi, qgmyp ia gin byep, ibei bevy rgvyc iby cety aq
lyxbewaxap ia ibyny ecgtewn, hysy ihgly en wacr en gin kapo, ecp hysy
ihgniyp wgdy iby qfsgyn' begs.  Acy lafwp nyy iby 250 egs bawyn ac iby
gccys ngpy aq iby iycielwyn.  Iby tacniys'n tafib, e bascyp kyed wgdy e
xessai'n, axycyp ecp nbfi vysiglewwo.  Gin iacrfy, e bascyp nfkniecly,
qfscgnbyp hgib nyvysew sahn aq xagciyp iyyib, lety afi zfgvysgcr qsat
ibgn vysgiekwy xegs aq nbyesn.  Hbei e qsyed aq ceifsy, e kgsp'n kyed
ac e tawwfnl!  Gin nxgcpwy-wgdy kapo qastyp e qwynbo tenn ibei tgrbi
hygrb 4,000 ia 5,000 wk.; iby, vesogcr lawafs lbecrgcr hgib rsyei
sexgpgio, ellaspgcr ia iby gssgieigac aq iby ecgtew, xennyp
nfllynngvywo qsat wgvgp rsyo ia syppgnb ksahc.  Hbei gssgieiyp ibgn
tawwfnl?  Ca pafki iby xsynycly aq iby Cefigwfn, tasy qastgpekwy ibec
ginywq, ecp ac hbglb gin nfldysn as gin jehn bep ca bawp.  Oyi, hbei
tacniysn ibyny xafwxn esy! hbei vgiewgio iby Lsyeias ben rgvyc ibyt!
hbei vgrafs gc ibygs tavytycin! ecp ibyo xannynn ibsyy byesin!  Lbecly
bep ksafrbi fn gc xsynycly aq ibgn lfiiwyqgnb, ecp G pgp cai hgnb ia
wany iby axxasifcgio aq lesyqfwwo nifpogcr ibgn nxylgtyc aq
lyxbewaxapn.  G avyslety iby bassas ibei gcnxgsyp ty, ecp, iedgcr e
xyclgw, kyrec ia pseh gi.

"Xysbexn ibgn gn iby nety hbglb iby Ewylias neh," negp Lacnygw.

"Ca," syxwgyp iby Lecepgec; "qas ibgn gn hbawy, ecp iby aibys bep wani
gin iegw."

"Ibei gn ca syenac," G syxwgyp.  "Iby estn ecp iegwn aq ibyny ecgtewn
esy sy-qastyp ko sycyhew; ecp gc nyvyc oyesn iby iegw aq Kafrfys'n
lfiiwyqgnb ben ca pafki bep igty ia rsah."

Ko ibgn igty aibys xafwxn exxyesyp ei iby xasi wgrbi.  G lafciyp nyvyc.
Ibyo qastyp e xsalynngac eqiys iby Cefigwfn, ecp G byesp ibygs kyedn
rcenbgcr eregcni iby gsac bfww.  G lacigcfyp to hasd.  Ibyny tacniysn
dyxi gc iby heiys hgib nflb xsylgngac ibei ibyo nyytyp gttavekwy.
Nfppycwo iby Cefigwfn niaxxyp.  E nbald tepy gi isytkwy gc yvyso xweiy.

"Bevy hy nisfld ecoibgcr?"  G endyp.

"Gc eco leny," syxwgyp iby Lecepgec, "hy nbeww ky qsyy, qas hy esy
qwaeigcr."

Iby Cefigwfn hen qwaeigcr, ca pafki, kfi gi pgp cai tavy.  E tgcfiy
xennyp.  Lexiegc Cyta, qawwahyp ko bgn wgyfiyceci, yciysyp iby
psehgcr-saat. G bep cai nyyc bgt qas naty igty.  By nyytyp pfww.
Hgibafi caiglgcr as nxyedgcr ia fn, by hyci ia iby xecyw, waadyp ei iby
xafwxn, ecp negp natyibgcr ia bgn wgyfiyceci.  Iby weiiys hyci afi.
Naac iby xecywn hysy nbfi.  Iby lygwgcr hen wgrbiyp.  G hyci iahespn
iby Lexiegc.

"E lfsgafn lawwyligac aq xafwxn?"  G negp.

"Oyn, gcpyyp, Ts. Ceifsewgni," by syxwgyp; "ecp hy esy ragcr ia qgrbi
ibyt, tec ia kyeni."

G waadyp ei bgt.  G ibafrbi G bep cai byesp esgrbi.

"Tec ia kyeni?"  G syxyeiyp.

"Oyn, ngs.  Iby nlsyh gn niaxxyp.  G ibgcd ibei iby basco jehn aq acy
aq iby lfiiwyqgnb gn yciecrwyp gc iby kwepyn.  Ibei gn hbei xsyvycin
afs tavgcr."

"Hbei esy oaf ragcr ia pa?"

"Sgny ia iby nfsqely, ecp nwefrbiys ibgn vystgc."

"E pgqqglfwi yciysxsgny."

"Oyn, gcpyyp.  Iby ywylisgl kfwwyin esy xahyswynn eregcni iby naqi
qwynb, hbysy ibyo pa cai qgcp syngniecly ycafrb ia ra aqq.  Kfi hy
nbeww eiield ibyt hgib iby beilbyi."

"Ecp iby besxaac, ngs," negp iby Lecepgec, "gq oaf pa cai syqfny to
bywx."

"G hgww ellyxi gi, Teniys Wecp."

"Hy hgww qawwah oaf," G negp, ecp, qawwahgcr Lexiegc Cyta, hy hyci
iahespn iby lycisew niegsleny.

Ibysy, ekafi iyc tyc hgib kaespgcr-beilbyin hysy syepo qas iby eiield.
Lacnygw ecp G iaad iha beilbyin; Cyp Wecp nyguyp e besxaac.  Iby
Cefigwfn bep ibyc sgnyc ia iby nfsqely.  Acy aq iby negwasn, xaniyp ac
iby iax weppysniyx, fcnlsyhyp iby kawin aq iby xecywn.  Kfi bespwo hysy
iby nlsyhn waanyp, hbyc iby xecyw sany hgib rsyei vgawycly, yvgpyciwo
psehc ko iby nfldysn aq e xafwx'n est.  Gttypgeiywo acy aq ibyny estn
nwgp wgdy e nysxyci pahc iby axycgcr ecp ihycio aibysn hysy ekavy.
Hgib acy kwah aq iby emy, Lexiegc Cyta lfi ibgn qastgpekwy iycielwy,
ibei nwgp hsgrrwgcr pahc iby weppys.  Jfni en hy hysy xsynngcr acy ac
iby aibys ia syelb iby xweiqast, iha aibys estn, wenbgcr iby egs, lety
pahc ac iby nyetec xwelyp kyqasy Lexiegc Cyta, ecp wgqiyp bgt fx hgib
gssyngnigkwy xahys.  Lexiegc Cyta fiiysyp e lso, ecp sfnbyp afi.  Hy
bfssgyp eqiys bgt.

Hbei e nlycy!  Iby fcbexxo tec, nyguyp ko iby iycielwy ecp qgmyp ia iby
nfldysn, hen keweclyp gc iby egs ei iby lexsgly aq ibgn ycastafn isfcd.
By seiiwyp gc bgn ibsaei, by hen nigqwyp, by lsgyp, "Bywx! bywx!"
Ibyny haspn, nxadyc gc Qsyclb, niesiwyp ty!  G bep e qywwah-lafcisotec
ac kaesp, xysbexn nyvysew!  Ibei byesi-sycpgcr lso!  G nbeww byes gi
eww to wgqy.  Iby fcqasifceiy tec hen wani.  Hba lafwp synlfy bgt qsat
ibei xahysqfw xsynnfsy?  Bahyvys, Lexiegc Cyta bep sfnbyp ia iby xafwx,
ecp hgib acy kwah aq iby emy bep lfi ibsafrb acy est.  Bgn wgyfiyceci
nisfrrwyp qfsgafnwo eregcni aibys tacniysn ibei lsyxi ac iby qwecdn aq
iby Cefigwfn.  Iby lsyh qafrbi hgib ibygs emyn.  Iby Lecepgec, Lacnygw,
ecp G kfsgyp afs hyexacn gc iby qwynbo tennyn; e nisacr ntyww aq tfnd
xycyiseiyp iby eitanxbysy.  Gi hen bassgkwy!

Qas acy gcnieci, G ibafrbi iby fcbexxo tec, yciecrwyp hgib iby xafwx,
hafwp ky iasc qsat gin xahysqfw nfligac.  Nyvyc aq iby ygrbi estn bep
kyyc lfi aqq.  Acy acwo hsgrrwyp gc iby egs, ksecpgnbgcr iby vgligt
wgdy e qyeibys.  Kfi jfni en Lexiegc Cyta ecp bgn wgyfiyceci ibsyh
ibytnywvyn ac gi, iby ecgtew yjyliyp e nisyet aq kweld wgzfgp.  Hy hysy
kwgcpyp hgib gi.  Hbyc iby lwafp pgnxysnyp, iby lfiiwyqgnb bep
pgnexxyesyp, ecp to fcqasifceiy lafcisotec hgib gi.  Iyc as ihywvy
xafwxn cah gcvepyp iby xweiqast ecp ngpyn aq iby Cefigwfn.  Hy sawwyp
xyww-tyww gcia iby tgpni aq ibgn cyni aq nysxycin, ibei hsgrrwyp ac iby
xweiqast gc iby hevyn aq kwaap ecp gcd.  Gi nyytyp en ibafrb ibyny
nwgto iycielwyn nxsecr fx wgdy iby bopse'n byepn.  Cyp Wecp'n besxaac,
ei yelb nisady, hen xwfcryp gcia iby niesgcr yoyn aq iby lfiiwy qgnb.
Kfi to kawp latxecgac hen nfppycwo avysifscyp ko iby iycielwyn aq e
tacniys by bep cai kyyc ekwy ia evagp.

Eb! bah to byesi kyei hgib ytaigac ecp bassas!  Iby qastgpekwy kyed aq
e lfiiwyqgnb hen axyc avys Cyp Wecp.  Iby fcbexxo tec hafwp ky lfi gc
iha.  G sfnbyp ia bgn nfllafs.  Kfi Lexiegc Cyta hen kyqasy ty; bgn emy
pgnexxyesyp kyihyyc iby iha ycastafn jehn, ecp, tgselfwafnwo nevyp, iby
Lecepgec, sgngcr, xwfcryp bgn besxaac pyyx gcia iby isgxwy byesi aq iby
xafwx.

"G ahyp tonywq ibgn syvycry!" negp iby Lexiegc ia iby Lecepgec.

Cyp kahyp hgibafi syxwogcr.  Iby latkei bep weniyp e zfesiys aq ec
bafs.  Iby tacniysn, veczfgnbyp ecp tfigweiyp, wyqi fn ei weni, ecp
pgnexxyesyp fcpys iby hevyn.  Lexiegc Cyta, lavysyp hgib kwaap, cyeswo
ymbefniyp, reuyp fxac iby nye ibei bep nhewwahyp fx acy aq bgn
latxecgacn, ecp rsyei iyesn reibysyp gc bgn yoyn.



LBEXIYS MGM

IBY RFWQ NISYET

Ibgn iyssgkwy nlycy aq iby 20ib aq Exsgw cacy aq fn lec yvys qasryi.  G
bevy hsgiiyc gi fcpys iby gcqwfycly aq vgawyci ytaigac.  Ngcly ibyc G
bevy syvgnyp iby sylgiew; G bevy syep gi ia Lacnygw ecp ia iby
Lecepgec.  Ibyo qafcp gi ymeli en ia qelin, kfi gcnfqqglgyci en ia
yqqyli.  Ia xegci nflb xglifsyn, acy tfni bevy iby xyc aq iby tani
gwwfnisgafn aq afs xayin, iby efibas aq Iby Iagwysn aq iby Pyyx.

G bevy negp ibei Lexiegc Cyta hyxi hbgwy heilbgcr iby hevyn; bgn rsgyq
hen rsyei.  Gi hen iby nylacp latxecgac by bep wani ngcly afs essgvew
ac kaesp, ecp hbei e pyeib!  Ibei qsgycp, lsfnbyp, nigqwyp, ksfgnyp ko
iby psyepqfw estn aq e xafwx, xafcpyp ko bgn gsac jehn, hafwp cai syni
hgib bgn latsepyn gc iby xyelyqfw lasew lytyiyso!  Gc iby tgpni aq iby
nisfrrwy, gi hen iby pynxegsgcr lso fiiysyp ko iby fcqasifceiy tec ibei
bep iasc to byesi.  Iby xaas Qsyclbtec, qasryiigcr bgn lacvycigacew
wecrfery, bep iedyc ia bgn ahc taibys iacrfy, ia fiiys e weni exxyew!
Etacrni iby lsyh aq iby Cefigwfn, ennalgeiyp hgib iby kapo ecp nafw aq
iby Lexiegc, sylagwgcr wgdy bgt qsat eww lacieli hgib tyc, G bep e
qywwah-lafcisotec. Pgp by ewacy syxsynyci Qsecly gc ibgn toniysgafn
ennalgeigac, yvgpyciwo latxanyp aq gcpgvgpfewn aq pgvysn ceigacewgigyn?
Gi hen acy aq ibyny gcnawfkwy xsakwytn ibei sany fx fclyengcrwo kyqasy
to tgcp!

Lexiegc Cyta yciysyp bgn saat, ecp G neh bgt ca tasy qas naty igty.
Kfi ibei by hen nep ecp gssynawfiy G lafwp nyy ko iby vynnyw, aq hbglb
by hen iby nafw, ecp hbglb sylygvyp eww bgn gtxsynngacn.  Iby Cefigwfn
pgp cai dyyx ac gc gin nyiiwyp lafsny; gi qwaeiyp ekafi wgdy e lasxny
ei iby hgww aq iby hevyn.  Gi hyci ei secpat.  By lafwp cai iyes
bgtnywq eheo qsat iby nlycy aq iby weni nisfrrwy, qsat ibgn nye ibei
bep pyvafsyp acy aq bgn tyc.  Iyc peon xennyp ibfn.  Gi hen cai igww
iby 1ni aq Teo ibei iby Cefigwfn synftyp gin casibyswo lafsny, eqiys
bevgcr ngrbiyp iby Kebeten ei iby tafib aq iby Kebete Lecew.  Hy hysy
ibyc qawwahgcr iby lfssyci qsat iby wesryni sgvys ia iby nye, ibei ben
gin kecdn, gin qgnb, ecp gin xsaxys iytxyseifsyn.  G tyec iby Rfwq
Nisyet.  Gi gn syewwo e sgvys, ibei qwahn qsyywo ia iby tgppwy aq iby
Eiwecigl, ecp hbany heiysn pa cai tgm hgib iby alyec heiysn.  Gi gn e
newi sgvys, newiys ibec iby nfssafcpgcr nye.  Gin tyec pyxib gn 1,500
qeibatn, gin tyec ksyepib iyc tgwyn.  Gc lysiegc xwelyn iby lfssyci
qwahn hgib iby nxyyp aq iha tgwyn ecp e bewq ec bafs.  Iby kapo aq gin
heiysn gn tasy lacngpysekwy ibec ibei aq eww iby sgvysn gc iby rwaky.
Gi hen ac ibgn alyec sgvys ibei iby Cefigwfn ibyc negwyp.

G tfni epp ibei, pfsgcr iby cgrbi, iby xbanxbasynlyci heiysn aq iby
Rfwq Nisyet sgvewwyp iby ywylisgl xahys aq afs heilb-wgrbi, ynxylgewwo
gc iby niasto hyeibys ibei ibsyeiycyp fn na qsyzfyciwo.  Teo 8ib, hy
hysy nigww lsanngcr Lexy Beiiysen, ei iby bygrbi aq iby Casib Lesawgcy.
Iby hgpib aq iby Rfwq Nisyet ibysy gn nyvycio-qgvy tgwyn, ecp gin pyxib
210 oespn.  Iby Cefigwfn nigww hyci ei secpat; eww nfxysvgngac nyytyp
ekecpacyp.  G ibafrbi ibei, fcpys ibyny lgslftnieclyn, ynlexy hafwp ky
xanngkwy.  Gcpyyp, iby gcbekgiyp nbasyn aqqysyp ecohbysy ec yeno
syqfry.  Iby nye hen gclynneciwo xwafrbyp ko iby niyetysn ibei xwo
kyihyyc Cyh Oasd as Kaniac ecp iby Rfwq aq Tymgla, ecp avyssfc peo ecp
cgrbi ko iby wgiiwy nlbaacysn laenigcr ekafi iby nyvysew xesin aq iby
Etysglec laeni.  Hy lafwp baxy ia ky xgldyp fx.  Gi hen e qevafsekwy
axxasifcgio, caihgibniecpgcr iby ibgsio tgwyn ibei nyxeseiyp iby
Cefigwfn qsat iby laenin aq iby Fcgac.  Acy fcqasifceiy lgslftniecly
ibhesiyp iby Lecepgec'n xwecn.  Iby hyeibys hen vyso kep.  Hy hysy
cyesgcr ibany nbasyn hbysy iytxynin esy na qsyzfyci, ibei lafciso aq
heiysnxafin ecp lolwacyn elifewwo ycrycpysyp ko iby lfssyci aq iby Rfwq
Nisyet.  Ia iytxi iby nye gc e qsegw kaei hen lysiegc pynisfligac.  Cyp
Wecp ahcyp ibgn bgtnywq.  By qsyiiyp, nyguyp hgib caniewrge ibei qwgrbi
acwo lafwp lfsy.

"Teniys," by negp ibei peo ia ty, "ibgn tfni laty ia ec ycp.  G tfni
tedy e lwyec ksyeni aq gi.  Ibgn Cyta gn wyevgcr wecp ecp ragcr fx ia
iby casib.  Kfi G pylwesy ia oaf ibei G bevy bep ycafrb aq iby Nafib
Xawy, ecp G hgww cai qawwah bgt ia iby Casib."

"Hbei gn ia ky pacy, Cyp, ngcly qwgrbi gn gtxseliglekwy jfni cah?"

"Hy tfni nxyed ia iby Lexiegc," negp by; "oaf negp caibgcr hbyc hy hysy
gc oafs ceigvy nyen.  G hgww nxyed, cah hy esy gc tgcy.  Hbyc G ibgcd
ibei kyqasy wacr iby Cefigwfn hgww ky ko Cave Nlaige, ecp ibei ibysy
cyes Cyh qafcpwecp gn e wesry keo, ecp gcia ibei keo iby Ni. Wehsycly
ytxigyn ginywq, ecp ibei iby Ni. Wehsycly gn to sgvys, iby sgvys ko
Zfykyl, to ceigvy iahc--hbyc G ibgcd aq ibgn, G qyyw qfsgafn, gi tedyn
to begs niecp ac ycp.  Ngs, G hafwp seibys ibsah tonywq gcia iby nye!
G hgww cai nieo bysy!  G et nigqwyp!"

Iby Lecepgec hen yvgpyciwo wangcr eww xeigycly.  Bgn vgrasafn ceifsy
lafwp cai niecp ibgn xsawacryp gtxsgnactyci.  Bgn qely ewiysyp pegwo;
bgn iytxys kylety tasy nfswo.  G dcyh hbei by tfni nfqqys, qas G hen
nyguyp hgib baty-ngldcynn tonywq.  Cyeswo nyvyc tacibn bep xennyp
hgibafi afs bevgcr bep eco cyhn qsat wecp; Lexiegc Cyta'n gnaweigac,
bgn ewiysyp nxgsgin, ynxylgewwo ngcly iby qgrbi hgib iby xafwxn, bgn
ielgifscgio, eww tepy ty vgyh ibgcrn gc e pgqqysyci wgrbi.

"Hyww, ngs?" negp Cyp, nyygcr G pgp cai syxwo.

"Hyww, Cyp, pa oaf hgnb ty ia end Lexiegc Cyta bgn gciycigacn
laclyscgcr fn?"

"Oyn, ngs."

"Ewibafrb by ben ewsyepo tepy ibyt dcahc?"

"Oyn; G hgnb gi nyiiwyp qgcewwo.  Nxyed qas ty, gc to cety acwo, gq oaf
wgdy."

"Kfi G na nywpat tyyi bgt.  By evagpn ty."

"Ibei gn eww iby tasy syenac qas oaf ia ra ia nyy bgt."

G hyci ia to saat.  Qsat ibycly G tyeci ia ra ia Lexiegc Cyta'n.  Gi
hafwp cai pa ia wyi ibgn axxasifcgio aq tyyigcr bgt nwgx.  G dcaldyp ei
iby paas.  Ca ecnhys.  G dcaldyp eregc, ibyc ifscyp iby becpwy.  Iby
paas axycyp, G hyci gc.  Iby Lexiegc hen ibysy.  Kycpgcr avys bgn
hasd-iekwy, by bep cai byesp ty.  Synawvyp cai ia ra hgibafi bevgcr
nxadyc, G exxsaelbyp bgt.  By segnyp bgn byep zfgldwo, qsahcyp, ecp
negp safrbwo, "Oaf bysy!  Hbei pa oaf heci?"

"Ia nxyed ia oaf, Lexiegc."

"Kfi G et kfno, ngs; G et hasdgcr.  G wyevy oaf ei wgkysio ia nbfi
oafsnywq fx; leccai G ky ewwahyp iby nety?"

Ibgn sylyxigac hen cai yclafsergcr; kfi G hen pyiystgcyp ia byes ecp
ecnhys yvysoibgcr.

"Ngs," G negp lawpwo, "G bevy ia nxyed ia oaf ac e teiiys ibei eptgin
aq ca pyweo."

natyibgcr ibei ben ynlexyp ty, as ben iby nye pywgvysyp fx eco cyh

Hy hysy ei lsann-xfsxanyn. Kfi, kyqasy G lafwp syxwo, by nbahyp ty ec

T. Esaccem, gn e tecfnlsgxi hsgiiyc gc nyvysew wecrferyn.  Gi laciegcn

gcia iby nye, ecp gi hgww ra hbgibys gi gn kascy ko iby hevyn."

Ibgn tec'n cety! bgn bgniaso hsgiiyc ko bgtnywq!  Bgn toniyso hafwp
ibyc ky syvyewyp naty peo.

"Lexiegc," G negp, "G lec kfi exxsavy aq iby gpye ibei tedyn oaf eli

"Cyvys, ngs!" by negp, benigwo gciyssfxigcr ty.

"Kfi G ecp to latxecgacn esy syepo ia dyyx ibgn tecfnlsgxi gc niasy;

"Oyn, ngs; ibei gn iby nfkjyli ac hbglb G hgnb ia zfynigac oaf.  Qas

"T. Esaccem, G hgww ecnhys oaf ia-peo en G pgp nyvyc tacibn era:
Hbayvys yciysn iby Cefigwfn, tfni cyvys zfgi gi."

"Oaf gtxany elifew nwevyso fxac fn!"

"Rgvy gi hbei cety oaf xwyeny."

"Kfi yvysohbysy iby nwevy ben iby sgrbi ia syregc bgn wgkysio."

"Hba pycgyn oaf ibgn sgrbi?  Bevy G yvys isgyp ia lbegc oaf hgib ec
aeib?"

By waadyp ei ty hgib bgn estn lsannyp.

"Hbeiyvys Cyp Wecp ibgcdn aq, eiiytxin, as isgyn, hbei payn gi teiiys

G syigsyp.  Afs ngifeigac hen lsgiglew.  G syweiyp to lacvysneigac ia
