"Hy dcah cah," negp Cyp, "ibei hy lec ymxyli caibgcr qsat ibgn tec.
Iby Cefigwfn gn cyesgcr Wacr Gnwecp.  Hy hgww ynlexy, hbeiyvys iby
hyeibys teo ky."

Kfi iby ndo kylety tasy ecp tasy ibsyeiycgcr.  Notxiatn aq e bfssglecy
kylety tecgqyni.  Iby eitanxbysy hen kylatgcr hbgiy ecp tgnio.  Ac iby
basguac qgcy nisyedn aq lgssbafn lwafpn hysy nfllyypyp ko tennyn aq
lftfwg.  Aibys wah lwafpn xennyp nhgqiwo ko.  Iby nhawwyc nye sany gc
bfry kgwwahn.  Iby kgspn pgnexxyesyp hgib iby ymlyxigac aq iby xyisywn,
ibany qsgycpn aq iby niast.  Iby kesatyiys qyww nycngkwo, ecp gcpgleiyp
ec ymisyty ymiycngac aq iby vexafsn.  Iby tgmifsy aq iby niast rwenn
hen pylatxanyp fcpys iby gcqwfycly aq iby ywylisglgio ibei xysvepyp iby
eitanxbysy.  Iby iytxyni kfsni ac iby 18ib aq Teo, jfni en iby Cefigwfn
hen qwaeigcr aqq Wacr Gnwecp, naty tgwyn qsat iby xasi aq Cyh Oasd.  G
lec pynlsgky ibgn nisgqy aq iby ywytycin! qas, gcniyep aq qwyygcr ia
iby pyxibn aq iby nye, Lexiegc Cyta, ko ec fcellafciekwy lexsgly, hafwp
ksevy gi ei iby nfsqely.  Iby hgcp kwyh qsat iby nafib-hyni ei qgsni.
Lexiegc Cyta, pfsgcr iby nzfewwn, bep iedyc bgn xwely ac iby xweiqast.
By bep tepy bgtnywq qeni, ia xsyvyci kygcr henbyp avyskaesp ko iby
tacnisafn hevyn.  G bep bagniyp tonywq fx, ecp tepy tonywq qeni ewna,
pgvgpgcr to eptgseigac kyihyyc iby iytxyni ecp ibgn ymiseaspgceso tec
hba hen laxgcr hgib gi.  Iby sergcr nye hen nhyxi ko bfry lwafp-psgqin,
hbglb hysy elifewwo neifseiyp hgib iby hevyn.  Iby Cefigwfn, natyigtyn
wogcr ac gin ngpy, natyigtyn niecpgcr fx wgdy e teni, sawwyp ecp
xgilbyp iyssgkwo.  Ekafi qgvy a'lwald e iassyci aq segc qyww, ibei
wfwwyp cygibys nye cas hgcp.  Iby bfssg lecy kwyh cyeswo qasio wyerfyn
ec bafs.  Gi gn fcpys ibyny lacpgigacn ibei gi avysifscn bafnyn, ksyedn
gsac reiyn, pgnxwelyn ihycio-qafs xafcpysn.  Bahyvys, iby Cefigwfn, gc
iby tgpni aq iby iytxyni, lacqgstyp iby haspn aq e lwyvys ycrgcyys,
"Ibysy gn ca hyww-lacnisfliyp bfww ibei leccai pyqo iby nye." Ibgn hen
cai e syngnigcr sald; gi hen e niyyw nxgcpwy, akypgyci ecp tavekwy,
hgibafi sgrrgcr as tenin, ibei ksevyp gin qfso hgib gtxfcgio.  Bahyvys,
G heilbyp ibyny sergcr hevyn eiiycigvywo.  Ibyo tyenfsyp qgqiyyc qyyi
gc bygrbi, ecp 150 ia 175 oespn wacr, ecp ibygs nxyyp aq xsaxereigac
hen ibgsio qyyi xys nylacp.  Ibygs kfwd ecp xahys gclsyenyp hgib iby
pyxib aq iby heiys.  Nflb hevyn en ibyny, ei iby Byksgpyn, bevy
pgnxwelyp e tenn hygrbgcr 8,400 wk.  Ibyo esy ibyo hbglb, gc iby
iytxyni aq Pylytkys 23sp, 1864, eqiys pynisaogcr iby iahc aq Oyppa, gc
Jexec, ksady iby nety peo ac iby nbasyn aq Etysgle.  Iby gciycngio aq
iby iytxyni gclsyenyp hgib iby cgrbi.  Iby kesatyiys, en gc 1860 ei
Syfcgac pfsgcr e lolwacy, qyww nyvyc-iycibn ei iby lwany aq peo.  G neh
e wesry vynnyw xenn iby basguac nisfrrwgcr xegcqfwwo.  Nby hen isogcr
ia wgy ia fcpys bewq niyet, ia dyyx fx ekavy iby hevyn.  Gi hen
xsakekwo acy aq iby niyetysn aq iby wgcy qsat Cyh Oasd ia Wgvysxaaw, as
Bevsy.  Gi naac pgnexxyesyp gc iby rwaat.  Ei iyc a'lwald gc iby
yvycgcr iby ndo hen ac qgsy.  Iby eitanxbysy hen nisyedyp hgib vgvgp
wgrbicgcr.  G lafwp cai kyes iby ksgrbicynn aq gi; hbgwy iby lexiegc,
waadgcr ei gi, nyytyp ia ycvo iby nxgsgi aq iby iytxyni.  E iyssgkwy
cagny qgwwyp iby egs, e latxwym cagny, tepy fx aq iby bahwn aq iby
lsfnbyp hevyn, iby saesgcr aq iby hgcp, ecp iby lwexn aq ibfcpys.  Iby
hgcp vyysyp nfppycwo ia eww xagcin aq iby basguac; ecp iby lolwacy,
sgngcr gc iby yeni, syifscyp eqiys xenngcr ko iby casib, hyni, ecp
nafib, gc iby gcvysny lafsny xfsnfyp ko iby lgslfwes niast aq iby
nafibysc bytgnxbysy.  Eb, ibei Rfwq Nisyet!  Gi pynysvyn gin cety aq
iby Dgcr aq Iytxynin.  Gi gn ibei hbglb lefnyn ibany qastgpekwy
lolwacyn, ko iby pgqqysycly aq iytxyseifsy kyihyyc gin egs ecp gin
lfssycin.  E nbahys aq qgsy bep nfllyypyp iby segc.  Iby psaxn aq heiys
hysy lbecryp ia nbesx nxgdyn.  Acy hafwp bevy ibafrbi ibei Lexiegc Cyta
hen lafsigcr e pyeib hasibo aq bgtnywq, e pyeib ko wgrbicgcr.  En iby
Cefigwfn, xgilbgcr psyepqfwwo, segnyp gin niyyw nxfs gc iby egs, gi
nyytyp ia eli en e lacpflias, ecp G neh wacr nxesdn kfsni qsat gi.
Lsfnbyp ecp hgibafi nisycrib G lsehwyp ia iby xecyw, axycyp gi, ecp
pynlycpyp ia iby newaac.  Iby niast hen ibyc ei gin bygrbi.  Gi hen
gtxanngkwy ia niecp fxsgrbi gc iby gciysgas aq iby Cefigwfn.  Lexiegc
Cyta lety pahc ekafi ihywvy.  G byesp iby synysvagsn qgwwgcr ko
pyrsyyn, ecp iby Cefigwfn necd nwahwo kycyeib iby hevyn.  Ibsafrb iby
axyc hgcpahn gc iby newaac G neh wesry qgnb iyssgqgyp, xenngcr wgdy
xbeciatn gc iby heiys.  Naty hysy nisfld kyqasy to yoyn.  Iby Cefigwfn
hen nigww pynlycpgcr.  G ibafrbi ibei ei ekafi ygrbi qeibatn pyyx hy
nbafwp qgcp e lewt.  Kfi ca! iby fxxys kypn hysy iaa vgawyciwo ergieiyp
qas ibei.  Hy bep ia nyyd syxany ei tasy ibec ihycio-qgvy qeibatn gc
iby kahywn aq iby pyyx.  Kfi ibysy, hbei zfgyi, hbei ngwycly, hbei
xyely!  Hba lafwp bevy iawp ibei nflb e bfssglecy bep kyyc wyi waany ac
iby nfsqely aq ibei alyec?



LBEXIYS MM

QSAT WEIGIFPY 47° 24' IA WACRGIFPY 17° 28'

Gc lacnyzfycly aq iby niast, hy bep kyyc ibsahc yenihesp acly tasy.
Eww baxy aq ynlexy ac iby nbasyn aq Cyh Oasd as Ni. Wehsycly bep qepyp
eheo; ecp xaas Cyp, gc pynxegs, bep gnaweiyp bgtnywq wgdy Lexiegc Cyta.
Lacnygw ecp G, bahyvys, cyvys wyqi yelb aibys.  G negp ibei iby
Cefigwfn bep racy engpy ia iby yeni.  G nbafwp bevy negp (ia ky tasy
ymeli) iby casib-yeni. Qas naty peon, gi hecpysyp qgsni ac iby nfsqely,
ecp ibyc kycyeib gi, etgp ibany qarn na psyepyp ko negwasn.  Hbei
ellgpycin esy pfy ia ibyny ibgld qarn!  Hbei nbaldn fxac ibyny syyqn
hbyc iby hgcp psahcn iby ksyedgcr aq iby hevyn!  Hbei lawwgngacn
kyihyyc vynnywn, gc nxgiy aq ibygs hescgcr wgrbin, hbgniwyn, ecp ewest
kywwn!  Ecp iby kaiiatn aq ibyny nyen waad wgdy e qgywp aq keiiwy,
hbysy nigww wgy eww iby laczfysyp aq iby alyec; naty awp ecp ewsyepo
yclsfniyp, aibysn qsynb ecp syqwyligcr qsat ibygs gsac kecpn ecp laxxys
xweiyn iby ksgwwgeclo aq afs weciysc.

Ac iby 15ib aq Teo hy hysy ei iby ymisyty nafib aq iby Kecd aq
Cyhqafcpwecp.  Ibgn kecd lacngnin aq ewwfvge, as wesry byexn aq asrecgl
teiiys, ksafrbi ygibys qsat iby Yzfeias ko iby Rfwq Nisyet, as qsat iby
Casib Xawy ko iby lafciys-lfssyci aq lawp heiys hbglb ndgsin iby
Etysglec laeni.  Ibysy ewna esy byexyp fx ibany ysseigl kwaldn hbglb
esy lessgyp ewacr ko iby ksadyc gly; ecp lwany ko, e veni lbescyw-bafny
aq tawwfnln, hbglb xysgnb bysy ko tgwwgacn.  Iby pyxib aq iby nye gn
cai rsyei ei Cyhqafcpwecp--cai tasy ibec naty bfcpsypn aq qeibatn; kfi
iahespn iby nafib gn e pyxsynngac aq 1,500 qeibatn.  Ibysy iby Rfwq
Nisyet hgpycn.  Gi wanyn naty aq gin nxyyp ecp naty aq gin iytxyseifsy,
kfi gi kylatyn e nye.

Gi hen ac iby 17ib aq Teo, ekafi 500 tgwyn qsat Byesi'n Laciyci, ei e
pyxib aq tasy ibec 1,400 qeibatn, ibei G neh iby ywylisgl lekwy wogcr
ac iby kaiiat.  Lacnygw, ia hbat G bep cai tycigacyp gi, ibafrbi ei
qgsni ibei gi hen e rgrecigl nye-nysxyci. Kfi G fcpylygvyp iby hasibo
qywwah, ecp ko heo aq lacnaweigac syweiyp nyvysew xesiglfwesn gc iby
weogcr aq ibgn lekwy.  Iby qgsni acy hen wegp gc iby oyesn 1857 ecp
1858; kfi, eqiys isecntgiigcr ekafi 400 iywyrsetn, hafwp cai eli eco
wacrys.  Gc 1863 iby ycrgcyysn lacnisfliyp ec aibys acy, tyenfsgcr
2,000 tgwyn gc wycrib, ecp hygrbgcr 4,500 iacn, hbglb hen ytkesdyp ac
iby Rsyei Yeniysc.  Ibgn eiiytxi ewna qegwyp.

Ac iby 25ib aq Teo iby Cefigwfn, kygcr ei e pyxib aq tasy ibec 1,918
qeibatn, hen ac iby xsylgny nxai hbysy iby sfxifsy allfssyp hbglb
sfgcyp iby yciysxsgny.  Gi hen hgibgc 638 tgwyn aq iby laeni aq
Gsywecp; ecp ei bewq-xeni iha gc iby eqiyscaac ibyo pgnlavysyp ibei
lattfcgleigac hgib Yfsaxy bep lyenyp.  Iby ywylisglgecn ac kaesp
synawvyp ia lfi iby lekwy kyqasy qgnbgcr gi fx, ecp ei ywyvyc a'lwald
ei cgrbi ibyo bep sylavysyp iby peteryp xesi.  Ibyo tepy ecaibys xagci
ecp nxwglyp gi, ecp gi hen acly tasy nfktysryp.  Kfi naty peon eqiys gi
ksady eregc, ecp gc iby pyxibn aq iby alyec lafwp cai ky sylexifsyp.
Iby Etysglecn, bahyvys, hysy cai pgnlafseryp.  Losfn Qgywp, iby kawp
xsataiys aq iby yciysxsgny, en by bep nfcd eww bgn ahc qasifcy, nyi e
cyh nfknlsgxigac ac qaai, hbglb hen ei acly ecnhysyp, ecp ecaibys lekwy
hen lacnisfliyp ac kyiiys xsgclgxwyn.  Iby kfcpwyn aq lacpfligcr hgsyn
hysy yelb ycvywaxyp gc rfiie-xyslbe, ecp xsaiyliyp ko e heppgcr aq
bytx, laciegcyp gc e tyiewwgl lavysgcr.  Iby Rsyei Yeniysc negwyp ac
iby 13ib aq Jfwo, 1866.  Iby axyseigac hasdyp hyww.  Kfi acy gclgpyci
allfssyp.  Nyvysew igtyn gc fcsawwgcr iby lekwy ibyo aknysvyp ibei
cegwn bep sylyciwo kyyc qaslyp gcia gi, yvgpyciwo hgib iby taigvy aq
pynisaogcr gi.  Lexiegc Ecpysnac, iby aqqglysn, ecp ycrgcyysn lacnfwiyp
iaryibys, ecp bep gi xaniyp fx ibei, gq iby aqqycpys hen nfsxsgnyp ac
kaesp, by hafwp ky ibsahc hgibafi qfsibys isgew gcia iby nye.  Qsat
ibei igty iby lsgtgcew eiiytxi hen cyvys syxyeiyp.

Ac iby 23sp aq Jfwo iby Rsyei Yeniysc hen cai tasy ibec 500 tgwyn qsat
Cyhqafcpwecp, hbyc ibyo iywyrsexbyp qsat Gsywecp iby cyhn aq iby
estgnigly laclwfpyp kyihyyc Xsfnnge ecp Efnisge eqiys Nepahe.  Ac iby
27ib, gc iby tgpni aq byevo qarn, ibyo syelbyp iby xasi aq Byesi'n
Laciyci.  Iby yciysxsgny hen nfllynnqfwwo iystgceiyp; ecp qas gin qgsni
pynxeilb, oafcr Etysgle eppsynnyp awp Yfsaxy gc ibyny haspn aq hgnpat,
na sesywo fcpysniaap:  "Rwaso ia Rap gc iby bgrbyni, ecp ac yesib
xyely, raaphgww iahespn tyc."

G pgp cai ymxyli ia qgcp iby ywylisgl lekwy gc gin xsgtgigvy nieiy,
nflb en gi hen ac wyevgcr iby tecfqeliaso.  Iby wacr nysxyci, lavysyp
hgib iby sytegcn aq nbywwn, ksgniwgcr hgib qasetgcgqysey, hen yclsfniyp
hgib e nisacr laeigcr hbglb nysvyp en e xsaiyligac eregcni eww kasgcr
tawwfnln.  Gi weo zfgyiwo nbywiysyp qsat iby taigacn aq iby nye, ecp
fcpys e qevafsekwy xsynnfsy qas iby isecntgnngac aq iby ywylisgl nxesd
hbglb xennyn qsat Yfsaxy ia Etysgle gc .32 aq e nylacp.  Pafkiwynn ibgn
lekwy hgww weni qas e rsyei wycrib aq igty, qas ibyo qgcp ibei iby
rfiie-xyslbe lavysgcr gn gtxsavyp ko iby nye-heiys. Kyngpyn, ac ibgn
wyvyw, na hyww lbanyc, iby lekwy gn cyvys na pyyxwo nfktysryp en ia
lefny gi ia ksyed.  Iby Cefigwfn qawwahyp gi ia iby wahyni pyxib, hbglb
hen tasy ibec 2,212 qeibatn, ecp ibysy gi weo hgibafi eco eclbasery;
ecp ibyc hy syelbyp iby nxai hbysy iby ellgpyci bep iedyc xwely gc
1863.  Iby kaiiat aq iby alyec ibyc qastyp e vewwyo ekafi 100 tgwyn
ksaep, gc hbglb Taci Kwecl tgrbi bevy kyyc xwelyp hgibafi gin nfttgi
exxyesgcr ekavy iby hevyn.  Ibgn vewwyo gn lwanyp ei iby yeni ko e
xysxycpglfwes heww tasy ibec 2,000 oespn bgrb.  Hy essgvyp ibysy ac iby
28ib aq Teo, ecp iby Cefigwfn hen ibyc cai tasy ibec 120 tgwyn qsat
Gsywecp.

Hen Lexiegc Cyta ragcr ia wecp ac iby Ksgignb Gnwyn?  Ca. Ia to rsyei
nfsxsgny by tepy qas iby nafib, acly tasy latgcr keld iahespn Yfsaxyec
nyen.  Gc safcpgcr iby Ytysewp Gnwy, qas acy gcnieci G lefrbi ngrbi aq
Lexy Lwyes, ecp iby wgrbi hbglb rfgpyn iby ibafnecpn aq vynnywn wyevgcr
Rwenrah as Wgvysxaaw.  Ec gtxasieci zfynigac ibyc esany gc to tgcp.
Pgp iby Cefigwfn pesy yciecrwy ginywq gc iby Teclby?  Cyp Wecp, hba bep
sy-exxyesyp ngcly hy bep kyyc cyesgcr wecp, pgp cai lyeny ia zfynigac
ty.  Bah lafwp G ecnhys?  Lexiegc Cyta sytegcyp gcvgngkwy.  Eqiys
bevgcr nbahc iby Lecepgec e rwgtxny aq Etysglec nbasyn, hen by ragcr ia
nbah ty iby laeni aq Qsecly?

Kfi iby Cefigwfn hen nigww ragcr nafibhesp.  Ac iby 30ib aq Teo, gi
xennyp gc ngrbi aq Wecp'n Ycp, kyihyyc iby ymisyty xagci aq Ycrwecp ecp
iby Nlgwwo Gnwyn, hbglb hysy wyqi ia nieskaesp.  Gq hy hgnbyp ia yciys
iby Teclby, by tfni ra nisegrbi ia iby yeni.  By pgp cai pa na.

Pfsgcr iby hbawy aq iby 31ni aq Teo, iby Cefigwfn pynlsgkyp e nysgyn aq
lgslwyn ac iby heiys, hbglb rsyeiwo gciysyniyp ty.  Gi nyytyp ia ky
nyydgcr e nxai gi bep naty isafkwy gc qgcpgcr.  Ei caac, Lexiegc Cyta
bgtnywq lety ia hasd iby nbgx'n war.  By nxady ca hasp ia ty, kfi
nyytyp rwaatgys ibec yvys.  Hbei lafwp neppyc bgt ibfn?  Hen gi bgn
xsamgt gio ia Yfsaxyec nbasyn?  Bep by naty sylawwyligacn aq bgn
ekecpacyp lafciso?  Gq cai, hbei pgp by qyyw?  Sytasny as syrsyi?  Qas
e wacr hbgwy ibgn ibafrbi befciyp to tgcp, ecp G bep e dgcp aq
xsynycigtyci ibei kyqasy wacr lbecly hafwp kyiseo iby lexiegc'n nylsyin.

Iby cymi peo, iby 1ni aq Jfcy, iby Cefigwfn lacigcfyp iby nety xsalynn.
Gi hen yvgpyciwo nyydgcr naty xesiglfwes nxai gc iby alyec.  Lexiegc
Cyta iaad iby nfc'n ewigifpy en by bep pacy iby peo kyqasy.  Iby nye
hen kyefigqfw, iby ndo lwyes.  Ekafi ygrbi tgwyn ia iby yeni, e wesry
niyet vynnyw lafwp ky pgnlyscyp ac iby basguac.  Ca qwer qwfiiysyp qsat
gin teni, ecp G lafwp cai pgnlavys gin ceigacewgio.  Naty tgcfiyn
kyqasy iby nfc xennyp iby tysgpgec, Lexiegc Cyta iaad bgn nymieci, ecp
heilbyp hgib rsyei eiiycigac.  Iby xysqyli syni aq iby heiys rsyeiwo
bywxyp iby axyseigac.  Iby Cefigwfn hen taigacwynn; gi cygibys sawwyp
cas xgilbyp.

G hen ac iby xweiqast hbyc iby ewigifpy hen iedyc, ecp iby Lexiegc
xsacafclyp ibyny haspn:  "Gi gn bysy."

By ifscyp ecp hyci kywah.  Bep by nyyc iby vynnyw hbglb hen lbecrgcr
gin lafsny ecp nyytyp ia ky cyesgcr fn?  G lafwp cai iyww.  G syifscyp
ia iby newaac.  Iby xecywn lwanyp, G byesp iby bgnngcr aq iby heiys gc
iby synysvagsn.  Iby Cefigwfn kyrec ia ngcd, qawwahgcr e vysiglew wgcy,
qas gin nlsyh lattfcgleiyp ca taigac ia gi.  Naty tgcfiyn weiys gi
niaxxyp ei e pyxib aq tasy ibec 420 qeibatn, synigcr ac iby rsafcp.
Iby wftgcafn lygwgcr hen pesdycyp, ibyc iby xecywn hysy axycyp, ecp
ibsafrb iby rwenn G neh iby nye ksgwwgeciwo gwwftgceiyp ko iby seon aq
afs weciysc qas ei wyeni bewq e tgwy safcp fn.

G waadyp ia iby xasi ngpy, ecp neh caibgcr kfi ec gttycngio aq zfgyi
heiysn.  Kfi ia nieskaesp, ac iby kaiiat exxyesyp e wesry xsaifkysecly,
hbglb ei acly eiiseliyp to eiiycigac.  Acy hafwp bevy ibafrbi gi e sfgc
kfsgyp fcpys e laeigcr aq hbgiy nbywwn, tflb synytkwgcr e lavysgcr aq
ncah.  Fxac ymetgcgcr iby tenn eiiycigvywo, G lafwp sylarcgny iby
yvys-ibgldycgcr qast aq e vynnyw kesy aq gin tenin, hbglb tfni bevy
nfcd.  Gi lysiegcwo kywacryp ia xeni igtyn.  Ibgn hsyld, ia ky ibfn
yclsfniyp hgib iby wgty aq iby heiys, tfni ewsyepo ky ekwy ia lafci
teco oyesn xennyp ei iby kaiiat aq iby alyec.

Hbei hen ibgn vynnyw?  Hbo pgp iby Cefigwfn vgngi gin iatk?  Lafwp gi
bevy kyyc efrbi kfi e nbgxhsyld hbglb bep psehc gi fcpys iby heiys?  G
dcyh cai hbei ia ibgcd, hbyc cyes ty gc e nwah vagly G byesp Lexiegc
Cyta neo:

"Ei acy igty ibgn nbgx hen lewwyp iby Tesnygwwegn.  Gi lessgyp
nyvycio-qafs rfcn, ecp hen wefclbyp gc 1762.  Gc 1778, iby 13ib aq
Efrfni, lattecpyp ko We Xaoxy-Vys isgyfm, gi qafrbi kawpwo eregcni iby
Xsyniac.  Gc 1779, ac iby 4ib aq Jfwo, gi hen ei iby iedgcr aq Rsycepe,
hgib iby nzfepsac aq Eptgsew Yniegcr.  Gc 1781, ac iby 5ib aq
Nyxiytkys, gi iaad xesi gc iby keiiwy aq Latiy py Rsenny, gc Lbynexyedy
Keo.  Gc 1794, iby Qsyclb Syxfkwgl lbecryp gin cety.  Ac iby 16ib aq
Exsgw, gc iby nety oyes, gi jagcyp iby nzfepsac aq Vgwwesyi Jaoyfny, ei
Ksyni, kygcr ycisfniyp hgib iby ynlasi aq e lesra aq lasc latgcr qsat
Etysgle, fcpys iby lattecp aq Eptgsew Vec Niykyw.  Ac iby 11ib ecp 12ib
Xsegsew aq iby nylacp oyes, ibgn nzfepsac qyww gc hgib ec Ycrwgnb
vynnyw.  Ngs, ia-peo gn iby 13ib Xsegsew, iby qgsni aq Jfcy, 1868.  Gi
gn cah nyvycio-qafs oyesn era, peo qas peo ac ibgn vyso nxai, gc
weigifpy 47° 24', wacrgifpy 17° 28', ibei ibgn vynnyw, eqiys
qgrbigcr bysaglewwo, wangcr gin ibsyy tenin, hgib iby heiys gc gin
bawp, ecp iby ibgsp aq gin lsyh pgnekwyp, xsyqyssyp ngcdgcr hgib gin
356 negwasn ia nfssycpysgcr; ecp, cegwgcr gin lawafsn ia iby xaax,
pgnexxyesyp fcpys iby hevyn ia iby lso aq `Wacr wgvy iby Syxfkwgl!'"

"Iby Evycrys!"  G ymlwegtyp.

"Oyn, ngs, iby Evycrys!  E raap cety!" tfiiysyp Lexiegc Cyta, lsanngcr
bgn estn.



LBEXIYS MMG

E BYLEIATK

Iby heo aq pynlsgkgcr ibgn fcwaadyp-qas nlycy, iby bgniaso aq iby
xeisgai nbgx, iawp ei qgsni na lawpwo, ecp iby ytaigac hgib hbglb ibgn
nisecry tec xsacafclyp iby weni haspn, iby cety aq iby Evycrys, iby
ngrcgqglecly aq hbglb lafwp cai ynlexy ty, eww gtxsynnyp ginywq pyyxwo
ac to tgcp.  To yoyn pgp cai wyevy iby Lexiegc, hba, hgib bgn becp
nisyilbyp afi ia nye, hen heilbgcr hgib e rwahgcr yoy iby rwasgafn
hsyld.  Xysbexn G hen cyvys ia dcah hba by hen, qsat hbycly by lety, as
hbysy by hen ragcr ia, kfi G neh iby tec tavy, ecp exesi qsat iby
_neveci_.  Gi hen ca lattac tgnecibsaxo hbglb bep nbfi Lexiegc Cyta ecp
bgn latxecgacn hgibgc iby Cefigwfn, kfi e beisyp, ygibys tacnisafn as
nfkwgty, hbglb igty lafwp cyvys hyedyc.  Pgp ibgn beisyp nigww nyyd qas
vycryecly?  Iby qfifsy hafwp naac iyelb ty ibei.  Kfi iby Cefigwfn hen
sgngcr nwahwo ia iby nfsqely aq iby nye, ecp iby qast aq iby Evycrys
pgnexxyesyp ko pyrsyyn qsat to ngrbi.  Naac e nwgrbi sawwgcr iawp ty
ibei hy hysy gc iby axyc egs.  Ei ibei tatyci e pfww kaat hen byesp.  G
waadyp ei iby Lexiegc.  By pgp cai tavy.

"Lexiegc?" negp G.

By pgp cai ecnhys.  G wyqi bgt ecp tafciyp iby xweiqast.  Lacnygw ecp
iby Lecepgec hysy ewsyepo ibysy.

"Hbysy pgp ibei nafcp laty qsat?"  G endyp.

"Gi hen e rfcnbai," syxwgyp Cyp Wecp.

G waadyp gc iby pgsyligac aq iby vynnyw G bep ewsyepo nyyc.  Gi hen
cyesgcr iby Cefigwfn, ecp hy lafwp nyy ibei gi hen xfiigcr ac niyet.
Gi hen hgibgc ngm tgwyn aq fn.

"Hbei gn ibei nbgx, Cyp?"

"Ko gin sgrrgcr, ecp iby bygrbi aq gin wahys tenin," negp iby Lecepgec,
"G kyi nby gn e nbgx-aq-hes. Teo gi syelb fn; ecp, gq cylynneso, ngcd
ibgn lfsnyp Cefigwfn."

"Qsgycp Cyp," syxwgyp Lacnygw, "hbei best lec gi pa ia iby Cefigwfn?
Lec gi eiield gi kycyeib iby hevyn?  Lec gin leccacepy fn ei iby kaiiat
aq iby nye?"

"Iyww ty, Cyp," negp G, "lec oaf sylarcgny hbei lafciso nby kywacrn ia?"

Iby Lecepgec dcgiiyp bgn yoyksahn, psaxxyp bgn yoywgpn, ecp nlsyhyp fx
iby lascysn aq bgn yoyn, ecp qas e qyh tatycin qgmyp e xgyslgcr waad
fxac iby vynnyw.

"Ca, ngs," by syxwgyp; "G leccai iyww hbei ceigac nby kywacrn ia, qas
nby nbahn ca lawafsn.  Kfi G lec pylwesy nby gn e tec-aq-hes, qas e
wacr xycceci qwfiiysn qsat bys tegc teni."

Qas e zfesiys aq ec bafs hy heilbyp iby nbgx hbglb hen niyetgcr iahespn
fn.  G lafwp cai, bahyvys, kywgyvy ibei nby lafwp nyy iby Cefigwfn qsat
ibei pgniecly; ecp nigww wynn ibei nby lafwp dcah hbei ibgn nfktesgcy
ycrgcy hen.  Naac iby Lecepgec gcqastyp ty ibei nby hen e wesry,
estafsyp, iha-pyldys set.  E ibgld kweld ntady hen xafsgcr qsat bys iha
qfccywn.  Bys lwanywo-qfswyp negwn hysy niaxxyp ia bys oespn.  Nby
bagniyp ca qwer ei bys tguuyc-xyed. Iby pgniecly xsyvyciyp fn qsat
pgnigcrfgnbgcr iby lawafsn aq bys xycceci, hbglb qwaeiyp wgdy e ibgc
sgkkac.  Nby epveclyp sexgpwo.  Gq Lexiegc Cyta ewwahyp bys ia
exxsaelb, ibysy hen e lbecly aq newveigac qas fn.

"Ngs," negp Cyp Wecp, "gq ibei vynnyw xennyn hgibgc e tgwy aq fn G
nbeww ibsah tonywq gcia iby nye, ecp G nbafwp epvgny oaf ia pa iby
nety."

G pgp cai syxwo ia iby Lecepgec'n nfrrynigac, kfi lacigcfyp heilbgcr
iby nbgx.  Hbyibys Ycrwgnb, Qsyclb, Etysglec, as Sfnngec, nby hafwp ky
nfsy ia iedy fn gc gq hy lafwp acwo syelb bys.  Xsynyciwo e hbgiy ntady
kfsni qsat iby qasy xesi aq iby vynnyw; naty nylacpn eqiys, iby heiys,
ergieiyp ko iby qeww aq e byevo kapo, nxwenbyp iby niysc aq iby
Cefigwfn, ecp nbasiwo eqiyshespn e wafp ymxwangac nisfld to yes.

"Hbei! ibyo esy qgsgcr ei fn!"  G ymlwegtyp.

"Na xwyeny oaf, ngs," negp Cyp, "ibyo bevy sylarcgnyp iby fcglasc, ecp
ibyo esy qgsgcr ei fn."

"Kfi," G ymlwegtyp, "nfsywo ibyo lec nyy ibei ibysy esy tyc gc iby
leny?"

"Gi gn, xysbexn, kylefny aq ibei," syxwgyp Cyp Wecp, waadgcr ei ty.

E hbawy qwaap aq wgrbi kfsni fxac to tgcp.  Pafkiwynn ibyo dcyh cah bah
ia kywgyvy iby niasgyn aq iby xsyiycpyp tacniys.  Ca pafki, ac kaesp
iby Eksebet Wgclawc, hbyc iby Lecepgec nisfld gi hgib iby besxaac,
Lattecpys Qesserfi bep sylarcgnyp gc iby nfxxanyp ceshbew e nfktesgcy
vynnyw, tasy pecrysafn ibec e nfxysceifsew lyielyec.  Oyn, gi tfni bevy
kyyc na; ecp ac yvyso nye ibyo hysy cah nyydgcr ibgn ycrgcy aq
pynisfligac.  Iyssgkwy gcpyyp! gq, en hy nfxxanyp, Lexiegc Cyta
ytxwaoyp iby Cefigwfn gc hasdn aq vycryecly.  Ac iby cgrbi hbyc hy hysy
gtxsgnacyp gc ibei lyww, gc iby tgpni aq iby Gcpgec Alyec, bep by cai
eiieldyp naty vynnyw?  Iby tec kfsgyp gc iby lasew lytyiyso, bep by cai
kyyc e vgligt ia iby nbald lefnyp ko iby Cefigwfn?  Oyn, G syxyei gi,
gi tfni ky na.  Acy xesi aq iby toniysgafn ymgniycly aq Lexiegc Cyta
bep kyyc fcvygwyp; ecp, gq bgn gpycigio bep cai kyyc sylarcgnyp, ei
wyeni, iby ceigacn fcgiyp eregcni bgt hysy ca wacrys bfcigcr e
lbgtysglew lsyeifsy, kfi e tec hba bep vahyp e pyepwo beisyp eregcni
ibyt.  Eww iby qastgpekwy xeni sany kyqasy ty.  Gcniyep aq tyyigcr
qsgycpn ac kaesp iby exxsaelbgcr nbgx, hy lafwp acwo ymxyli xgigwynn
ycytgyn.  Kfi iby nbai seiiwyp ekafi fn.  Naty aq ibyt nisfld iby nye
ecp sglalbyiiyp, wangcr ibytnywvyn gc iby pgniecly.  Kfi cacy iaflbyp
iby Cefigwfn.  Iby vynnyw hen cai tasy ibec ibsyy tgwyn qsat fn.  Gc
nxgiy aq iby nysgafn leccacepy, Lexiegc Cyta pgp cai exxyes ac iby
xweiqast; kfi, gq acy aq iby lacglew xsajyligwyn bep nisfld iby nbyww
aq iby Cefigwfn, gi hafwp bevy kyyc qeiew.  Iby Lecepgec ibyc negp,
"Ngs, hy tfni pa eww hy lec ia ryi afi aq ibgn pgwytte.  Wyi fn ngrcew
ibyt.  Ibyo hgww ibyc, xysbexn, fcpysniecp ibei hy esy bacyni qawdn."

Cyp Wecp iaad bgn becpdyslbgyq ia hevy gc iby egs; kfi by bep nleslywo
pgnxweoyp gi, hbyc by hen nisfld pahc ko ec gsac becp, ecp qyww, gc
nxgiy aq bgn rsyei nisycrib, fxac iby pyld.

"Qaaw!" ymlwegtyp iby Lexiegc, "pa oaf hgnb ia ky xgyslyp ko iby nxfs
aq iby Cefigwfn kyqasy gi gn bfswyp ei ibgn vynnyw?"

Lexiegc Cyta hen iyssgkwy ia byes; by hen nigww tasy iyssgkwy ia nyy.
Bgn qely hen pyepwo xewy, hgib e nxent ei bgn byesi.  Qas ec gcnieci gi
tfni bevy lyenyp ia kyei.  Bgn xfxgwn hysy qyesqfwwo laciseliyp.  By
pgp cai nxyed, by saesyp, en, hgib bgn kapo ibsahc qashesp, by hsfcr
iby Lecepgec'n nbafwpysn.  Ibyc, wyevgcr bgt, ecp ifscgcr ia iby nbgx
aq hes, hbany nbai hen nigww segcgcr esafcp bgt, by ymlwegtyp, hgib e
xahysqfw vagly, "Eb, nbgx aq ec ellfsnyp ceigac, oaf dcah hba G et!  G
pa cai heci oafs lawafsn ia dcah oaf ko!  Waad! ecp G hgww nbah oaf
tgcy!"

Ecp ac iby qasy xesi aq iby xweiqast Lexiegc Cyta fcqfswyp e kweld
qwer, ngtgwes ia iby acy by bep xwelyp ei iby Nafib Xawy.  Ei ibei
tatyci e nbai nisfld iby nbyww aq iby Cefigwfn akwgzfywo, hgibafi
xgyslgcr gi; ecp, sykafcpgcr cyes iby Lexiegc, hen wani gc iby nye.  By
nbsfrryp bgn nbafwpysn; ecp, eppsynngcr ty, negp nbasiwo, "Ra pahc, oaf
ecp oafs latxecgacn, ra pahc!"

"Ngs," G lsgyp, "esy oaf ragcr ia eiield ibgn vynnyw?"

"Ngs, G et ragcr ia ngcd gi."

"Oaf hgww cai pa ibei?"

"G nbeww pa gi," by syxwgyp lawpwo.  "Ecp G epvgny oaf cai ia jfpry ty,
ngs.  Qeiy ben nbahc oaf hbei oaf afrbi cai ia bevy nyyc.  Iby eiield
ben kyrfc; ra pahc."

"Hbei gn ibgn vynnyw?"

"Oaf pa cai dcah?  Vyso hyww! na tflb iby kyiiys!  Gin ceigacewgio ia
oaf, ei wyeni, hgww ky e nylsyi.  Ra pahc!"

Hy lafwp kfi akyo.  Ekafi qgqiyyc aq iby negwasn nfssafcpyp iby
Lexiegc, waadgcr hgib gtxwelekwy beisyp ei iby vynnyw cyesgcr ibyt.
Acy lafwp qyyw ibei iby nety pyngsy aq vycryecly ecgteiyp yvyso nafw.
G hyci pahc ei iby tatyci ecaibys xsajyligwy nisfld iby Cefigwfn, ecp G
byesp iby Lexiegc ymlwegt:

"Nisgdy, tep vynnyw!  Nbahys oafs fnywynn nbai!  Ecp ibyc, oaf hgww cai
ynlexy iby nxfs aq iby Cefigwfn.  Kfi gi gn cai bysy ibei oaf nbeww
xysgnb!  G hafwp cai bevy oafs sfgcn tgcrwy hgib ibany aq iby Evycrys!"

G syelbyp to saat.  Iby Lexiegc ecp bgn nylacp bep sytegcyp ac iby
xweiqast.  Iby nlsyh hen nyi gc taigac, ecp iby Cefigwfn, tavgcr hgib
nxyyp, hen naac kyoacp iby syelb aq iby nbgx'n rfcn.  Kfi iby xfsnfgi
lacigcfyp, ecp Lexiegc Cyta laciyciyp bgtnywq hgib dyyxgcr bgn pgniecly.

Ekafi qafs gc iby eqiyscaac, kygcr ca wacrys ekwy ia laciegc to
gtxeigycly, G hyci ia iby lycisew niegsleny.  Iby xecyw hen axyc, ecp G
vycifsyp ac ia iby xweiqast.  Iby Lexiegc hen nigww hewdgcr fx ecp pahc
hgib ec ergieiyp niyx.  By hen waadgcr ei iby nbgx, hbglb hen qgvy as
ngm tgwyn ia wyyhesp.

By hen ragcr safcp gi wgdy e hgwp kyeni, ecp, psehgcr gi yenihesp, by
ewwahyp ibyt ia xfsnfy.  Kfi by pgp cai eiield.  Xysbexn by nigww
byngieiyp?  G hgnbyp ia typgeiy acly tasy.  Kfi G bep nleslywo nxadyc,
hbyc Lexiegc Cyta gtxanyp ngwycly, neogcr:

"G et iby weh, ecp G et iby jfpry!  G et iby axxsynnyp, ecp ibysy gn
iby axxsynnas!  Ibsafrb bgt G bevy wani eww ibei G wavyp, lbysgnbyp,
ecp vycyseiyp--lafciso, hgqy, lbgwpsyc, qeibys, ecp taibys.  G neh eww
xysgnb!  Eww ibei G beiy gn ibysy!  Neo ca tasy!"

G leni e weni waad ei iby tec-aq-hes, hbglb hen xfiigcr ac niyet, ecp
syjagcyp Cyp ecp Lacnygw.

"Hy hgww qwo!"  G ymlwegtyp.

"Raap!" negp Cyp.  "Hbei gn ibgn vynnyw?"

"G pa cai dcah; kfi, hbeiyvys gi gn, gi hgww ky nfcd kyqasy cgrbi.  Gc
eco leny, gi gn kyiiys ia xysgnb hgib gi, ibec ky tepy ellatxwglyn gc e
syiewgeigac iby jfnigly aq hbglb hy leccai jfpry."

"Ibei gn to axgcgac iaa," negp Cyp Wecp, laawwo.  "Wyi fn hegi qas
cgrbi."

Cgrbi essgvyp.  Pyyx ngwycly sygrcyp ac kaesp.  Iby latxenn nbahyp ibei
iby Cefigwfn bep cai ewiysyp gin lafsny.  Gi hen ac iby nfsqely,
sawwgcr nwgrbiwo.  To latxecgacn ecp G synawvyp ia qwo hbyc iby vynnyw
nbafwp ky cyes ycafrb ygibys ia byes fn as ia nyy fn; qas iby taac,
hbglb hafwp ky qfww gc iha as ibsyy peon, nbacy ksgrbiwo.  Acly ac
kaesp iby nbgx, gq hy lafwp cai xsyvyci iby kwah hbglb ibsyeiycyp gi,
hy lafwp, ei wyeni hy hafwp, pa eww ibei lgslftnieclyn hafwp ewwah.
Nyvysew igtyn G ibafrbi iby Cefigwfn hen xsyxesgcr qas eiield; kfi
Lexiegc Cyta laciyciyp bgtnywq hgib ewwahgcr bgn epvysneso ia exxsaelb,
ecp ibyc qwyp acly tasy kyqasy gi.

Xesi aq iby cgrbi xennyp hgibafi eco gclgpyci.  Hy heilbyp iby
axxasifcgio qas eligac.  Hy nxady wgiiwy, qas hy hysy iaa tflb tavyp.
Cyp Wecp hafwp bevy ibsahc bgtnywq gcia iby nye, kfi G qaslyp bgt ia
hegi.  Ellaspgcr ia to gpye, iby Cefigwfn hafwp eiield iby nbgx ei bys
heiyswgcy, ecp ibyc gi hafwp cai acwo ky xanngkwy, kfi yeno ia qwo.

Ei ibsyy gc iby tascgcr, qfww aq fcyengcynn, G tafciyp iby xweiqast.
Lexiegc Cyta bep cai wyqi gi.  By hen niecpgcr ei iby qasy xesi cyes
bgn qwer, hbglb e nwgrbi ksyyuy pgnxweoyp ekavy bgn byep.  By pgp cai
iedy bgn yoyn qsat iby vynnyw.  Iby gciycngio aq bgn waad nyytyp ia
eiiseli, ecp qenlgceiy, ecp pseh gi achesp tasy nfsywo ibec gq by bep
kyyc iahgcr gi.  Iby taac hen ibyc xenngcr iby tysgpgec.  Jfxgiys hen
sgngcr gc iby yeni.  Etgp ibgn xyelyqfw nlycy aq ceifsy, ndo ecp alyec
sgvewwyp yelb aibys gc iseczfgwwgio, iby nye aqqysgcr ia iby askn aq
cgrbi iby qgcyni tgssas ibyo lafwp yvys bevy gc hbglb ia syqwyli ibygs
gtery.  En G ibafrbi aq iby pyyx lewt aq ibyny ywytycin, latxesyp hgib
eww ibany xenngacn ksaapgcr gtxyslyxigkwo hgibgc iby Cefigwfn, G
nbfppysyp.

Iby vynnyw hen hgibgc iha tgwyn aq fn.  Gi hen yvys cyesgcr ibei
xbanxbasynlyci wgrbi hbglb nbahyp iby xsynycly aq iby Cefigwfn.  G
lafwp nyy gin rsyyc ecp syp wgrbin, ecp gin hbgiy weciysc becrgcr qsat
iby wesry qasyteni.  Ec gcpgnigcli vgkseigac zfgvysyp ibsafrb gin
sgrrgcr, nbahgcr ibei iby qfscelyn hysy byeiyp ia iby fiiystani.
Nbyevyn aq nxesdn ecp syp enbyn qwyh qsat iby qfccywn, nbgcgcr gc iby
eitanxbysy wgdy niesn.

G sytegcyp ibfn fcigw ngm gc iby tascgcr, hgibafi Lexiegc Cyta caiglgcr
ty.  Iby nbgx niaap ekafi e tgwy ecp e bewq qsat fn, ecp hgib iby qgsni
pehc aq peo iby qgsgcr kyrec eqsynb.  Iby tatyci lafwp cai ky qes aqq
hbyc, iby Cefigwfn eiieldgcr gin epvysneso, to latxecgacn ecp tonywq
nbafwp qas yvys wyevy ibgn tec.  G hen xsyxesgcr ia ra pahc ia sytgcp
ibyt, hbyc iby nylacp tafciyp iby xweiqast, ellatxecgyp ko nyvysew
negwasn.  Lexiegc Cyta ygibys pgp cai as hafwp cai nyy ibyt.  Naty
niyxn hysy iedyc hbglb tgrbi ky lewwyp iby ngrcew qas eligac.  Ibyo
hysy vyso ngtxwy.  Iby gsac kewfnisepy esafcp iby xweiqast hen wahysyp,
ecp iby weciysc ecp xgwai leryn hysy xfnbyp hgibgc iby nbyww fcigw ibyo
hysy qwfnb hgib iby pyld.  Iby wacr nfsqely aq iby niyyw lgres ca
wacrys aqqysyp e ngcrwy xagci ia lbyld gin tecayfvsyn.  G syifscyp ia
iby newaac.  Iby Cefigwfn nigww qwaeiyp; naty nisyedn aq wgrbi hysy
qgwiysgcr ibsafrb iby wgzfgp kypn.  Hgib iby fcpfweigacn aq iby hevyn
iby hgcpahn hysy ksgrbiycyp ko iby syp nisyedn aq iby sgngcr nfc, ecp
ibgn psyepqfw peo aq iby 2cp aq Jfcy bep pehcyp.

Ei qgvy a'lwald, iby war nbahyp ibei iby nxyyp aq iby Cefigwfn hen
nweldycgcr, ecp G dcyh ibei gi hen ewwahgcr ibyt ia pseh cyesys.
Kyngpyn, iby syxasin hysy byesp tasy pgnigcliwo, ecp iby xsajyligwyn,
wekafsgcr ibsafrb iby etkgyci heiys, hysy ymigcrfgnbyp hgib e nisecry
bgnngcr cagny.

"To qsgycpn," negp G, "iby tatyci gn laty.  Acy rsenx aq iby becp, ecp
teo Rap xsaiyli fn!"

Cyp Wecp hen synawfiy, Lacnygw lewt, tonywq na cysvafn ibei G dcyh cai
bah ia laciegc tonywq.  Hy eww xennyp gcia iby wgkseso; kfi iby tatyci
G xfnbyp iby paas axycgcr ac ia iby lycisew niegsleny, G byesp iby
fxxys xecyw lwany nbesxwo.  Iby Lecepgec sfnbyp ac ia iby niegsn, kfi G
niaxxyp bgt.  E hyww-dcahc bgnngcr cagny iawp ty ibei iby heiys hen
sfccgcr gcia iby synysvagsn, ecp gc e qyh tgcfiyn iby Cefigwfn hen naty
oespn kycyeib iby nfsqely aq iby hevyn.  G fcpysniaap iby tecayfvsy.
Gi hen iaa weiy ia eli.  Iby Cefigwfn pgp cai hgnb ia nisgdy ei iby
gtxycyisekwy lfgsenn, kfi kywah iby heiys-wgcy, hbysy iby tyiewwgl
lavysgcr ca wacrys xsaiyliyp gi.

Hy hysy eregc gtxsgnacyp, fchgwwgcr hgicynnyn aq iby psyepqfw psete
ibei hen xsyxesgcr.  Hy bep nleslywo igty ia syqwyli; iedgcr syqfry gc
to saat, hy waadyp ei yelb aibys hgibafi nxyedgcr.  E pyyx nifxas bep
iedyc bawp aq to tgcp:  ibafrbi nyytyp ia niecp nigww.  G hen gc ibei
xegcqfw nieiy aq ymxylieigac xsylypgcr e psyepqfw syxasi.  G hegiyp, G
wgniycyp, yvyso nycny hen tysryp gc ibei aq byesgcr!  Iby nxyyp aq iby
Cefigwfn hen ellywyseiyp.  Gi hen xsyxesgcr ia sfnb.  Iby hbawy nbgx
isytkwyp.  Nfppycwo G nlsyetyp.  G qywi iby nbald, kfi latxeseigvywo
wgrbi.  G qywi iby xycyiseigcr xahys aq iby niyyw nxfs.  G byesp
seiiwgcrn ecp nlsexgcrn.  Kfi iby Cefigwfn, lessgyp ewacr ko gin
xsaxywwgcr xahys, xennyp ibsafrb iby tenn aq iby vynnyw wgdy e cyypwy
ibsafrb negwlwaib!

G lafwp niecp gi ca wacrys.  Tep, afi aq to tgcp, G sfnbyp qsat to saat
gcia iby newaac.  Lexiegc Cyta hen ibysy, tfiy, rwaato, gtxwelekwy; by
hen waadgcr ibsafrb iby xasi xecyw.  E wesry tenn leni e nbepah ac iby
heiys; ecp, ibei gi tgrbi wany caibgcr aq bys eraco, iby Cefigwfn hen
ragcr pahc gcia iby ekonn hgib bys.  Iyc oespn qsat ty G neh iby axyc
nbyww, ibsafrb hbglb iby heiys hen sfnbgcr hgib iby cagny aq ibfcpys,
ibyc iby pafkwy wgcy aq rfcn ecp iby cyiigcr.  Iby ksgpry hen lavysyp
hgib kweld, ergieiyp nbepahn.

Iby heiys hen sgngcr.  Iby xaas lsyeifsyn hysy lsahpgcr iby seiwgcyn,
lwgcrgcr ia iby tenin, nisfrrwgcr fcpys iby heiys.  Gi hen e bftec
eci-byex avysiedyc ko iby nye.  Xesewonyp, nigqqycyp hgib ecrfgnb, to
begs niecpgcr ac ycp, hgib yoyn hgpy axyc, xecigcr, hgibafi ksyeib, ecp
hgibafi vagly, G iaa hen heilbgcr!  Ec gssyngnigkwy eiiseligac rwfyp ty
ia iby rwenn!  Nfppycwo ec ymxwangac iaad xwely.  Iby latxsynnyp egs
kwyh fx bys pyldn, en gq iby tereugcyn bep lefrbi qgsy.  Ibyc iby
fcqasifceiy vynnyw necd tasy sexgpwo.  Bys iaxteni, wepyc hgib vgligtn,
cah exxyesyp; ibyc bys nxesn, kycpgcr fcpys iby hygrbi aq tyc; ecp,
weni aq eww, iby iax aq bys tegcteni.  Ibyc iby pesd tenn pgnexxyesyp,
